Sole Proprietor of Copyright  
**Panditabhushana V. SUBRAHMANYA SASTRI**  
65, 3rd Cross Road, Basavangudi  
**Bangalore—4**

**INTRODUCTION**  
**\_\_\_\_**

 It is with pleasure that we place this new work, *viz*. Horasara **होरासार** with English translation, etc.. before the learned public, inasmuch as this was a mere name for a long time past just like the works of the celebrated Bhasa (**भास**). That this is an ancient authoritative work is evidenced by the fact that the learned Mantreswara embodies in his Phaladeepika, Adhyaya XXIV, the effects of the Ashtakavarga found in this work, *viz*., Horasara, with due acknowledgment. It is a well-known fact among astrologers that Mantreswara was a true follower of the great Varahamihira and Kalyanavarman. From this, it is clear that the author of Phaladeepika held the Hora-sara in high esteem; and this fact redounds to the glory of the present work.

 The editor of the journal of the Maharaja’s Sanskrit College, Mysore, has earned the gratitude of the public by bringing to light for the first time this valuable work on Astrology. This work purports to be written by no less a person than Prithuyasas, son of the celebrated astronomer of Ujjain, *viz*., Varahamihira; for in the colophon at the end of every Chapter, we read that this work has been written by Prithuyasas, son of Varahamihira. Apart from this, we do not find any statement or assertion anywhere in the body of the text, that this work is composed by Prithuyasas, son of Varahamihira as is found in the very first verse of the **षट्पञ्चाशिका—**

 **“प्रणिपत्य रविं मूर्ध्ना वराहमिहिरात्मजेन पृथुयशसा”**. But this omission will not stand in the way of deciding the authorship of this work, for there are other evidences to show that this work must have been written by the same Prithuyasas. It is well known that Varahamihira was a great devotee of the Sun-God. His son, likewise was a staunch worshipper of the same Deity, as is evidenced by the benedictory verse of the **षट्पञ्चाशिका** In the present work too, the author pays his devout homage to the Sun on the model of Varahamihira See how the benedictory verse of this work—

**जयति जगेदकहेतुर्विश्वात्मा सर्वलोकदीपकरः।  
अनुदितमुदयविनाशस्थितिकर्त्तां भास्करो दिनाधीशः॥**

is practically a paraphrase of Varahamihira’s prayer—

**मूर्त्तित्वे परिकल्पितः शशमृतो वर्त्मापुनर्जन्मना-  
मात्मेत्यात्मविदाम् ऋतुश्चयजतां भर्त्तासरज्योतिषाम्।  
लोकानां प्रलयोद्भवस्थितिविभुश्चानेकधा यः श्रुतौ-  
वाचं नः सददात्वनेककिरणस्त्रैलोकपदीपो रविः॥**

 Similarly, the present author says on page 305—

**रक्तसुमाक्षतगन्धैः सम्पूज्य दिवाकर नमस्कृत्य।  
प्रष्टा स्वशक्तिविभवैर्दैवज्ञं पूजयेद्ग्रहान्ध्यात्वा॥**

 Another point to be considered in this connection is that the word **होरा**–Hora, means the famous work BrihatJataka of Varahamihara. This Horasara is nothing but an easy abridgment of the same work done for the benefit of humanity. This is what he states in the last stanza of this work—

**होराशास्त्रसमुद्रं प्रमथ्य धीमन्दराद्रिणा सम्यक्।  
लोकस्यालोककरः शास्त्रशशाङ्कः सम्मुत्क्षिप्तः॥**

 This verse is wholly taken by our author from the **बृहत्संहिता** CVI—1 of Varahamihira. So also the verses XVI—24 to 27 are actual quotations of **बृहत्संहिता** LXVII—89 to 92, and so is the XXXII—20, of **बृ. जा.**, XXVIII—7. That only a son could use his father’s property as his own is an accepted fact, for says the **श्रुति “आत्मावै पुत्रनामासि”**. So also does our author make full use of Varahamihira's **अङ्गविद्या** and **शाकुनं** in the last chapter of this work, in addition to his following closely the path chalked out by Varahamihira. Like the latter, he adverts to ancient authorities like Maya, Yavana, Siddhasena, Prabodha, Mandavya, Vishnugupta (or Chanakya), Jeevasarman and Brahmasaunda. All these lead us to the conclusion that the colophon must have been written by the author himself, who is none other than the illustrious son of the illustrious Varahamihira.

 We have already discussed the date of Varahamihira in our Introduction to the Brihat Samhita (See p. v) Prithuyasas should therefore be assigned to the latter half of the 6th Century A. D. The object of Prithuyasas in writing this work is to make the abstruse. Hora Sastra intelligible to persons of average intelligence. One may put the question here as to why this is necessary, when his father himself has already simplified and abridged it in his **लघुजातक.** According to the present author, even this **लघुजातक** was not within easy reach or understanding of ordinary men. That is why he took up the task of writing this work in order to simplify and also to supplement his father’s great work.

 As stated above, the arrangement of the topics here closely follows that of the **बृहज्जातक**. This will be clear from a comparison of the two lists of the names of Chapters. Sometimes our author combines in one and the same Chapter the topics of two Chapters in the Brihat Jataka. For example, the **निषेकाध्याय** and the **जन्माध्याय** of the latter are combined here in the **निषेकजन्माध्याय**. In the case of **दशाफल** and **अन्तर्दशाफल**, Prithuyasas waxes eloquent and gives very many useful ideas not seen elsewhere. He treats very elaborately of the **दशाफल**
in nine Chapters VIII to XVI. There is no section in this work corresponding to the **द्रेष्काणाध्याय**, but in its stead, he gives the **अंशशीलाध्याय**, where some new principles and subjects are brought to our notice. For example, he gives the fatal period for persons born in each **अंश**—for one born in the Karkataka **अंश** the 8th, 18th, 21st, 22nd, 72nd and 80th years are dangerous. Just like his father, Prithuyasas too is not in favour of two or more planets combining in a single house. He says it is as bad as the mixture of honey and ghee. Unlike his father, he gives the effects of the conjunction of three and four planets also. Regarding the **अन्तर्दशा **effect, the learned author states a very important principle in the following Sloka,

**अन्तर्दशाधिपक्षेत्रे वर्तते भास्करो यदि।  
तस्मिन् काले दशाप्रोक्तफलं भवति निश्चितम्॥**

in Chapter XXXI. **नक्षत्रजातकाध्याय** (Nakshatrajatakadhyaya) is one of the important and special features of this work, because it treats of the Udu-Dasa system which his father does not treat of. Even the learned Kalyana Varman is not aware of it. Prithuyasas enunciates some important principles in this Chapter. He says that the Udu Dasa system may be calculated with reference to either the natal star or the star that is rising in the Ascendant (*vide* xxx-2). The final stage of all Dasas is bad. The Dasa of an asterism in which a malefic is situated will cause a good deal of trouble to the native at a period which is proportional to the distance travelled by the lord of the Dasa in the star he is in. Similarly, when the twelve houses are divided into three groups of four Rasis each, if there is a weak malefic without benefic aspect in the first group and if the native is passing through the Dasa of that planet in the initial stage of his life then the end of this Dasa will prove fatal to him. Similarly on page 284 (verse No 30), he states a new principle. The birth of a son in the same star as that of the father is dangerous to the mother. Similarly, the identity of stars between the mother and the son is harmful to the father. Chapter XVII treating of the effects of Ashtakavarga is very important and a special feature of this work inasmuch as he declares **“सर्वकर्मफलोपेतमष्टवर्गं विदुर्बुधाः** (Verse 75). The Ashtakavarga shows the effects of all actions. Without this, it is very difficult to know the good and bad results of men’s actions. It is said that Siddhasena (**सिद्धसेन**) has treated of this subject very elaborately and our author has taken only the essence out of it. According to him, the Ashtavarga Dasa system is the best of all.

 Mantreswara, as stated above, has taken only the quintessence of Chapter XVII of this work in his work (Chapter XXIV). He has quoted *verbatim* a few verses of the Horasara and some he has paraphrased in his own words chapters.

 This work contains 32 chapters. The **बृहज्जातक** contains 28 (27+1), the **सारावली** 54 (27×2) and the **फलदीपिका** 28 (27+1) chapters. What may be the rationale behind this number? We know that there are 27 asterisms and if we add **अभिजित्** (Abhijit) also the number becomes 28. Both Varahamihira and Mantreswara must have had this idea at the back of their mind when they chose this number. In the **सारावली** this number must have been doubled. Prithuyasas also must have had some special reason for choosing the number 32, which has a mystic significance. The throne that was presented to the great Vikramaditya had 32 dolls supporting it. Similarly the age of 32 in a person’s life is a very significant period. It may prove a turning point in his life. One may renounce the world and become a great Yogin, or, one may shuffle off one’s mortal coil. That is why **द्वात्रिंशद्योगे** is dangerous in a person’s horoscope.

* *The number 32 is to be computed as 16 x 2. Sixteen is a favourite number attributed to the Moon who is the starting point for astrological infeernces and the very planet who influences the Moon the most, The Moon’s **कलाः** are 16 (Vide: Amara Kosa 1 Kanda—**कला तु षोडशो भागो बिम्बोऽस्त्री मण्डलं त्रिषु॥** and my edition of Uttara Kalamrita—Chapter IV—Sloka 28. It is quite probable that Prithuyasas wanted to associate the Moon with his work and this argument appears rational.

 This work in a way specializes in different kinds of **आयुर्दाय** and several kinds of Yogas, Rajayogas, etc. Hence this number seems to have been selected by the author with this object in view.

 In Chapter VII dealing with **आयुर्दाय**, there is also some speciality Varahamihira speaks of only four kinds of reduction, *viz*; **नीचार्द्वहरण** i. e., reduction by half of the life-period contributed by a planet that is debilitated, (2) **शत्रुक्षेत्रहरण** reduction by a third, (3) **अस्तङ्गतहरण** reduction by half for the planet that is eclipsed, and (4) **दृश्यार्द्धहरण** reduction for malefics in the visible half by full ½ etc.; but Prithuyasas speaks of two more reductions, *viz*., (1) **युद्धहरण**—reduction by ⅓ for a planet that is defeated in a fight, and (2) **श्रसुंरसन्निकर्षहरण** for the luminaries, by ¼ (or ¹/¹² ?). According to Varahamihira, the number of years contributed by the Lagna corresponds to the number of Navamsas that have risen, while Prithuyasas says **“लग्नेश्वरांशकसमानि”** etc i.e., the number of years corresponding to the number of the Navamsas reckoned from Mesha occupied by the lord of the Lagna. The present author gives direction as to when the different systems of Ayurdaya are to be resorted to. In Chapter XVIII also, he gives the following valuable information: A person will be married during the sub-period of the planet owning the Navamsa of the lord of the 7th house in the person’s birth-chart. The death of a brother may take place when Saturn passes thro’ the Rasi indicated by the sum-total of the figures of the lords of the 6th, 8th and 12th houses. One may quit the world during the Dasa of the planet presiding over the Navamsa in which Rahu is posited. Similarly, the month of death is to be found out by multiplying the Sun’s figure in minutes by that of Rahu (in minutes) and dividing the product by 21,600 and then by adding this quotient to the Sun’s figure, which will indicate some Rasi. There is a Yoga called Bhagya Yoga mentioned among the Raja Yogas, which is brought into existence, when all the planets including the Ascendant are in odd signs and when the Moon is waxing and when the birth is at day-time; in the case of females, the signs and time of birth being altered. Similarly he gives some very valuable ideas in the Chapter on ‘Lost Horoscopes’.

 In view of all the instructive aspects of the work mentioned above, we are sure that the public will welcome it with eagerness. We shall deem our efforts amply rewarded if the learned public feel enriched in their knowledge through the present publication. It is also our earnest prayer that all human beings attain the goal of their existence by doing their tasks on this earthly plane in accordance with the wishes of the lord as indicated by the Planets.

Basavangudi, }                        
V. Subrahmanya Sastri  
Bangalore City } M. Ramakrishna Bhat.  
15th July 1949. }

॥श्री गणेशाय नमः॥

**॥होरासारः॥**

**प्रथमोऽध्यायः**  
**\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_**

**जयति जगदेकहेतुर्विश्वात्मा सर्वलोकदीपकरः।  
अनुदिनमुदयविनाशस्थितिकर्ता भास्करो दिनाधीशः॥१॥**

 *Sloka* 1.—There flourishes the (divine) Sun, the lord of the Day, who is the sole cause and the soul of the Universe, whose rays illumine all the worlds and who daily brings about creation, destruction and protection.

**निमिषादिवत्सरान्तः कालो राशिप्रमाणमेकैकः।  
गणितस्कन्धे प्रोक्तं पूर्वं ग्रहलक्षणैः सार्धम्॥२॥**

 *Sloka* 2.—Time beginning with a second (time taken for a wink) and ending with a year and the measure of each sign of the zodiac have been already treated of along with the characteristics of planets in the section on astronomical calculations.

 Vide the 3 Skandhas referred to in Brihat Samhita.

**होरास्कन्धे सम्यग्दशाविभागः पुरा विनिर्दिष्टः।  
विस्तारिशास्त्रमार्गैर्न शक्यते मन्दबुद्धिभिर्ज्ञातुम्॥३॥**

 *Sloka* 3.—The differentiation of the various Dasa periods has already been well explained in the section on Horoscopy. But it cannot be grasped by the dull-witted who require a very elaborate scientific method.

 Here the author refers to the stiff nature of Varahamihira's Brihat Jataka.

**तस्मात्प्रयोगसिद्धैराचार्यैर्यत्फलं प्रोक्तम्।  
तत्स्पष्टार्थं वक्ष्ये होराशास्त्रार्णवात्सारम्॥४॥**

 *Sloka* 4.—Hence, I shall state the essence of the ocean of the Horary Science in order to clarify the effects that have been declared by the (ancient) teachers whose predictions have proved correct by experience.

**मेषवृषमिथुनकर्कटसिंहाः कन्या तुला च वृश्चिककः।  
धन्वी मकरः कुम्भो मीनाविति राशिनामानि॥५॥**

 *Sloka* 5.—The names of the twelve signs in their order are, Mesha, Vrishabha, Mithuna, Karkata, Simha, Kanya, Tula, Vrischika, Dhanus, Makara, Kumbha and Meena.

**कन्या सानलसस्या प्लबगाऽथ तुलाधरो घटी मीनौ।  
नक्रो मृगास्य उक्तो नरोऽश्वजघनो धनुष्पाणिः॥६॥**

**मेषवृषसिंहकर्कटकीटास्ते तु स्वनामसदृशचराः।  
नरमिथुनं दण्डधरं वीणासक्तं च विज्ञेयम्॥७॥**

 *Slokas* 6-7.—Sign Kanya (Virgo) is represented by a maiden seated in a boat (raft) holding fire and corn ; Tula by a man holding scales; Kumbha, by one holding a pot; Meena, by a pair of fish ; Makara, by a crocodile endowed with a deer's face; and Dhanus, by a man with a bow and having equine hips. The signs Mesha, Vrishabha, Simha, Karkata and Vrischika have forms (*ht*. move) in accordance with their names. And sign Mithuna is to be understood to be a human couple (man and woman) holding a staff and a lute respectively.

**अलिझषमकरकुलीरा जलात्मका जलचराश्च विज्ञेयाः।  
तौलिघटवृषभकन्या जलाश्रितास्तत्प्रदेश निरताः स्युः॥८॥**

**स्थलराशयस्तु शेषाः सिंहो गिरिगह्वरप्रदेशस्थः।  
सानुप्रदेशनिरतो मेषो नगराश्रितस्तुलाधारी॥९॥**

**ग्रामचरो मिथुनाख्यो रणभूमिचरो धनुर्धरो राशिः।  
कर्कटवृश्चिकमीनाः कीटाख्या वृश्चिको विशेषेण॥१०॥**

 *Slokas* 8-10.—Signs Vrischika, Meena, Makara and Karkata are known as watery signs and they are aquatic also ; while Tula, Kumbha, Vrishabha and Kanya are dependent on water (water-resorters), and delight in places abounding in water. The rest, (*viz*., Mesha, Mithuna, Simha and Dhanus) are called land-signs. Sign Simha has its abode in the region of mountain caves; Mesha, of plateaus, and Tula, of cities. Sign Mithuna has its habitation in villages; and Dhanus, in battle-fields. Signs Karkata, Vrischika and Meena are called Keetas (reptiles) ; especially so, Vrischika.

**चापान्त्यो मकरादिर्वृषमेषमृगेश्वराश्चतुश्चरणाः।  
घटमिथुन तुला कन्याश्चापस्यार्धं मनुष्यसञ्ज्ञाः स्युः॥११॥**

 *Sloka* 11.—The latter half of Dhanus, the first half of Makara, Mesha, Vrishabha and Simha are called quadruped signs; and Kumbha, Mithuna, Tula, Kanya and the first half of Dhanus, are styled human (biped) signs.

**लग्नं प्राप्ता द्विपदा बलान्विता मध्यगाश्चतुश्चरणाः।  
सर्वे कीटा अस्ते हिबुके जलचारिणस्तथा बलिनः॥१२॥**

* Sloka* 12.—The biped signs are strong when they happen to be the Ascendant; the quadruped ones, when they happen to be the 10th house ; all the reptile signs, the 7th house ; and the aquatic ones, the 4th house,

**ऋक्षद्वयं सपादं राशौ राशौ क्रमेण संयोज्यम्।  
नव नव पादसमेता मेषाश्विन्यादिमीन पौष्णान्ताः॥१३॥**

 *Sloka* 13—Each sign is constituted by two stars and a quarter; so, the twelve signs are regularly made up of two and a quarter stars beginning with Aswini, each sign consisting of nine quarter stars beginning with Aswini in Mesha and ending with Revati in Meena.

**पूषाश्विन्योः सन्धाबहिमघयोर्ज्येष्ठमूलयोः सन्धौ।  
घटिका गण्डान्ता इह चतुस्समाश्चा परे षडिति॥१४॥**

 *Sloka* 14.—One Ghatika (a period of 24 minutes) at the junction of the stars Revati and Aswini, Aslesha and Magha, and Jyeshtha and Mula is called Gandanta (of evil consequence) This dangerous period lasts for four years ; but according to others, for six years.

**अजमृगतौलिकुलीरा नवांशकाद्याः क्रमादजादीनाम्।  
स्वगृहाद्राश्यंशेशा द्रेक्काणेशाः स्वपञ्चनवमेशाः॥१५॥ **

 *Sloka* 15.—The first Navamsas of the 12 Rasis beginning with Mesha are respectively Mesha, Makara, Tula and Karkataka, taken thrice. The lords of the various Navamsas of the Rasis take their names according to the names of the Rasis which they (Navamsas) bear; and the lords of the Dwadasamsas of any Rasi begin from that Rasi. The lords of the Drekkanas of a sign are in order those of the particular sign, the 5th house and the 9th house from it.

**शरपञ्चाष्ट च सप्त च पञ्च च भागाः क्रमेण विषमेषु।  
आरार्किजीवसौम्याः शुक्रश्चैषां समेषु विपरीताः॥१६॥**

 *Sloka* 16.—In the odd signs, Mars, Saturn, Jupiter, Mercury and Venus have respectively 5°, 5°, 8°, 7° and 5° ; and in the even signs, this is to be taken in the reverse order.

**अजवृषभचापमकराः पृष्ठत उद्यन्ति कर्किणा युक्ताः।  
मिथुनयुता निशिबलिनो मीनस्तिर्यङ्मुखश्च सन्ध्यायाम्॥१७॥**

**शीर्षोदया विमिथुनाः शेषा दिवसे बलान्विताः सततम्।  
स्वामिज्ञजीवयुक्ता दृष्टा वा राशयो बलाढ्याश्च॥१८॥**

 *Slokas* 17-18.—Signs Mesha, Vrishabha, Dhanus, Makara and Karkataka rise with their hind part, and are strong by night along with Mithuna, while Meena rises with its faces turned in opposite directions (i. e., both-ways) and is strong during the twilight. The rest without Mithuna rise with their head and are always strong by day. The signs become strong, when they are conjoined with or aspected by their respective lords, Mercuury or Jupiter.

**पुंस्त्री सञ्ज्ञे भवतो राशीनामस्थिराचलद्विगुणाः।  
मेषादीनां सिद्धा भूयो भूयश्चरस्थिरद्विगुणाः॥१९॥**

 *Sloka* 19.—The Rasis from Mesha onwards are alternately male and female. They are also termed moveable, fixed and dual, respectively, repeated four times.

**अजहरिचापा भूपा विप्रा मीनालिचन्द्रभवनानि।  
घटमिथुनतुला वैश्याः कन्यामकरवृषभास्तु शूद्राः स्युः॥२०॥**

* Sloka* 20.—Signs Mesha, Simha and Dhanus are Kshatriyas; Meena, Vrischika and Karkataka are Brahmins ; Kumbha, Mithuna and Tula are Vaisyas; and Kanya, Makara and Vrishabha, Sudras.

 See **जा-पा**–I–20 and Notes.

**मूर्धमुखकण्ठवाहाहृदयोदरवस्तिगुह्यानि।  
ऊरू जानू जङ्घे चरणाविति राशयोऽजाद्याः॥२१॥**

 *Sloka* 21.—The signs from Mesha onwards represent in order the head, face, neck, arms, heart, stomach, groins, private parts, thighs, knees, shanks and feet (of Kalapurusha).

**लग्नाद्विचिन्तनीयाः क्रमेण पूर्वोक्तदेहभेदास्ते।  
होराक्रमेण चिन्त्या देहस्याङ्गेषु पूर्वपश्चिमता॥२२॥**

 *Sloka* 22.—It is from the Ascendant and other houses that the parts of the body mentioned above are to be considered in their order. The limbs of the body from the head onwards are to be deduced from the Lagna, etc.

**रक्तसितहरित पाटल परिधूम्रपाण्डुरचित्रकृष्णाश्च।  
कनकसमपिङ्गकर्बुरबभ्रुकवर्णास्त्वजादीनाम्॥२३॥**

 *Sloka* 23.—The colours of the 12 signs are in order red, white, green, pink, brown, grey, variegated, black, golden, yellow, variegated and deep brown.

**अनिमेषमेषराशी ह्रस्वौ वृषकुम्भयोस्तु वक्रतनुः।  
मृगमिथुनकर्किचापा दीर्घाः शेषास्तु मध्यमा ज्ञेयाः॥२४॥**

 *Sloka* 24.—The signs Meena and Mesha are short. Vrishabha and Kumbha are crooked ; Makara, Mithuna, Karkataka and Dhanus are long, and the rest are of medium length.

**क्रियतावुरुजितुमकुलीरलेयपाथोनजूककौर्प्याख्याः।  
तौक्षिक आकोकेरो हृद्रोगश्चान्त्यभं चेत्थम्॥२५॥**

 *Sloka* 25.—The 12 Rasis in their order are also known as (1) Kriya (2) Tavuru (3) Jituma (4) Kulira (5) Leya (6) Pathona (7) Juka (8) Kaurpi (9) Taukshika (10) Akokera (11) Hridroga and (12) Chettha.

**सङ्ख्याभिधानमपरैर्मेषादीनां क्रमेण निर्दिष्टम्।  
अलिसञ्ज्ञाष्टमराशेर्वनगिरिसञ्ज्ञा मृगेश्वरस्य स्यात्॥२६॥**

 *Sloka* 26.—Others have given the signs Mesha and others, numeral names in order. Accordingly, the name 'Ali' signifies the 8th Rasi and the name 'Vanagiri' is given to Simha.

**तन्वर्थसहजबान्धवपुत्रारिकलत्रनैधनानि पुनः।  
धर्मक्रियायविगमा भावा होरादिषु ज्ञेयाः॥२७॥**

 *Sloka* 27.—The twelve houses beginning with the Ascendant are also known as (1) Tanu (body), (2) Artha (wealth), (3) Sahaja (brother), (4) Bandhava (relative), (5) Putra (son), (6) Ari (enemy), (7) Kalatra (wife), (8) Naidhana (death), (9) Dharma (virtue), (10) Kriya (work), (11) Aya (income) and (12) Vigama (loss) respectively.

**उदयसुखकामदशमं केन्न्द्रं तस्मात्परं फणपराख्यम्।  
आपोक्लिमं च परतस्तस्मात् त्रिविधास्तु राशयः कल्प्याः॥२८॥**

 *Sloka* 28.—There are three kinds of houses, *Viz*., (1) Kendra, (2) Phanapara and (3) Apoklima. The Ascendant, the fourth, the seventh and the tenth houses are called Kendras ; the 2nd, 5th, 8th and 11th houses, are termed Phanaparas ; and the 3rd, 6th, 9th and 12th houses, Apoklimas.

**केन्द्रस्य कण्टकमथो चतुष्टयं चेति नामनी द्वे स्तः।  
आपोक्लिमं तु चरमं फणपरसञ्ज्ञं तु मध्यकेन्द्रं च॥२९॥**

 *Sloka* 29.—The term Kendra has two other names—Kantaka and Chatushtaya, while the Apoklima has another name *viz*., Charama. The Phanapara is otherwise known as Madhya Kendra.

**चतुरस्रं वधहिबुकं षट्कोणं लाभषष्ठयोः सञ्ज्ञा  
त्रिषडेकादशदशमान्युपचयसञ्ज्ञानि कथितानि॥३०॥**

 *Sloka* 30.—The 4th and the 8th houses constitute what is known as Chaturasra (square). The 6th and 11th houses are called by the name of Shat Kona. The 3rd, 6th, 10th and 11th houses are termed Upachaya (houses of increase).

 * *With regard to the **उपचय** (Upachaya) houses, the following is another view : **एके उपचयत्वं न नित्यमिति वदन्ति॥**

**अथोपचयसञ्ज्ञा स्यात् त्रिलाभरिपुकर्मणाम्।  
न चेद्भवन्ति ते दृष्टाः पापैः स्वस्वामिशत्रुभिः॥**

* *that is, “the term **उपचय** (Upachaya) is applied to the 3rd, 6th 10th, and 11th houses, provided they are not aspected by malefics, or by planets inimical to the lords of those houses." This view is not however accepted by Varahamihira.

**जामित्रमस्तभवनं द्यूनं कामश्च चित्तसञ्ज्ञं च।  
दुश्चिक्य सहजविक्रमतृतीयकं तुल्यनाम स्यात्॥३१॥**

 *Sloka* 31.—Other names for the 7th house are Jamitra, Astabhavana, Dyuna, Kama and Chitta, and those for the 3rd are Duschikya, Sahaja and Vikrama (valour).

**आस्पदमाज्ञा दशमं कर्म च मेषूरणं खमध्यस्थम्।  
हिबुकं सुखं च वेश्म च पातालं वारि बन्धुतुल्याख्यम्॥३२॥**

 *Sloka* 32.—The synonyms of the 10th house are Aspada (place), Ajna (command), Karma (profession or work), Meshurana and Khamadhyasttha (situated in the zenith of the sky) or Kha and Madhyasttha. The 4th house is otherwise called Hibuka. Sukha (happiness), Vesma (home), Patala (nether world), Vari (water) and Bandhu (relative).

**सुतधर्मयोस्त्रिकोणं सुतस्य च त्रित्रिकोणमपि नवकम्।  
भाग्यं गुरुः शुभं वा तस्मिन्नभिधानमेकैकम्॥३३॥**

 *Sloka* 33.—The 5th and 9th houses are known as Trikona ; the 9th alone is called Tritrikona; it is also termed Bhagya (fortune), Guru (father) and Subha (auspicious).

**रिष्फं द्वादशभवनं लोपस्थानं व्ययं च निर्दिष्टम्।  
वित्तं कुटुम्बभवनं वाक्स्थानं मङ्गलं समाख्यातम्॥३४॥**

 *Sloka* 34.—The 12th house is otherwise known as Rippha, Lopastthana (house of disappearance), and Vyaya (loss). The 2nd house is called Vitta (wealth), Kutumba bhavana (house of family), Vakstthana (house of speech) and Mangala (auspiciousness).

**रन्ध्रं निधनं प्रोक्तं चाष्टम राशिर्विनाशदुखं च।  
ऋक्षं भवनं क्षेत्रं होरा राशिश्च तुल्यार्थाः॥३५॥**

 *Sloka* 35.—The 8th house is known by the names of Randhra (hole), Nidhana (death), Vinasa (destruction) and Duhkha (misery). The terms Riksha, Bhavana (house), Kshetra, Hora or Rasi, all mean the same thing.

**उदयाख्यं प्राग्लग्नं लेखा होरा समानाख्या।  
राशीनामभिधानं पूर्वाचार्यैः समुद्दिष्टम्॥३६॥**

 *Sloka* 36.—The Ascendant has the following names :—Udaya (rising), Praglagna, Lekha and Hora. Thus the above synonyms of the Rasis (Houses) have been given by the ancient teachers.

**राश्यर्धमिति च होरा ललाटरेखेति विश्रुता होरा।  
कालपरिज्ञानार्थं होराख्यां केचिदिच्छन्ति॥३७॥**

इति श्री वराहमिहिरसुत श्रीपृथुयशोविरचिते होरासारे राशिविभागाध्यायः प्रथमः॥

* Sloka* 37.—The word Hora is also known as a half of a Rasi. It is also known as Lalata Rekha (line on the forehead). Some astrologers want the Hora for ascertaining the exact time.

 Thus ends the first Adhyaya called Rasi Vibhaga (classification of the Signs) of the work Horasara, written by Prithuyasas, the son of Varahamihira.

**\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_**

**द्वितीयोऽध्यायः**

**भौमसितज्ञेन्द्वर्का बुधभृगुभौमार्यमन्दशनिगुरवः।  
मेषादीनामीशा राशीनामंशकानां च॥१॥**

 * Sloka* 1.—The lords of the 12 Rasis and the Amsas bearing their names are in their order, Mars, Venus, Mercury, the Moon, the Sun, Mercury, Venus, Mars, Jupiter, Saturn, Saturn, and Jupiter.

**अर्केन्दू होरेशौ विषमे सममे निशाकरोष्णांशू।  
मेषवृषमिथुनकटकाः प्राच्यादीशास्त्रिकोणसंयुक्ताः॥२॥**

 *Sloka* 2.—The lords of the Horas in odd signs are the Sun and the Moon respectively; while, in the even ones, they are the Moon and the Sun respectively. The lords of the four quarters from the East are in order Mesha, Vrishabha, Mithuna and Kataka with their respective Trikona houses; i. e., Mesha, Simha and Dhanus represent the East ; Vrishabha, Kanya and Makara, the South ; Mithuna, Tula and Kumbha, the West ; and Karkataka, Vrischika and Meena, the North.

**अर्कादीनामुच्चाः क्रियवृषमृगयुवतिकर्किमीनतुलाः।  
दशशिख्यष्टाविंशतितिथिशरनक्षत्रविंशतिभिरंशैः॥३॥**

**अत्युच्चराशिभागाः सूर्यादीनां क्रमेण निर्दिष्टाः।  
स्वोच्चात्सप्तमराशिर्नीचः स्यादंशकात्परमः॥४॥**

 *Slokas* 3-4.—The exaltation signs of the planets from the Sun onwards are in order (1) Mesha (2) Vrishabha (3) Makara (4) Kanya (5) Karkataka (6) Meena and (7) Tula. The highest Exaltation degrees in the several Rasis are in their order the 10th, 3rd, 28th, 15th, 5th, 27th and 20th The 7th house from a planet's exaltation sign is its Depression sign and the particular degree in that, its lowest Depression point.

**कन्यायामुच्चांशाद्बुधस्य परतस्त्रिकोणसञ्ज्ञं च।  
विंशतिभागादूर्ध्वं क्षेत्रं त्रिविधं तु विज्ञेयम्॥५॥**

 *Sloka* 5.—In sign Kanya, the portion of 5° that is beyond the exaltation point of Mercury is called his Moolatrikona. Similarly, beyond the 20th degree therein it is his Swakshetra. Thus, the sign has a triple function: *viz*, Uchcha, Moolatrikona and Swakshetra.

**उच्च भागत्रितयं वृष इन्दोस्तु त्रिकोणमपरेऽंशाः।  
जूके त्रिकोणभवनं विंशतिभागैः परं भृगोः क्षेत्रम्॥६॥**

 *Sloka* 6.—In Vrishabha, the first 3° portion is the exaltation of the Moon and the remaining portion, her Moolatrikona In Tula, the first 20° portion is the Moolatrikona of Venus and the rest, his own house (Swakshetra)

**विंशतिरंशाः सिंहे त्रिकोणमपरे स्वभवनमर्कस्य।  
कुम्भे त्रिकोणनिजभे रविजस्य रवेर्यथा सिंहे॥७॥**

 *Sloka *7.—In Simha, the first 20° portion is the Moolatrikona; and the rest, Swakshetra of the Sun. in the same manuer, Saturn has his Moolatrikona and Swakshetra in Kumbha, *i. e.* 20° Moolatrikona and the remaning 10° Swakshetra.

**मेषे द्वादशभागैस्त्रिकोणमपरे स्वभवनमारस्य।  
आदौ धनुषि शरांशैस्त्रिकोणमपरे स्वभवनमिन्द्रगुरोः॥८॥**

 *Sloka* 8.—The first 12° portion of Mesha is the Moolatrikona and the remaining 18°, Swakshetra of Mars. Similarly the first 5° portion of Dhanus is the Moolatrikona and the rest Swakshetra of Jupiter.

**स्वस्वत्रिकोणभवनादुपचयजामित्रभवनानि।  
सोच्चं क्षेत्रं हित्वा तेषामीशास्तु शत्रवो ज्ञेयाः॥९॥**

**अन्येषां राशीनामीशान् सुहृदः प्रचिन्तयेन्मतिमान्।  
शत्रुसुहृद्भवनेशा मध्यास्त्रिविधा ग्रहाः प्रोक्ताः॥१०॥**

 *Slokas* 9-10.—The lords of the 3rd, 6th, 7th, 10th and 11th houses from their respective Moolatrikona houses happen to be the enemies of the various planets. This rule does not apply to the lords of their exaltation-Rasis. A learned man should consider the lords of the other Rasis to be the friends of the several planets. Planets are said to be of three kinds: friends, enemies and neutrals among themselves.

 *For example, the Moolatrikona of the Sun is Simha. So according to the above rule, Venus, Saturn and Mercury become the enemies of the Sun. Mercury is only his neutral as he has only one chance, while the others have two.*

**अन्योन्यमायसहजव्ययधनबन्ध्यास्पदस्थिताः सुहृदः।  
तात्कालिकास्त्वमित्राः शेषेषु गृहेषु चेत्कल्प्याः॥११॥**

 *Sloka* 11.—Planets that are posited in the 11th and 3rd houses from each other, the 12th and 2nd, and the 4th and 10th, become mutual friends for the time being, while those posited in other houses are to be taken as mutual enemies likewise.

**रविशुक्रभौमसर्पाः सौरेन्दू सौम्यवाक्पती क्रमशः।  
प्राच्यादीनां नाथा बलान्विताः सर्वकालेषु॥१२॥**

 *Sloka* 12—The lords of the eight quarters beginning with the East are in order (1) the Sun (2) Venus (3) Mars (4) Rahu (5) Saturn (6) the Moon (7) Mercury and (8) Jupiter They are strong at all times.

**जामित्रं चतुरश्रं त्रिकोणमाज्ञां तृतीयमेतानि।  
स्वस्थानाद्वीक्षन्ते ग्रहाः क्रमेणैव बोद्धव्याः॥१३॥**

**सम्पूर्णं पादोनं रूपार्धं पादमेव किरणाः स्युः।  
विंशतिरष्टौ दशदशरविमनवः षोडशैव किरणानाम्॥१४॥**

**सूर्यादीनां सङ्ख्या राशीनामीश्वरोक्तकिरणाः स्युः।**

 *Slokas* 13,14,14½.—Planets have a full aspect of the 7th house; three-fourths of an aspect over the 4th and 8th houses; half an aspect over the 5th and 9th; and a quarter aspect of the 3rd and 10th houses all counted from their respective positions. The rays belonging to the seven planets from the Sun onwards are in order (1) 2, (2) 8, (3) 10, (4) 10, (5) 12, (6) 14, and (7) 16. The rays of the Rasis are the same as those of their lords.

**रविगुरुभौमाः पुरुषाः स्त्रियस्तथा राहुभार्गवशशाङ्काः॥१५॥  
मृत्यु सुतनीलसौम्या नपुंसकाश्चेति विज्ञेयाः**

 *Slokas* 15, 15½—The Sun, Jupiter and Mars are known to be males; Rahu, Venus and the Moon, females; and Ketu, Saturn and Mercury, eunuchs.

**शुक्रगुरू विप्रेशौ रविभौमौ क्षत्रियौ च विट् चन्द्रः॥१६॥**

**अन्तरजातिः सौम्यो वृषलो मन्दोऽन्त्यजातिरिन्दुरिपुः।**

 *Sloka* 15½-16½.—Jupiter and Venus preside over Brahmins; the Sun and Mars are Kshatriyas; the Moon is a Vaisya; Mercury is of mixed breed; Saturn is a Sudra; and Rahu is an outcaste.

**राहु शनि केतु भौमाः क्रूराः पापो रविः शशी कृष्णः॥१७॥**

**बुधगुरुशुक्राः सौम्याः शुक्लः सौम्यः शशी ज्ञेयः।**

 *Sloka* 16½-17½.—Rahu, Saturn, Ketu, Mars and the Sun are to be understood as malefics; so also the Moon, in the dark fortnight. Mercury, Jupiter and Venus are known as benefics; so is the Moon in the bright fortnight.

**शुक्रबुधौ राजसिकौ गुरुशशिरवयस्तु सात्विका ज्ञेयाः॥१८॥**

**भौमशनिसैंहिकेयास्तमोगुणाः सर्वकार्येषु।**

 *Sloka* 17½-18½.—Mercury and Venus are of the quality of Rajas (greed); Jupiter, the Sun and the Moon of Satva (goodness); and Mars, Saturn and Rahu, of Tamas (darkness), in all their actions.

**पित्ताधिकौ रविकुजौ वातश्लेष्माधिकौ तु चन्द्रसितौ॥१९॥**

**वाताधिकोऽर्कपुत्रः शशिजो मिश्रश्च समुदीर्णः।**

 * Sloka* 18½-19½.—The Sun and Mars have Pitta (bile) as the prominent element in their constitution; the Moon and Venus. Vata and Kapha (wind and phlegm); Saturn, Vata (wind); Mercury is said to have a mixture of the three humours in his constitution.

**रक्तश्यामो भानुश्चन्द्रो गौरः कुजोऽतिरक्तश्च॥२०॥**

**दूर्वाकारः सौम्यो हिरण्यवर्णो गुरुः स्वभावेन।**  
**सितवर्णो भृगुसूनुर्नीलनिभो भास्करिः शिखी धूम्रः॥२१॥**

**बहुवर्णोऽसितसूनुस्त्वपरो नीलाञ्जनोपमो राहुः  
सौम्योऽपि राशिवर्णो ग्रहयोगे तद्ग्रहोक्तवर्णगुणः॥२२॥**

**स्वांशक्षेत्रगतो वा ग्रहयोगविवर्जितो निजोक्तगुणः।  
अन्यर्क्षग्रहयुक्तस्तद्ग्रहतद्वर्णमिश्रनिजवर्णः॥२३॥**

 *Slokas* 20-23.—By nature, the Sun is dark-red in colour; the Moon, white; Mars, deep-red; Mercury, of the colour of Durva grass (green); Jupiter, of golden hue; Venus, white; Saturn, blue (black); Ketu, brown (mud-coloured); Mandi or Gulika, multi-coloured; and Rahu resembles the dark collyrium. Though the colour assigned to a Rasi is pleasant or good, it assumes the shade of the planet it is conjoined with A planet not conjoined with another, when posited in his own Kshetra or Amsa will reveal fully his natural qualities (such as colour, etc.); if, on the other hand, he be posited in another's Rasi (or Amsa) or conjoined with another planet, he would have his natural colour influenced by (mixed with) those of the Rasi or the planet as the case may be.

**चतुरश्राङ्गः सविता पिङ्गाक्षो नातिरोमकेशतनुः।  
अस्थिरवासोऽप्यलसो दुर्बलजानुः प्रसन्नमुखवचनः॥२४॥**

 *Sloka* 24.—The Sun has a square body, pink eyes, sparse hair, on the body and head. He has no permanent residence in any place. He is lazy, weak-kneed and has a prepossessing countenance and pleasing words.

**दीर्घो** **मृदुस्वभावश्चन्द्रो मतिमान् घृणी नयज्ञश्च।  
वातश्लेष्मप्रकृतिः शुक्लाम्बरभूषणः सुवृत्ततनुः॥२५॥**

 *Sloka* 25.—The Moon is tall (long), of tender heart intelligent, compassionate, proficient in polities (knower of morality or manners), of the nature of wind and bile, adorned with white clothes and ornaments and is perfectly round-bodied.

**चपलो विघातकुशलो रक्ताक्षः पैत्तिकोऽग्निशस्त्राङ्कः।  
विकृतस्वरोऽतिशौर्यः कृशोदरोऽङ्गारको विनीतश्च॥२६॥**

 *Sloka* 26.—Mars is fickle-minded, expert in striking or killing others (or even creating obstacles), red-eyed, of a bilious nature, marked with fire and weapons, of queer (cruel) voice, very valorous, and modest (well-trained). He is slender-waisted.

**श्यामेक्षणो नयज्ञो मध्याकारः स्थिरास्थिरोहृष्टः।  
बहुवार्त्तान्वितहास्यो विद्वान् सौम्यस्त्रिदोषसंयुक्तः॥२७॥**

 *Sloka* 27.—Mercury has dark eyes, is well-versed in politics, of medium size or height, partly firm and partly fickle, jolly, humorous, being enriched with all sorts of information, learned and of the nature of the three humours.

**स्थूलात्मा दीर्घतनुर्मध्याक्षो बुद्धिमान् नयज्ञश्च।  
श्लेष्माधिकोऽतिवाग्मी पीतान्बरभूषणो गुरुः श्रेष्ठः॥२८॥**

 *Sloka* 28.—Jupiter has a corpulent and long (tall) body, moderate eyes, is intelligent, well versed in politics, has bile prominent in his constitution, is very eloquent, is adorned with yellow clothes and ornaments and is noble.

**कान्तः** **सुभगः शुक्रो वातश्लेष्माधिको विशालमतिः।  
स्थूलवपुः स्त्रीवशगो विकटाक्षो वञ्चनस्वभावतः॥२९॥**

 *Sloka* 29.—Venus is amiable, attractive (lovely ), of the nature of wind and bile, broad-minded, corpulent, hen-pecked, of uncouth eyes, and by nature given to fraud.

**स्थूलनखदन्तकेशो मायावी दीर्घबाहुपादश्च।  
वातात्मकः सिरालुर्मन्दोऽप्यलसो न शान्तमतिः॥३०॥**

 *Sloka* 30.—Saturn has very prominent nails and teeth, thick and rough hair, is deceptive by nature, of long hands and feet, bilious in constitution, full of veins, lazy and of a disturbed or cruel mind.

**बालाकारो भौमः कुमारवेषो गुरोस्त्रिंशत्।  
शुक्रः षोडशवर्षः पञ्चाशद्वर्षको रविर्ज्ञेयः॥३१॥**

**शशिनः सप्ततिवर्षाण्यशीतिरार्कैः शतं** **तु राहोः स्युः।**

 *Slokas* 31-31½.—Mars has the appearance of a child, and Mercury, that of a boy; Jupiter's age is 30 years; Venus', 16 years; and the Sun is of 50 years. The Moon's age is 70 years; Saturn's, 80 years and Rahu's, 100 years.

**येषां** **प्रसूतिकाले बलान्वितो यो ग्रहो विशेषेण॥३२॥**

**तस्य स्वभावरूपं जनने नॄणां सदा चिन्त्यम्।**

 *Sloka* 32-32½.—It is a general rule that men get the nature and appearance of that planet which is by far the strongest at the time of their birth.

**आदित्योऽर्को** **रविर्भानुर्भास्करश्च दिवाकरः॥३३॥**

**मार्तण्डः सविता सूर्यस्तीक्ष्णांशुः स्यादिनो रविः।**

 *Sloka* 33-33½.—The Sun's synonyms are Aditya, Arka, Ravi, Bhanu, Bhaskara, Divakara, Marthanda, Savita, Surya, Teekshnamsu and Ina.

**चन्द्रः शशी शशाङ्कश्च विधुः सोमो निशाकरः॥३४॥**

**शीतांशुरुडुनाथः स्यादिन्दुश्चन्द्रमसो विदुः।**

 *Sloka* 34-34½.—The Moon's names are Chandra, Sasin, Sasanka, Vidhu, Soma, Nisakara, Seetamsu, Udunatha and Indu.

**आरो** **वक्रो महीजश्च रुधिरो रक्त एव च॥३५॥**

**अङ्गारक इति ख्यातः क्रूरदृक्तुल्यवाचकः।**

 *Sloka* 35-35½.—The names of Mars are Aara, Vakra, Maheeja, Rudhira, Rakta, Angaraka and Kruradrik,

**सौम्यो विद्ज्ञो बुधश्चेति सोमजो बोधनस्तथा॥३६॥**

**एते सौम्यस्य पर्यायाः कुमारश्च विधोः सुतः।**

 *Sloka* 36-36½.—The synonyms of Mercury are Saumya, Vid, Jna, Budha, Somaja, Bodhana, Kumara and Vidhusuta.

**जीवोऽङ्गिरः** **सुरगुरुर्मन्त्री वाचस्पतिस्तथा॥३७॥**

**आर्यो बृहस्पतिः सूरिर्वागीशः सदृशार्थकः।**

 *Sloka* 37-37½.—The names of Jupiter are Jeeva, Angiras, Suraguru, Mantri, Vachaspati, Arya, Brihaspati, Suri and Vageesa.

**शुक्रो** **भृगुर्भृगुसुत आस्फुजिच्च सितस्तथा॥३८॥**

**उशना दैत्यपूज्यश्च काव्यः कविरिति स्मृतः।**

 *Slokas* 38-38½.—The names of Venus are Sukra, Bhrigu, Bhrigusuta, Asphujit, Sita, Usanas, Daityapujya, Kavya and Kavi.

**कोणो मन्दः शनिः कृष्णः सूर्यपुत्रो यमस्तथा॥३९॥**

**पङ्गुः शनैश्चरः सौरिः कालश्छायासुतः समः।**

 *Sloka* 39-39½.—The synonyms of Saturn are Kona Manda, Sani, Krishna, Suryaputra, Yama, Pangu, Sanaischara, Sauri, Kala and Chayasuta.

**राहुस्तमोऽसुरोऽगुश्च स्वर्भानुश्च विधुन्तुदः॥४०॥**

**पातश्च सैहिकेयश्च भुजङ्गोऽहिश्च ते समाः।**

* Sloka* 40-40½—The names of Rahu are Rahu, Tamas, Asura, Swarbhanu, Vidhuntuda, Pata, Saimhikeya, Bhujanga and Ahi.

**शिखी केतुर्ध्वजो धूमो मृत्युपुत्रोऽनलस्तथा॥४१॥**

**सामान्येतानि सर्वेषां ग्रहाणां च विदुर्बुधाः।**

इति श्रीवराहमिहिरसुतश्रीपृथुयशोविरचिते होरासारे ग्रहलक्षणाध्यायो द्वितीयः।

 *Sloka* 41-41½.—The synonyms of Ketu are Sikhin, Ketu, Dhwaja, Dhuma, Mrityuputra and Anala. These are thus the different names of the several planets according to the ancient teachers.

 Thus ends the Second Adhyaya styled Grahalakshana or the Characteristics of Planets in the work Horasara, written by Prithuyasas, the son of Varahamihira.

—————  
**तृतीयोऽध्यायः**

**उदगयने स्वक्षेत्रे स्वोच्चे स्वांशत्रिभागहोरासु।  
स्वदिने बलवान् भानुर्मित्रक्षेत्रेषु मध्यबलः॥१॥**

**राशिप्रमुखे भानुर्बलवान् मध्याश्रितस्तु मध्यबलः।  
राश्यन्ते बलहीनः सन्ध्यायां ग्रस्तकाले च॥२॥**

 *Slokas* 1-2.—The Sun is said to be strong when he is in the Northerly course (Uttarayana), when he is posited in his own house, his exaltation Rasi, Navamsa, Drekkana or Hora, He is also strong in his own day (Sunday). But in the houses of his friends, he is of moderate strength. He is strong when posited in the initial portion of a Rasi; of medium strength in the middle of a Rasi and weak at the end of it. He is likewise weak during twilights as well as during eclipses.

**चन्द्रो वृषभं यातो दक्षिणमार्गे स्वभे स्वहोरायाम्।  
रात्रौ स्वांशे स्वदिने स्वद्रेक्काणे बलान्वितः प्रोक्तः॥३॥**

**प्रतिपत्पूर्वदशाहे मध्यबलः शीतगुः सिते पक्षे।  
श्रेष्ठो द्वितीयदशके स्वल्पबलश्चन्द्रमास्तृतीये च॥४॥**

**उत्तरपथं प्रयातः प्रदक्षिणं वा ग्रहाणां च।  
सौम्ययुतो दृष्टो वा सर्वग्रहवीक्षितो बली चन्द्रः॥५॥**

**अबलः प्रवेशकाले मध्यबलो मध्यमाश्रितश्चन्द्रः।  
राश्यन्ते बलयुक्तः पूर्णः स्थानेषु सर्वेषु॥६॥**

 *Slokas* 3-6.—The Moon is said to be strong in Vrishabha Rasi, in her Southerly course, own house, her own Hora, at night, in her own Navamsa, in her own day (Monday) and in her own Drekkana. She is of moderate strength in the first ten days of the bright fort-night, very strong in the second ten-day-period and weak in the last ten days. When the Moon is towards the North of planets or goes in a clock-wise direction around the planets, or when she is conjoined with or aspected by benefics, or when she is aspected by all the other planets, she becomes strong. She is weak in the beginning of a Rasi (at the time of entering it), of middling strength when posited in the middle, and strong when posited at the end of a Rasi. She is strong in all houses when she is full.

**निर्जितशत्रुर्वक्रस्तेजस्वी मकरकुम्भमीनेषु।  
याम्यायने च बलवान् रात्रौ च धरासुतः प्रोक्तः॥७॥**

**स्वांशे क्षेत्रे स्वदिने स्वद्रेक्काणे बलान्वितो भौमः।  
दशमर्क्षस्थो बलवान् समस्तराशौ तु विज्ञेयः॥८॥**

**आदावतिबलयुक्तो हीनबलो मध्यमाश्रितो रक्तः।  
भवनानामवसाने मध्यबलश्चैव विज्ञेयः॥९॥**

 *Slokas* 7-9.—Mars is said to be strong when he is victorious in a planetary war, when he is retrograde, when he is brilliant, when he is posited in Makara, Kumbha or Meena, in his Southerly course and at night. He is also strong in his own Navamsa, his own house, in his own day and in his own Drekkana. He is strong in any Rasi that happens to be the 10th Bhava. He is very strong in the beginning of a Rasi, weak in the middle, and of moderate strength at the end of a Rasi.

**रविमुक्तश्चापगतः क्षेत्राद्यंशं गतो बली सौम्यः।  
रात्रौ दिवा च बलवान् वक्रो बलवान् विनार्कयुतिम्॥१०॥**

**राशिमुखे मध्यबलः सम्पूर्णबलश्च मध्यसंयातः।  
राश्यन्ते बलहीनो द्रेक्काणे मिथुनभे च बलयुक्तः॥११॥**

 *Slokas* 10-11.—Mercury is strong when he emerges after being eclipsed by the Sun, when he is posited in Dhanus, when in his own Kshetra, Amsa, etc. (in his own day also) and both by day and night. He is strong when retrograde except during his eclipse. He is moderately strong in the beginning of Rasis, very strong in the middle and weak at the end of Rasis. He is strong in his own Drekkana and in Mithuna.

**जीवः स्वक्षेत्रगतः कर्कटराशौ च वृश्चिके नियतम्।  
उदगयने पूर्वाह्णे द्रेक्काणनवांशके जयी बलवान्॥१२॥**

**राशिमुखे मध्यबलः सम्पूर्णबलश्च मध्यमं यातः।  
राश्यन्ते बलहीनो वक्रो बलवान् न नीचराशौ स्यात्॥१३॥**

* Slokas* 12-13.—Jupiter is possessed of utmost strength when he is posited in his own house, in signs Karkataka and Vrischika, as well as in the forenoon, in his Northerly course, in his own decanate and Navamsa, and when he is victorious in a planetary war. He is moderately strong in the initial portion of a Rasi, very strong in the middle, and weak at its end. He is strong when retrograde, provided he is not in his depression sign.

**त्रिकषट्कमण्डलगतो वक्रो भानोः पुरःसरं यातः।  
स्वगृहोच्चगोत्तरस्थः शुक्रो बलवान् दिनापरार्धे च॥१४॥**

**राश्यादौ बलहीनो मध्ये बलवान् विनिर्गमे मध्यः।  
चन्द्रसमागमकाले युद्धेष्वेवं विजयी स्यात्॥१५॥**

 *Slokas* 14-15.—Venus is strong when he is posited in the 3rd, 6th and 12th houses, when retrograde, when in advance of the Sun, in the afternoon, in his own house, when in exaltation and when posited to the North of planets. He is weak in the beginning of a Rasi, strong in the middle, and moderately strong at the end. He is strong when he is conjoined with the Moon and also when he is victorious in a planetary fight.

**कृष्णे निशि वक्रगतः स्वगृहतुलादक्षिणायनगतश्च।  
उद्यंश्च मन्दगामी निर्जितशत्रुश्च विज्ञेयः॥१६॥**

**मन्दोऽबलः प्रवेशे मध्येऽल्पबलो बली गमनकाले।  
सर्वस्थानेषु शनिर्बलान्वितं केचिदिच्छन्ति॥१७॥**

 *Slokas* 16-17.—Saturn is strong in the dark fortnight, at night, when he is retrograde, in his own house, in Tula, in his Southerly course, while just rising (in the Lagna), while moving slowly and when victorious in fight. He is weak in the beginning of a Rasi, moderately strong in the middle, and strong at the end. Some declare Saturn to be strong in all positions.

**वृषमेषालिकुलीरे** **घटराशिसमन्विते बली राहुः।  
चन्द्रार्कयोगकाले परिवेषे राशिनिर्गमे बलवान्॥१८॥**

 *Sloka* 18.—Rahu is said to be strong in signs Mesha, Vrishabha, Karkataka, Vrischika and Kumbha. So is he when in conjunction with the Sun and the Moon, during Parivesha (misty circle around the Sun or the Moon) and at the end of a Rasi.

**चापापरार्द्धमीने कन्यावृषयोर्बलान्वितः केतुः।  
केतोर्दर्शनकाले शक्रधनुर्दर्शने च रात्रौ च॥१९॥**

 *Sloka* 19.—Ketu is strong in the latter half of Dhanus, in the signs Meena, Kanya and Vrishabha. He is also strong at night, or when a meteor or the rainbow is sighted.

**चापाजसिंहमीनेष्वर्को लग्नाश्रितो बली भवति।  
तेष्वेव कर्मराशौ विज्ञेयोऽन्यत्र बलहीनः॥२०॥**

 *Sloka* 20.—The Sun is strong in signs Mesha, Simha, Dhanus and Meena when they happen to be the Lagna or the 10th house. Elsewhere he is weak.

**प्रालेयांशुर्मिथुने कन्यायां चापि लग्नगो बलवान्।  
मीने हयपूर्वार्द्धे जामित्रगतश्च बलयुक्तः॥२१॥**

**वृषराशिसन्निविष्टश्चापार्धे पश्चिमे च कर्मस्थः।  
कर्कटकमिथुनयोरपि चन्द्रः पातालमाश्रितो बलवान्॥२२॥**

 *Slokas* 21-22.—The Moon is said to be strong in Mithuna, Kanya, the first half of Dhanus or Meena, when she occupies the Lagna or the 7th house.

 Another interpretation. The Moon is strong in Mithuna and Kanya when they happen to be the Lagna; in signs Meena and the first half of Dhanus. She is also strong when in Vrishabha as well as in the latter half of Dhanus when they happen to be the 7th or the 10th house. So is she when posited in Mithuna and Karkataka when they happen to be the 4th house.

**प्राग्लग्ने क्षितिसूनुर्बलान्वितः कुम्भराशिना सार्द्धम्।  
कर्कटवृश्चिकयोरपि पत्नीस्थानं समाश्रितो बलवान्॥२३॥**

**मृगपूर्वार्द्धे मिथुने कर्मणि चापार्द्धके सपाताले।  
निरुपहतवर्णवीर्यो बलान्वितः स्वत्रिकोणे च॥२४॥**

 *Slokas* 23-24.—Mars is strong in Kumbha when it is the Ascendant. Similarly, he is strong in Karkataka and Vrischika when they happen to be the 7th house. He is strong in the first half of Makara, in Mithuna when it is the 10th house, and in the first half of Dhanus when it is the 4th house. So is he when his brilliance and valour are not obsucred, and when he is posited in his own house and his Moolatrikona house.

**मृगसिंहकर्किवृश्चिकलग्नस्थः स्वांशके बली सौम्यः।  
पातालस्यश्चापे वृषभेऽस्तमये झषे च कर्मस्थः॥२५॥**

* Sloka* 25.—Mercury is strong in Makara, Simha, Karkataka and Vrichiska when they happen to be the Lagna and in his own Navamsa. He is strong in Dhanus as the 4th house, in Vrishabha as the 7th house and in Meena as the 10th house.

**सिंहवृषाजधनुर्द्धरवृश्चिकमीनेषु** **लग्नगो बलवान्।  
कर्मणि पातालगतो बलवाञ्जीवोऽबलोऽन्यत्र॥२६॥**

 *Sloka* 26.—Jupiter is strong in Mesha, Vrishabha, Simba, Vrischika, Dhanus and Meena which happen to be the Ascendant, the 4th house or the 10th house. Elsewhere, he is weak.

**सिंहाजकुम्भकौर्पिषु लग्नस्थो भार्गवः स्वराशौ च।  
बलवांश्चापान्त्यगतो वृश्चिकराशौ च पत्नीस्थः॥२७॥**

**हयपूर्वार्द्धे मीने हरिवृश्चिकयोस्तु कर्मदेशस्थः।  
बलवान् सितो जितारिर्मृगपश्चार्द्धे च हिबुकस्थः॥२८॥**

 *Slokas* 27.28.—Venus is strong in Mesha, Simha, Vrischika and Kumbha when any one of them happens to be the Lagna; in the latter half of Dhanus and Vrischika identical with the 7th house; in the first half of Dhanus, in Meena, Simha and Vrischika as the 10th house; and in the latter half of Makara as the 4th house. He is also strong in his own Rasi or when he is victorious in a fight.

**कुम्भे तुलाधरे च प्राच्यां हिबुके च सूर्यजो बलवान्।  
मेषूरणे च सिंहे पृष्ठोदयवर्जितेऽस्तमये॥२९॥**

 *Sloka* 29.—Saturn is strong in Tula and Kumbha as the Ascendant or the 4th house; in Simha as the 10th house; and in a sign that does not rise with its hind part as the 7th house.

**लग्नस्थौ बुधजीवौ कर्मणि सूर्यारकौ च दिग्बलिनौ।  
हिबुके भृगुचन्द्रमसावस्तमये सूर्यनन्दनश्चापि॥३०॥**

**आपोक्लिबेष्ववीर्या मध्यबलाः फणपराश्रिताः सर्वे।  
केन्द्राश्रिताश्च बलिनः सदा ग्रहाः कीर्तिता यवनैः॥३१॥**

 *Slokas* 30-31.—Mercury and Jupiter in the Lagna, the Sun and Mars in the 10th house, the Moon and Venus in the 4th, and Saturn in the 7th, have directional strength. All the planets are weak in the Apoklima houses; moderately strong in Phanaparas and always strong in the Kendras. So declare the Yavanas.

 In Sloka 30, **शुक्रेन्दू पाताले द्यूने सौरो नवांशकेऽप्येवम्।** is another reading.

**सौराद् द्विगुणो भौमो बलवान् भौमाच्चतुर्गुणः सौम्यः।  
जीवोऽष्टगुणः सौम्याज्जीवादष्टाधिको भृगुर्बलवान्॥३२॥**

**शुक्राद्धि षोडशबलश्चन्द्रो भानुस्ततोऽधिको द्विगुणः।  
तद्वद् द्विगुणः सर्वेषां राहुर्बलवान् निसर्गतश्च॥३३॥**

 *Slokas* 32-33.—Mars is twice as strong as Saturn; Mercury is four times as strong as Mars; Jupiter is eight times as Mercury; Venus, 8 times as Jupiter; the Moon, 16 times as Venus; the Sun, twice as the Moon; and Rahu who has in-born strength and who is the strongest of all the planets, is twice as strong as the Sun.

**चन्द्रार्कौ बलयुक्तौ कुजादयः प्रोक्तमार्गबलहीनाः।  
शुभफलदास्ते सर्वे दशासु योगेषु सञ्चिन्त्याः॥३४॥**

 *Sloka* 34.—If in a nativity the Sun and the Moon are very strong and Mars and others weak according to the rules given above, all the planets are to be considered to yield only good effects in their respective Dasa periods and yogas (by conjunctions or special configurations).

 The idea is that in spite of the weakness of the other planets, the luminaries being strong influence all the planets for good.

**भानामवस्थानगताः क्रमेण मन्दार्यभौमार्कसितज्ञचन्द्राः।  
तेषामधःस्थानगतो बलीयान् राहुर्महीमण्डलमूर्धसंस्थः॥३५॥**

* Sloka* 35.—Saturn, Jupiter, Mars, the Sun, Venus, Mercury and the Moon are the planets arranged *seriatim* according to the length of the time they abide in the zodiacal signs. Rahu (ascending node) whose position is at the topmost of the Earth's orbit has predominating strength when he occupies a position below the planets above-mentioned, i. e., when he is *before* or to the east of them. They become stronger and stronger as they occupy lower and lower positions among the signs of the zodiac. But Rahu becomes strong when he occupies the top of the Earth's circle, i. e., the 10th house.

**प्रोक्तप्रकारैः प्रबलान्विता ये मौढ्याश्रितास्ते ह्यबला भवन्ति।  
भावेषु योगेषु दशाफलेषु न सम्यगुक्तानि फलानि सन्ति॥३६॥**

 *Sloka* 36.—The planets which are endowed with strength according to the rules enumerated above become weak if they be eclipsed by the Sun. Hence they do not produce the good effects that are declared to fructify in their Dasa periods, Yogas and their Bhavas.

 However strong a planet may be, still it will not produce any good effect, if it be eclipsed; and during its Dasa, only bad effects will accrue to the native This applies also to the Bhava which the planet occupies; i. e. it will only spoil the Bhava. Similarly, if the planet forms any yoga, even that will be harmed by the said planet.

**सौम्यग्रहैर्बलयुतैः सुभगास्तेजस्विनः सुरूपाश्च।  
सौम्याद्बलिभिः पापैर्मूर्खा पापाः प्रजायन्ते॥३७॥**

इति श्रीवराहमिहिरसुतश्रीपृथुयशोविरचिते होरासारे बलनिरूपणाध्यायस्तृतीयः॥

 *Sloka* 37.—Benefic planets being strong (uneclipsed also) usher into the world men that are fortunate (amiable), brilliant (valorous) and handsome. If, on the other hand, the malefics are stronger than the benefics, only idiots and sinful persons will be born.

Thus ends the 3rd Adhyaya called the 'Enumeration of Strength'.  
-----------

**चतुर्थोऽध्यायः**

**अङ्गनाजन्मपीडर्क्षं याते ताराधिपे तथा।  
रक्तेक्षिते युते वा स्यादार्तवं गर्भकारणम्॥१॥**

 *Sloka* 1.—When the Moon in her transit is posited in an Apachaya house in a woman's nativity and is aspected by or conjoined with Mars, menses will set in which will (be the cause of) lead to her pregnancy (conception).

**बालवृद्धातुरावन्ध्या मुक्त्वा चान्यासु लक्षणम्।  
त्रयोदशनिशाः स्नानादृतुकालं प्रचक्षते॥२॥**

** ***Sloka* 2—-Barring children, old, sickly and barren women, the Ritu Kala (period of conception) in the case of other women is declared to be 13 nights after bathing (on the 4th day).

**स्त्रीणामुपचयस्येन्दौ शुभपुङ्ग्रहवीक्षिते।  
शुभोदये युग्मरात्रौ निषिञ्चेत्पुत्रधारणम्॥३॥**

 *Sloka* 3.—When the Moon occupying an Upachaya house with respect to a woman's nativity is aspected by the male benefic planet, or rises with it, sexual union should take place on a night of even number (or the seed must be sown) for bearing a son.

**रवीन्दुशुक्रजीवैर्वा स्वर्क्षे वा स्वांशकोदये।  
भौमदृष्टे युते वाऽपि पुंयोगाः स्युरिमे स्मृताः॥४॥**

** ***Sloka* 4.—The following are the yogas leading to the sexual union to be effective (for the birth of a son):—(1) The Sun, the Moon, Venus and Jupiter being posited in their own houses ; (2) in their own Navamsas; or (3) in the Ascendant and being aspected by or conjoined with Mars.

**लग्नस्थो वा सुतस्थो वा धर्मस्थो वा बली गुरुः।  
प्रोत्तर्क्षे शुभवारे स्याद्धारयेद्गर्भमुत्तमम्॥५॥**

 *Sloka* 5.—Jupiter strong and posited in the Ascendant, the 5th or the 9th house, or in any of the houses mentioned in the previous verse (or in a good asterism) and on an auspicious week day, leads to the conception of a male child in the womb.

**लग्नात्मजेशौ संयुक्तावन्योन्यं वाऽपि वीक्षितौ।  
क्षेत्रे परस्परस्थौ वा पुत्रयोगा इमे स्मृताः॥६॥**

**लग्नं मुक्त्वा तु विषमं बलवान् भास्करात्मजः।  
स्थितस्तु पुत्रदो ज्ञेयो नान्यग्रहयुतेक्षितः॥७॥**

**पुङ्ग्रहाः षष्ठलाभस्थाः पञ्चमेशो बली यदा।  
सर्वे विषमराशिस्थाः पुत्रयोगा इमे स्मृताः॥८॥**

 *Slokas* 6-8.—The following are the yogas that lead to the birth of a son:—(1) The conjunction of the lords of the Lagna and the 5th house; (2) the mutual aspect of these two lords; (3) exchange of places between the lords; (4) Saturn being strong, posited in an odd house except the Lagna and not being aspected by or conjoined with any other planet; (5) all the male planets occupying the 6th or (and) the 11th house; (6) the lord of the 5th house being very strong; and (7) all the planets occupying odd houses. (All these refer to the **आधान**.)

**चन्द्रशुक्रौ युतौ वाऽपि पञ्चमे दशमेऽपि वा।  
स्वर्क्षे वास्वांशके वाऽपि स्त्रीयोगाः शास्त्रलक्षिताः॥९॥**

**राहूदये चन्द्रदृष्टे विपरीतेऽथवा यदि।  
चन्द्रहोरागते शुक्रे केन्द्रस्थे वा तथैव च॥१०॥**

* Slokas* 9-10.—The following are the female producing yogas laid down in the science:—(1) the conjunction of the Moon and Venus either in the 5th house or the 10th house (2) their occupying their own Rasis; (3) they being in their own Navamsas; (4) Rahu in the Lagna being aspected by the Moon; (5) the Moon in the Lagna being aspected by Rahu; (6) Venus in the lunar Hora and (7) Venus in a Kendra.

**द्व्यङ्गस्थिते बुधे लग्ने दृष्टे वा दशमेऽपि वा।  
यमलं कुरुते योगं पुंस्त्रियो राशिसंश्रयात्॥११॥**

 *Sloka* 11.—When Mercury is in the Lagna identical with a dual sign or when such a Lagna is aspected by Mercury, or when Mercury is in the 10th house, twins will be born, the sex of the twins being decided by the Rasis and Amsas occupied by the above.

**युग्मर्क्षगौ चन्द्रशुक्रौ द्व्यंशस्थौ वा बुधोदये।  
विषमेष्वारजीवौ वा यमलः स्यान्न संशयः॥१२॥**

 *Sloka* 12.—There will undoubtedly be born twins under the following yogas; (1) the Moon and Venus both posited in even signs, or in dual Navamsas; (2) Mercury in the Lagna and Mars and Jupiter in odd signs (or Amsas).

 \[In the above case if Mercury occupies Mithuna or Dhanus and the same Navamsa, or if Mercury aspects the Lagna, both in male dual Rasi or Amsa, there will be two boys, otherwise, girls.\]

**अन्योन्यमभिवीक्षेते चन्द्रादित्यौ दिवा यदि।  
बुधमन्दौ तथा रात्रौ षण्डयोगद्वयं भवेत्॥१३॥**

 *Sloka* 13.—If the Sun and the Moon aspect each other at day time or (2) if Mercury and Saturn aspect each other at night, eunuchs will be born under these two yogas.

**विबीजिनामिमे योगा निष्फलाश्च भवन्ति हि।  
अन्धाश्च नृगुणैर्हीना यथा योगास्तथाविधाः॥१४॥**

 *Sloka* 14.—The above yogas (planetary positions) will be utterly null and void for persons without the seed or virility, just as blind men are devoid of manly qualities. So the blind and these yogas stand on a par with each other.

**कललं प्रथमे मासि तस्य मासाधिपो भृगुः।  
द्वितीये मासि भौमस्तु गर्भः पिङ्गा(ण्डा)क्षबीजवत्॥१५॥**

**गर्भाङ्कुरस्तृतीये स्यात्तस्य मासाधिपो गुरुः।  
मज्जास्थिसम्भवो मासि चतुर्थे भास्करोऽधिपः॥१६॥**

**पञ्चमे मासि सोमस्तु त्वङ्मेदोरक्तसम्भवः।  
सर्वाङ्गसम्भवः षष्ठे तस्य मासाधिपः शनिः॥१७॥**

**ज्ञानेन्द्रियप्रवेशस्तु सप्तमे मासि सोमजः।  
भवनेशोऽष्टमे मासि क्षुत्तृष्णासम्भ्रमो भवेत्॥१८॥**

**उद्वेगो गर्भसंस्थस्य मासीशो नवमे शशी।  
प्रसूतिर्दशमे मासि मासेशो भास्करः स्मृतः॥१९॥**

**मासलक्षणयुक्तश्चेद्गर्भः सुखमवाप्नुयात्।  
ऊनाधिकगुणांस्तस्य ज्ञात्वा प्रसवमादिशेत्॥२०॥**

 *Slokas* 15-20.—In the first month of pregnancy, the foetus will be in the form of only coagulated blood and is presided over by Venus; in the second month, it resembles the seed of Pingaksha and is presided over by Mars; in the third, it is in the form of a sprout and is presided over by Jupiter; in the fourth, it gets marrow and bones and is presided over by the Sun; in the fifth, skin, fat and blood are produced in it, and the lord of the month is the Moon; in the sixth month, all the limbs arise and the month is presided over by Saturn; in the seventh month, the senses make their appearance and the month is presided over by Mercury; in the eighth month, the child in the womb feels hunger and thirst, and the month is presided over by the lord of the **आधान** Lagna; in the ninth month the child gets movements or pain and the month is presided over by the Moon; and in the tenth month, delivery of the child will take place, and the lord of the month is the Sun. If the foetus be endowed with the characteristics prescribed for each month, it will develop without any trouble (i. e., if the lords of the months be not be afflicted by malefics and so on). The delivery should be predicted after a careful survey of the strength or otherwise of the presiding planets of the several months.

**यस्य मासाधिपो रक्तो भग्नो वाऽस्तङ्गतोऽपि वा।  
तस्मिन् मासे क्षयं याति प्रसवो न भविष्यति॥२१॥**

 *Sloka* 21.—In the particular month whose lord is afflicted, defeated or eclipsed, the child in the womb will perish and it will not be delivered safe.

**गर्भाधाने चरे राशौ दशमे मासि सूयते।  
स्थिरे चैकादशे मासि ह्युभये द्वादशे सवः॥२२॥**

** ***Sloka* 22.—If the Lagna at impregnation be a moveable sign (if the Moon at the time be posited in a....), the delivery will take place in the 10th month; if it be a fixed one, delivery will be in the 11th month ; and if in a dual sign, it will be in the 12th month.

**निषेककाले यत्प्रोक्तं फलं प्रश्नेः तदादिशेत्।  
गर्भप्रश्ने च नारीणामारूढे विषमर्क्षगे॥२३॥**

**पुङ्ग्रहेण युते दृष्टे गर्भस्थः पुरुषो भवेत्।**  
**पुंराशिस्पर्शने देहे पुमान् भवति निश्चयात् ॥२४॥**

**पुरुषस्पर्शने प्रष्टा पुरुषाक्षरमुच्चरेत्।  
देहस्य दक्षिणे भागे स्पर्शनेन पुमान् भवेत्॥२५॥**

**अन्यथा स्त्रीप्रसूतिः स्यात् स्त्रीग्रहेण युतेक्षितात्।**

 *Slokas* 23–25½.—The effects declared for the **आधान** (inpregnation ) should be applied to queries as well. If the Arudha Lagna, in respect of a query regarding the sex of a child in a woman's womb, be an odd sign, aspected by and conjoined with male planets, then the child will be a male one. If the querist should touch a man, utter a male syllable, or touch the right side of his body, then the child may be a male one. Otherwise, when the Lagna is aspected by or conjoined with a female planet, a female child should be predicted.

**लग्नेन्द्वोर्यो बलवांस्तस्य द्विरसांशकान्वितो राशिः।  
यावांस्तस्मात्तावति परतो राशौ विधौ स्थिते प्रसवः॥२६॥**

**तत्कालेन्दुनवांशाञ्जामित्रे शीतगौ स्थिते सूतिः।  
उदयनवांशाधिपतेः क्षेत्रं याते विधौ तदा प्रसवः॥२७॥**

**रात्रिदिनराशिभान् भुक्त्वा तावद्गते दिवारात्रौ।  
हिबुकेशे बलयुक्ते शुभयोगे वा सुखी गर्भः॥२८॥**

इति श्रीवराहमिहिरसुतश्रीपृथुयशोविरचिते होरासारे निषेकजन्माध्यायश्चतुर्थः॥

 *Slokas* 26-28.—Of the Lagna and the Moon at the time of query find which is stronger. Note the Dwadasamsa of this stronger significator. When the Moon transits through a Rasi which is as many signs removed from the sign indicated by the Dwadsamsa, the birth of the child may be predicted.

 **Note:**—For example, let us assume that the Moon is in Vrishabha in Tula-Dwadasamsa, and that the Moon is stronger than the Lagna. Then the birth may be predicted when the Moon transits through Meena—which is the 6th from Tula, since Tula Dwadasamsa is the 6th Dwadasamsa in Vrishabha.

 The birth may also take place when the Moon is posited in the 7th house from the Rasi owning the Navamsa of the Moon at the time of the query; or it may happen when the Moon is posited in the house of the lord of the rising Navamsa; or it may happen when so much of the day or night is passed as the fraction of the Lagna which is a night or a day sign as the case may be. The child in the womb will be quite all right when the lord of the 4th house (from the Prasna Lagna) is strong, or is conjoined with benefics (or aspected by benefics).

Thus ends the 4th Adhyaya entitled the “Impregnation and Births.”  
--------------

**पञ्चमोऽध्यायः**

**अथ मातापित्ररिष्टं सूतिकालस्य लक्षणम्।  
प्रवक्ष्यामि समासेन सद्यो मरणमेव च॥१॥**

 *Sloka* 1.—I shall now succinctly treat of the evil effects accruing to the parents of a child and also define the characteristics of the time of its birth and (the causes of) its sudden death.

**जातस्य पूर्वषट्कस्था ये ग्रहास्ते शुभप्रदाः।  
ये ग्रहाः परषट्कस्था परोक्षफलदायकाः॥२॥**

 *Sloka* 2.—The planets that are posited in the first six signs in a nativity yield good effects (in the first half of the life), while those in the latter six signs, in the second half.

 A better interpretation would be only those planets that are in the first six signs yield good results which can be experienced by the native, while those in the other produce good effects which he cannot enjoy directly. He may enjoy in dreams; he may be spoken highly of in his absence etc.,

**भानुः पिता च जन्तूनां चन्द्रो माता तथैव च।  
तयोर्बलाबलं ज्ञात्वा पितृमातृगुणान्वदेत्॥३॥**

** ***Sloka* 3.—The Sun and the Moon are the father and the mother respectively of living beings. Hence, one should pronounce the qualities of the parents after ascertaining the strength and weakness of these two luminaries.

**पापदृष्टो युतो भानुः पापमध्यगतोऽपि वा।  
पित्ररिष्टं विजानीयाच्छिशोर्जातस्य निश्चयात्॥४॥**

 *Sloka* 4.—If the Sun be aspected by, conjoined with, or hemmed in between malefics, there will certainly arise trouble (evil effects), it must be understood, to the father of the child born.

**भानोष्षष्ठाष्टमर्क्षस्थै पापैः सौम्यविवर्जितैः।  
चतुरश्रगतैर्वाऽपि पित्ररिष्टं समादिशेत्॥५॥**

 *Sloka* 5.—When the 6th and 8th, or the 4th and 8th houses from the Sun are occupied by malefics alone, without the association of benefics, trouble to the father must be declared.

**भामांशकस्थिते भानौ स्वपुत्रेण निरीक्षिते।  
प्राक्जन्मनो निवृत्तिः स्यान्मृतिर्वाऽपि शिशोः पितुः॥६॥**

 *Sloka* 6—When the Sun occupying an Amsa of Mars is aspected by Saturn, the child's elder brother (or sister) will quit the world or the father of the child may die.

**भौमे सूर्यांशकयुते सुखभे धर्मभेऽपि वा।  
नेक्षिते(तो) गुरुशुक्राभ्यां नेक्षते पितरं शिशुः॥७॥**

 *Sloka* 7—If Mars occupying an Amsa belonging to the Sun or Saturn in the 4th or the 9th house be not aspected by Jupiter or Venus, the child will not see the father, i. e, the latter will die before its birth.

 **भौमः सौरांशकगतः** is another reading in the first line.

**मात्ररिष्टं तु चन्द्रेण ज्ञात्वैवं पूर्ववद्वदेत्।  
क्षीणचन्द्रात् त्रिकोणस्थैः पापैः सौम्यविवर्जितैः॥८॥**

**मात्ररिष्टं तु चन्द्रेण ज्ञात्वैवं पूर्ववद्वदेत्।**

 *Slokas* 8,8½—Harm to the mother will have to be predicted as before through the Moon When malefics without any benefic association occupy the 5th and 9th houses reckoned from the waning (weak) Moon, the boy will undoubtedly be bereaved of the mother as before.

**एकांशस्थौ तु मन्दारौ यत्र कुत्र स्थितावपि॥९॥**

**शशिकेन्द्रगतौ वाऽपि द्विमातृभ्यां स जीवति।**

 * Sloka* 9,9½—When Saturn and Mars occupying the same Amsa (Navamsa) are posited any where or are in Kendra house or houses with respect to the Moon, the child lives with two mothers (does not live with its lawful mother).

 **मात्रा सह न जीवति** is another reading.

**तयोर्बलाबलेनैव पितृमातृगृहोद्भवः॥१०॥**

**मूर्तिर्बलान्विता यस्य पितृवेश्मनि सम्भवः।**

 *Sloka* 9½–10½—Through the strength or weakness of the two, viz., Saturn and Mars, the birth of the child in the house of the father and the mother respectively should be inferred. If the Lagna be very strong, the birth will be in the father's house.

**चरराश्यंशके भानौ चराश्यंशकोदये॥११॥**

**शिशोः पितान्यदेशस्थः सूतौ लग्नं न पश्यति।**

 *Sloka* 11,11½.—When both the Sun and the Lagna occupy a moveable sign and a moveable Amsa, the father of the child will be in a foreign place, provided the Sun does not aspect the Lagna.

**लग्नं न पश्यति विधौ चरराश्यंशके स्थिते॥१२॥**

**परोक्षगः पिता तस्य सूतिकाले न संशयः।**

 *Sloka* 12,12½.—When the Moon occupying a moveable Rasi and Amsa does not aspect the Lagna, the father is undoubtedly in a distant place at the time of birth of the child.

**वागीशे नीचसंस्थे च चन्द्रे राश्यंशसन्धिगे॥१३॥**

**मूको वाऽपि जडोवाऽपि सौम्यैः पापसमन्वितैः।**

 *Sloka* 13,13½—When Jupiter is posited in his debilitation sign, the Moon is at the junction of two Rasis or two Amsas, and the benefics are conjoined with malefics, the child born will be dumb or imbecile.

**भाग्यबन्धुगताः पापाः लग्नेशे बलवर्जिते॥१४॥**

**जन्मकाले पिता रोगी कुजदृष्टेऽथवा युते।**

 *Sloka* 14,14½.—When the lord of the Lagna is weak and aspected by or conjoined with Mars, and malefics occupy the 4th and 9th houses, the father is bedridden at the time of the birth.

**अर्काशकस्थिते मन्देऽप्यर्केणैव निरीक्षिते॥१५॥**

**सूतिकाले पिता दुःखी शिशो रिःफाष्टमेऽपि वा।**

 *Sloka* 15,15½ —When Saturn occupying a Navamsa of the Sun is also aspected by him or is posited in the 8th or the 12th Bhava, the child's father will be miserable at the time of birth.

**न पश्यति गुरौ चन्द्रं लग्नं च परजातकः॥१६॥  
सार्केन्दुनेक्षिते जीवे सूर्येन्दू पापसंयुतौ।**

 *Sloka* 16,16½— When the Moon or the Lagna is not aspected by Jupiter, the child is born of a paramour. The same effect should be declared if Jupiter is aspected by the Moon in conjunction with the Sun, and if the Sun and the Moon are associated with malefics.

**गुरुराश्यंशके चन्द्रे चन्द्रराश्यंशके गुरौ॥१७॥**

**परस्परांशराशिस्थौ चन्द्रार्कौ नैव जारजः।  
पूर्वोक्तयोगसम्भूतो परैर्जात इतीष्यते॥१८॥**

 *Slokas* 17-18.—When the Moon is posited in a Rasi or Navamsa belonging to Jupiter, or Jupiter is in a Rasi or Navamsa owned by the Moon, or when the Sun and the Moon are posited each in the other's Rasi or Amsa, the child should be positively declared to be legitimate and not born of a paramour, while those born under the yogas mentioned in the previous verse are to be pronounced as illegitimate.

**कालस्याङ्गविभागेषु यस्मिन् राशौ शुभाः स्थिताः।  
तत्र लक्ष्मव्रणादीनि चिन्तयेत्तन्निमित्ततः॥१९॥**

 *Sloka* 19—Among the signs which represent the various limbs of Kalapurusha, note which Rasis are occupied by benefics; one should expect in those limbs some marks (moles), scars (ulcers) etc. caused by those planets.

 Note. Benefics cause only moles and such other marks, while malefics do ulcers, etc.

**सद्यो मरणयोगा हि बहवः शास्त्रदर्शिताः। (लक्षिताः।)  
तेभ्यः सिद्धान्तयोगास्तु वक्ष्यन्तेऽत्र समासतः॥२०॥**

 *Sloka* 20—Many yogas leading to the sudden death of a child have been enumerated in the Sastras (science). I shall here briefly mention only the most important ones from among them.

**पित्रोर्दोषैर्मृताः केचित् केचिद्बालग्रहैर्मृताः।  
अपरे रिष्टयोगेभ्य (योगाद्यै) स्त्रिविधा बालमृत्यवः॥२१॥**

 *Sloka* 21.— Child-mortality is of three kinds: vis. (1) Some children die on account of the faults of their parents; (2) some die owing to Balagrahas (certain demons) and (3) others die owing to malignant planetary positions.

**एवं सूक्ष्मतरं ज्ञात्वा शिशोर्दोषगुणान्वदेत्।  
आद्वादशाब्दं मर्त्यानामायुर्ज्ञातुं न शक्यते॥२२॥**

**जपहोमचिकित्साद्यैर्बालं रक्षेद्गुणाधिकैः।**

 *Slokas* 22, 22½.—One should begin to predict the merits and demerits of a child only after ascertaining thus the aforementioned things minutely. It is not possible to ascertain the longevity of human beings until they are 12 years of age. Hence children should be protected through Japa (incantations of holy Mantras, worship of the Fire-God, performance of sacrifices, by administering medicines, etc.,) all of which are productive of immense good.

** ** न तु जीविनः in another reading for गतजीविनाः।

**राशिसन्धिषु ये जातास्ते बाला गतजीविनाः॥२३॥**

**पापदृष्टो युतो वाऽपि निःसंशयमिति स्मृतम्।  
गण्डान्तेषूद्भवो मर्त्यः पितृमातृकुलान्तकः॥२४॥**

**यदि जीवेत्सभूपालो गजवाजिसमन्वितः।**

 *Slokas* 23-24½.—Those children that are born at the junction of two signs are either born dead or are shortlived. This is all the more certain, it is said, when the Lagna is aspected by, or is conjoined with malefics. One born in a Gandanta (Adh I Sl. 4 *supra*) Tara will destroy the entire families of his parents. But if he lives at all, he will become a king rich in elephants and horses.

**चन्द्रादित्यौ तृतीयस्थौ क्रूरभे क्रूरसंयुतौ॥२५॥  
व्याधिं तस्य विजानीयात् त्रिवर्षं नातिवर्तते।**

 *Sloka* 25,25½.—When the Sun and the Moon are posited in the 3rd house identical with a malefic sign and in conjunction with malefics in a nativity the native, it should be noted, will fall ill and take his exit before he completes three years.

**होरायाः कण्टकस्थेन्दौ निधनेशसमन्विते॥२६॥  
निधनस्थः परः कश्चिज्जातमात्रो विनश्यति।**

 *Sloka* 25½-26½.—If the Moon occupy a Kendra house with respect to the Lagna and be conjoined with the lord of the 8th house and if the 8th house be also occupied by a planet, the child will die immediately after birth.

**सहितौ चन्द्रजामित्रे यस्याङ्गारकभास्करौ॥२७॥  
राहूदये तथा जात आदशाहान्मृतो भवेत्।**

 *Sloka* 27,27½.—If at a birth, Mars and the Sun be jointly posited in the 7th house from the Moon and Rahu occupy the Lagna, then the child will die within ten days.

**चतुरश्रं गताः पापा वामदक्षिणतोऽपि वा॥२८॥**

**तदा यो व्याधिमाप्नोति दशरात्रं स जीवति।**  
**उद्यद्द्रेक्काणजामित्रे यस्य स्याद्दारुणो ग्रहः॥२९॥**

**क्षीणचन्द्रो विलग्नस्थः सद्यो हरति जीवितम्।**

 *Slokas* 29-29½.—When a malefic planet occupies the 7th house from the rising decanate, and the waning Moon is in the Lagna, the child will die immediately.

**अपोक्लिबे स्थिताः सर्वे ग्रहा बलविवर्जिताः॥३०॥  
षण्मासं वा द्विमासं वा तस्यायुः समुदाहृतम्।**

 *Sloka* 30-30½.—When all the planets are weak and occupy the Apoklima houses (3rd, 6th, 9th and 12th) reckoned from the Lagna, the child's longevity, it is declared, is only 2 months, or 6 months at the most.

**विलग्नाधिपतिर्नीचे निधने वाऽस्तगो भवेत्॥३१॥  
कृच्छ्रेण जीवितं विद्यान्मृतप्रायो भविष्यति।**

** **वार्कजोऽपि वा is another reading.

 *Sloka* 30½-31½.—If at a birth the lord of the Lagna be in depression, posited in the 8th house or be eclipsed, (or Saturn be in a similar position), the child will drag on a precarious existence and will be almost dead.

**केतोरुदयः पूर्वं पश्चादुल्कादिपतननिर्घाताः।  
रौद्रे सति च मुहूर्ते प्राणेभ्यस्त्यज्यते जन्तुः॥३२॥**

 *Sloka* 32.—A being that is born during a cruel Muhurta, when a Ketu is rising and immediately there are the fall of meteors, portentous thunder and the like, it will lose its life immediately.

**तीव्रफ(ब)ल राजयोगा यवनाद्यैर्ये विनिर्मितास्तेषु।  
जायन्ते खलु कुलजारिष्टं तेषु प्रसूतानाम्॥३३॥**

 *Sloka* 33.—Those that are born in the Rajayogas enumerated by the Yavanas and others, and whose effects are very harmful (cruel), will bring harm to the members of their family.

**ग्रहणपरिवेषकाले जातः पापग्रहे विलग्नस्थे।  
पापेन दृश्यमाने जीवति पक्षत्रयं त्रिमासे वा॥३४॥**

 लग्नेशे बलहीने is another reading.

 *Sloka* 34.—One born during an eclipse or when there is a misty circle around the Sun or the Moon, when a malefic is posited in the Lagna or when a malefic aspects it (or when the lord of the Lagna is weak), will. live for three fortnights or three months.

**अंशाधिपजन्मपती लग्नपतिश्चास्तमुपागता यस्य।  
जन्मावसरे मरणं तस्य भवेत्कतिपयाहेन॥३५॥**

 *Sloka* 35.—One, in whose nativity the lords of the Lagna, the sign occupied by the Moon and its Navamsa Rasi are all eclipsed, will die in a few days.

**सन्धिचतुष्टयकाले जन्तोर्मृत्युं समादिशेत्तज्ज्ञः।  
पापयुतो दृष्टो वा चन्द्रः सौम्यैरदृष्टयुतः॥३६॥**

 *Sloka* 36.—A wise man should predict the death of beings born at the four types of junctions, or when the Moon is conjoined with or aspected by a malefic, and when no benefics are in conjunction with or are aspecting her.

 For सन्धि चतुष्टय see सं-नि-III-23.

**उदयात्मजास्तरन्ध्रनवमव्ययसंस्थितः सपापेन्दुः।  
मरणमवश्यं कुरुते सौम्यग्रहवीक्षितो युतो न स्यात्॥३७॥**

 *Sloka* 37.—If the Moon be aspected by or conjoined with malefics and not benefics, or if she be associated with malefics and occupies the Lagna, the 5th, 7th, 8th, 9th or 12th house and at the same time be not aspected by or conjoined with benefics, she will certainly bring about the death of the native.

**लग्नाधिपजन्मपती षष्ठाष्टमरिःफगौ प्रसवकाले।  
अस्तमितौ मरणकरौ राशिप्रमितैर्वदेद्वर्षैः॥३८॥**

 *Sloka* 38.—If the lords of the Lagna and the sign occupied by the Moon be posited in a nativity in the 6th, 8th or 12th house, or be eclipsed, they will conspire to destroy the native in as many years as the number of the Rasi they occupy denotes.

**षष्ठाष्टमगे चन्द्रे लग्ने लग्नाधिपे दिवाजातः।  
दृष्टे शुभाशुभखगैः कृष्णेन्दौ वाऽपि सोऽल्पायुः॥३९॥**

 *Sloka* 39.—When the Moon is posited in the 6th or the 8th house and the Lagna is occupied by its lord, or when the waning Moon is aspected by both benefics and malefics, one born by day will be short-lived.

**लग्नाधिपतिश्चन्द्रो मरणपदस्थो हि कृष्णतां यातः।  
राहुयुतो दृष्टो वा निधनं स्यात्सप्तमे वर्षे॥४०॥**

 *Sloka* 40.—The lord of the Lagna or the waning Moon occupying the 8th house and being aspected by or conjoined with Rahu, will cause the native's death in the 7th year.

**क्षीणं यदा शशाङ्कं पश्येद्राहुः समागतः क्रूरेः।  
जन्मेशेऽस्तमयस्थे निधनं षष्ठाष्टमे वर्षे॥४१॥**

 *Sloka* 41.—When Rahu associated with malefics aspects the weak Moon, or when the lord of the sign occupied by the Moon is eclipsed (or occupies the 7th house), the native will die in the 6th or the 8th year.

**होराधिपतिर्द्यूने राहयुतो मरणमेव विदधाति।  
दिवसैस्त्रिसप्तसङ्ख्यैर्मासे वर्षेऽथवा नियतम्॥४२॥**

 *Sloka* 42.—The lord of the Lagna occupying in conjunction with Rahu the 7th house causes certain death in 21 days, months or years.

**अर्केन्दुयोगराशिः पापयुतो यस्य केन्द्रनवमस्थः।  
निधनं कुरुतेऽवश्यं विषजलयोगान्न सन्देहः॥४३॥**

 *Sloka* 43.—Find the Rasi represented by the addition of the Sphutas of the Sun and the Moon. If the same, a Kendra house or the 9th house from the said Rasi be occupied by a malefic, death will undoubtedly happen owing to poison or drowning.

**यस्याष्टमगे पापे लग्नेशे पापसंयुते केन्द्रे।  
सौम्ययुतिदृष्टिहीने निधनं स्यात्सप्तमे वर्षे॥४४॥**

 *Sloka* 44—When at a birth a malefic occupies the 8th house and the lord of the Lagna associated with a malefic is in a Kendra without the aspect or association of benefics, the child born will die in the 7th year.

**रविणा युक्तः शशिजः सौम्यैर्दृष्टो विनाशयति नूनम्।  
एकादशभिर्वर्षैर्देवाङ्केऽपि स्थितं जातम्॥४५॥**

 *Sloka* 45.—If Mercury associated with the Sun be aspected by benefics, the yoga will undoubtedly bring about the death of the child in 11 years though ensconced on the lap of Gods.

**दानं धेनो रुद्ररोद्रीमुखानं भाग्यो भानुर्गोत्रजायानखेन।  
पुत्री नित्यं मृत्युभागाः क्रमाद्वै मेषादीनां तेषु जातो गतायुः॥४६॥**

 *Sloka* 46.—The fateful degrees in the several signs from Mesha onwards are in their order 8, 9, 22, 22, 25, 14, 4, 23, 18, 20, 21 and 10. One born in these degrees (in the Lagna) will die soon.

 Cf. सारावली, where it is stated almost in similar terms, except for Kanya whose fateful degree is 1°. But there it is stated that these are the fateful degrees of the Moon in the several signs.

**चान्द्रं रूपं लोकशूरो वग्ज्ञः कुड्ये चित्रं भाग्यलोको मुखानाम्।  
मेने राज्यं मृत्युभागाः प्रदिष्टा मेषादीनां वर्णसङ्ख्याभिरिन्दोः॥४७॥**

 *Sloka* 47—The fateful degrees of the Moon in the several signs beginning with Mesha are in their order 26. 12, 13, 25, 24, 11, 26, 14, 13, 25, 5 and 12.

 This agrees fully with बृहत्प्राजापत्य; the wording of फलदीपिका, is the same.

**मृत्युभागगतश्चन्द्रः पापयुक्तो न सौम्ययुक।  
निधने वाऽपि केन्द्रे वा मात्रा सह विनश्यति॥४८॥**

 *Sloka* 48.—When the Moon occupying the fateful portion of a sign is associated with malefics without any benefics, or is posited in the 8th or a Kendra house, the child will die along with its mother.

**लग्रेशो बलयुक्तश्चेत् त्रिकोणे केन्द्रगोऽपि वा।  
अरिष्टयोगे जातोऽपि बालो जीवति निश्चयात् ॥ ४९ ॥**

 *Sloka* 49.—Though born in an Arishta yoga, a child will certainly live long, provided the lord of the Lagna is strong and occupies a Kendra or Trikona house.

**बली केन्द्रोपगः सौम्यो निधनेशविवर्जितः।  
अरिष्टयोगनाशाय प्रश्ने वा जननेऽपि वा॥५०॥**

 *Sloka* 50.—A strong benefice unassociated with the lord of the 8th house and occupying a Kendra conduces to the nullification of an Arishta yoga at birth or query.

**क्षेत्रे ग्रहस्तनौ वाऽपि सुखभे दशमेऽपि वा।  
नार्कयुक्तो बली यस्य योगारिष्टं विनश्यति॥५१॥**

 *Sloka* 51.—If a strong planet unassociated with the Sun be posited in the 1st, 4th or 10th house, the Arishta yoga, will be nullified.

**अनेकारिष्टयोगेषु बालो जीवति यत्नतः।  
जातस्य चन्द्रलग्ने तु सर्वग्रहनिरीक्षिते॥५२॥**

**नश्यन्त्यरिष्टयोगा हि तमिस्रमिव भानुना।**

**इति श्रीवराहमिहिरसुतश्रीपृथुयशोविरचिते होरासारेऽरिष्टयोगाध्यायः पञ्चमः॥**

 *Sloka* 52,52½.—When there are many Arishta (harmful) yogas (planetary combinations), the child lives with difficulty; but if the Moon (or the Lagna) be aspected by all the planets, the native's Arishta yogas perish away as darkness does through the Sun.

Thus ends the 5th Adhyaya on 'Arishta yogas.'

**————**

**षष्ठोऽध्यायः**

**उक्तं बालारिष्टं योगारिष्टं प्रयत्नतो वक्ष्ये।  
योगारिष्टदशायामुभयोस्तुल्यं यदा रिष्टम्॥१॥**

 *Sloka* 1.—The Arishta for children has been already explained Now I shall expound with all care the Yogarishtas (planetary combinations that bring about death in various periods) During the Dasa of a planet that produces a Yoga if there be also Balarishta, then the Arishta produced will be very great.

**होरेश्वरेऽर्कसंस्थे जन्मेशे वाऽपि सौम्यदृग्धीने।  
केन्द्रगतैः पापैः स्याद्विंशत्यब्दे मृतिर्नूनम्॥२॥**

 *Sloka* 2.—When the lord of the Lagna or of the Janma Rasi is conjoined with the Sun and is not aspected by any benefic, and when the malefics are posited in Kendras, the native will surely die in his 20th year.

**भौमे लग्नं याते रविमन्दौ केन्द्रगौ बलोद्रिक्तौ।  
आविंशतेर्मृतिः स्याद्भङ्गो वा रोगयुक्तो वा॥३॥**

 *Sloka* 3.—When Mars is posited in the Lagna and the Sun and Saturn possess great strength and occupy Kendras, the native will die within 20 years; in the absence of that, he will have fracture in his limbs or be afflicted with some disease.

**कुजरवियुक्ते लग्ने चरराशौ मध्यसंस्थिते जीवे।  
सुतधर्मगते चन्द्रे जातस्याविंशतेर्मृतिर्भवति॥४॥**

 *Sloka* 4.―If the Lagna be a moveable sign and be conjoined with Mars and the Sun, Jupiter be posited in the 10th house, and the Moon be in the 5th or 9th house, the person's death will happen before 20 years.

**नीचांशगतश्चन्द्रोऽप्यष्टमसंस्थः क्षयी च मरणकरः।  
सौरिकुजाभ्यां दृष्टस्तस्यायुः पञ्चविंशतिः परमम्॥५॥**

 *Sloka* 5.—The waning Moon when posited in the 8th house and in her debilitation Amsa will bring about the person's death. The native will live at the most 25 years when the Moon under the above Yoga is aspected. by Saturn and Mars.

**चन्द्राष्टमगैः पापैः सौम्यैरापोक्लिबस्थितैर्विबलैः।  
चन्द्रे निधनारिगते तस्यायुः पञ्चविंशतिः परमम्॥६॥**

 *Sloka* 6.—When malefics occupy the 8th house from the Moon and benefics are weak, and occupy the Apoklima houses (3rd, 6th, 9th and 12th), and the Moon, is in the 6th or the 8th, the person will live at the most for 25 years.

**लग्नेन्द्वोर्निधनपती केन्द्रगतावष्टमे ग्रहः कश्चित्।  
लग्नहिमांशू विबलौ जातस्यायुः परन्त्रिंशत्॥७॥**

 *Sloka* 7.—When the lords of the 8th houses reckoned both from the Lagna and the Moon are posited in Kendras, and there is a planet in the 8th house (from the Lagna), and the Lagna and the Moon are weak, the native will live for 30 years at the most.

**अर्थव्ययर्क्षसंस्थौ क्रूरौ जीवोरगप्रसंयुक्तौ।  
सप्ताष्टमयोश्चन्द्रो जातस्यायुः परं त्रिंशत्॥८॥**
