 *Sloka* 8.—When two malefics conjoined with Jupiter and Rahu are posited in the 2nd and 12th houses and when the Moon occupies the 7th or the 8th house, the native's life will last at the most for 30 years.

**अर्कस्यास्तमयस्थः क्रूरो जीवोरगप्रसंयुक्तः।  
षष्ठाष्टमगश्चन्द्रो जातस्यायुः परं त्रिंशत्॥९॥**

 *Sloka* 9—When a malefic is eclipsed by the Sun and is conjoined with Jupiter and Rahu, and the Moon is posited in the 6th or the 8th, the native will live for 30 years.

**गुरुणा युक्तः शुक्रो लग्नगतः पञ्चमे कुजार्कियुते।  
वलरहितश्चेच्चन्द्रो योगे जातोऽल्पजीविनो नियतम्॥१०॥**

 In the 2nd line, जीवितः पुरुषः is another reading.

 *Sloka* 10.—When Venus in conjunction with Jupiter occupies the Ascendant, Mars conjoined with Saturn is in the 5th house, and the Moon is weak, the person born under this Yoga will surely be short-lived.

**अष्टाविंशतिवर्षे मरणं चन्द्रार्कराहवः सहिताः।  
कुर्वन्ति तदा जन्तोर्जीवे व्ययगे तथा नियतम्॥११॥**

 *Sloka* 11.—The Sun, the Moon and Rahu joined together conspire to bring about the death of the native in his 28th year; and it will be certain if Jupiter should also be posited in the 12th house.

**लग्नाष्टमपतिचन्द्रौ केन्द्रगतावष्टमे ग्रहः कश्चित्।  
द्वाविंशे मरणं स्यान्न शुभैर्युक्तेक्षिते केन्द्रे॥१२॥**

 *Sloka* 12.—When the Moon and the lord of the 8th house from the Lagna occupy Kendra houses and when there is a planet in the 8th house, the native will die at the age of 32 years, provided no Kendra house is aspected by or is conjoined with benefics.

**क्षीणश्चन्द्रः स्वर्क्षे निधनेशे केन्द्रगेऽष्टमे पापे।  
लग्नेशे बलहीने जातस्यायुः परं त्रिंशत्॥१३॥**

 *Sloka* 13.—When the waning Moon is posited in her own house, the lord of the 8th is in a Kendra and a malefic occupies the 8th, and when the lord of the Lagna is also weak, the native's maximum lease of life will be 30 years.

**होरानिधनाधिपयोः स्फुटयोगः केन्द्रमृत्युराशिस्थः।  
तत्र समेतः पापो निधनं स्यात्सप्तविंशवर्षे तु॥१४॥**

 *Sloka* 14.—Add up the figures denoting the positions of the lords of the 1st and the 8th houses. If this sum reveals a Kendra or the 8th house, and if a malefic should occupy it, the native will die in his 27th year.

 In the 1st पाद, Yavana Jataka reads as होराजन्माधिपयोः॥

**रन्ध्रेश्वरे कोणगते विलग्ननाथेऽष्टमस्थेऽशुभयुक्तदृष्टे।  
जातश्चतुर्विंशतिवर्षजीवी शुभेक्षितौ तावपि मृत्युरेव॥१५॥**

 *Sloka* 15.—When the lord of the 8th house is in a Kona (5th or 9th), and the lord of the Lagna is in the 8th conjoined with or aspected by malefics, the native will live only for 24 years, even if these two planets be aspected by benefics.

**पापोदये सुरगुरौ शनिदृष्टे राहुणा समेते वा।**  
**यः कश्चिन्निधनगतो मरणं जनयेद्द्विनेत्रसङ्ख्याब्दैः॥१६॥**

 *Sloka* 16.—When a malefic planet is rising in the Lagna and Jupiter is aspected by Saturn or is associated with Rahu, and when the 8th house is occupied by some planet, the native will die in 22 years.

 चापोदये is another reading for पापोदये.

**होरशे लग्नगते सक्रूरौ चन्द्रभास्करौ हिबुके।  
निधनेशे केन्द्रगते जातस्यायुः परं त्रिंशत्॥१७॥**

 *Sloka* 17.—When the lord of the Lagna occupies the Lagna itself, the Sun and the Moon are in conjunction with malefics in the 4th house and the lord of the 8th is in a Kendra the native's maximum lease of life is 30 years.

 सुतगौ is another reading for हिबुके। रन्ध्रगते is another reading for केन्द्रगते।

**अष्टमाधिपतौ केन्द्रे लग्नेशे बलवर्जिते।  
त्रिंशद्वर्षाण्यसौ जीवेद्द्वात्रिंशन्मितमेव वा॥१८॥**

 *Sloka* 18.—When the lord of the 8th house is posited in a Kendra and the lord of the Ascendant is enfeebled, the person born will live for 30 or 32 years.

**आपोक्लिबस्थिते चन्द्रे लग्नेशे तत्र संस्थिते।  
पापेक्षिते बलैर्हीने जीवेद्दशचतुर्गुणान्॥१९॥**

 *Sloka* 19.—When both the Moon and the lord of the Lagna, are weak and aspected by malefics, and are posited in an Apoklima house (jointly or separately), the person born will live for 40 years.

 In the last quarter, जीवेन्नेत्रगुणाब्दकान् and जवित्यष्टचतुर्गुणान् are two other readings.

**गुरुशुक्रौ च केन्द्रस्थौ लग्नेशः पापसंयुतः।  
आपोक्लिबस्थः सन्ध्यायां जातस्यायू रवित्रयम्॥२०॥**

 *Sloka* 20.—When Jupiter and Venus occupy Kendras, and the lord of the Lagna is associated with malefics and is posited in an Apoklima house, one born during Sandhya (twilight) will live for 36 years.

**पापमध्यगते सूर्ये लग्नस्थे शत्रुवेश्मनि।  
जातः स्याद्रोगपीडार्त्तः परमायू रवित्रयम्॥२१॥**

 *Sloka* 21.—When the Sun, surrounded by malefics, occupies the Lagna identical with a sign owned by his enemy, one born under this Yoga will be always sickly, and his maximum lease of life will be 36 years.

**रवीन्दू लग्नगौ यस्य केन्द्राष्टमविवर्जितैः।  
सौम्यैर्गुलिकवेलायां जातस्यायू रवित्रयम्॥२२॥**

 *Sloka* 22—When the Sun and the Moon occupy the Lagna, and benefics, any house other than a Kendra and the 8th, on born during Gulika's time will live for 36 years.

**अष्टमनाथे लग्ने स्थिरराशौ जायते नरो यस्तु।  
चत्वारिंशद्वर्षे मरणं रन्ध्रे शुभेन संयुक्ते॥२३॥**

 *Sloka* 23.—When the lord of the 8th house is in the Lagna identical with a fixed sign and when the 8th house is occupied by a benefic, the person born will meet with his death at the age of 40 years.

**लग्नेशे निधनांशस्थे लग्नांशे निधनेश्वरे।  
पापयुक्ते तदा जातः पञ्चाशद्वर्षजीवितः॥२४॥**

 *Sloka* 24.—When the lord of the Lagna is posited in a Navamsa owned by the 8th house, and the lord of the 8th house is in a Navamsa belonging to the Lagna and is also conjoined with a malefic, the person born will live for 50 years.

**ग्रहैर्विरहिते केन्द्रे लग्नेशः पापवर्जितः।  
षष्टिवर्षात्परं नायुः पापैः पञ्चमसंस्थितैः॥२५॥**

 *Sloka* 25.—When no planet occupies the Kendras, and the lord of the Lagna is unassociated with malefics and when malefics occupy the 5th house, the native will not live for more than 60 years.

**लग्नेशे व्ययसंयुक्ते क्षीणे पापयुतेऽपि वा।  
षष्टिवर्षात्परं नायुर्न च लग्ने बृहस्पतिः॥२६॥**

 *Sloka* 26.—When the lord of the Lagna is weak, conjoined with malefics or posited in the 12 house, the native will not live for more than sixty years provided Jupiter does not occupy the Lagna.

**अष्टमाधिपतौ केन्द्रे भौमे लग्नं समाश्रिते।  
अर्कार्कजौ त्रिषष्ठस्थौ जीवेद्रुद्रचतुष्टयम्॥२७॥**

 In the last quarter जीवेद्रुद्रांश्चतुर्गुणानू is another reading.

 *Sloka* 27.—When the lord of the 8th house is posited in a Kendra, Mars is in the Lagna, and the Sun and Saturn occupy the 3rd and 6th, the native will live for 44 years.

**वर्गोत्तमांशगे चन्द्रे लग्नस्थे पापवीक्षिते।  
सौम्यैर्बलविहीनैश्च द्वादशाब्दांश्चतुर्गुणान्॥२८॥**

 *Sloka* 28.—When the Moon, posited in a Vargottamamsa and aspected by malefics, occupies the Lagna, and when the benefics are devoid of strength, the person born will live for 48 years.

**सौम्यैः पापांशकर्क्षस्यैः पापैः केन्द्रगतैस्तथा।  
मध्यमायुरयं योगः सौम्यः केन्द्रविवर्जितैः॥२९॥**

 *Sloka* 29—.When benefics occupy malefic signs or Amsas, malefics are in Kendras and benefics in houses other than Kendras, a Yoga is produced which gives medium life.

**उदयगते द्विशरीरे मन्दे चन्द्रेऽष्टमे व्यये वाऽपि।  
जातस्तत्र मनुष्यो जीवति वर्षं द्विपञ्चाशम्॥३०॥**

 *Sloka* 30.—When the Lagna is a dual sign, and the Moon and Saturn are posited in the 8th or the 12th house, the person born will live for 52 years, (or, when Saturn occupies the Lagna identical with a dual sign, and the Moon is in the 8th or 12th house, etc.)

**अलिकर्कियुते लग्ने सूर्ये पापान्विते शशी धनगः।  
गुरुरहिते केन्द्रे स्याच्छतार्धवर्षं च तस्यायुः॥३१॥**

 *Sloka* 31.—When the Sun in conjunction with a malefic occupies the Lagna identical with Karkataka or Vrischika, the Moon is in the 2nd house and when Jupiter occupies a house other than a Kendra, the native lives for 50 years.

**चतुरश्रगताः पापा लग्नात्कुर्वन्ति मध्यमायुर्हि।  
चन्द्रात्तथैव पापाः सौम्यैरनबेक्षिता न संयुक्ताः॥३२॥**

 *Sloka* 32.—Malefics, posited in the 4th and 8th houses from the Lagna or from the Moon, give only a medium lease of life, provided they are neither aspected by nor conjoined with benefics.

**सुखदशमे पापाश्चेन्निधने पापान्विते व्यये चन्द्रे।  
गुरुशुक्रावेकगतौ जातस्तत्रैव मध्यमायुः स्यात्॥३३॥**

* * *Sloka* 33.—When malefics are posited in the 4th, and 10th, the Moon is in the 12th, and Jupiter and Venus are conjoined somewhere, the native will have medium span of life.

**शन्यंशे लग्नेशे निधनेश्वरसंयुते निशानाथे।  
षष्ठेऽष्टमव्यये वा जातस्य परामायुरष्टपञ्चाशत्॥३४॥**

 *Sloka* 34.—When the lord of the Lagna occupies a Navamsa owned by Saturn, and the Moon conjoined with the lord of the 8th house is in any of the houses viz 6th, 8th and 12th, the person born will live for 58 years at the most.

**षष्ठाष्टमव्ययगतैर्ग्रहैः समस्तैर्नृपालयोगः स्यात्।  
अस्मिन्योगे जन्तोः परमायुश्चाष्टपञ्चाशत्॥३५॥**

 *Sloka* 35.—When all the planets are posited in the Dus-stthanas (6th 8th, and 12th) a Raja yoga is formed. Those that are born under this yoga will live for a maximum period of 59 years.

**लग्नाधीशान्मृत्युषष्ठव्ययस्थाः पापाः सन्तो नैधनं वर्जयित्वा।  
अस्मिन् योगे जायते यो मनुष्यस्तस्यायुः स्यात् षष्टिवर्षं प्रसिद्धम्॥३६॥**

 *Sloka* 36.—When malefics are posited in the 6th, 8th and 12th houses reckoned from the lord of the Lagna, and benefics in any house or houses other than the 8th, the person concerned will live for 60 years for certain.

**होराजन्माधिपती ह्यस्तगतौ मृत्युराशिसंयुक्तौ।  
लग्नचतुष्टयरहिते देवगुरौ पञ्चषष्टिवर्षाणि॥३७॥**

 *Sloka* 37.—When the lords of the Lagna and of the sign occupied by the Moon are eclipsed and posited in the 8th house (it may also mean—are posited in the 7th or the 8th), and Jupiter is posited in any house other than the Lagna and the Kendras, the person born will live for 65 years.

**अर्ककुजमन्दयुक्ते लग्ने बलवर्जिते सुराचार्ये।  
चन्द्रे व्ययात्मजे वा सप्ततिवर्षं तु जीवितं विद्यात्॥३८॥**

 *Sloka* 38.—When the Sun, Mars and Saturn are posited in the Lagna, Jupiter is weak and the Moon is in the 5th or the 12th house, the native will live for 70 years.

 In the 2nd line, some books read आत्मजर्क्षे for आत्मजे वा, and च जीवति प्रायः for तु जीवितं विद्यात्।

**चतुराद्यैर्ग्रहैर्युक्ता लग्नद्वित्रिसुखा यदि।  
चिरायुस्तत्र जातश्च ज्ञानवानर्थवान् भवेत्॥३९॥**

 *Sloka* 39.—When the first four houses beginning with the Lagna contain four or more planets, one born under this Yoga will be long—lived, wise and wealthy.

**पञ्चमादिषु तैर्योगे षष्टिवर्षं स जीवति।  
नवमादिषु तैः सर्वैरल्पायुस्तत्र जातकः॥४०॥**

 *Sloka* 40.—When the four houses beginning with the 5th contain 4 or more planets, the native will live for 60 years ; if all the planets should occupy the last four houses, he will be short—lived.

**क्रूरर्क्षस्थैः करैः सौम्यैः केन्द्राश्रितैरशीत्यब्दम्।  
जीवति तत्रोद्भूतो मिश्रैर्वा षष्टिवर्षं च॥४१॥**

 *Sloka* 41.—When malefics are posited in malignant houses, and benefics are in Kendras, the native will live for 80 years If the above be mixed, i. e., malefics and benefics in malignant houses, and the same in Kendras, the person born will live for 60 years.

**गुरुचन्द्रौ हिबुकस्थौ लग्नेशे लाभगे बलाढ्ये स्यात्।  
सौम्ये दशमं याते त्वशीतिवर्षं च परमायुः॥४२॥**

 *Sloka* 42.—When Jupiter and the Moon occupy the 4th house, the lord of the Lagna is strong and is in the 11th house and Mercury is posited in the 10th, the maximum lease of life is 80 years.

**जीवांशकस्था रविभौममन्दाः केन्द्रं गता लग्नगते सुरेड्ये।  
रन्धं विनान्यत्र गतास्तु शेषाः पञ्चान्विताशीतिमुशन्ति तस्य॥४३॥**

* * *Sloka* 43.—When the Sun, Mars and Saturn, all occupying Jupiter's Navamsa, are posited in Kendras, Jupiter is in the Lagna, and the rest are in houses other than the 8th, wise men declare 85 years for the native.

**क्रूरर्क्षस्थैः क्रूरैः सौम्यक्षेत्रेषु संस्थितैः सौम्यैः।  
होरेशे च बलाढ्ये जातः परमायुराप्नोति॥४४॥**

 *Sloka* 44.—When malefics and benefics occupy malefic and benefic houses respectively and when the lord of the Lagna is strong, the native will attain long life.

**यदि नैधनगो भौमस्त्वर्को होरागतोऽपि वा प्रसवे।  
केन्द्रे चेत्सुरपूज्ये प्राणिति जातोऽत्र वर्षशतम् ॥४५॥**

 *Sloka* 45.—When in a nativity Mars occupies the 8th house, the Sun Lagna and Jupiter, a Kendra, the person lives for 100 years. (Another interpretation: Even when the Sun and Mars occupy the Lagna and the 8th respectively, the person will live for 100 years provided Jupiter occupies a Kendra.)

**केन्द्रत्रिकोणनिधनेषु न यस्य पापा  
लग्नाधिपः सुरगुरुश्च चतुष्टयस्थौ।  
भुक्त्वा सुखानि विविधानि च (सु) पुण्यकर्मा  
जीवेच्च वत्सरशतं स विमुक्तरोगः॥४६॥**

 *Sloka* 46.—He in whose nativity, the Kendras, Trikonas and the 8th house are devoid of malefics, and the lord of the Lagna and Jupiter occupy Kendras, will live for 100 years enjoying good health and all kinds of happiness and doing meritorious deeds.

 In the 1st पाद, विपापकेषु is another reading for नयस्य पापाः।

**चरांशकस्था रविभौममन्दाः स्थिरांशकस्थौ भृगुदेवपूज्यौ।  
शेषास्तु युग्मांशमुपागताश्चेद्दीर्घायुरत्रावनिपालकोऽपि॥४७॥**

 *Sloka* 47.—When the Sun, Mars and Saturn occupy moveable Navamsas, Jupiter and Venus, fixed ones, and the rest, dual ones, the person will enjoy long life and may even become a king.

**ओजांशकस्थितशुभाः सुखधर्मसंस्थाः  
पापास्तु युग्मभवनांशकलग्नसंस्थाः।  
चन्द्रो विलग्नभवने यदि पूर्णरश्मि-  
र्जातोऽत्र याति शतमायुररोगतां च॥४८॥**

 *Sloka* 48.—When benefics occupying odd Navamsa Rasis are posited in the 4th and 9th, malefics occupying even ones are posited in the Lagna and the Moon in full strength (with full rays) is in the Lagna, the person born under the Yoga lives for full 100 Years and in good health.

**लग्नाधिपोऽतिबलवानशुभैरदृष्टः  
केन्द्रस्थितः शुभखगैरवलोक्यमानः।  
मृत्युं विधूय विदधाति सुदीर्घमायुः  
सार्धं गुणैर्बहुभिरूर्जितराजलक्ष्म्या॥४९॥**

 *Sloka* 49.—The lord of the rising sign when possessed of great strength and unaspected by malefic planets, but aspected by benefic ones and occupying a Kendra position wards off death and secures to the child long life graced with the strong virtues of a vigorous sovereignty.

**लग्नेश्वरादतिबली निधनेश्वरोऽसौ  
केन्द्रस्थितो निधनरिःफगतैश्च पापैः।  
तस्यायुरल्पमथवा यदि मध्यमायु-  
रुत्साहसङ्कटवशात्परमायुरेति॥५०॥**

 *Sloka* 50.—When the lord of the 8th house being stronger than the lord of the Lagna occupies a Kendra, and malefics occupy the 8th and the 12th houses, the person born will be short—lived, or, if he lives a medium life, he may drag on his existence without energy.

**अथामितायुर्योगलक्षणम्।**

 Now the author gives the definition of Yogas for an unlimited span of life.

**एकांशकस्था बुधजीवशुक्रास्त्वेकर्क्षगा लग्नमुपागताश्च।  
धर्मे शनौ जन्मनि यस्य जन्तो रसायनाद्यैर्युगमायुरेति॥५१॥**

 *Sloka* 51.—When Mercury, Jupiter and Venus are posited in the same Navamsa, Rasi or Lagna, and Saturn is in the 9th house, the person born under the Yoga lives for a Yuga (1000 years) with the aid of tonics and so forth.

**एकांशकस्था बुधजीवमन्दा धर्मे स्थिता लग्नमुपागताश्च।  
षष्ठेऽष्टमे वा हिबुके च यस्य सहस्रवर्षद्वयमत्र जातः॥५२॥**

 *Sloka* 52.—When Mercury, Jupiter and Saturn (or Venus) are posited in the same Navamsa and in the 1st, 4th, 6th, 8th or the 9th house, the person born will live for 2000 years.

 In the 1st half बुधजीवशुक्राः is another reading.

**जीवांशकस्था सकला ग्रहेन्द्राः केन्द्राश्रिता धर्मधनाश्रिता वा।  
जातो नरः प्रव्रजितोऽथ बाल्ये युगान्तमायुर्बहुशास्त्रकर्ता॥५३॥**

 *Sloka* 53.—When all the planets occupying a Navamsa of Jupiter are posited in Kendras, in the 9th or the 2nd houses, the person born under this Yoga will take to asceticism in his boyhood itself, compose many Sastraic works and live for a complete Yuga.

**मन्दांशकस्था रविभौमजीवाः केन्द्राश्रिता धर्मयुता बलाढ्याः।  
क्षेत्रावसाने हिमगौ विलग्ने युगान्तमायुः श्रियमभ्युपैति॥५४॥**

 *Sloka* 54.—When the Sun, Mars and Jupiter (or Venus) each occupying a Navamsa of Saturn are strong, posited in Kendras or in the 9th house and the Moon is in the Lagna at the end of a Rasi, the person born will live for a Yuga and attain wealth.

 In the 1st पाद, रविभौमशुक्राः is another readng.

**धर्मेश्वरे धर्मगते च यस्य भौमेन दृष्टे हिमगौ कुजांशे।  
मुनीश्वरोऽयं मुनियोगजातः शास्त्रादिकर्ता युगमायुरेति॥५५॥**

 *Sloka* 55.—When the lord of the 9th house occupies that house itself and is aspected by Mars, and when the Moon occupies an Amsa of Mars (and is aspected by Mars?) the person born under the ascetic Yoga will be a great sage and a writer of Sastraic and other works and live for a Yuga.

**अक्षीणचन्द्रे सुहृदुच्चभांशे लाभाश्रिते लग्नमुपागते वा।  
धर्मस्थिते सूर्यसुते बलाढ्ये जातोऽत्र दीर्घायुरसङ्ख्यवर्षः॥५६॥**

 *Sloka* 56.—When the Moon is not waning, occupies a friend's house or Amsa or her exaltation Rasi or Amsa, and is posited in the 11th house or the Lagna, and Saturn in strength is in the 9th house, the person born under this Yoga will live for countless years.

**गुरुमन्दावेकस्थाकांशगतौ स्वधर्मकर्मस्थौ।  
अर्कोदये ससौम्ये जातो मुनिवल्लभोऽत्र दीर्घायुः॥५७॥**

 *Sloka* 57.—When Jupiter and Saturn are conjoined and occupy the same degree in the 2nd, 9th or the 10th house, and the Sun along with Mercury is rising, the person born will be a favourite of sages and long-lived.

**अतिदीर्घायुर्योगे जातो मुनिवज्जितेन्द्रियो भूत्वा।  
दिव्यौषधप्रयोगाद्बिलं प्रविष्टः करोति मन्त्रजपान् ॥५८॥**

 *Sloka* 58.—One born under a Yoga for inordinately long life will have the senses under control like a sage, be repeating sacred hymns and dwell in a cave by the application of divine medicines.

 This shows that our ancients possessed means whereby they could make their bodies small or big, light or heavy, etc.

**इत्यादियोगा यवनोपदिष्टा मयेरिताः प्राक्तनकर्मयोगात्।  
सर्वान् विनिश्चित्य दशान्तराले छिद्रेषु योगोक्तफलं नियोज्यम्॥५९॥**

**इति श्रीवराहमिहिरसुतश्रीपृथुयशोविरचिते होरासारेऽरिष्टयोगाध्यायः षष्ठः॥**

 *Sloka* 59.—I have thus stated the above Yogas expounded by the Yavanas (Greeks) with the help of my previous Karma (actions). The cumulative effects of the Yogas will have to be declared in the untoward periods during the Dasas and their Bhuktis, after carefully analys— ing all the Yogas.

Thus ends the 6th Adhyaya on the 'Ascertainment of longevity under Special Yogas.'  
-------------

**सप्तमोऽध्यायः**

**अथ तेषां योगानामेकतमस्मिन्नगश्च ये जाताः।  
तेषां दशानुनयनं स्पष्टं वक्ष्यामि यत्नतश्चाहम्॥१॥**

 *Sloka* 1.—I shall now explain clearly and carefully the method of arriving at the exact Dasa-periods for those that are born under any one of the Yogas shown in the previous Chapter.

**मययवनसिद्धसेनप्रबोधमाण्डव्यविष्णुगुप्ताद्यैः।  
आयुर्दायविभागो नॄणां सम्यक् पुरातनैः कथितः॥२॥**

 *Sloka* 2.—The various systems of computing men's (total life period contributed by the planets) have been well expounded by the ancients such as Maya, Yavana, Siddhasena, Prabodha, Mandavya and Vishnugupta.

**Pindayus**

**एकोनविंशतिसमा भानोश्चन्द्रस्य पञ्चकृतिरब्दाः।  
भौमस्य तु तिथिसङ्ख्या बुधस्य षट्कद्वयं विनिर्दिष्टम्॥३॥**

**पञ्चदशाब्दाश्च गुरोः शुक्रस्याप्येकविंशतिः कथिताः।  
मन्दस्य विंशतिसमाः परमोच्चस्था ग्रहाः प्रयच्छन्ति॥४॥**

 *Slokas* 3-4.—When the planets, the Sun and others, are in their highest exaltation degrees, they contribute in their order 19, 25, 15, 12, 15, 21 and 20 years towards a man's total life-period.

**स्वोच्चादर्धं नीचे तदन्तरस्थेऽनुपाततः कल्प्यम्।  
विधिनैवं खचराणां दशानुनयनं क्रमेण कर्तव्यम्॥५॥**

 *Sloka* 5.—A planet occupying its lowest debilitation-point contributes only half the number of years given above; the number of years it contributes when it occupies an intermediate position (between debilitation and exaltation) will have to be found out by the rule-of three process. In this manner, the Dasa-periods of all the planets in their order have to be calculated.

**नीचोच्चविवरगगतिं स्वदशापिण्डेन ताडयेद्धीमान्।  
षष्ट्यादिशेषणीयं वर्षान्तं कल्पयेद्यथान्यायम्॥६॥**

**यद्युच्चान्तिकविवरं पिण्डाच्छोध्यं ग्रहस्य तस्यायुः।  
नीचसमीपाद्विवरं पिण्डार्धयुतं ग्रहस्य तस्यायुः॥७॥**

 * Slokas* 6-7.—A wise astrologer should multiply the difference in degrees between a planet's debilitation-point and its actual position in the nativity by one half of its total number of Pindayurdaya years and then deduce the period of Ayurdaya contributed by the planet.

**मूढारिदृश्यहरणं युद्धासुरसन्निकर्षहरणं च।  
हरणानि ज्ञात्वैवं गुरूपदेशेन कर्तव्यम्॥८॥**

* Sloka* 8.—Deductions such as are for planets that are eclipsed, that are in inimical houses, and that are in the visible half of the zodiac, as well as for those that are at war and those that are in close proximity to Rahu(?), will have to be made after ascertaining them from the preceptor's instructions,

**तस्यैवमंशकदशामेवं कृत्वा व्ययादिहरणं च।  
पूर्वदशासु समार्धं त्यक्त्वा शेषं ग्रहस्य शुद्धायुः॥९॥**

 * Sloka* 9.—The life-period according to the Amsayurdaya-system should thus be calculated by the above. method and the deductions for planets posited in the six Rasis beginning with the 12th house counted backwards will have also to be made likewise. Leaving off an exact half of the years contributed by those planets which are under the above circumstances, viz, eclipse, debilitation, etc., the remaining should be taken as the net period of years contributed by the several planets towards the longevity of the person.

**एकद्वित्रिचतुर्थपञ्चमरसान् भागान् हरन्ति व्यया-  
द्वामं यात्सुपदक्रमेण भवने पापेषु सत्सूक्तवत्।  
अर्थं याति शुभाशुभैस्तु सहिते पापस्य भागं हरेत्  
त्र्याद्येष्वेकगतेषु वीर्यहरणं कुर्यान्न शेषेषु च॥१०॥**

 * Sloka* 10.—When malefics occupy the six signs beginning with the 12th house counted backwards, deductions from their contributions will have to be made in the order of 1, ½,⅓, ¼ , ⅕, and ⅙ respectively ; when benefics occupy these houses, the reductions enjoined are a half of the above ones in the several houses; when both benefics and malefics are combined in these houses, the reductions due to the malefics alone need be made; and when more than two planets are posited in a house, the reducton due to the strongest of them alone should be made. and not for the others.

**त्र्यंशं रिपोर्भवनगेऽवनिजं च मुक्त्वा  
चास्तं गतेऽर्धहरणं शनिशुक्रवर्जम्।  
भङ्गे त्रिकांशमथवा सुरसन्निकर्षे  
चन्द्रार्कयोः क्षयमुपैति तदर्धकार्धम्॥११॥**

* Sloka* 11.—All planets except Mars occupying inimical houses will lose a third of their contribution; one eclipsed will lose half of its contribution execpt Venus and Saturn; one defeated in a planetary fight will lose ⅓; and the Sun and the Moon in conjunction with Rahu (or Ketu?) lose 1½ th of their contribution.

**होरेश्वरांशकसमानि ददाति लग्नं  
लग्ने शुभे बलयुते चतुरंशयुक्तम्।  
पापान्वितेऽपि विबले चतुरंशदनिं  
होरादशा तु विधिना परिकल्पिता स्यात्॥१२॥**

* Sloka12.*—The Lagna contributes as many years as the number of the Navamsa (counted from Mesha) progressed by the lord of the Lagna. When the Lagna. is strong and is occupied by a strong benefic, the years should be increased by ¼th of the Ayus obtained. The Ayus should be quadrupled when the lord of the Lagna is conjoined with benefics or friends. When the Lagna is weak or conjoined with malefics, a fourth of the Ayus should be deducted. Thus should the Dasa of the Lagna be calculated.

**उच्चनीचविधिनायुराप्यते यत्र सम्यगधियोगसम्भवः।  
सद्गृहत्वमुपगच्छति लग्नं यत्र चास्तभवनं ग्रहयुक्तम्॥१३॥**

 * Sloka*13.—The longevity is correctly arrived at by calculating a planet's exact position from its exaltation and debilitation, where there is some benefic conjunction, or when the Lagna is strong and is a benefic house, or when the 7th house is occupied.

 Another interpretation:—Where there is good planetary conjunction for the Lagna, the Ayus is obtained by उच्चनीचविधि. The Lagna becomes strong and benefic when there is a planet in the 7th house.

**उच्चनीचदशामार्गं सामान्यं सर्वदेहिनाम्।  
दशासंस्कारभेदेन द्विप्रकारं प्रचक्षते॥१४॥**

 *Sloka*14.—The method of finding the total lifeperiod of a person by the उच्चनीय process is common to all beings; but, it is of two kinds on account of the difference between Dasa and Samskara (process of rectification by proper deductions, etc.)

**कुर्याद्दशासु संस्कारमंशकैर्बलवत्तरैः।  
तयोर्बलाबलेनैव कल्पयेन्मतिमान्नरः॥१५॥**

 *Sloka *15.—For the various Dasa periods, rectification or deductions (संस्कार) will have to be made through the strongest of the Navamsas. And this will have to be made by an intelligent astrologer after considering the relative strength of the two.

**Amsayus—अथांशायुः**

**राश्यंशकला गुणिता द्वादशनवभिर्ग्रहस्य भगणेभ्यः।  
द्वादशहृतावशिष्टं वर्षाद्युपलक्षितं यथान्यायम्॥१६॥**

* Sloka*16.—The figures of a planet in signs, degrees, minutes are to be multiplied by 108 and divided by 12. The remainder will indicate according to the rule the years, etc., contributed by the planet.

**स्वांशत्रिभागनिजगृहवर्गोत्तमसंस्थिते द्वयं गुणकः।  
वक्रोच्चयोस्त्रिगुणितं नीचेऽर्धं क्षीयते विशेषेण॥१७॥**

 * Sloka *17.—When a planet occupies its own Navamsa, Drekkana, Rasi, or Vargottama Navamsa, the multiplier is 2. The Ayurdaya has to be trebled when the planet is retrograde or is in exaltation, and halved when the planet is in depression.

**पूर्वोक्तहरणमस्मिन् कुर्याद्भौमस्य शत्रुहरणं च।  
उदितनवांशकसदृशानब्दानुदयस्य कल्पयेन्मतिमान्॥१८॥**

* Sloka*18.—The deductions referred to above in connection with Pindayus must be done here too except for Mars and also while occupying an inimical house. And an intelligent astrologer should allot as many years for the Lagna as there are Navamsas that have risen in it.

**अंशोद्भवं विलग्नात्पैण्डं भानोर्निसर्गजं चन्द्रात्।  
एतेषां यो बलवांस्तस्यामुं कल्पयेद्दायम्॥१९॥**

* Sloka* 19.—Of the several kinds of Ayurdaya, the Amsayurdaya system should be adopted when the Lagna is strongest; the Pinda one when the Sun is powerful and the Nisargajayus when the Moon is endowed with full strength.

**क्षेत्रोच्चमित्रभागे ग्रहैः समस्तैस्तदांशजनितश्च।  
अर्केन्दुलग्नरहितैर्ग्रहैस्तदांशोद्भवो दशामार्गः॥२०॥**

* Sloka* 20.*—*When all the planets are posited in their own houses, exaltation signs or friend's houses or Navamsas, then the Amsayurdaya system should be adopted; so also will be the case when planets are not associated with the Sun, the Moon or the Lagna.

**अथ जीवशर्मायुः Jeevasarmayus.**

**अपरं दशानुनयनं स्वयमार्गेण जीवशर्मोक्तम्।  
तस्मादायुर्दायं वक्ष्ये विषयप्रकारं च॥२१॥**

* Sloka* 21.*—*There is another method of finding out the Dasa (total life period) expounded by Jeevasarman according to his own doctrine. (A planet contributes according to him, one-seventh of the maximum period of of man's existence i. e., 120 years, 5 days.) Hence, I shall now treat of that system of Ayurdaya and also the procedure for calculating the same.

 Vide also जा-पा V 17-Notes.

 परमायुषः स्वरांशो महदायो जीवशर्मणाप्युक्तः॥ is another reading.

**नीचोच्चविवरगकला विभज्य ननतायरैः समा लब्धाः।  
रम्य नल नात गुणिता विभज्य तेनैव मासदिननाड्यः॥२२॥**

* * *Sloka* 22.*—*Find the difference between a planet's actual position and its debilitation-point and convert the Fame into minutes. Divice the result by 21660. The quotient thus obtained will give the years. Multiply the remainder by 12 and divide the product by 21600 and the quotient will reveal the months. Again multiply the remainder by 30 and divide the product as before. The quotient will give the days. Now multiply the remainder got, by 60 and divide as before, and the quotient will give the Ghatis.

**सय(17)यज्ञ(1)रुद्र(22)ज(8)बला(35)च्छोध्यं तुङ्गात्समीपतः पिण्डम्।  
नीचसमीपात्पिण्डं विवरं यदि तेषु संयोज्यम्॥२३॥**

 Sloka 23.—If the planet occupies a position close to its exaltation point, subtract the figure representing its position from 17 years, 1 month, 22 days, 8 ghatikas and 34 Vighatikas. If it is near its debilitation-point, then the difference should be added to them.

**हरणं यत्पूर्वोक्तं प्रथमेऽप्यत्रापि कारयेत्प्राज्ञः।  
मन्दसितमूढहरणं भौमस्य न शत्रुहरणं च॥२४॥**

 Sloka 24.—A wise man should do all the deductions mentioned already, save for Saturn and Venus when they are eclipsed and for Mars when he occupies an inimical house

**होरायामुदितांशप्रमाणमायुर्ददाति लग्नं च।  
पापग्रहे तु लग्ने चतुरंशस्त्यज्यतेऽन्यथा तु युतिः॥२५॥**

 Sloka 25.—The Lagna contributes for a man's life as many years as there are Navamsas that have risen. If there should be a malefic posited in the Lagna, the contribution for the Lagna will have to be reduced by onefourth. If, on the other hand, a benefic occupies it, the contribution should be enhanced by a fourth.

**अर्थव्ययर्क्षौ ग्रहसम्प्रयुक्तौ लग्नाद्व्ययार्थौ शशिलग्नराशेः।  
ग्रहेण युक्तौ यदि जीवशर्ममतं गुरौ मध्यगतेऽम्बुगे वा॥२६॥**

**सर्वे ग्रहा नीचसमीपसंस्थास्तत्प्रोक्तमार्गे बलवर्जितास्तु।  
कश्चिद्ग्रहो लग्नगतोऽस्तगो वा तदा स्वरां (7) शेन दशा प्रकल्प्या॥२७॥**

 *Slokas* 26–27.*—*In the opinion of Jeevasarman, if there be planets occupying both the 2nd and the 12th houses from the Lagna or from the Moon, or if Jupiter occupy the 10th or the 4th house, if all the planets be near their debilitation point and be weak, or be posited in the Lagna or the 7th house, the contribution of each of the several planets will have to be fixed at th of the total period of human life.

**अथ भिन्नाष्टवर्गे त्रिकोणशोधनम्–**  
Trikona reduction in Bhinnashtakavarga.

**राशिचक्रं यथामार्गं निक्षिप्येष्टग्रहस्य च।  
त्रिकोणशोधनं कुर्यादादौ सर्वेषु राशिषु॥२८॥**

 *Sloka* 28.—Drawing the Rasi-chakra as usual and putting the benefic dots of the Ashtaka Varga of the planet required, the Trikona reduction should first be gone through for all the Rasis.

**त्रिकोणास्तु कथं प्रोक्ता मेषसिंहहयाः क्रमात्।  
वृषकन्यामृगास्याश्च तुलाकुम्भयमास्तथा॥२९॥**

**कर्किवृश्चिकमीनास्ते त्रिकोणाः स्युः परस्परम्।  
त्रिकोणेषु च यन्न्यूनं तत्तुल्यं त्रिषु शोधयेत्॥३०॥**

**एकस्मिन् भवने शून्ये तत्त्रिकोण न शोधयेत्।  
भवनद्वयशून्यत्वे शोधयेदन्यमन्दिरम्।३१॥**

**समत्वे सर्वगेहेषु सर्वं संशोधयेद्बुधः।**

 *Slokas* 29–31.—Mesha, Simha and Dhanus; Vrishabha, Kanya and Makara; Mithuna, Tula and Kumbha; and Karkataka, Vrischika and Meena are called Trikonas among themselves or to one to another Trikonas, whichever figure is least, the same should be substituted in the other two.If one of the three be void of benefic dots, no reduction need be made. If two out of the three be vacant, remove the figure in the third also. If all the three houses should have equal number of dots, remove all the three figures.

**अथैकाधिपत्यशोधनम्**

**एवं त्रिकोणं संशोध्य पश्चादेकाधिपत्यजम्॥३२॥**

**क्षेत्रद्वये फलानि स्युर्यदि संशोधयेद्बुधः।  
क्षीणेन सह चान्यस्मिञ्च्छोधयेद्ग्रहवर्जिते॥३३॥**

**ग्रहयुक्ते फलैर्हीने ग्रहहीने फलाधिके।  
ऊनेन सह चान्यस्मिञ्च्छोधयेद्ग्रहवर्जिते॥३४॥**

**फलाधिके ग्रहोपेते चान्यस्मिन् सर्वमुत्सृजेत्।  
सग्रहाग्रहतुल्यत्वे सर्वं संशोध्यमग्रहात्॥३५॥**

**उभयोर्ग्रहसंयोगे न संशोध्यं कदाचन।  
उभाभ्यां ग्रहहीनाभ्यां समत्वे सकलं त्यजेत्॥३६॥**

**एकस्मिन् भवने शून्ये न संशोध्यं कदाचन।  
कुलीरसिंहयो राश्योः पृथक क्षेत्रफलं स्मृतम्॥३७॥**

 *Slokas* 32-37.—Having thus done the reduction in respect of Trikonas, one should do that for those pairs of Rasis having a common lord in the way described below: Should the two houses owned by a planet both contain benefic dots it is only then that a wise astrologer should resort to this reduction. When one of the signs owned by a planet contains a smaller number of benefic dots than the other which is void of any planet, the smaller number should be adopted for both the signs. When the sign occupied by a planet contains a greater number of benefic dots than the other having no planet in it, remove all the dots from the latter. If there be an equal number of benefic dots in both the houses owned by a planet and if one of them alone be occupied, remove all the dots from the other. When both the houses are occupied by planets, no reduction need be made. When both the signs are without planets and contain an equal number of benefic dots, remove the dots from both. If one of the houses be devoid of benefic dots, no reduction need be effected. The benefic dots in the signs Karkataka and Simha should not be disturbed, but kept in tact:

 राशिगुणाकारः—Rasi multipliers.

**शोध्यावशिष्टं संस्थाप्य राशिमानेन वर्धयेत्।  
ग्रहयुक्ते तु तद्राशौ ग्रहमानेन वर्धयेत्॥३८॥**

**गोसिंहौ दशगुणितौ वसुभिर्मिथुनालिनौ।  
वणिङ्मेषौ च मुनिभिः कन्यकामकरौ शरैः॥३९॥**

**शेषाः स्वसङ्ख्यागुणिताः राशीनां गुणकाः स्मृताः।**

 *Slokas* 38-39½.—The resultant figures remaning after the above-mentioned two reductions in the several signs are to be multiplied each by its corresponding Rasimultiplier. If a particular Rasi be occupied by a planet, then the number of benefic dots should be further multiplied by the respective planet-multiplier. The Rasimultiplier for Vrishabha and Simha is 10; for Mithuna and Vrischika, 8; for Mesha and Tula, 7; for Kanya and Makara, 5; and the multipliers for the remaining signs are Karkataka, 4, Kumbha, 11, Dhanus, 9 and Meena, 12.

 ग्रहगुणाकरः—Planet—multipliers.

**जीवारशुक्रसौम्या दशवसुसप्तेन्द्रियैः क्रमाद्गुणिताः॥४०॥**

**बुधसङ्ख्या शेषाणां राशिगुणा ग्रहगुणाः पृथक् कार्याः।**  
**राशीनां गुणकारैश्च फलानि गुणयेत् पृथक्॥४१॥**

**सति तत्र ग्रहैर्युक्ते गुणयेद्ग्रहसङ्ख्यया।**

* Slokas* 40–41½.—The multipliers for Jupiter, Mars, Venus and Mercury are 10, 8, 7 and 5 and for the rest, it is the same as for Mercury, i. e., 5. The Rasimultipliers and planet–multipliers should be treated separately. The benefic dots in the several Rasis should be separately multiplied by the Rasi–multiplier. If there is a planet also in the Rasi, the number of benefic dots should be multiplied by the planet-multiplier.

** अथ ग्रहायुः—**Planets' Contribution to Life.

**एवं सङ्गुण्य संयोज्य सप्तभिर्गुणयेत्पुनः॥४२॥**

**सप्तविंशतिसम्भक्तात्तस्माल्लब्धं तु वत्सराः।  
शिष्टं रूपैर्नगैर्नीचैर्हत्वा हृत्वा पृथक् पृथक्॥४३॥**

**हारेण तेन लब्धाः स्युर्मासाहर्घटिकाः क्रमात्।  
सप्तविंशतिवर्षाणि मण्डलं परिकीर्तितम्॥४४॥**

**तद्भागशुद्धाः सङ्ग्राह्या मण्डलाधिकवत्सराः।**

 * Sloka* 42-44½.—Having thus multiplied separately and added the products, the result should be multiplied by 7 and divided by 27. The quotient will represent the number in years contributed by the planet. When the remainder is multiplied by 12 and divided by 27, we get the number of months Similarly, when the remainder now obtained is multiplied by 30 and divided by 27, we get the number of days; and lastly, when the last remainder is multiplied by 60 and divided by 27, we get the number of Ghatikas. 27 years constitute a Mandala. When a figure divided by 27 yields a remainder, the remainder alone should be taken as the number of years contributed.

**अन्योन्यमर्धहरणं ग्रहयोगे तु कारयेत्॥४५॥**

**नीचेऽर्धमस्तगेऽप्यर्धं हरणं तत्र कारयेत्।  
शत्रुक्षेत्रे त्रिभागोनं दृश्यार्द्धहरणं तथा॥४६॥**

**रणभङ्गे त्रिकांशोनं तथा पातेऽर्कचन्द्रयोः।  
बहुले हरणे प्राप्ते कारयेद्बलवत्तरम्॥४७॥**

**पश्चात्संयोज्य तत्सर्वं वाराङ्गेन विवर्धितम्।  
मातङ्गलब्धं शुद्धायुर्भवतीति न संशयः॥४८॥**

 * Slokas* 45-48.—When a planet is conjoined with another, the contributions of both the planets should be reduced by a half. If a planet be debilitated or eclipsed, then also it will lose half its contribution. A planet posited in an enemy's house will lose ⅓ of its contribution. The reduction in the contribution of planets that are posited in the visible half of the zodiac will have to be made as before. For a planet vanquished in planetary war or occupying a position within the (पात) range of the Sun and the Moon, a reduction by a third should be made. When several reductions crop up for a single planet, only the greatest need be done. The figures for the several planets should be added up and multiplied by 324 and divided by 365. The quotient got will be undoubtedly the net Ayus contributed by all the planets.

**पूर्ववद्दिनमासाब्दं कृत्वा तस्य दशा भवेत्।  
एवं ग्रहाणां सर्वेषां दशां कुर्यात् पृथक् पृथक्॥४९॥**

 * Sloka* 49.—The Dasa of each planet in terms of years, months, days etc., should be found out in the above manner. Thus should the Dasas of all the planets be found out separately.

**अष्टवर्गदशामार्गः सर्वेषामुत्तमोत्तमः।  
केन्द्रेष्वन्यतमस्थे शशिनि ग्रहसंयुतेऽष्टवर्गेण।**  
**आयुर्दायं कुर्याद्दशमर्क्षे क्रूरसौम्ययुते॥५०॥**

 *Sloka* 50-50½.—Of all the systems of Dasas (Ayus), the Ashtakavarga one is the very best. One's Ayurdaya should be computed by the Ashtakavarga process, when the Moon in conjunction with a planet is posited in one of the Kendras, and the 10th house is occupied by both benefics and malefics.

** ** अथ समुदायाष्टवर्गायुः—

**अष्टवर्गं समुद्धृत्य ग्रहाणां राशिमण्डले।  
प्राग्वत् त्रिकोणं संशोध्य पश्चादेकाधिपत्यम्॥५१॥**

* * *Sloka* 51.—Find the total of all the benefic dots in each of the Rasis of the 7 Ashtakavargas, and you get the Sarvashtaka varga figures. Now, effect first the Trikona reduction as before and then, the Ekadhipatya one.

**एकस्मिन् मण्डलाधिक्ये शोधयेच्चक्रमण्डलम्।  
द्वादशैव तु गृह्णीयादेवं सर्वेषु राशिषु॥५२॥**

* Sloka* 52.—If the figure in any Rasi exceed 12, then subtract from it 12 or multiplies of 12 (if necessary) and keep the remainder in tact. All the Rasis should be similarly treated.

**पूर्वोक्तगुणकारैस्तैर्वर्धयेच्च पृथक् पृथक्।  
एकीकृत्य तु तत्सर्वं सप्तभिर्गुणयेत्पुनः॥५३॥**

**सप्तविंशत्या च भाज्यं लब्धमायुः प्रदृश्यते।  
द्वादशादिगुणं शिष्टं मासाद्यं हारभाजितम्॥५४॥**

* Slokas* 53-54.—These should then be multiplied by their respective Rasi and Graha multipliers and their sumtotal should be further multiplied by 7 and then divided by 27. The quotient will reveal the requisite Ayus in years, months, days, etc.

**शतोर्ध्वं यदि तत्पिण्डं मण्डलोनाव (100) शेषयेत्।  
शतमेव तु गृह्णीयाद्दीर्घायुर्योगसम्भवे ॥५५॥**

**सर्वं संयोज्य तत्पिण्डं वाराङ्गेन विवर्धितम्।  
मातङ्गभक्तं लब्धायुर्मातङ्गाब्दं प्रचक्षते॥५६॥**

 * Slokas 55-56.*—When the figure exceeds 100, remove as many hundreds as may be necessary. If the 'native be declared as long-lived, then 100 alone should be taken. The Ayus should then be rectified by multiplying the same by 324 and dividing by 365.

**सर्वग्रहेभ्यः शुद्धायुः पिण्डरूपं विनिर्दिशेत्।  
ग्रहाणां तु विभागार्थमुपायस्त्विह कथ्यते॥५७॥**

 * Sloka 57.*—The rectified Ayus got from all the planets should be shown in a collective form. The actual contributions derived from each of the several planets should be ascertained in the following manner.

**व्यस्ताष्टवर्गकदशा चैकीभूता घटकृता।  
तमेव हारं सर्वेषामनष्टं स्थापयेत् क्वचित्॥५८॥**

 * Sloka 58*.—The Dasa-periods obtained through the Bhinnashtakavarga process should be totalled and converted into Ghatikas and this figure should be preserved as it is (without any reduction) for being used as divisor in the case of all planets.

**समस्ताष्टकनाड्यस्तु भिन्नाष्टकदशाहताः।  
भागहारहृताल्लब्धं ग्रहस्यायुर्भविष्यति॥५९॥**

* Sloka 59.*—The total Ashtakavarga Ghatikas referred to above should be multiplied by the several Bhinnashtakavarga Dasa-periods and then divided by the divisor aforesaid. The quotient will reveal the years contributed by the planets.

**दिनमासाब्दपर्यन्तं कृत्वा पूर्ववदाचरेत्।  
एवं ग्रहाणां सर्वेषां शुद्धायुः स्यात् पृथक् पृथक्॥६०॥**

 *Sloka 60*.—The days, months and years should be computed as mentioned above. Thus should be calculated the exact periods of Ayus contributed by each of the several planets.

**समुदायदशामार्गम् एवं क्रम उदाहृतः।  
राशितुल्यानि वर्षाणि प्रयच्छन्त्युदयो बली॥६१॥**

 *Sloka 61.*—The process of finding out the Dasaperiods of the several planets through the figures in the Sarvashtakavarga has been already explained. When the Lagna is strong, it contributes as many years as are signified by the Lagna Rasi.

**उभयत्रापि विज्ञाय लग्नदायं विनिर्दिशेत।  
अष्टवर्गदशामार्गं सर्वेषां सम्मतं विदुः॥६२॥**

 *Sloka 62*.—It is only after ascertaining by both the methods that one should fix up the years contributed by the Lagna. The process of finding out the Dasaperiods through the Ashtakavarga method is acceptable to all.

**गृहैक्यस्य दशाभावे भेदमार्गं प्रकल्पयेत्।  
तदोच्चनीचमार्गेण दशां कुर्याद्विचक्षणः॥६३॥**

 *Sloka 63*.—In the case of any difficulty in ascertaining the Dasaperiods of planets owing to their being conjoined with other planets, a different method should be resorted to. A clever astrologer should calculate the Dasas of the planets through their exaltation and depression positions.

**नीचारिभवनयातैर्ग्रहैः समस्तैस्तदंशगैर्वाऽपि।  
यवनाचार्यमतेन ग्नहदायं कल्पयेन्मतिमान्॥६४॥**

* Sloka 64.*—In the case of planets occupying depression, or inimical Rasis or Amsas, a wise astrologer should determine the contributions of the planets according to the method laid down by Sage Yavana.

**ग्रहसहिते केन्द्रस्थे चन्द्रे केन्द्राद्बहिः स्थितैः शेषैः।  
समुदायाष्टकविधिना ग्नहदायं कल्पयेन्मणित्थमतात्॥६५॥**

 *Sloka 65*.—When the Moon occupies a Kendra house in conjunction with another planet, and when the other planets are posited outside the Kendra houses, one ought to adopt the Samudayashtakavarga method for ascertaining the contributions of the several planets. This is the view of Manitha.

**एकत्र गतैः सर्वैः केन्द्रादन्यत्र संस्थितैर्जन्तोः।  
आयुर्दायविभागैर्दशाफलं ज्ञायते नैव॥६६॥**

 *Sloka 66*.—If, at a birth, all the planets are posited in a single house other than a Kendra, the effects of the Dasa-periods arising through the Ayurdaya contributions of the planets cannot be ascertained at all.

**अल्पायुर्योगभवा दीर्घायुर्योगजास्तु ये मनुजाः।  
तेषां दशाविभागैरायुर्ज्ञातुं न शक्यते नूनम्।६७॥**

 *Sloka 67*.—In the case of people born with only a short lease of life and of those endowed with long life, it is not at all possible to determine life through the planetary Dasa-periods.

**षष्ठाष्टमव्ययगतैः पापैरल्पायुरादिशेत्तज्ज्ञः।  
सोम्यैर्विपरीतं स्यान्मिथखगैर्मध्यमायुरादेश्यम्॥६८॥**

**इति श्रीवराहमिहिरसुतश्रीपृिथुयशोविरचिते होरासारे आयुर्दायाध्यायः सप्तमः॥**

 *Sloka 68*.—In the case of persons born with malefics posited in the 6th, 8th, and 12th houses, astrologers declare short life. If benefics occupy these houses, it will be reverse. If mixed, he will have middle, life.

Thus ends the 7th Adhyaya on 'Ayurdaya' in the work Horasara,  
written by Prithuyasas, the son of Varahamihira.

**———**

**अष्टमोऽध्यायः**

**अथ दशाफलनिरूपणम्॥**  
**———**

**होरादिनेशशाशिनां प्रबलो भवेद्य-**  
** स्तत्कण्टकादिषु गता कथिता दशेशाः।  
पूर्वा दशातिबलिनः सदृशोऽब्दवृन्दो  
  साम्ये भवेच्च शरदां प्रथमोदितस्य॥१॥**

 *Sloka 1*.—Of the Lagna, the Sun and the Moon, whichever is strongest, his Dasa comes first. Then follow in their order of strength those that are situated in the Kendra and other houses. If they possess equal strength, that which gives a larger number of years will lead. If there be equality even in the number of years contributed, that which rises first after the next conjunction will take precedence; and when the risings are also simultaneous, that which has the first mention will have the lead.

**वयोमुखेषु त्रिषु च त्रयः स्युर्लग्नार्कचन्द्रा बलसन्नियोगात्।  
यथाबलं कालविधानमेत्य त्रिधाऽऽहिता हि त्रिभिरेव विद्यात्॥२॥**

 * Sloka 2.*—According to the strength of the Lagna the Sun and the Moon, the three stages of life of the native will be effective, in order. It should be understood that it is through these three significators that the effectiveness (strength) or otherwise of these three stages is to be, ascertained or determined.

 See बृ जा, VIII–1. Also श्री–प. p–121.

**स्वोच्चास्थितो मित्रभगः स्ववर्गे स्वर्क्षेऽपि चान्यैरशुभैरदृष्टः।  
जन्माधिपस्तद्गुणवीर्यवान् स्यात्तज्जन्मकालेऽपि शुभप्रदः स्यात्॥३॥**

 *Sloka 3*.—If the owner of the sign occupied by the Moon be exalted, occupy a friend's house, be in his own Varga, or his own Rasi and have no aspect of other malefics, he will reveal in a powerful manner all the planet's qualities and prove propitious to the native even from his very birth.

**त्रिषट्कलाभेषुगतैः समस्तैः सौम्यैः सुखादीनि भवन्ति बाल्ये।  
तत्रैव पापैर्वयसोऽन्त्यकाले जायार्थपुत्रा हि भवन्ति सम्यक्॥४॥**

 *Sloka 4*.—If all the benefics, occupy the 3rd, 6th, and 11th houses, the person concerned will enjoy all happiness in his early period of life. If malefics should occupy the same houses, he will have wife, wealth and children and all comforts in his later life.

**लग्नस्य पूर्वं न भवेद्दशा तु यदा तदा त्वन्यदशा भवेत्सा।  
जन्ये तु नेच्छन्ति परे तु केचिद्गुरुप्रसादेन च लभ्यमेतत्॥५॥**

 * Sloka 5.*—If at a birth, the Lagna Dasa does not occur first, then another Dasa will take its place. But others do not accept this view. As this involves a conflict of opinions, the correct procedure must be understood only by the grace of one's teacher.

**उच्चान्निवृत्ते त्ववरोहिसञ्ज्ञा क्रमात् क्षयं यान्ति दशाफलानि।  
आरोहिणी स्वेच्चमुखाभिलाषे क्रमेण सर्वं फलमातनोति॥६॥**

 * Sloka 6.*—When a planet leaves off his exaltation, its Dasa is termed at and its effects gradually fail to give fruit. A planet on its way to its exaltation is termed ringo and its effects begin to ripen fully.

**तुङ्गसुहृत्स्वगृहांशे नीचे रिपुभेऽस्तसंस्थिते वाऽपि।  
तस्य दशा मिश्रफला दशा परार्द्धे शुभप्रदा ज्ञेया॥७॥**

 *Sloka 7*.—In the case of a planet whether exalted, in a friend's Rasi or Amsa, in depression, in an inimical sign, or in an eclipsed state, the effects of the Dasa will only be mixed. At the latter half of the Dasa, it will prove auspicious.

**सविता दशाफलानां प्रापयिता चन्द्रमाः प्रबोधयिता।  
आदित्यचन्द्रवशगाः सर्वे ताराग्रहा ज्ञेयाः॥८॥**

 * Sloka 8*.—It is the Sun that promotes the effects of the Dasas to happen and it is the Moon that gives life and revives the same. All the planets are under the influence of the two luminaries and are termed (only) starry in their influence.

**चन्द्रावनेयसोमजभृगुसुतगुरुसूर्यमन्दानाम्।  
क्रमशो दशापरिग्रह इष्टा नैसर्गिकी शुभा प्रोक्ता॥९॥**

 * Sloka 9.*—The Moon, Mars, Mercury, Venus, Jupiter, the Sun and Saturn in their order claim their Dasa periods in the Nisarga System and prove auspicious in their (respective) turns.

**कष्टगृहे कष्टांशे मूढेऽपि निसर्गसंस्थिताः शुभदाः।  
शस्तगृहे शस्तांशे निसर्गयोगास्तु राज्यफलदाः स्युः॥१०॥**

 *Sloka 10*.—A planet miserably placed in a Rasi or Amsa or even eclipsed will prove benefic in giving effects if it happens to be his Dasa under the Naisargika system. If he should also occupy an auspicious Rasi or Amsa, the yoga will confer on the person concerned wealth and even kingdom.

**यस्य नवांशकहोरा भास्करसञ्ज्ञा प्रवृद्धफलदा स्यात्।  
शशिभागांश्चकहोरा सुषुप्तिचिन्तासु फलदा स्यात्॥११॥**

 *Sloka 11*.—The effect of a planet placed in a Navamsa or Hora owned by the Sun will be fully felt, while in a Navamsa or Hora belonging to the Moon, the effect will appear only in dreamy reveries.

**पाकपतौ लग्नस्थे स्वोच्चे स्वर्क्षे त्रिभागदशमे स्वे।  
तस्य दशा पुष्टफला तेषु नवांशस्थितेषु मध्यफला॥१२॥**

 * Sloka 12.*—When the lord of the Dasa occupies the Lagna, is in his exaltation, in his own Rasi or in his own decanate, his Dasa will prove fully benefic in effect. If he should occupy only the Navamsas of the abovementioned places, the effect will only be mixed.

**चन्द्रस्तु दशारम्भे कुलीरभवनस्थितो यदा भवति।  
स्त्रीदोषकृत्पशुघ्नः कुजभवने हन्ति वास्तुपतिम्॥१३॥**

 *Sloka 13*.—If at the commencement of a Dasa the Moon should occupy Kataka, the native concerned will do some harm to a woman, and will be a killer of cattle; if he should occupy a sign of Mars, he will kill the owner of the house he is living in.

**विद्याशास्त्रज्ञानं मित्रप्राप्तिं करोति बुधराशौ।  
सुखगृहमानावाप्तिं जीवगृहे दिशति शीतकरः॥१४॥**

 *Sloka 14*.—Acquisition of learning, proficiency in Sastras, getting new friends, all these will be had when the Moon is in Mercury's Rasi. When the Moon is in Jupiter's Rasi, the native will have happiness, acquire a dwelling, and and receive veneration.

**शौक्रेऽन्नपानमतुलं सौख्यं चन्द्रो विनाशं च।  
परिणतवनिताप्रीतिं सौरगृहे प्रेष्यकर्मरतिम्॥१५॥**

 *Sloka 15*.—If the Moon at the time aforesaid occupy a sign owned by Venus, the person concerned will have food and drink in plenty, and enjoy complete happiness; there is also a possibility of danger to his life. If, at the time, the Moon should occupy a house of Saturn, he will have immense satisfaction with his wedded wife. He will be engaged in doing mean acts.

**दुर्गारण्यनिवासं कर्षणकर्मसु रतिं महोत्साहम्।  
सिंहे शशी प्रकुरुते स्त्रीपुत्रविवादमनिशं वा॥१६॥**

 *Sloka 16*.—Living in a dense forest, intense liking in acts causing torment to others, engaged all the time in quarrels with one's wife and children, all these will be the result when the Moon occupies Simha.

**मित्रोच्चोपचयस्थाने त्रिकोणे सप्तमेऽपि वा।  
पाकेश्वरे स्थितश्चन्द्रः कुरुते सत्फलां दशाम्॥१७॥**

 * Sloka 17*.—If the lord of the Dasa occupy at the time a friendly, or exaltation house, an Upachaya house, a Trikona, or the 7th house, the Moon will generally cause benefic effects.

**विपरीतगतश्चन्द्रो दशादौ पर्यवस्थितः।  
स्वोच्चगस्यापि खेटस्य दशा न प्रतिपूजिता॥१८॥**

 *Sloka 18.*—If, at the commencement of a Dasa, the Moon should occupy an untoward house, the lord of the Dasa, though placed in exaltation, will not reciprocate the benefic effects that are ordinarily expected.

**एतैः प्रकारैर्बहुभिरवधार्य विवेकिना।  
शुभाशुभपरिज्ञानं पुरुषं प्रतिचिन्तयेत्॥१९॥**

**इति श्रीवराहमिहिरसुतश्रीपृथुयशोविरचिते होरासारे दशाफलनिरूपणाध्यायोऽष्टमः।**

 *Sloka 19.*—It is by examining in such various ways that a wise man should determine the good and bad effects that may befall the native.

Thus ends the 8th Adhyaya on "Dasaphalanirupanam in the  
work Horasara, written by Prithuyasas, the son of Varahamihira.

**—————**

**नवमोऽध्यायः**

**अथ सूर्यदशाफलम्॥**

The Sun's Dasa and its Effects.

**भानोर्दशानुभूतो विदेशवासी वनाद्रिदुर्गचरः॥  
द्विजदेववह्निभूपैः शास्त्रैर्भैषज्यतो धनप्राप्तिः॥१॥**

 *Sloka 1*.—At the time when the Sun's Dasa is progressing, the person concerned will live in foreign countries, roam about forests, mountains and fortresses. There will be influx of money through Brahmins, fire, sovereign, the arts and medicines.

**मन्त्राभिचारकुशलो विघातकुशलश्चमूपतिश्चण्डः।  
विख्यातकर्मनिरतो धीमान्विस्पष्टवागनिष्टश्च॥२॥**

 *Sloka 2*.—He will become clever in the use of Mantras, spells, in creating obstacles to others, will become the head of an army and brave. He will be engaged in a great meritorious work, will become learned, clever in talking and disagreeable.

**व्यालमृगोरगहन्ता दारसुतस्थानवर्जितश्चपलः।  
ऋणवानदीनवचनो नेत्रोदरदन्तकर्णरोगी स्यात्॥३॥**

 * Sloka 3*.—He will kill wild beasts, deer, and snakes; he will be without wife and children, become bereft of his place and fickle. He will contract debts, will speak harshly and will suffer from eye-disease, belly ache, tooth ache and ear-disease.

**नृपतस्करादिपीडा बन्धुद्वेषः स्वगोत्रनाशार्थः।  
सामान्यमेतदुक्तं राशिविशेषान्वितं फलं वक्ष्ये॥४॥**

 * Sloka 4*.—Trouble from the Sovereign, thieves, etc. misunderstanding with relations, destruction of cattle, and loss of wealth, these will generally be the effects. I shall now describe the effects with special reference to the several Rasis.

**भानोरुच्चदशायां बहुप्रतापः स्वधर्मकर्मरतः।  
नृपजनितार्त्तिं लभते पित्रार्जितवित्तदेशकर्माढ्यः॥५॥**

 *Sloka 5.*—During the Sun's Dasa when the Sun is in exaltation, the person concerned will do many courageous deeds; he will be intent in doing religious works. There will be trouble caused by the sovereign. He will inherit paternal property, become popular and famous through his good actions.

**उच्चातिक्रान्तदशा भानोरुदरामयं शिरोरोगम्।  
स्वजनविरोधं कुरुते चतुष्पदाद्यैर्भयं समाप्नोति॥६॥**

 *Sloka* 6.—The Dasa of the Sun when he has fallen from exaltation will bring on diseases of the stomach, head-ache, misunderstanding with one's relations and danger from cattle and the like.

**भानोर्दशा वृषस्था कृषिपशुसुतदारवर्जितं जनयेत्।  
हृद्गुह्यनेत्ररोगी बन्धुक्लेशान्वितोऽपि मानी स्यात्॥७॥**

 *Sloka* 7.—During the Sun's Dasa when he is in sign Vrishabha, the person concerned will leave off agriculture, be without cattle, sons and wife. He will suffer from disease in the private parts, have eye-complaints, affliction through relations. He will however preserve his selfrespect.

**मिथुने भानुदशायां शास्त्रकलाकाव्यगोष्ठशिल्परतः।  
कृषिपशुधनधान्याद्यैः संयुक्तो ज्ञातितो धनप्राप्तिः॥८॥**

 *Sloka* 8.—In the Sun's Dasa when he is in sign Mithuna, the person will be busy in learning the Sastras, Arts poetry, etc. He will busy himself with agriculture, cattle, wealth, grain, etc. and will acquire money through his Dayadins.

**दिवसकरस्य दशायां चन्द्रगृहे ख्यातिमान् नृपात्तधनः।  
स्त्रीनिर्जितोऽनिलात्मा पितृबन्धुविवर्जितोऽतिर्तीक्ष्णश्च॥९॥**

 *Sloka* 9.—During the Sun's Dasa when the Sun is in Kataka, the person will get fame and wealth from the King. He will be henpecked, will be fasting, separated from parents and relations and will be very pungent (in his speech).

**क्षेत्रदशायां भानोरनेकवित्तान्वितो नृपसमो वा।  
दुर्गेऽरण्ये कृषिमान् सुतदारसमन्वितोऽतिविख्यातः॥१०॥**

 *Sloka* 10.—In the Sun's Dasa when the Sun is in his own house, the native will be endowed with all kinds of luxuries and be equal to a King. He will live in an impenetrable forest and be engaged in agriculture; he will live with his wife and children and will get wide fame.

**कन्यारूढदशायां भानोः पशुमार्गतः सिद्धिः।  
द्विजदेवधनप्राप्तिः स्त्रीजननं लोकमान्यश्च॥११॥**

 *Sloka* 11.—During the Sun's Dasa when the Sun is in Kanya, the person will get wealth through rearing cattle; there will be acquisition of money through Brahmins and Gods; he will beget daughters, and will command respect of people.

**अतिनीचदशा भानोः कृषिसुतमित्रार्थदारनाशकरी।  
लभते विदेशगमनं चोरानलसाध्वसं जनयेत्॥१२॥**

 *Sloka* 12.—When the Sun's Dasa is in progress and the Sun is occupying his depression sign Tula, there will be loss in agriculture; he will lose children, friends, wealth and wife; he will proceed to a foreign country, and there will be fear from thieves and fire.

**नीचातिक्रान्तदशा सूर्यस्य नृपाद्धनं सुखं कुरुते।  
स्त्रीद्वेषजनितदुःखं जनयति परवञ्चना धनप्राप्तिम्॥१३॥**

 *Sloka* 13.—In the Sun's Dasa when the Sun has quitted his depression sign, the native will easily get wealth from the Sovereign. There will be mental affliction caused through a woman. He will earn money through deceiving others.

**अज्ञो रणप्रतापी वृश्चिकराशिस्थभास्करदशायाम्।  
विषतोयशस्त्रपीडा पितुर्जनन्याश्च दुर्गमो भवति॥१४॥**

 *Sloka* 14.—During the Sun's Dasa when the Sun is posited in sign Vrischika, the person concerned will evince dullness; there will be trouble through poison,water and weapons; he will not have free access to his parents.

**कार्मुकभानुदशायां स्वपुत्रदारान्वितो धनाढ्यश्च।  
द्विजनृपतिजनितपूजा शास्त्रश्रुतिगेयवाद्यसन्तुष्टः॥१५॥**

 *Sloka* 15.—When the Sun is in Dhanus and his Dasa is in progress, the native will be happy surrounded by his wife and children and he will get much wealth. He will be respected by Brahmins and the King, and he will derive great satisfaction through Sastras, Vedas, music and musical instruments.

**मकरे भानुदशायां परकार्यरतो न याति धनपुत्रौ।  
स्त्रीदोषजनितदुःखी पाण्ड्वामयपीडिऽतोऽङ्गहीनो वा॥१६॥**

 *Sloka* 16.—When the Sun is in Makara, and his Dasa is ripening, the native will interest himself in other people's affairs; he will not command money; his children will forsake him; he will suffer misery through the faults caused through his wife; and he will be troubled through jaundice or from loss of a limb.

**कुम्भे भानुदशायां हृद्रोगसमन्वितो विनष्टसुतः।  
पिशुनः परान्नभोजी भार्याजनवन्धुवैरी स्यात्॥१७॥**

 *Sloka* 17—When the Sun is in Kumbha and his Dasa is ripening the native will suffer from heart-disease, he will lose children, become a slanderer; he will eat at other people's table; and will be hated by his wife and other relations.

**भानुदशायां मीने स्त्रीप्रीत्या लब्धमानधनसौख्यः।  
विषमज्वरपीडा स्यात् सुतचिन्तावान् नरेन्द्रसमः॥१८॥**

 *Sloka* 18.—During the Sun's Dasa and when the Sun occupies sign Meena, the person concerned will become happy, command respect and wealth, all through his partner's love. He will suffer from remittent fever and will be thinking about his children; and will be like a king.

**अष्टमसंस्थस्य दशा भानोरुच्चेऽपि दोषवृद्धिकरी।  
षष्ठदशा व्रणपीडां कुरुते पितृमातृदोषवृद्धिकरी॥१९॥**

 *Sloka* 19—During the advent of the Sun's Dasa and when the Sun is posited in the 8th house, the effects will, in spite of the Sun holding an exalted position, prove malefic. If the Sun be in the 6th house at the time, the person will suffer from ulcer; he will not get any benefit from either of his parents.

**पुरुषप्रथमदशायां फलं तु वाच्यं शुभाशुभं वाऽपि।  
सद्यो मरणं योगै रुणद्धि स दशाफलं न चायाति॥२०॥**

 *Sloka* 20.—During the first Dasa in the case of a male, the effects whether good or bad should be predicted. Should there be his exit from the world immediately, the effects of the Dasa will not happen.

**मातापितृदोषाभ्यां क्वचिन्निरुद्धं दशाफलं ज्ञेयम्।  
तस्माद्योगान् सम्यक् परीक्ष्य पश्चाद्दशाफलं चिन्त्यम्॥२१॥**

 *Sloka* 21.—On account of the sins committed by the two parents—the mother and the father—there may be a break in the happening of the effects in certain cases. It is therefore imperative that the Yogas should be first examined carefully before any attempt is made to predict the effects of a Dasa.

**यस्यादौ भानुदशा मातापितृदोषदा सपक्षघ्नी।  
लग्रदशा क्लेशकरी चन्द्रदशा ज्ञानविघ्नकरी॥२२॥**

**इति श्रीवराहमिहिरसुतश्रीपृिथुयशोविरचिते होरासारे सूर्यदशाफलाध्यायो नवमः॥**

 *Sloka* 22.—If at a birth the Sun's Dasa should begin first and if the Sun be not favourable to the mother as well as the father, it will bring on paralysis to the child. If the Lagna Dasa should happen first, it will cause If it be the Moon's Dasa, it will retard the acquisition of knowledge and learning.

Thus ends the 9th Adhyaya on the Sun's Dasa and his effects  
in Horasara, a work composed by Prithuyasas.

————

**दशमोऽध्यायः**

**अथ चन्द्रदशाफलम्**

**सामान्येन तु षोढा चन्द्रदशा कथ्यते मणित्थाद्यैः।  
शुक्लस्य प्रथमतिथेरारभ्यारोहिणी दशा शशिनः॥१॥**

 *Sloka* 1.—The Moon's Dasa aud its effects are generally classified in six ways by sage Manittha and others. The Dasa is declared to be waxing or increasing in the case of the Moon from the first lunar day onwards.

**कृष्णा द्वितिथिप्रभृतिकदर्शान्ता चावरोहिणीन्दुदशा।  
जलधिजलोत्थितिकाले नृृणां सूतौ दशा शशाङ्कस्य॥२॥**

 Sloka 2.—From the Dwitiya Tithi in the dark half (16th lunar day) till the end of the New Moon, (the birth may happen at any time within this interval) the Moon's Dasa is known as अवरोहिणी or descending. Should a birth take place at a time when the waves of the ocean are rising,

**आरोहिणीति विदिता विपरीता सावरोहिणी ख्याता।  
नीचाच्च्युतस्य हि दशा हिमगोरारोहिणी कथिता॥३॥**

 *Sloka* 3.—it is termed आरोहिणी or ascending. If it be contrarywise, it is called अवरोहिणी**.** Where the Moon has left his नीच or depression, then also her Dasa is known as आरोहिणी.

**तुङ्गाच्च्युतस्यं तु दशाऽवरोहिणी निगदिता शशिनः।  
रोहावरोहभेदः सम्यक् त्रिविधः पुरातनैः कथितः॥४॥**

 *Sloka* 4.—If at a birth the Moon has fallen from her exaltation, her Dasa is termed अवरोहिणी- descending. The difference between आरोह and अवरोह is distinguished in three ways by the ancients.

**आरोहत्रययुक्ता चन्द्रदशा सर्वसिद्धिकरी।  
आरोहदशारूढो मर्त्यः स्यात्सर्वलोकविख्यातः॥५॥**

**अवरोहदशाप्राप्तौ पुरुषस्य यथाक्रमं क्षयो भवति।  
चन्द्रे प्रोक्तबलारूढे शशिहोरागता ग्रहाः॥६॥**

**अशुभास्ते शुभं दद्यू रवेरेवं शशी यथा।**

 *Slokas* 5-6½ —There are three kinds of आरोह (Aroha) in the Moon's Dasa well-known to all. They bring on success in everything. When the अवरोह (Avaroha) Dasa begins to dawn, there will be naturally decay in everything for the person concerned.

 When the Moon is endowed with the minimum strength, and the planets are all in lunar Hora, though malefic in character, they give good effects. During the Sun's Dasa when he is in a similar situation he will prove auspicious like the Moon.

**चन्द्रदशान्वितकाले मन्त्री नृपसम्मतोऽतिमानी स्यात्।  
देवद्विजमन्त्राद्यैर्धनवान्विनयान्वितः कलाज्ञश्च॥७॥**

 *Sloka* 7.—When the Moon's Dasa is in progress, the person concerned will become a friend of the king and become his counsellor and highly honoured. He will get wealth through divine favor, Brahmins, spells, etc. He will possess modesty and will be skilled in the arts.

**मधुमधुरगन्धकुसुमैः फलवृक्षैर्वित्तवाननियतार्थः।  
ख्यातो बहुप्रतापः सदाटनः स्त्रीप्रजान्वितो धीमान्॥८॥**

 *Sloka* 8.—He will get good and sweet-smelling flowers, possess fruit-bearing trees and command unlimited wealth; he will become very famous and noted for his valour; he will be always on his legs, beget daughters and will be highly intelligent.

**देवद्विजार्चनरतः परोपकारी मृदुस्वभावश्च।  
नृत्यादिकर्मकुशलः कफानिलात्मा जलादिधर्मपरः॥९॥**

 *Sloka* 9.—He will be intent in honouring the Gods and Brahmins, helping others and will possess a good heart. He will be skilled in dancing and other allied arts. He has wind and phlegm in his composition.

**बलवान् स्वजनविरोधी निद्रालस्यं मदान्वितः क्षीणे।  
सामान्यमेतदुक्तं प्रतिराशिफलं यथाक्रमं वक्ष्ये॥१०॥**

 *Sloka* 10.—He will possess bodily strength, will hate his own relations, will be sleepy and lazy, intoxicated and powerless. The general effects have thus been described. I shall give in detail the separate effect due to the Moon occupying each of the several Rasis.

**मेषाश्रितचन्द्रदशा स्त्रीसुतलाभं विदेशकर्मरतिम्।  
सहजविनाशं कुर्यादसद्द्रव्ययाथशिरोरुहं जनयेत्॥११॥**

 *Sloka* 11.—The Dasa of the Moon when posited in Mesha will bring to the native the acquisition of a wife and children. He will take pleasure in doing great acts. He will lose a brother through ill-gotten wealth. He will suffer from head-ache.

**स्वोच्चगतस्य हिमांशोर्दशाधिरोहे नृपस्य राज्याप्तिः।  
बहुसुतरत्नसमृद्धः स्त्रीणां वशगो गजाश्वपशुमांश्च॥१२॥**

 *Sloka* 12.—During the advent of the Moon's Dasa when the Moon is exalted, there will be the acquisition of a kingdom. He will have many sons and jewels; he will be under the influence of women. He will have elephants, horses and cattle.

**मूलत्रिकोणगेन्दोर्दशाभियातो नरो विदेशरतः।  
कृषिविक्रयाद्धनाप्तिः स्वजनद्वेषी कफानिलार्त्तः स्यात्॥१३॥**

 *Sloka* 13.—During the Dasa of the Moon when she is in her Moolatrikona Rasi, the person concerned will be spending his time in foreign countries; he will earn money through agriculture, will hate his own relations and will suffer from wind-disease and phlegmatic troubles.

**वयसो मध्यमभागे चन्द्रदशायां महासुखी धनवान्।  
द्विजदेवमन्त्रिभावैः सम्पन्नो युवतिवल्लभो भवति॥१४॥**

 *Sloka* 14.—During the middle portion of the Moon's Dasa, the person concerned will be in the height of his happiness and command immense wealth. He will be moving with Brahmins and Gods and become the favourite of his wife.

 In the last quarter नृपतिवल्लभो भवति is another reading.

**पूर्वार्द्धे सम्भूतो जननीमृत्युकरोऽतिपापरुतः।  
पश्चादर्द्धे वृषभे पितुर्वियोगं शशी कुरुते॥१५॥**

 *Sloka* 15.—In the first half of the Dasa, there will happen the demise of the mother. He will be intent in committing sinful acts. In the latter half when the Moon is in Vrishabha, she will cause the death of the father.

**द्विजदेवाश्रितकार्यो मतिमान् धनवस्त्रभोगसम्पन्नः।  
मिथुने चन्द्रदशायां स्थानात् स्थानान्तरं व्रजति॥१६॥**

 *Sloka* 16.—At the time of the Moon's Dasa when she is in Mithuna, the native will be busy attending to Gods and Brahmins; will be learning and command wealth, clothes and other enjoyments. He will be moving from place to place.

**चन्द्रदशायां क्षेत्रे जलकृषिपशुधान्यवित्तवान् भवति।  
ज्योतिर्ज्ञानकलाज्ञो गुह्यरुगार्तो वनाद्रिदुर्गचरः॥१७॥**

 *Sloka* 17.—When the Moon's Dasa is in progress and when she is in Karkataka, the person gets wealth through water, lands, agriculture, cattle and corn. He will be skilled in Astrology and other sciences. He will suffer from trouble in the anus. He will be roaming through forests, mountains and fortresses,

**सिंहे चन्द्रदशायां ज्ञानधनाप्तिर्मनोरथं लभते।  
स्वजनश्रेष्ठो मतिमान् विकलाङ्गो नातिपुत्रवान् सुभगः॥१८॥**

 *Sloka* 18.—During the Moon's Dasa when she is in Simha, there will be acquisition of learning, and wealth. One's desires will be fulfilled. He will become the chief among his relations, and will acquire knowledge. He will lose one of his limbs; he will not have many issue. He will be amiable.

**कन्यायां चन्द्रदशा विदेशगमनं परस्त्रियालाभम्।  
काव्यकलास्वतिनिपुणं कुरुते स्वल्पार्थकार्यसिद्धिकरम्॥१९॥**

 *Sloka* 19.—During the Moon's Dasa when she is in Kanya, the person will move to foreign places, will get another lady companion; will become proficient in Poetry and the Arts. He will succeed in a business with a small capital.

**चन्द्रदशायां जूके स्त्रीकृतदोषाश्च मानहानिः स्यात्।  
भग्नोत्साही चपलो दारिद्र्यवशो मनोदुःखी॥२०॥**

 *Sloka* 20.—During the Moon's Dasa when the Moon is in Tula, his behaviour with the other sex will be questionable; and his honour will be at stake. His enthusiasm will be curbed; he will become fickle, suffer from penury and feel miserable.

**नचिदशायां मरणं हिमगुर्व्याधिं त्वनेकविधम्।  
कुरुते दारवियोगं सन्नोत्साहं स्वबुद्धिपरितापम्॥२१॥**

 *Sloka* 21.—In the Moon's Dasa when she is in her depression sign, he may meet with his end, suffer from various ills and lose his wife; he will have a break in his enthusiasm and get insulted by his relations.

**नीचोन्मुक्तदशायां शशिनः कथितोऽल्पविक्तयुवतीशः।  
क्रयविक्रयाद्धनाप्तिर्मर्मस्वतिरोगवान् स्वपक्षघ्नः॥२२॥**

 *Sloka* 22.—In the Moon's Dasa when the Moon has left her depression Rasi, the person concerned will get a young damsel of limited means, He will earn money through trading; he will suffer from a severe disease in his private parts or from paralysis.

**चन्द्रदशायां चापे गजाश्वनाथो निवासबहुलः स्यात्।  
पूर्वार्जितधननाशो पुत्रसुखी बहुधनी भवति॥२३॥**

 *Sloka* 23.—During the Moon's Dasa when she is in Dhanus, the person concerned will own elephants, horses and many residences. He will lose his ancestral property. He will be happy through his sons and will become immensely rich.

**मकरे चन्द्रदशायां स्पर्धावान् दीननृत्यगृहवासी।  
स्त्रीमेदिनीप्रजीर्णो लोके श्रुतवान् न चातिघनपुत्रः॥२४॥**

 *Sloka* 24.—In the Moon's Dasa when she is in Makara, the native will be of an emulative nature. He will be wifeless and landless. He will be conversant with the Vedas. He will not have many issue and will possess limited wealth.

**कुम्भे चन्द्रदशायां प्रवर्तने क्षीणवृत्तिरभ्यासे।  
बहुॠणभोगी चपलः कुस्त्रीसक्तो गुदोदरार्तिः स्यात्॥२५॥**

 *Sloka* 25.—During the Moon's Dasa when she is in Kumbha, the native will adopt a low profession, will contract large debts, will be fickle-minded and addicted to a vile woman. He will suffer from trouble in the anus.

**वर्गोत्तमांशगविधोर्दाये बलवद्विरोधितो निःस्वः।  
दन्ताक्षिकर्णपीडाः स्वपुत्रदारैः परित्यक्तः॥२६॥**

 *Sloka* 26.—During the Dasa of the Moon when she has attained a Vargottamamsa, the native will lose all his wealth through the enmity of a powerful person. He will suffer from tooth-ache, eye-disease and disease in the ear. He will be left uncared for by his wife and children.

**मीने चन्द्रदशायां जलार्थभोगी सदाटनो धीमान्।  
गोमहिषदारपुत्रैः समन्वितो विगतशत्रुगणः॥२७॥**

 *Sloka* 27.—When the Moon is in Meena and her Dasa is in progress, the native will enrich himself through pearls and other sea-products. He will be always roam- ing. He will be intelligent. He will have buffaloes and will live with his wife and children and be free from enemies.

**मीनसवर्गोत्तमशशिदाये निधिसङ्ग्रहं सुखं लभते।  
कन्यापिताङ्गहीनो मातापितृवर्जितो भवेद्बाल्ये॥२८॥**

 *Sloka* 28.—When the Moon has attained a Vargottamamsa in Meena, the person concerned will get a treasure and be happy. He will be the father of daughters; he will be defective of some limb and will be devoid of the company of his parents during childhood.

**वर्गोत्तमगदशायां मुक्तस्थानेष्वभीष्टफललाभः।  
स्वकुलश्रेष्ठो मतिमान् बलधर्मपरोऽतिविद्वांश्च॥२९॥**

 *Sloka *29.—During the Dasa of the Moon when she has attained a Vargottamamsa, his desired objects signified by the Rasi last left will be duly fulfilled. He will become the chief of his family, intelligent and intent in doing virtuous acts and will be very learned.

**चन्द्रे व्ययभवनस्थे सर्वोपायैर्धनागमः पूर्णे।  
क्षीणे रिपुनीचस्थे पूर्वोक्तफलं क्षणात् क्षणं नश्येत्॥३०॥**

 *Sloka* 30.—If the Moon should occupy the 12th house and her Dasa be in progress, the person will acquire wealth by all possible means. Should the Moon in the above case be in the dark half and in depression or inimical house, the wealth mentioned above will disappear every moment.

**क्षीणाष्टमगहिमांशोर्दाये व्याध्यादिपीडितो मनुजः।  
स्त्रीकृतदोषनिमित्तैर्दारिद्र्याद्युन्नतिं लभते॥३१॥**

 *Sloka* 31.—When the Moon in the dark half is occupying the 8th house, the person concerned will be troubled with diseases. Through faults committed with women, he will be reduced to abject poverty.

**नीचाष्टमविधुदाये मरणं व्याध्यादिमाप्नुयात्सततम्।  
तादृशविधौ सपापे निधनं वा जातिविभ्रंशः॥३२॥**

 *Sloka* 32.—When the Moon is in depression or occupying the 8th house and her Dasa is in progress, the native will meet with his end or constantly suffer from diseases. If the Moon in the above condition be also conjoined with a malefic, he will meet with his end or will be expelled from his caste.

**मौढ्यं गते हिमांशौ राज्याच्चैव च्युतिर्मनोदुःखी।  
पाण्ड्वामयादिरोगैर्निपीडितो वारिजं भयं भवति॥३३॥**

 *Sloka* 33.—If the Moon become obscure or eclipsed, the native will have a fall from his position, will be mentally afflicted, suffer from jaundice and similar diseases. There will further be risk from water.

**षष्ठदशा व्यसनकरी क्षीणे नृृणां स्वबन्धुनाशकरी।  
पूर्णे नृणां धनाप्तिं जनयति खलु केवलं नियतम्॥३४॥**

 *Sloka* 34.—When the Moon's Dasa happens to be the sixth in order and she is in the dark half, there will be suffering by the people and destruction of one's relatives When she is in the bright half, there will be acquisition of wealth only.

**उदयगते राज्याप्तिः कर्मगते स्त्रीप्रजार्थसम्पत्तिः।  
एवं चन्द्रदशाफलमंशकचारैस्तथैव वक्तव्यम्॥३५॥**

इति श्रीवराहमिहिरसुत श्रीपृथुयशोविरचिते होरासारे चन्द्रदशाफलाध्यायो

दशमः॥

* Sloka* 35.—When the Moon is in the Lagna and her Dasa is in progress, the native will become the owner of an estate. When she occupies the 10th house, the period will be marked by the acquisition of girls, wealth, etc. Thus will be the effects of the Moon's Dasa. The effects will be similar when the Moon progresses in the several Amsas.

Thus ends the 10th Adhyaya entitled “the Moon’s Dasa and its effects” in the work Horasara, etc.

**\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_**

**एकादशोऽध्यायः**

अथ कुजदशाफलम्

**आदित्यपूर्वषट्कस्था ये ग्रहास्तेऽप्यधोमुखाः।  
अपरस्थाश्च ये भानोरूर्ध्वास्यास्ते सुखप्रदाः॥१॥**

* Sloka* 1.—When planets are posited in the first six signs counted from that of the Sun, they are said to be having the face downwards; while those situated in the other six are declared to be facing upwards and are productive of good.

**वक्रो यदावरोही स्यादारोही चानुवक्रमः।  
वक्रः स्वोच्चफलं दद्याद्दशा तस्य तु मध्यमा॥२॥**

**वक्रानुवक्रानुद्वीक्ष्य दशाफलमुदीरयेत्।  
ताराग्रहाणां सर्वेषामेवं ज्ञात्वा विचक्षणः॥३॥**

* Slokas* 2-3.—Mars whether in **अवरोह** or **आरोह** will give effects as in his exaltation, and his Dasa will be middling. It is only after ascertaining whether a planet is **वक्र** or **अनुवक्र**, an astrologer should predict the effects of his Dasa. The Dasas of all the non-luminary planets should be examined in this way.

**भौमस्य स्वदशाफलानि हुतभुग्भूवाहनाद्यैर्धनं  
भैषज्यानृतवञ्चनैश्च विविधैः क्रौर्यैर्धनस्यागमः।  
पित्तासृग्ज्वरबाधितश्च सततं नीचाङ्गनासेवित्तो  
विद्वेषी सुतदारबन्धुगुरुभिर्नष्टोऽन्यभाग्ये रतः॥४॥**

* Sloka* 4.—When the Dasa of Mars is in progress, one will earn money through fire, lands, carrying loads, medicine, falsehood, deceit, and doing various cruel deeds. He will suffer bilious troubles, bad blood, and fever. He will always be in the company of women of the low class. He will be forsaken by his wife, sons, relations and elders. He will interest himself in the welfare of others.

**मूलत्रिकोणसंस्थस्यारस्य दशा कुलान्वितं जनयेत्।  
सुतदारधनप्राप्तिः साहसकारी रतिप्रियो धीमान्॥५॥**

* Sloka* 5.—During the Dasa of Mars when he is posited in his Moolatrikona, one's mind will become distracted; there will be the acquisition of wife, children and money; he will do daring acts, will be fond of sexual pleasure and intelligent,

**मेषाश्रितभौमदशां प्राप्य नरो ख्यातिमान् महोत्साही।  
पित्तादिचोरबाधा बह्वायासेन सन्तप्तः॥६॥**

* Sloka* 6.—During the advent of the Dasa of Mars when the planet is posited in Mesha, the person born will become famous and very active. He will have bilious troubles, risk from thieves, and suffer from great mental pain.

**वृषभे भौमदशायां स्थितिहीनो रोगशोकसन्तप्तः।  
वाग्व्यसनी नातिसुतः परवित्तरतो न देवगुरुभक्तः॥७॥**

 *Sloka* 7.—When Mars occupies Vrishabha and his Dasa is in progress, the person concerned will be deprived of his position. He will be troubled with diseases and suffer mental anguish. He will be fond of oratory. His issue will be limited. He will live on other people’s bounty. He will have no respect for Gods or elders.

**मिथुने भौमदशायां विदेशवासी च कामसन्तप्तः।  
स्वजनेष्वमितविरोधी बहुव्यथातोऽन्निलाग्निसन्तप्तः॥८॥**

 *Sloka* 8.— If Mars be in Mithuna, the person concerned will in his Dasa be living in foreign places. He will be learned in the arts and scriptures. He will have great hatred towards his relations. He will be troubled with much mental anguish, windy complaints and fever.

**भौमदशायां शशिमे तोयोद्यानाग्निवित्तवान् गुणवान्।  
दारसुतबन्धुहीनो विकलाङ्गो लोकधूर्तः स्यात्॥९॥**

* Sloka* 9.—In the Dasa of Mars when he is posited in the Moon’s Rasi (Kataka), the person will earn money through water-products, maintaining gardens, fire, etc. He will possess amiable qualities. He will be bereft of wife, sons and relations, and will be defective of some limb. He will be clever in cheating other people.

**नीचादूर्ध्वदशायां भौमस्य गुणातिरेकविख्यातः।  
बलवान् प्रधानवैरी गुह्यरुगार्तो गजाश्वसम्पन्नः॥१०॥**

* Sloka* 10.—When Mars is moving upwards from his depression point, the person concerned will become famous for his eminent qualities. He will possess great strength and will be a chief among the opponents. He will suffer from trouble in the anus. He will possess elephants and horses.

**सिंहाश्रितभौमदशा कुरुते जननायकं महोत्साहम्।  
सुतदारवित्तहीनं पुरुषं शस्त्राग्निपीडितं जनयेत्॥११॥**

* Sloka* 11.—During the Dasa of Mars when Mars is occupying Simha the native will become a leader of men and very energetic. He will be devoid of sons, wife and wealth. He will be hit by a weapon and be subjected to risk from fire.

**कन्याश्रितभौमदशां प्राप्य स्थानं धनं सुखं लभते।  
यज्ञक्रियासु निपुणो विषमाक्षो भूमिदारपुत्राप्तः॥१२॥**

* Sloka* 12.—In the Dasa of Mars when Mars occupies sign Kanya, the native will get a status, wealth, and happiness. He will be clever in sacrificial duties. He will have uneven eyes. He will possess lands, wife and children.

**तौलिनि भौमदशायां मेढ्रुजा स्त्रीकृतार्थपरिहीणः।  
परिजनकलहोद्रिक्तो गजाश्वहीनोऽङ्गहीनो वा॥१३॥**

* Sloka* 13.—During the Dasa of Mars when he occupies sign Tula, the person concerned will suffer from ulcer in his generating organ; his wealth will be lost through dissipation; he will have frequent quarrels with the servants, will not possess elephants or horses, or he will be defective of some limb.

**अलिगतभौमदशायां पुरुषः स्यात् सर्वतत्वविद्येशः।  
कृषितो धनधान्याप्तिर्मित्रद्वेषी विषाग्निशस्त्रहतः॥१४॥**

* Sloka* 14.—When Mars occupies Scorpio and his Dasa is in progress, the person becomes versed in philosophy. He will earn money through agriculture and get wealth and corn. He will hate his friends. There will be risk from poison, fire and weapons.

**चापे भौमदशायां द्विजदेवनृपादिभिर्धनं लभते।  
दुःसाध्य कार्यकर्ता कलहप्रायोऽतिमान्यश्च॥१५॥**

* Sloka* 15.—The effects of the Dasa of Mars when Mars is in Dhanus are **:** the person will acquire wealth through Brahmins, Gods kings, etc. He will success- fully finish impossible acts; will promote quarrels. He will command great respect.

**भौमात्युच्चदशायां वाहनसुखराज्यरत्नसम्पन्नः।  
अनिवारितरणवेगः प्रधानजनबन्धुमान् भवति॥१६॥**

* Sloka* 16.—When Mars occupies his highest exaltation and his Dasa is in progress, the person concerned will have vehicular comforts, good status, and get pearls. His eagerness for combat will be uncontrolled. He will become an important personage among his relations.

**अत्युच्चाक्रान्तदशा मकरे भौमस्य यत्नतोऽर्थाप्तिम्।  
व्यालमृगोरगशस्त्रः पीडां कुरुतेऽल्पजातिसन्तोषम्॥१७॥**

* Sloka* 17.—During the Dasa of Mars when he is in his highest exaltation in Makara, the person concerned will be very vigorous in earning money, There will be trouble from reptiles, quadrupeds and weapons. He will help the low people and make them happy.

**कुम्भे भौमदशायामाचारविवर्जितोऽतिमानी स्यात्।  
दारिद्र्यदुःखतप्तो दुर्मार्गरतिर्विनष्टतनयश्च॥१८॥**

 *Sloka* 18.—When Mars occupies Kumbha and his Dasa is in progress, the native will be irreligious in his conduct; he will be very proud, suffer misery through poverty and fall to vicious ways. He will also lose children.

**मीने भौमदशायां रोगी विगतात्मजो व्ययार्तश्च।  
ऋणवान् विदेशवासी विचर्चिकाद्यैर्व्रणैश्च परिभृतः॥१९॥**

 *Sloka* 19.—When Mars is in Meena and his Dasa is in progress, the native will be suffering from diseases, will lose children. The expenditure will be heavy. He will contract debts, live in foreign places and will be afflicted with itches, wounds, etc.

**वर्गोत्तमगस्य दशा भौमस्य करोति लोकविख्यातम्॥  
तद्भावफलं द्विगुणं लभते सङ्ग्रामविश्रुतो बलवान्॥२०॥**

 *Sloka* 20.—When Mars has attained a Vargottamamsa, and when his Dasa is in progress, the person concerned will get wide fame. The effects of the Bhava (occupied by Mars) will become doubled. He will become strong and celebrated in the military.

**नीचांशगभौमदशा सदाटनं वितनुते मनोदुःखम्।  
फलसन्निकर्षनाशं श्रेष्ठं त्यक्त्वाऽधमं भजते॥२१॥**

 *Sloka* 21.—During the Dasa of Mars when he is in a depression Amsa, the native will always be roaming from place to place; he will be mentally unhappy. The fruits of the beneficial effect will be destroyed when they are almost ripe. He will take to the worst leaving the best.

**भौमस्यास्तदशायां सर्वोपद्रवयुता विनाशमतिः।  
क्रमयोगोदयराशिषु राश्युक्तफलानि सिध्यन्ति॥२२॥**

 *Sloka* 22.—During the Dasa of Mars when he is eclipsed, the person concerned will be troubled with all kinds of worries, and his mind will be in a destructive mood. When Mars is in other conditions and in houses rising or bestowing Yogas, the happy effects corresponding to the Rasis concerned will fully materialise.

**अष्टम भौमस्य दशा शत्रुविरोधं मृतिं विवादं वा।  
जनयति च सर्वविघ्नं बन्धुनिमित्तात्स्वमानहानिं वा॥२३॥**

 *Sloka* 23.—When Mars is posited in the 8th house and his Dasa is in progress, the native will have misunderstanding with his enemies, will meet with his end or have unpleasant litigation. litigation. He will encounter obstacles for everything he begins to do for his relations or may even lose his honor.

**ऊर्ध्वास्य तुङ्गभवनस्थित भूमिजस्य  
कर्मायगस्य हि दशा विदधाति राज्यम्।**  
**जित्वा रिपून्विपुलवाहन सैन्ययुक्तां  
राज्यश्रियं वितनुते निधिकृन्न दाता॥२४॥**

इति श्रीवराहमिहिरसुतश्री पृथुयशोविरचिते होरासारे  
कुजदशाफलाध्याय एकादशः॥

* Sloka* 24—When Mars is facing upwards, occupying his exaltation house, is in the 10th or the 11th, house, his Dasa will bestow a kingdom to the native. The native will conquer his enemies, will command many vehicles, a large army and other adjuncts of a kingdom and a good treasury ; he will not however be liberal.

Thus ends the 11th Adhyaya entitled the “effects of the Dasa of Mars”  
in the work Horasara composed by Prithuyasas,  
son of Varahamihira.

**द्वादशोऽध्यायः**

अथ बुधदशाफलम्

**सौम्यदशायां लभते विद्याविनियोग मिश्रबन्धुधनम्।  
कृषियज्ञयाजनाद्यैः स्ववृत्तिकार्यैर्धनं समाप्नोति॥१॥**

 *Sloka* 1.—When the Dasa of Mercury sets in one will be engaged in imparting education, moving with his relatives and acquiring wealth through agriculture, per- forming Sacrifices and other usual duties.  
 **लिपि** is another reading for **कृषि,**

**शिल्पादिकर्मकुशलो गीतज्ञो गेयवाद्यसन्तुष्टः।  
गृहभाजनादियुक्तश्रेङ्गितवेत्ता कुतूहलाभाषी॥२॥**
