 *Sloka* 2.—He will be skilled in the Arts and other crafts, versed in singing and fond of vocal and instrumental music. He will possess all necessary house-hold utensils, clever in understanding others’ minds and a pleasant talker.

**भार्याप्रियो विनीतो विद्वान् गुरुसम्मतोऽल्परोगश्च।  
बन्धुपरिव्राण्मित्रैर्नखायुधैर्वा भवेत्पीडा॥३॥**

 *Sloka* 3.—He will be fond of his wife, will be humble, learned, agreeable to his elders and free from disease. He will be surrounded by his relations and friends. He will have trouble through claws or weapons.

**सुभगो न सञ्चितार्थो मारुतकफपित्तरुग्विकारी स्यात्।  
पीडां कुरुते नित्यं मन उपतापं च कष्टदशाम्॥४॥**

 *Sloka* 4.—He will be amiable, will have no hoarded wealth, will be troubled with windy, phlegmatic and bilious diseases, will be emotional, always distressed in mind and miserable.

**अत ऊर्ध्वं प्रत्येकं राश्यंशदशाफलानि सौम्यस्य।  
वक्ष्यन्तेऽत्र समासात् पूर्वाचार्यैश्च कथितानि॥५॥**

 *Sloka* 5.—Hereafter are described in a succinct manner the effects of the Dasa of Mercury due to his occupying the several Rasis and Amsas as mentioned by the ancient sages.

**मेषगतज्ञदशायां विज्ञानोत्साहसङ्गतो धीमान्।  
शौर्यानृतशाट्यरतो निजधनहीनोऽन्यभाग्यरतः॥६॥**

 *Sloka* 6.—When Mercury is occupying Mesha and when his Dasa is in progress, the person concerned will take delight in teaching others, will be intelligent, power- ful, will utter falsehoods, possess no wealth of his own and will be depending on other's bounty.

**सौम्यदशायां वृषभे मातुरनिष्टो धनान्वितः ख्यातः।  
ऋणवान् बन्धुनिमित्तैः कुदारतनयान्वितो गलार्तिः स्यात्॥७॥**

 *Sloka* 7.—During the Dasa of Mercury posited in Vrishabha, he will displease his mother; he will have money and become famous. He will contract debts for the sake of his relatives; will be cursed with a bad wife, and his sons will be wicked in disposition. He will suffer from disease in the throat.

**मिथुने सौम्यदशायामनेकवित्तान्वितोऽतिभोगी स्यात्।  
नैकसुतदारनाथो द्विमातृको ज्ञातिवल्लभो धीमान्॥८॥**

 *Sloka* 8.—When Mercury occupies Mithuna and his Dasa is in progress, he will be in possession of various kinds of wealth, and enjoyments. He will have wives and children. He will have two mothers, will be a great friend to his paternal relations and intelligent,

**बन्धुजनपीडितात्मा विदेशनिरतोऽल्पसौख्यसम्पन्नः।  
काव्यकलार्जितवित्तश्चन्द्रगृहे बुधदशायां तु॥९॥**

 *Sloka* 9.—With a mind troubled by one's relations, intent in dwelling in foreign countries and with little happiness, the person born spends Mercury’s Dasa through the earnings made with the help of his study of Poetry and Arts, when Mercury is posited in sign Karkataka.

**सिंहाश्रितसौम्यदशा ज्ञानधनैश्वर्य वर्जितं जनयेत्।  
भ्रातृसुखबन्धुहीनः स्त्रीद्वेषी लोकविश्रुतो भवति॥१०॥**

 *Sloka* 10.—When Mercury occupies Simha and his Dasa is in progress, he may lose his brothers; there will be no happiness to him; and all his relations will forsake him. He will hate his wife. He will become celebrated.

**उच्चाश्रितसौम्यदशा ज्ञानधनैश्वर्यसम्पदं कुरुते।  
लिपिलेख्यकाव्यनिरतो नीतिज्ञो निर्जितारिपक्षश्च॥११॥**

 *Sloka* 11.—During the Dasa of Mercury when he is in his exaltation, the person will acquire more knowledge, wealth, etc. He will be engaged in writing works, and become learned, and he will overpower his enemies.

**मूलत्रिकोणभागेषूद्यत्सु दशा बुधस्य विख्यातम्।  
कुरुते विदेशसक्तं स्वगुणबलाभ्यां धनं लभते॥१२॥**

 *Sloka* 12.—When Mercury has attained his Moolatrikona, and his Dasa is in progress, the person concerned becomes famous in a foreign place and he will get wealth through his good qualities and personal exertion.

**क्षेत्रांशकस्थितदशा कन्यायां सोमजस्य विकलाङ्गम्।  
जनयति च बन्धुवैरं सुखपशुधनवर्जितं जनयेत्॥१३॥**

 *Sloka 13.*—In the Dasa of Mercury when he is occupying his own Rasi or Navamsa, the person concerned will lose a limb; there will arise enmity with his relations; and he will be deprived of happiness, cattle and wealth.

**सप्तमराशौ बौध्यां वाग्मी विकलेक्षणो न शान्तमतिः।  
शिल्पादिकर्मकुशलो विपण्यजीवी गजाश्वदुःखकरः॥१४॥**

 *Sloka 14.*—When Mercuty occupies sign Tula and his Dasa is in progress, the person born will become an orator; his eyes will become impaired and he will have no peace. He will become clever in mechanical arts and will be earning by trading in stalls. He will become unhappy through elephants and horses.

**कीटे सौम्यदशायामादानरतोऽल्पसन्तुष्टः।  
प्रेष्याङ्गनानुरक्तो स्वगृहश्रमसंयुतो दरिद्रश्च॥१५॥**

 *Sloka 15*.—In the Dasa of Mercury when he is posited in Vrischika, the native concerned will be eager to receive anything (from others) and will be satisfied with what little he may get. He will be addicted to a servantmaid, will be burdened with the management of his own household and become miserable.

**कार्मुकसंस्थदशायां बुधस्य गणनायकोऽथवा मन्त्री।  
नामद्वयं च लभते कृषिपशुधनधान्यसंयुतो भवति॥१६॥**

 *Sloka 16*.—When Mercury is posited in Dhanus and his Dasa is in progress, the person will become a leader of men or a minister; he will also get a title. He will earn money through lands, cattle and corn.

**सौम्यस्य मृगदशायामृणवान् परकार्यकृत्कुदेशरतः।  
अटनोऽल्पजनस्निग्धो मायामोहेन तापितशरीरः॥१७॥**

 * Sloka 17.—*In the Dasa of Mercury when he is posited in Makara, the person concerned will incur debts, will be intent in attending to other people's work, dwell-ing in other countries, will always be on his legs, attached to low people; and troubled through illusion.

**कुम्भगतज्ञदशायां तेजोहानिर्मिताशनो निःस्वः।  
बन्धुजनपीडितात्मा दुष्टस्त्रीनायको विदेशरतः॥१८॥**

 * Sloka 18.—*When Mercury occupies Kumbha and his Dasa is ripening, the native will suffer loss of energy, will be moderate in his diet and moneyless. He will be worried by his relations, will be cursed with a bad wife and spending his time in foreign places.

**मीनाश्रितसौम्यदशा प्रशस्तवेदार्थशास्त्रपारगतम्।  
धर्मादिचिन्तनपरं प्रधानजनवल्लभं कुरुते॥१९॥**

 *Sloka 19.—*When Mercury is in Meena and his Dasa is in progess, the native will be engaged in the exposition of the Vedas and will be commended by all. His mind will be bent on doing virtuous acts and he will thus become the chief friend of the people.

**नीचगसौम्यदशायामालोलो बन्धुसत्वगुणहीनः।  
कृष्याशनोऽल्पजीवी मृदुरोगसमाश्रितोऽन्यगेहस्थः॥२०॥**

 *Sloka 20.*—When Mercury is in his depression Rasi and his Dasa is operating, the person born will have an agitated mind. He will be without any relatives, will have no vitality. He will live through agriculture, humble in his means, be weak in constitution, and plunged in disease. He will live in others' houses.

**नीचाष्टमगस्य दशा सौम्यस्य विषायुधादिपश्वाद्यैः।  
जनयति पीडां नित्यं कुकर्मनिरतोऽल्पसत्वगुणयुक्तः॥२१॥**

 * Sloka 21.—*Mercury's Dasa when he is occupying his depression sign identical with the 8th house will cause trouble to the native through poison, weapon, beasts etc. He will be bent in doing always vicious acts. His quality of goodness will be nil.

**अस्तगसौम्यदशा तु क्षेत्रत्यागं सदा मनोदुःखम्।  
पाण्ड्वामयकासाद्यैः पीडां कुरुते धनक्षयं चापि॥२२॥**

 *Sloka 22.*—The Dasa of Mercury when he is eclipsed will bring on loss in lands, and perpetual mental affliction. The native will suffer from jaundice, sickness, catarrh; etc. He will also lose money.

**वर्गोत्तमगदशायां सौम्यस्य शुभाशुभानि वर्धन्ते।**  
**उक्तफलाद्वित्रिगुणं सर्वत्र शुभाशुभैश्च मिश्रफलम्॥२३॥**

 *Sloka 23—*During the Dasa of Mercury when he has attained a Vargottamamsa, auspicious occasions will be of frequent occurrence; the effects mentioned above will increase by two or three-folds. Good and bad will always happen in a mixed way and produce mixed effects.

**कर्मायोदयबन्धुषु मिश्रफला सोमजस्य दशा।  
लभते स्वकुलाधिक्यं ज्ञानसुखार्थादिसंयुतं जनयेत्॥२४॥**

**सर्वत्र बुधदशायां मिश्रफलं प्राक्तनैर्विनिर्दिष्टम्।**

**इति श्रीवराहमिहिरसुतश्रीपृथुयशोविरचिते होरासारे बुधदशाफलाध्यायो**  
**द्वादशः॥**

 *Sloka 24, 24½—*When Mercury occupies the 10th, the 11th, the 1st or the 4th house, the effects of Mercury's Dasa will be mixed. The native will become the head of his family, will be endowed with knowledge, happiness, wealth, etc. The effects will always be of a mixed nature ; so say the sages.

Thus ends the 12th Adhyaya entitled "Mercury's Dasa and its effects" in Horasara, a work composed by Sri Prithuyasas, son of Sri Varahamihira.

**———————**

**त्रयोदशोऽध्यायः**

**अथ गुरुदशाफलम्॥**

**जीवस्य दशां प्राप्य प्रशस्तवेदार्थशास्त्रपाठरतः।  
धर्मादिवर्गचिन्ता प्रधानजनवल्लभोऽतिमेधावी॥१॥**

 *Sloka 1.—*When Jupiter's Dasa augurs, the person concerned will engage himself in the commendable act of learning the Vedas and their meaning. His mind will be thinking of the four ends of life, viz., **धर्म, अर्थ, काम** and **मोक्ष**. He will become the favourite of the chief men of the place, and will be very intelligent.

**अध्ययनदेवतार्चागदजययज्ञक्रियदिभिर्वित्तम्।  
जन्मप्रभावतोऽर्थान् नृपप्रसादाद्धनं समाप्नोति॥२॥**

 * Sloka 2.—*In the Dasa of Jupiter, one acquires money through study, worship of Gods, medicine, performance of sacrifices for getting victory, etc. Owing to one's high birth, he also acquires wealth through royal favour.

**अश्वादिवाहनाप्तिं भूम्यम्बरदारपुत्रसम्पन्नः।  
सत्सङ्गतिः कुलाढ्यो बलाढ्यता भूपतित्वं वा॥३॥**

 * Sloka 3.—*He will get horses and other vehicles, will obtain lands, clothes, wife, sons, etc; he will move in high good circles, will be strong and robust in health and may even obtain kingship.

**कार्येषु सूक्ष्मबुद्धिस्त्रिकालविद् ज्ञानकर्मकुशलश्च।  
प्लिहविद्रधिगुल्माद्यैर्निपीडितश्चोर्ध्वरोगी स्यात्॥४॥**

 * Sloka 4.*—He will be keen in all his actions, knowing the past, present and future, and clever in his duties. He will suffer from spleen, abscess, etc. He will further suffer from Urdhva Roga.

**एतानि सर्वराशिषु जीवस्य दशाफलानि निर्दिश्य।  
प्रत्येकं राशिफलं तस्मादूर्ध्वं समादिशेत्तज्ज्ञः॥५॥**

 *Sloka 5.—*All the above have to be mentioned as the effcts of Jupiter's Dasa in all the Rasis generally. Then the astrologer may predict the special effects appro- priate for each of the several signs.

**जीवदशायां मेषे गणनाथो ज्ञानवान् नरेन्द्रधनी।  
दारसुतमित्रभोगैः समन्वितो विगतशोकश्च॥६॥**

 *Soka 6.—*When Jupiter is in Mesha and his Dasa is in progress, the native will become the head of a group of men, will be intelligent, equal to a king and rich. He will have all comforts of a wife, children, friends and enjoyments and will be free from all sorrows.

**वृषभाश्रितजीवदशा प्रवर्तने शत्रुपीडितो दुःखी।  
देशेऽन्यत्र निवासः स्वल्पोत्साहाद्धनं समाप्नोति॥७॥**

 * Sloka 7.—*When Jupiter is in Vrishabha and his Dasa is commeneing, the person will be troubled by enemies and will be unhappy. He will live in a foreign place and earn money with a very small effort.

**मिथुने जीवदशायां स्त्रीद्वेषी वित्तवान् कृषिप्रायः।  
कुलजगुणप्रद्वेषी मातुरनिष्टोऽङ्गहीनो वा॥८॥**

* Sloka 8.—*During the Dasa of Jupiter posited in Mithuna, the person will hate women, command money, his occupation being mostly through agriculture. He will have an aversion to his own relations. He will hate his mother, or suffer loss of some limb.

**उच्चाश्रितदेवगुरोर्दशाविपाके स्वजन्मवृत्तिकरः।  
राज्यसुखभोगवृद्धिर्विशुद्धनामान्वितो धनी विद्वान्॥९॥**

 *Sloka 9.—*When Jupiter occupies his exaltation and his Dasa is in progress, the person concerned will pursue his usual occupation and his enjoyments will increase. He will be spotless in character, wealthy and learned.

**उच्चातिक्रान्तदशा जीवस्य सदाटनं कुदाररतम्।  
पितृमातृदुःखतप्तं पूर्वार्जितवित्तविक्रयं कुरुते॥१०॥**

 *Sloka 10.—*In the Dasa of Jupiter when Jupiter has passed his exaltation, the native will always be roaming about; he will have a bad wife. His parents will be in a sorrowful plight and he will be mentally afflicted thereby.

**सिंहे जीवदशायां धर्माध्यक्षो नृपाच्च सम्पत्तिम्।  
लभते गुणातिरेकात्पशुसुतदारादिवित्तवान् भवति॥११॥**

 *Sloka 11.—*When Jupiter occupies Simha and his Dasa is in progress, the native will be a judge, will get wealth from the sovereign for his eminent qualities. He will be endowed with cattle, wife, wealth, etc.

**कन्याश्रितजीवदशा नृपदारसमाश्रयाद्धनं कुरुते।  
शूद्रादिनीचकलहप्रवर्तते स्थानसम्भ्रमं कुरुते॥१२॥**

**पशुजां वृद्धिं वित्तं विद्याम्बरवाहनावाप्तिम्॥१३॥**

 *Slokas 12-13—*When Jupiter is occupying Kanya and his Dasa is progressing, the person gets money through the sovereign, and his wife. He will promote quarrel with Sudras and other low people. He will be moving about from place to place. By rearing cattle, he will increase his wealth and learning and also obtain cloths and vehicles.

 ** नृपपूजां दारसङ्ग्रहं कुरुते** is another reading in Sloka 12.

**तौलिनि जीवदशायां मन्दोत्साही स्वदारपुत्रघ्नः।  
दुष्टव्रणाप्तदेहो दिवसे दिवसे मिताशनो भवति॥१४॥**

 * Sloka 14.—*If Jupiter be in Tula and his Dasa is commencing, the native's vigour will get slackened; het will kill his wife and sons; he will suffer from a bad ulcer, and day by day, his meal will get reduced.

**अष्टमजीवदशायां सुरकार्यरतोऽटनो महोत्साही।  
ऋणवाननेकभावैः प्रजानुरक्तो नियमशीलः॥१५॥**

 * Sloka 15.—*When Jupiter is in the 8th Rasi and his Dasa has set in, the person concerned will be engaged in the work of the Gods, always roaming, and very vigorous and busy. He will incur debts in various ways; he will be much attached to the people and will be of good disposition

**मूलत्रिकोणसंस्थितगुरोर्दशायां जनाधिको धीमान्।  
मन्त्री मण्डलपो वा प्रमदावशगो धनी सुखी भवति॥१६॥**

 *Sloka 16.—*If Jupiter occupy his Moolatrlkona Rasi and his Dasa begins, the person will become an important personage, intelligent, a minister or a King himself. He will come under the influence of young women, be wealthy and happy.

**चापगतस्य दशायां गुरोः प्रवासाद्धनं सुखं लभते।  
यज्ञक्रियासु निरतो गोमान् कृषिवित्तसङ्ग्रहं कुरुते॥१७॥**

 *Sloka 17.—*When Jupiter is in Dhanus and his Dasa is beginning, the person feels happy by short sojourns and also gets money. He will engage himself in a sacrificial duty. He will possess cattle, and earn wealth through agriculture.

**नीचे जीवदशायां प्रवर्तते बन्धुशोकसन्तापी।  
परकार्यकृद्दरिद्रो जठरामयकर्णगुह्यरोगी स्यात्॥१८॥**

 *Sloka 18.*—When Jupiter is in depression and his Dasa is in progress, he will begin to cause trouble and sorrow to his relatives; he will be doing work for others, will be poor and miserable, suffer stomach ache, eardisease and disease in the private parts.

**मृगमुखजीवदशायां वनवासनिषादधनलाभौ।  
कृष्याश्रयोपजीवी भूरुहजलवञ्चनादिभिः क्लेशः॥१९॥**

 *Sloka 19*.—When Jupiter is occupying sign Makara and his Dasa is in progress, the person concerned betakes himself to dwell in forest-tracts and gets money through hunters ; he will live by agriculture. He will be afflicted. being duped by Brahmins, tricks in water, etc.

**कुम्भाश्रितदेवगुरोर्दशाविपाके स्वनामशौर्यधनम्।  
पिशुनोऽल्पकर्मजीवी स्वजनद्वेषोऽर्थनाशः स्यात्॥२०॥**

 *Sloka 20.*—During the Dasa of Jupiter who is posited in Kumbha, one gets wealth by the use of his name and bodily prowess. He will be a slanderer, earn his livelihood by doing vile acts and hate his own people. He will waste his money.

**मीनाश्रितदेवगुरोर्दशाविपाके कुलाधिको धीमान्।  
विद्याकथाप्रभेदैर्धनवान् प्रमदाप्रियो विनीतश्च॥२१॥**

 *Sloka. 21.*—When Jupiter occupies Meena and his Dasa is in progress, the person will become a chief in the family, be intelligent, will earn money through imparting learning, story telling, etc. He will be liked by young women and he will be modest.

**वर्गोत्तमगदशायां देवाचार्यस्य पूजितो लोके।  
बहुलं धनं च लभते सुतदारमाश्रयी कृशाङ्गः स्यात्॥२२॥**

 *Sloka 22.—*During the Dasa of Jupiter when he has attained a Vargottamamsa, the person concerned will be honoured by the people; he will also get much wealth; he will live in the company of his wife and children. He will become emaciated.

**मूढस्य देवेन्द्रगुरोर्दशायां प्रवर्तते दुःखसुखं च तुल्यम्।  
नीचारिभेष्वात्मजदारवित्तनाशाश्च रोगा बहवो भवेयुः॥२३॥**

**इति श्रीवराहमिहिरसुत श्रीपृथुयशोविरचिते होरासारे गुरुदशाफलाध्यायो**  
**त्रयोदशः॥**

 *Sloka 23.—*When Jupiter is eclipsed and when his Dasa is in progress, the person concerned will have misery and happiness in equal proportion. When Jupiter occupies his depression or inimical sign, he will lose children, wife and wealth. He will also suffer from many ailments.

Thus ends the 13th Adhyaya in Horasara, a work composed by  
Sri: Prithuyasas, the son of Sri: Varahamihira.

**——————**

**चतुर्दशोऽध्यायः**

**॥अथ शुक्रदशाफलम्॥**

**सामान्यसर्वराशिषु शुक्रस्य दशाफलं समाचक्षे।  
स्त्रीभूषणाम्बरसुखप्रमोदसत्कारमानधनलाभः॥१॥**

 *Sloks 1.—*I am describing the effects of the Dasa of Venus when he is generally occupying any one of the several Rasis. In these periods, the person concerned will obtain women, ornaments, clothing and similar things promoting to his happiness, respect, honor and wealth.

**कन्दर्पशास्त्रनिपुणो नानाविद्याश्रितोऽतिमेधावी।  
नृत्तादिगीतकुशलो दाक्षिण्याप्तोऽन्नदानशीलश्च॥२॥**

 * Sloka 2—*He will become an adept in the Sexual science, study various Arts and become very intelligent. He will be clever in dancing and music. He will be courteous and of a disposition to feed others.

**क्रयविक्रयेषु कुशलो गोमान् बहुदारवान् सुतार्थयुतः।  
पूर्वार्जितधनभोक्ता गुणविख्यातः क्रियोद्युक्तः॥३॥**

 *Sloka 3.—*He will be clever in buying things and selling them. He will possess cows and other cattle. He will have many wives and children and will be rich. He will enjoy ancestral wealth, and be noted for his good. qualities. He will be engaged in his work.

**वातकफपित्तरोगी भ्रातृसुतस्नेहतो महादुःखी।  
नीचैर्वैरं लभते कष्टमथो धर्मवैरिभिः प्रीतिः॥४॥**

 *Sloka 4.—*He will suffer from windy, phlegmatic and bilious complaints, will be greatly afflicted and troubled through his association with his brother's son. He will have misunderstandings with low people; and it is a great pity that his friends are only those that deviate from the righteous path.

**राशीनां प्रत्येकं शुक्रस्य दशाफलानि वक्ष्यन्ते।  
रिपुनीचांशकराशीन् निश्चित्य सत्फलं ब्रूयात्॥५॥**

 *Sloka 5.*—The effects of the Dasa of Venus when he occupies each of the several Rasis will be now described separatety. The good effects should be predicted only. after examining whether the Rasi and Navamsa occupied by Venus are not inimical or depression ones.

**शुक्रदशायां मेषे स्त्रीकृतसुखवित्तमानहानिः स्यात्।  
अटनोऽसहोऽल्पजीवी प्रभुशीलो राजयोषितो दयितः॥६॥**

 * Sloka 6*—When Venus is in Mesha and his Dasa is in progress, the person concerned will enjoy happiness through women. He will suffer loss of honor. He will be roaming about and will not be capable of endurance. He will lead a low and humble life. He will be of a lordly disposition. He will become the favourite of a princess.

**वृषभे शुक्रदशायां कृषिपशुदारान्वितो मतिमान्।  
बहुशास्त्रवित्सुदान्तः कन्याजनको नरेन्द्रदयितश्च॥७॥**

 *Sloko 7.*—If Venus be in Vrishabha and his Dasa sets in, the person concerned will be engaged in agriculture, will possess wife, and cattle and be intelligent. He will know many sciences, will be a Buddhist, father of daughters, and a favourite of the King.

**मिथुने शुक्रदशायामनेककार्यान्वितो महोत्साही।  
विस्मयकथाभिलाषी विदेशनिरतोऽर्थवान् भवति॥८॥**

 *Sloka 8.—*When Venus occupies Mithuna and his Dasa is in progress, the native will be engaged in many activities and will be very energetic. He will be fond of amazing anecdotes. He will be in foreign places and will be wealthy.

**चन्द्रगृहस्थस्य भृगोर्दशा विपाके स्वकार्य उद्युक्तः।  
द्विस्त्रीभरणसुशीलो बहुप्रकारैर्हि जीवनं कुरुते॥९॥**

 *Sloka 9.*—During the Dasa of Venus when he is in Karkataka, the person will be busy with his own duties; he will possess two wives, be of a good disposition, and he will make his living by various means.

**सिंहे शुक्रदशायां प्रवरस्त्रीसंश्रयाद्धनानि स्युः।  
परवित्तरतो धीमानल्पसुतो गोगणा विनश्यन्ति॥१०॥**

 * Sloka 10.—*During the Dasa of Venus when he is in Simha, there will be influx of wealth by the person's contact with a distinguished lady. He will be keen in getting other's wealth ; he will be intelligent. He will not have many children; and any herd of cattle he might own will perish.

**कन्याश्रितशुक्रदशाप्रवर्तने पूर्ववृत्तसुखहीनः।  
भग्नोत्साही चपलो विदेशवासी स्वदारसन्त्यक्तः॥११॥**

 *Sloka 11.*—When Venus occupies Kanya and his Dasa is commencing, the person will abandon his previous professson ; he will be bereft of happiness. His enthusiasm will be curbed, He will be fickle-minded, live in a foreign place being abandoned by his wife.

**वर्गोत्तमभृगुजदशापाके नृपचोरतोऽर्थहानिः स्यात्।  
अस्वस्थो बलहीनो भिक्षाशनवान् सदाटनो भवति॥१२॥**

 * Sloka 12.—*During the Dasa of Venus who has attained a Vargottama Navamsa, the person will incur loss of money through the sovereign or by theft. He will not keep good health and will be weak. He will always be roaming about and obtain his food by begging.

**मूलत्रिकोणसंस्थितभृगोर्दशायां विशिष्टनामयुतः।  
कृषिपशुधनधान्याद्यैः सम्पन्नो ज्ञानिनो धनाप्तिर्वा॥१३॥**

 *Sloka 13.—*When Venus is occupying his Moolatrikona Rasi and his Dasa is in progress, the person concerned will get a new title. He will command all agricultural products, cattle, wealth and corn or money from the wise.

**अटनो बहुप्रलापी परकर्मरतो निमित्तकलहाढ्यः।  
बहुऋणभागी पुरुषो वृश्चिकराशौ भृगोर्दशायां च॥१४॥**

 *Sloka 14.*—When Venus occupies Vrischika and his Dasa is in progress, the person will be wandering from place to place, prattling too much, intent on other people's work, promoting quarrels on some pretext or other and he will contract many debts.

**चापे शुक्रदशायां विनाशितारिः कुलाधिको मानी।  
काव्यकलास्वतिनिपुणो नृपदयितो दारपुत्रसन्तुष्टः॥१५॥**

 *Sloka 15.*—When Venus is in Dhanus and his Dasa is commencing, the person concerned will destroy his enemies; he will become the chief of his family and be respected. He will become very proficient in Poetry and the Arts, become the favourite of the king, and happy with his wife and chi dren.

**मकरे शुक्रदशायां क्लेशसहिष्णुः सुखी रिपुनिहन्ता।  
वातश्लेष्मप्रकृतिः कुत्सितदारो विदर्हितकुटुम्बः॥१६॥**

 *Sloka 16.*—In the Dasa of Venus when he occupies Makara, the native has to endure sorrows. He will vanquish his enemies and feel happy. He will be windy and phlegmatic in temperament, pessess a bad wife and his family will be a condenined one.

**कुम्भे शुक्रदशायामुद्वेगी रोगवान्नयज्ञश्च।  
परयुवतिगो व्रतघ्ने नीचाचारोऽल्पकर्मनिरतश्च॥१७॥**

 * Sloka 17*.—In the Dasa of Venus when he is posited in Kumbha, the person will be distressed in mind and suffer ill-health; he will be prudent. He will go to other females, will be irreligious, of a despicable conduct and engaged in vile pursuits.

**मीने शुक्रदशायां वंशधरो ज्ञानवान्नरेन्द्रधनी।  
कृषितो धनभागी स्यात् कमनीयवपुः प्रधानतां याति॥१८॥**

 *Sloka 18.*—During the Dasa of Venus when he is occupying Meena, he will become the chief of his family, possess great wisdom and become rich through royal favour. He will get money through agriculture, possess a handsome body, and will come to prominence.

**मीने वर्गोत्तमगे भृगोर्दशायां स्वमानगुणयुक्तः।  
रोगैर्निपीडितात्मा जलप्रतिष्ठादियत्नतो धर्मः॥१९॥**

 *Sloka 19.*—When Venus has attained a Vargottama Navamsa in sign Meena and his Dasa is in progress, the person concerned will possess good qualities and be respected. He will suffer diseases. He will undertake some irrigation work for the use of the public.

**स्वोच्चस्थितो भृगुसुतो व्ययकर्मगो वा  
 लाभेऽपि पापरहितो न तु पापदृष्टः।  
तस्याब्दपाकसमये बहुरत्नपूर्णो  
 धीमान् विशालनयनो निजवंशनाथः॥२०॥**

**इति श्रीवराहमिहिरसुतश्रीपृथुयशोविरचिते होरासारे शुक्रदशाफलाध्यायश्चतुर्दशः॥**

 * Sloka 20*.—When Venus is in his exaltation, the 10th, 11th or the 12th house without the conjunction or aspect of malefics and when his Dasa is progressing, the person will obtain many jewels, the pearls, etc. He will be endowed with a mighty intellect, broad outlook and will become the head of his famlly.

Thus ends the 14th Adhyaya in Horasara, a work composed by Sri Prithuyasas, the son of Sri: Varahamihira.

**———————**

**पञ्चदशोऽध्यायः**

**अथ शनिदशाफलम्**

**मन्दस्य दशां प्राप्य प्रथितो धीमाननेकशास्त्रज्ञः।  
वृन्दग्रामपुराणां नेता पितृतोऽधिको विधिज्ञश्च॥१॥**

** ** *Sloka 1.*—During the advent of Saturn's Dasa, one attains fame and becomes intelligent. He will study several Sastras. He will become the leader of a group, head of a village or town, attain to a greater position than that of his father. He will have studied all the rituals.

**गजतुरगगोधनाद्यैः सम्पन्नो ज्ञातितो धनप्राप्तिः।  
द्विजदेवपूजितात्मा पुराणभवनाश्रितोऽल्पसन्तुष्टः॥२॥**

* Sloka 2.*—He will have at his command elephants, horses, cows, etc. He will get money from his Dayadas. He will worship Brahmins and Gods: He will live in a house built very long before. He will be content with whatever little he gets.

**निद्रालस्यश्रमवान् स्वजनद्वेष्यो जराङ्गनासक्तः।  
धर्मप्रियो विनीतो देवायतनक्रियार्चनादिरतः॥३॥**

 *Sloka 3.*—He will be drowsy and weary, hated by his own people and addicted to old women. He will be a friend of the virtuous, humble in disposition, and engaged in works relating to Gods, temples, etc.

**वातकफाद्यैः पीडा विकलाङ्गो जायते कृशाङ्गो वा।  
सामान्यमेतदुक्तं राशौ प्रत्येकमंशकैर्वक्ष्ये॥४॥**

 * Sloka 4.*—He will suffer from windy and phlegmatic complaints, will be defective of some limb or lean in body. The above description is only too general. I shall give below the effects in each Rasi by the Navamsas.

**मन्ददशायां मेषे प्रवासनिरतोऽस्वतन्त्रवृत्तिश्च।  
पादादिचर्मरोगी मायावी भ्रातृबन्धुरहितश्च॥५॥**

 *Sloka 5*.—When Saturn is in Mesha and his Dasa is in progress, he will be absent and working under others. He will suffer from skin-disease from head to foot. He is deceitful in nature and is bereft of brothers or other near relations.

**कृषिधान्याप्तिर्नीचाद्भ्रष्ठस्य शनेर्दशासमये।  
पतनाद्यैः क्लेशाढ्यो नीचप्रायो निरुत्साहः॥६॥**

 *Sloka 6*.—When Saturn has left his depression and his Dasa is in progress, one gets corn and other agricultural products. He will suffer intense grief through falls, etc. He will be almost insignificant and without energy.

**वृषभे सौरिदशायां विशिष्टनामान्वितोऽतिमेधावी।  
राजा राजसमो वा युद्धेषु कृतश्रमोऽतिधर्मरतः॥७॥**

* Sloka 7*.—If Saturn be in Vrishabha and his Dasa be in progress, the person concerned gets a good title and becomes very intelligent. He will be a king or equal to a king for having rendered a great service in war and is keenly intent in doing virtuous deeds.

**मिथुने क्षमाविहीनो मन्ददशायां सुतार्थभोगरतः।  
स्त्रीचोरतोऽर्थहानिः परकार्यरतो रणार्दितो मनुजः॥८॥**

 * Sloka 8.*—During the Dasa of Saturn when he occupies sign Mithuna, the person born will be relentless. He will be with his children commanding all kinds of wealth, comfort and enjoyment. He will lose money through women and through theft. He will be intent in attending to other's work and distressed in war.

**मन्ददशायां शशिभे चिन्तायुक्तोऽस्वतन्त्रश्च।  
मातृसुतबन्धुहीनो नेत्रश्रवणादिदुर्बलो धीमान्॥९॥**

 *Sloka 9.*—When Saturn occupies Karkataka and his Dasa is in progress, the native will feel despondent and be depending on others. He will be bereft of his mother, sons and relations; his eyes and ears will become weak, but he will be intelllgent.

**सिंहे सिंहांशे वा मन्ददशायामनेकरोगयुतः।  
सुतदारबन्धुकलहो गोमहिषाश्वादिवित्तवान् भवति॥१०॥**

 *Sloka 10*.—When Saturn occupies the sign or Navamsa of Simha, and his Dasa is in progress, the person will suffer many ailments. Quarrels will arise with his wife, sons and relatives. He will command the comforts of possessing cows, buffaloes, horses etc, and will be wealthy.

**कन्याश्रितमन्ददशा ददाति विद्याधनं श्रमोत्पत्तिम्।  
भूरुह्वजलप्रमाथी गुरुद्विजाचार्ययोगिनां दयितः॥११॥**

 *Sloka 11.*—During the Dasa of Saturn when he occupies sign Kanya, the person will acquire learning, and will get money after great effort; he will not have any regard for Brahmins, nor care for any floods. He will be liked by his elders, Brahmins, preceptors and ascetics.

**उच्चाश्रितमन्ददशा ज्ञानधनैश्वर्यसम्पन्नम्।  
जनयति लोके श्रुतवान् स्वभावतोऽर्थागमं सुखं लभते॥१२॥**

 *Sloka 12.*—When Saturn is in his exaltation and his Dasa is in progress, the person concerned will be endowed with knowledge, wealth and power. He will be regarded by people as a great learned person, and he will earn money without much exertion.

**मन्ददशायां कीटे वधबन्धरतो वृथाटनोऽनृतवान्।  
कृपणो दयाविहीनो नीचजनानुग्रहोपजीवी स्यात्॥१३॥**

 *Sloka 13*.—When Saturn is posited in Vrischika and his Dasa sets in, the person concerned will engage himself in killing or capturing (animals). He will be wandering without any definite purpose. He will speak falsehood; he will be miserly, and merciless. He will find favour with low people and be depending on others.

**चापे मन्ददशायां स्वस्थो नृपसम्मतो नृपेन्द्रो वा।  
जीवधनादिप्राप्तिः सुतदारसमन्वितो रणोत्साही॥१४॥**

** ***Sloka 14.*—During the Dasa of Saturn when he is posited in Dhanus, the person will be independent, honoured by the king himself, get live-stock, and be in the midst of his sons and wife. He will be very active and persevering.

**मकरे मन्ददशायां बहुश्रमोत्पन्नवित्तवान् सुभगः।  
वन्ध्याजराङ्गनानां दयितो विश्वासतोऽर्थहानिः स्यात्॥१५॥**

 *Sloka 15.*—When Saturn occupies sign Makara and his Dasa is in progress, the native will do acts involving great exertion, command wealth and he will be prosperous. He will associate with barren females or old women and by thus doing lose much of his wealth.

**मूलत्रिकोणसंस्थितशनेर्दशायां सुखानि सिध्यन्ति।  
स्वकुलश्रेष्ठो मतिमान् कृषिपशुधनधान्यपुत्रवान् भवति॥१६॥**

 *Sloka 16.*—When Saturn occupies his Moolatrikona Rasi and his Dasa is in progress, the person enjoys many comforts; he will become the head of his family, intelligent, have success in agriculture and he will be endowed with cattle, corn, sons, etc.

**मीने मन्ददशायामल्पोत्साहाद्धनानि सिध्यन्ति।  
श्रेणीग्रामपुराणामीशो वनितादृतोऽपि मोक्षार्थी॥१७॥**

 *Sloka 17.*—When Saturn occupies Meena and his Dasa is in progress, the person born is able to earn money with a small exertion. He will be the head of a row of houses in a village. Though yearning for a damsel, he still longs for final emancipation.

**आयव्ययतुल्यधनो मूढदशायां शनेरसन्तोषः।  
क्षणभङ्गुरातिकीर्तिर्विविधैः क्लेशैश्च पीडितो भवति॥१८॥**

 *Sloka 18*.—In Saturn's Dasa, when Saturn is eclipsed, the person's income and expenditure will balance each other; he will not feel happy. He has a frail body; but his fame is very wide. He will be tormented by various mental cares.

**राश्यंशकफलमेवं प्रोक्तं बलवत्तरं तयोः कथितम्।  
राश्यंशकवलसाम्यं समानरूपं वदेत्प्राज्ञः॥१९॥**

 *Sloka 19.—*Thus have been declared the effects of Saturn's Dasa due to his occupation of a Rasi or an Amsa whichever is stronger. If they be equal in strength, a clever astrologer should declare effects after a suitable modification.

**एवं ग्रहाणां विविधैः प्रकारैर्दशाफलान्यत्र मयेरितानि।  
ज्ञात्वा नराणां प्रकृतिं समग्रां समादिशेत्तत्र समानरूपम्॥२०॥**

**इति श्रीवराहमिहिरसुत श्रीपृथुयशोविरचिते होरासारे शनिदशाफलाध्यायः पञ्चदशः॥**

 *Sloka 20.*—Thus have been described by me in various ways the effects of the Dasas of planets. After thoroughly understanding the nature of the persons, the astrologer should foretell the events suitably.

Thus ends the 15th Adhyaya entitled "Saturn's Dasa and his effects" in the work Horasara, a work composed by Sri Prithuyasas, the son of Sri; Varahamihira.

**————————**

**षोडशोऽध्यायः**

**॥अथ सङ्कीर्णदशाफलम्॥**

**अथ सङ्कीर्णदशायां स्थानसुखार्था भवन्ति बलहीनाः।  
परगृहनिवासशीलो लोके मान्योऽतिविद्वांश्च॥१॥**

 *Sloka 1.*—In the case of a Dasa of miscellaneous nature, the position (dignity?), happiness and wealth will only be weak and not strong. He will however adapt himself to live under the protection of others, command respect paid by people and will be highly learned.

**अनुवक्रस्य दशायां स्वमानशौर्यान्वितो धनी भवति।  
शस्तगृहे शस्तांशे रिःफाष्टमवर्जिते स्वराज्याप्तिः॥२॥**

 *Sloka 2.*—During the Dasa of a planet who is retrograde, one will have honor, combined with valour and will be moneyed. In the Dasa of a planet occupying an auspicious Rasi and Navamsa and free from quincunx position one will get a kingdom.

**नीचारिभवनसंस्थितवक्रदशायां कुकर्मरतः।  
बन्धुजनगर्हितात्मा विदेशनिरतोऽस्वतन्त्रश्च॥३॥**

 *Sloka 3.*—When a planet occupies his depression or inimical house and is also retrograde in motion, the person concerned will be engaged in doing vile acts. He will be reviled by his relations. He will dwell in a foreign place and be a servant under another.

**राहोर्दशान्तरस्थग्रहयोर्मध्ये द्विवर्षमतिदुःखम्।  
बन्धुविनाशं रोगं लभते शत्रोर्दशान्तरदशायाम्॥४॥**

 *Sloka 4.*—During one's Bhukti and another's Antara in Rahu's Dasa when Rahu is between two planets, the person will endure acute misery for a period of two years. He will lose relations, suffer disease when the Dasa and Antara Dasa of two inimical planets are operating.

**राहुयुतग्रहपाकः शुभदोऽप्यशुभेन तुल्यफलपाकः।  
पाकस्यान्ते व्याधिं दुःखं वा भ्रंशमावहति॥५॥**

 *Sloka 5.*—The Dasa of a planet conjoined with Rahu though otherwise auspicious will yield quite inauspicious results. At the close of the period, there will be disease, misery or a fall in one's position.

**होराजन्माधिपयोः शत्रुदशायां परिभ्रमं लभते।  
राज्यच्युतो विपक्षैरभिभूतोऽरिं समाश्रयति॥६॥**

 *Sloka 6*.—During the Dasa of a planet that is inimical to the lords of the Lagna and the sign occupied by the Moon, one will be rambling about, suffer degradation from his place and insult from his enemy by seeking refuge under him.

**नीचारिषष्ठव्ययसंश्रिता हि शुभाः प्रयच्छन्त्यशुभानि सर्वे।  
शुभेतरे तेषु गताः प्रयच्छन्त्यनेकदुःखानि दशासु तेषाम्॥७॥**

 *Sloka 7*.—Planets that are in depression or inimical Rasis or are placed in the 6th and 12th houses, though otherwise auspicious, prove inauspicious during their Dasas. Planets occupying untoward houses produce various miseries during their Dasa periods

**रोगं ददाति भृगुजः स्वगृहेऽष्टमस्थः  
 पापान्वितो मरणकृत् स्वदशावसाने।  
लग्नेश्वरोऽष्टमगतोऽप्युशुभेन सार्द्धं  
 तस्यान्तरान्तरदशा मरणं करोति॥८॥**

 * Sloka 8*.—When Venus occupies his own Rasi synchronous with the 8th house, he brings on disease to the native; and should he be also conjoined with a malefic, causes death at the close of the Dasa. If he be the lord of the Lagna and occupy the 8th house, and that too in conjunction with a malefic, his Dasa or Antardasa will bring about the death of the native.

**निधनाधिपतेः केन्द्रे स्थितस्य शुभदा दशा यदाऽस्तमितः।  
केन्द्रे राहुयुतो वा स तस्य काले मृतिं वदेत् प्राज्ञः॥९॥**

 *Sloka 9*.—When the lord of the 8th house occupies a Kendra, his Dasa period will, if he should be eclipsed or conjoined with Rahu, bring about the death of the native.

**निधनाधिपतेः केन्द्रे संस्थितस्य शुभा दशा।  
स एवार्कगतः केन्द्रे सराहुश्चेन्मृतिर्भवेत्॥**

**The above is another reading.**

**लग्नेश्वरोऽष्टमस्थो वा यदि तस्य दशान्तरे।  
प्राणसन्देहमाप्नोति दशान्ते जीवितं त्यजेत्॥१०॥**

 *Sloka 10*.—If the lord of the Lagna or the planet in the 8th house prove dangerous to the life of the native, he will die at the close of the Dasa.

**क्षेत्रोच्चसंस्थिता यस्य ये ग्रहाः केन्द्रलाभगाः।  
कारकाख्यग्रहा ज्ञेयाः खमध्यस्थो विशेषतः॥११॥**

 *Sloka 11.*—Planets occupying their own signs, their exaltation signs, if they should also be in a Kendra or the 11th house with respect to any planet, they become Karakas of the planet. That planet which occupies the 10th house of the said planet becomes a special agent.

**कर्मेशः केन्द्रगो वाऽपि कश्चित्कारकसञ्ज्ञितः।  
कर्मभाग्याधिपौ केन्द्रे स्थितौ यस्य शुभप्रदौ॥१२॥**

 *Sloka 12*.—Or, if any planet owning the 10th house occupy a Kendra position, he becomes the Karaka of the original planet. If the lords of the 10th and 9th houses occupy Kendra positions, they become Karakas and do good.

**कारकग्रहयुक्तौ चेत् स्वकुलश्रेष्ठतां व्रजेत्।  
तद्दशायां न सन्देहः स्वाभीष्टफलमाप्नुयात्॥१३॥**

 *Sloka 13.*—If there be two such Karakagrahas in any nativity, the person concerned will become an important member in the family. In the Dasa of such a planet, the person will surely have all his ambitions fulfilled.

**चन्द्राधिष्ठितराशेर्नाथो लग्नाधिपोऽथवा यस्य।  
केन्द्रगतः स सुरेड्यो वयसो मध्ये सुखं तस्य॥१४॥**

 *Sloka 14.*—If the lord of the sign occupied by the Moon or of the Lagna occupy a Kendra along with Jupiter, the native will enjoy happiness in the middle portion of the planet's Dasa.

**पापग्रहांशकदशा बाल्ये ज्ञानक्रियासु विघ्नकरी।  
मूढग्रहांशकदशा तथैव वाच्या न सन्देहः॥१५॥**

*** **Sloka 15.*—In the Dasa of a planet occupying a Navamsa of a malefic planet, obstacles for the native's learning will arise in one's boyhood. The same remark undoubtedly apply during his Dasa period, if the planet occupy a Navamsa of an eclipsed planet.

**स्वोच्चस्वक्षेत्रगतैर्बलिभिः केन्द्राश्रितैः कुजाद्यैश्च।  
रुचको भद्रो हंसो मालव्यः शश इति ख्यातः॥१६॥**

 *Sloka 16.*—When planets occupy their exaltation signs, or their own Rasis, possess strength and at the same time are in Kendra positions, five kinds of great men are ushered into the world who become widely known. According as Mars, Mercury, Jupiter, Venus and Saturn are placed in such a position, the Yogas are termed Ruchaka, Bhadra, Hamsa, Malavya and Sasa.

**योगा अमी न युक्ता यद्यन्यग्रहभवैर्बहुलयोगैः।  
उत्तमकुलजातानां नॄणां सम्यक् पृथक् फलं दद्युः॥१७॥**

 *Sloka 17.*—When these Yogas are not considered along with the Yogas caused by the other planets, they give their effects fully and separately to the several men born of high families.

**नित्यं धनैश्वर्ययुताः प्रसिद्धास्तेजस्विनः पुण्ययुता नरेन्द्राः।  
गजाश्वभाजो बहुरत्नपूर्णा दीर्घायुषस्ते पुरुषा भवन्ति॥१८॥**

 *Sloka 18.*—These men always command riches; they are of world-wide fame, are very powerful, coupled with moral merit, endowed with elephants, horses and various precious jewels; they are long-lived.

**बलरहितेन्दुरविभ्यां युक्तैर्भौमादिभिर्ग्रहैः पुरुषाः।  
न भवन्ति भूमिपाला दशासु तेषां सुतार्थसंयुक्ताः॥१९॥**

 *Sloka 19.—*These men with the five planets beginning with Mars, and with the two luminaries weak, do not become kings during their Dasas, but are only blessed with children and wealth.

**उत्तमयोगे जाता ये तेषां जीवनं सुखार्थयुतम्।  
विपरीते विपरीतं त्वित्याह ब्रह्मशौण्डाख्यः॥२०॥**

 *Sloka 20.*—People born in good Yogas live with all comfort and command all kinds of riches. When the yogas are adverse, they become likewise miserable. So says Brahma Sounda.

**तुङ्गाद्भ्रष्ठस्य दशा सर्वारम्भेषु निष्फलं कुरुते।  
होराधिपारिभवने भ्रष्ठदशा मृत्युमावहति॥२१॥**

 *Sloka 21*.—The Dasa of a planet fallen from his exaltation makes all enterprises begun under it fruitless. The Dasa of the planet owning the 6th (or the 8th) house reckoned from the lord of Lagna will indicate death if the said planet has fallen from exaltation.

 In the 2nd line होराधिपाष्टभवने is another reading.

**षष्ठाष्टमस्थोऽशुभदस्तु रौद्रो द्विषा शुभस्थानगतेन दृष्टः।  
स्वस्यां दशायां स करोति मृत्युं व्याध्यध्वतापादिपरिक्षयं वा॥२२॥**

 *Sloka 22*.—When an inauspicious planet occupies the 6th or the 8th house, or is aspected by an inimical planet posited in a benefic house he will bring about in his Dasa period the demise of the native through disease, or weariness in travelling, etc.

**व्योमाम्बुवाय्वग्निमहीस्वभावा जीवासुरेड्याकिम्महीजसौम्याः।  
छाया मरुत्पित्तकफानुरूपां मिश्रैस्तु मिश्रा बलिभिर्नृपस्य॥२३॥**

 *Sloka 23.*—Jupiter, Saturn, Venus, Mars and Mercury during their Dasas exhibit their respective characteristics due to the elements Ether, Water, Air Fire and Earth respectively through wind, bile and phlegm. If the planets be of a mixed nature (so far as their position in the horoscope is concerned), the effects also will be mixed.

**छाया शुभा शुभफलानि निवेदयन्ती  
 लक्ष्या मनुष्यपशुपक्षिषु लक्षणज्ञैः।  
तेजोगुणान् बहिरपि प्रविकासयन्ती  
 दीपप्रभास्फटिकरत्नघटस्थितेव॥२४॥**

 *Sloka 24.—*The bodily lustre (complexion) which indicates both good and bad effects and reveals the virtues of the heart, as does the flame of a lamp kept inside a crystal pot, the qualities of brilliance, may be observed by those well-versed in the science, in men, animals and birds.

**स्निग्धद्विजत्वङ्नखरोमकेशाच्छाया सुगन्धा च महीसमुत्था।  
तुष्ट्यर्थलाभाभ्युदयोन् करोति धर्मस्य चाहन्यहनि प्रवृत्तिम्॥२५॥**

 *Sloka 25.—*The lustre born of the element Earth, makes the teeth, skin, nails and hair on the body and head glossy, produces fine smell, bestows contentment, wealth, gain and rise in status, and causes engagement in religious and meritorious acts always.

**स्निग्धा सिताच्छहरिता नयनाभिरामा  
 सौभाग्यमार्दवसुखाभ्युदयान् करोति।  
सर्वार्थसिद्धिजननी जननीव चाप्या  
 छाया फलं तनुभृतां शुभमादधाति॥२६॥**

 * Sloka 26.—*The lustre born of the element Water, is glossy, white or pure, green, attractive to the eyes, gives amiable qualities, a soft nature, happiness, prosperity, all kinds of progress like a mother, and all-round good to human beings.

**चण्डाधृष्या पद्महेमाग्निवर्णा युक्ता तेजोविक्रमैः सप्रतापैः।  
आग्नेयीति प्राणिनां स्याञ्जयाय क्षिप्रं सिद्धिं वाञ्छितार्थस्य दत्ते॥२७॥**

* Sloka 27.—*The lustre born of the element, fire, is irascible, irresistible, of the hue of lotus, gold or fire, endowed with brilliance, valour and might; leads to victory of beings, and confers immediate accomplishment of the desired object.

**असितजलदकान्तिः पापगन्धोऽतिगूढो  
 मलिनपरुषकालः शोकसन्तापतप्तः।  
स भवति धनहीनः प्राक्तनार्थस्य हानि-  
 र्विचरति पवनोत्था यस्य कान्तिः शरीरे॥२८॥**

 *Sloka 28.—*The lustre born of the element, Air, is dark and is of the colour of the cloud, of foul smell, confounding, dusky, rough and leads to sorrows and suffering, without any wealth, and losing all ancestral property.

**शब्दार्थविन्यासपरः प्रगल्भो विज्ञानयुक्तो महितस्वभावः।  
श्लथाङ्गसन्धिः कृशपाणिपादौ व्योमप्रकृत्या पुरुषोऽतिदीर्घः॥ २९॥**

 * Sloka 29.*—The Lustre born of the element, Ether, will be a knower of words and their meanigs, will be an exponent in them, will be energetic, discerning, esteemed and revered by all, will have his joints loose, will have lean hands and feet, and a tall body.

**चिन्तास्वप्नानुभवे परिणमति फलं विहीनवीर्यस्य।  
पञ्चमहापुरुषोक्तच्छाया ह्येतानि योजयेदत्र॥३०॥**

 * Sloka 30*.—When planets are void of strength, the effects make themselves felt at least in dreamy reveries. The effects of the पञ्चमहापुरुष yogas are to be dealt with similarly should the planets be weak.

**आकृतिजातिप्रकृतीज्ञोत्वा सम्यक् फलं हि वक्तव्यम्।  
कुलदेशवयोऽनुगुणं दशाक्रमज्ञैर्यथान्यायम्॥३१॥**

**इति श्रीवराहमिहिरसुतश्रीपृथुयशोविरचिते होरासारे सङ्कीर्णफलाध्यायः षोडशः॥**

* Sloka* 31—After knowing the form (stature, etc), caste, nature (disposition), etc, thoroughly, the effects should be predicted in conformity with the family, country and age of the person concerned, by people versed in the subject

Thus ends the 16th Adhyaya entitled "Miscellaneous effects"  
of the Dasas in the work Horasara composed by Sri  
Prithuyasas, the son of Sri Varahamihira.

**——————**

**सप्तदशोऽध्यायः**

 The following are the Ashtakavarga places in the several Ashtakavargas of the Sun and other planets:

**रव्यष्टवर्गवाक्यानि—रविबिन्दुसङ्ख्याः–समष्टिः—४८**

**॥ अथाष्टवर्गफलम् ॥**

**ग्रहप्रभृतिसंस्थानं निर्दिशेदक्षरैः क्रमात्।  
राशिचक्रं लिखेद्भूमौ संयोज्याक्षरसङ्ख्यया॥ १॥**

**शून्याक्षरेण दशमं निर्दिशेद्विधिवत्ततः।  
सूर्यादिसग्नपर्यन्तमेतैर्वाक्यैर्विनिक्षिपेत्॥ २॥**

  *Slokas* 1–2—The several places reckoned from each of the several planets should be indicated by figures, the 10th one being represent by zero commencing with the Sun, etc., and ending with the Lagna in the several formulas, by writing on the ground the Rasi chakra.

**स्वेषु स्येष्वष्टवर्गेषु ग्रहाणां च पृथक् पृथक्।  
दशां द्वादशसम्भिन्नां योजयेत्तत्र तत्र हि॥ ३॥**

**ग्रहादिनां फलं ज्ञात्वा निर्दिशेच्च पृथक् पृथक्।**

 *Slokas* 3–31—The 12 kinds of the Dasa periods arising for the 12 houses should be separately entered for each of the several planets, and their effects determined.

**दशायां शून्यभावेषु शत्रुनीचगृहेषु च॥ ४॥**

**व्याध्यर्थनाशदुःखादींल्लभते नात्र संशयः।  
एकद्वित्रिफलं राशौ धनधान्यपशुक्षयः॥ ५॥**

** चत्वारि मध्यमानि स्युर्दशा तत्रैव मध्यमा।  
पञ्चमादिफलैर्युक्तं स्थानं स्यात्सर्वसिद्धिदम्॥ ६॥**

 *Slokas* 4–6—In the case of houses containing no benefic dots–houses owned or occupied by inimical planets, houses which are depressed (i. e., occupied by planets in depression)–the person will without fail suffer diseases, and untoward happenings. When there are 1, 2, or 3 benefic dots in a Rasi, there will be loss of wealth, corn or death of cattle, If there be four dots, the effects will be medium, and the Dasa then will also be middling. If the dots be 5 or more, the effects arising from that house will all be auspicious

**क्षेत्रोच्चोपचयस्थाने फलमेतदुदाहृतम्।  
पूर्वोक्तमार्गेण शुभमष्टवर्गं विनिर्दिशेत्॥ ७॥**

 * Sloka* 7—The effects should thus be predicted in the case of planets occupying their exaltation, own or Upachaya houses. The effects of benefic dots should be determined in the manner stated already.

**शुमानि द्विगुणं कुर्युरन्यथा चान्यथा भवेत्।  
एवं द्वादशमूर्त्यादिस्थानेषु च दशाफलम्॥ ८॥**

*Sloka* 8—The effects will be two–fold auspicious in good houses and two–fold bad, in bad houses. The extent of the effects in the 12 Bhavas beginning from the Lagna should be judged in this manner.

**मूर्त्तेः शरीरसम्पत्तिमङ्गोपाङ्गनिरूपणम्।**  
**सत्यं सौभाग्यवित्तं च द्वितीयस्थानतो विदुः॥ ९॥**

**स्वरं सत्त्वं विक्रमं च भ्रातरं च तृतीयभात्।  
सुखं बन्धुर्गुणश्चैव मातृचिन्ता च तुर्यतः॥ १०॥**

**स्वभावो बुद्धिविस्तारः पुत्रस्थानं तु पञ्चमम्।  
ज्ञातिशत्रुक्षतादीनि षष्ठेन विचिन्तयेत्॥ ११॥**

**प्रसवं दारसौभाग्यं सप्तमस्थानतो विदुः।  
आधिव्याधि मृतीर्नाशमष्टमं परिचक्षते॥ १२॥**

**भाग्यस्थानं गुरुस्थानं धर्मस्थानं ततः परम्।  
कर्माजीवस्तु दशमो प्रतापः पौरुषं श्रुतिः॥ १३॥**

**कीर्तिश्च ज्ञायते तत्र दृष्टादृष्टनिरूपणम्।  
ऐश्वर्यमर्थलाभं च विदुरेकादशाद्गृहात्॥ १४॥**

**द्वादशं तु व्ययस्थानं पापस्थानं प्रचक्षते।  
एवं द्वादश भावेषु चिन्तयेन्मतिमान्नरः॥ १५॥**

 * Slokas* 9–15—One's bodily growth or otherwise should be examined from the Lagna. Truthfulness, luck and wealth from the 2nd house. Voice, energy, valour and brothers, from the 3rd house; happiness, relations, qualities and mother should be determined through the 4th; one's nature, intelligence and children, from the 5th; one's Dayadis, enemies, wounds, etc, from the 6th ; progeny, marital gains, diseases, death and destruction, are to be declared from the 8th; about fortune, elders and virtue, from the 9th; occupation and living. from the 10th ; it is from this house that one has to seek for information about one's valour, prowess, learning and fame; all–seen and heard–about him should also be ascertained from this house. The 12th is called the house of expenditure. It is also called the house of sin. It is in this manner that an intelligent astrologer should examine the twelve houses.

**पापान्वितास्तु ये भावास्ते भावाः स्युर्विनाशिनः।  
सौम्याः सिद्धिकरा ज्ञेया मिश्रा मिश्रफलप्रदाः॥१६॥**

 *Sloka* 16– Houses occupied by malefics produce unfavourable effects; while if by benefics, they give good results. The effects will be medium, when the planets also are of medium nature.

**मित्रोच्चभवनस्थश्चेत्पापः शुभफलं दिशेत्।  
अरातिनचिभस्थश्चेच्छुभः पापफलं दिशेत्॥ १७॥**

 * Sloka* 17—If a planet occupy a friendly or exaltation house he will, though malefic, produce good effects. If he should be in his depression or inimical house he will, even if benefic, will give bad results.

**एवमादिफलैः सार्द्धं दशाफलमुदीरयेत्।  
आत्मप्रभावशक्तिश्च पितृचिन्ता रवेः फलम्॥१८॥**

* Sloka* 18.—It is only after examining these, the astrologer should predict the effects of the planet's Dasa. Anything about one's own self, influence, and vigour should be divined through the Sun.

**मनो बुद्धिप्रसादश्च मातृचिन्ता तु चन्द्रतः।  
भ्रातृसत्त्वगुणान् भूमिं भौमेन तु विचिन्तयेत्॥१९॥**

* Sloka* 19.— It is the Moon that determines the character of one's mind, royal favour and mother. It is through Mars that a person can ascertain his own courage, characteristic qualities, and lands.

**प्रज्ञावाक्कर्मविज्ञानं बुधेनैव विनिर्दिशेत्।  
गुरुणा देहपुष्टिं च बुद्धिपुत्रार्थसम्पदः॥२०॥**

* Sloka* 20.—It is Mercury that influences one's speech, action and discrimination. One ought to conjecture about one's physical development, genius, sons and wealth through Jupiter.

**शुक्राद्विवाहकर्म स्याद्भोगस्थानं च वाहनम्।  
आयुश्च जीवनोपायो मरणं च शनैश्चरात्॥२१॥**

* Sloka* 21.—Information regarding one's marriage, love affairs and vehicles is to be sought through Venus. It is Saturn that settles a person's period of life, livelihood and death.

**बलहीना ग्रहा ये स्युर्जन्मकाले सदा नृणाम्।  
तेषामुक्तं फलं हीनं विपरीतं शनेः स्मृतम्॥२२॥**

* Sloka* 22.—Where planets are weak at one's birth, their effects also will be weak; the reverse will be the case with regard to Saturn.

**स्वेषु स्वेष्वष्टवर्गेषु ग्रहोक्तफलमादिशेत्।  
अष्टवर्गादृते नैव दशाज्ञानं भवेत् ध्रुवम्॥२३॥**

*Sloka* 23.—All the planets reveal their effects in proportion to the number of benefic dots in the houses occupied by them. Without the aid of Ashtakavarga, it will not be possible to determine the exact nature of the effects in the native's several Dasas.

**आदित्याष्टकवर्गे च निक्षिप्याकाशचारिषु।  
अर्कस्थितस्य नवमो राशिः पितृगृहं स्मृतः॥२४॥**

**तद्राशिफल सङ्ख्यामिर्वर्धयेच्छोध्यपिण्डकम्।  
सप्तविंशतिसम्भाज्यं शेषर्क्षं याति भानुजे॥२५॥**

**तस्मिन् काले पितृक्लेशो भविष्यति न संशयः।  
तत्त्रिकोणगते वाऽपि पितुः पितृसमस्य वा॥२६॥**

**मरणं तस्य जानीयाद्दशाच्छिद्रमुदीक्ष्य च।**

* Sloka* 24–26½.—Find out the benefic dots revealed by the planets in the Sun's Ashtakavarga (of the native). The Rasi that is ninth from that occupied by the Sun is said to denote the house of his father; The **शोध्यपिण्ड** (*Vide Sloka 36 infra*) figure should be multiplied by the number of benefic dots in the house of the 'father'. The product should be divided by 27. When Saturn in his transit passes through the particular star revealed by the remainder, the demise of the father will surely happen. Or when Saturn transits a star triangular to the previous one, the father or a relative similarly placed will die. Thus should the astrologer declare, after due verification, if the Dasa at the time be a छिद्र one.

**चन्द्रलग्नाद् गुरुस्थानं याते सूर्यसुते सति॥२७॥**

**पित्रोर्नाशस्तत्र काले वक्ष्यते चार्कचन्द्रयोः।  
दशानुकूलकाले तु योजयेत्कालवित्तमः॥२८॥**

 *Sloka* 27–28.—When Saturn transits the 9th house reckoned from the Moon, the demise of the parents may be predicted at the time should the Dasas of the two luminaries be also in progress.

**लग्नात्सुखेश्वरांशेशदशायां च पितृक्षयः।  
सुखनाथदशायां वा पितृनाशस्त्वसंशयः॥२९॥**

* Sloka* 29.—The demise of the father may also occur during the Dasa of the planet owning the Navamsa of the lord of the 4th house. Or, it may happen without doubt during the Dasa of the lord of the 4th house.

**पितृजन्माष्टमे जातस्तदीशो लग्नगोऽपि वा।  
तेनैव पितृकार्याणि कारयेन्नान्यथा यतः॥३०॥**

** ***Sloka* 30.—Find out the owner of the 8th house reckoned from the 9th. When this or the planet occupying the Lagna has his Dasa in progress, the father's obsequies have to be performed and not at any other time.

**शुभेशे लाभलग्नस्थे चन्द्रलग्नाद्विशेषतः।  
मित्रग्रहसमायुक्ते माता पितृवशानुगा॥३१॥**

* Sloka* 31.—When the lord of the 9th house occupies the 11th or the Lagna—especially when the counting is reckoned from the place occupied by the Moon—and is in conjunction with a friendly planet, the mother also follows the fate of the father.

**तेनैव पितृकार्येषु कर्मशेषं समापयेत्।  
पितृजन्मतृतीयर्क्षे जातः पितृधनाभितः॥३२॥**

* Sloka* 32.—With that, the native should finish the parental rites that still remain. One born in the 3rd house of the father will inherit money from the father.

**पितृकर्मगृहे जातः पितृतुल्यगुणान्वितः।  
तदीशे लग्नसंस्थेऽपि पितृश्रेष्ठो भवेत्सुतः॥३३॥**

* Sloka* 33.—One born in a Rasi which is the 10th from that of his father will have characteristic qualities similar to those of his father Even if the lord of that Rasi occupy the Lagna, he will excel his father in merit.

**सूर्याष्टवर्गे यद्राशौ फलं शून्यं प्रजायते।  
विवाहव्यवहारादि तन्मासे वर्जयेत्सदा॥३४॥**

 *Sloka* 34.—In the Ashtakavarga of the Sun when there is a Rasi devoid of dots, one should always avoid that month for purposes of marriage and similar topics.

**कलहायासदुःखानि शून्यमासि च सन्ति हि।  
एवमादिफलं ज्ञात्वा मासं प्रतिसमाचरेत्॥ ३५॥**

 *Sloka* 35.—For, in a month void of benefic dots there may arise quarrels, weariness and misery; after knowing all these, one should prepare himself to meet the tide of events in that month.

**संशोध्य पिण्डं सूर्यस्य रन्ध्रमानेन वर्धयेत्।  
हृतात् द्वादशभिः शेषं मेषादिगणयेत्पुनः॥३६॥**

**तस्मिन्मासे मृतिं विद्यात्तत्त्रिकोणर्क्षकेऽपि वा।**

* Slokas* 36, 36½.—The शोध्यपिण्ड figures in the Ashtakavarga of the Sun should be multiplied by the number of benefic dots in the 8th house and divided by 12. In the month signified by the remainder when counted from Mesha, or in its triangular Rasi, one's demise may be expected.

**चन्द्राष्टवर्गं निक्षिप्य शून्यफलगते विधौ॥३७॥**

**तन्नक्षत्रं परित्यज्य शुभकार्याणि कारयेत्।**

* Sloka* 37-37½.—When the Moon transits a Rasi void of benefic dots in the Ashtakavarga of the Moon, one should shun that asterism for celebrating all auspicious events.

**चन्द्राष्टमे च नक्षत्रत्रितये च विशेषतः॥३८॥**

**आयासव्याधिदुःखानि लभते नात्र संशयः।**

* Slokas* 38, 38½.—Note the asterism that is in the 8th house from that of the Moon. When the Moon in her transit arrives in that asterism or its triangular ones, one will invariably get worry, disease and misery.

**चन्द्रात् सुखफलैः पिण्डं वर्धयेद्भैर्विभाजयेत्॥३९॥**

**शेषमृर्क्षं शनौ याते मातृहानिं विनिर्दिशेत्।  
तत्त्रिकोणेषु वा केचिदाहुछिद्रदशासु च॥ ४०॥**

 *Slokas* 39-40.—Multiply the शोध्यपिण्ड figures by the number indicating the benefic dots in the 4th house from the Moon aud divide the product by 12. When Saturn transits the star indicated by the remainder, the demise of the mother should be expected. The same event, may also be declared to happen when the transit takes place over an asterism triangular to the same or if there be a छिद्र Dasa at the time.

**चन्द्रलग्नात्सुखस्थाने युते रवितनूभुवा।  
दृष्टे वा तेन तत्स्थाने पूर्वाह्णे कालसङ्गमे॥४१॥**

**मृत्युं वा दूरगमनं निर्दिशेत्कालचिन्तकः।**

 *Slokas* 41,41½.—If Saturn occupy or aspect the 4th house reckoned from the Moon and the hour at the time before noon, one should declare the person's demise or a distant voyage.

**चन्द्रात्सुखाष्टमेशांशात् त्रिकोणे दिवसाधिपे॥४२॥**

**मातुर्वियोगं तन्मासे निर्दिशेल्लग्नतः पितुः।  
पितृवन्मातृचिन्तायां फलं सर्वं प्रकल्पयेत्॥४३॥**

* Slokas* 42-43.—Note the lords of the 4th and 8th houses counted from the Moon, and the Navamsas occupied by them. When the Sun transits a Rasi triangular to the same, the demise of the mother may come to pass in that month. The above has to be determined from. the father's Lagna Rasi. The events for the mother should be determined in the same way as for the father.

**भौमाष्टवर्गे सञ्चिन्त्या भ्रातृसम्पत्तथैव च।  
भौमो बलविहीनश्चेद् धीप्रयासान्वितो भवेत्॥४४॥**

* Sloka* 44.—In a similar manner, a brother's riches, etc.., have to be ascertained through the Ashtakavarga of Mars. If Mars be weak, there will be great difficulty in acquiring knowledge.

**बुधाष्टवर्गं संशोध्य शेषराशिगते शनौ।  
पुत्रमित्रविनाशादींल्लभते नात्र संशयः॥४५॥**

 *Sloka* 45.—Similar reductions have to be made in the Ashtakavarga figures of Mercury. When Saturn transits the Rasi signified by the remainder, loss of issue, of friends and other untoward events will without doubt happen.

**गुरोरष्टकवर्गे च सन्तानमपि कल्पयेत्।  
गुरोः फलानि यावन्ति सुतस्थाने स्थितानि च॥४६॥**

**शत्रुनीचग्रहफलं त्यक्त्वा तावन्त आत्मजाः।  
गुरोः सुतगृहे येऽंशास्तावन्तस्तनयाः स्मृताः॥४७॥**

**सुतभेशनवांशैर्वा समानांस्तनयान्वदेत्।**

* Sloka* 46-47½—From the Ashtakavarga of Jupiter, it is possible to fix up the issue that one will have. Find the number of benefic dots in the 5th house from Jupiter in his Ashtakavarga. The dots given by planets occupying their inimical and depression houses should be left out. The remainder will denote the number of issue. Note the Navamsa of the 5th house from Jupiter; its order from Mesha will signify the number required; or it may also be determined through the Navamsa (its order from Mesha) occupied by the lord of the 5th house.

**गुरोरष्टकवर्गे च शोध्यशेषफलेषु वै॥४८॥**

**क्रूराश्रितफलं त्यक्त्वा शेषास्तस्यात्मजाः स्मृताः।  
व्ययाष्टमसुतस्यैश्च पापैः क्षीणा हि सन्ततिः॥४९॥**

* Slokas* 48-49.—In the Ashtakavarga of Jupiter, find the total number of dots after reduction. The dots contained in the several Rasis occupied by malefics should be left out. The remainder will signify the number of the issue. Of these, the dots in the 12th, 8th and the 5th if occupied by malefics, will denote the number that die very early.

**गुरोरष्टकवर्गे चेत्सुतराशौ फलत्रयम्।  
अल्पात्मजः स विज्ञेयो गुरोः पश्चममेऽपि वा॥५०॥**

**तदीशयुक्तदृष्टे वा तदा पुत्रान्समादिशेत्।**

* Slokas* 50-50½.—In the Ashtakavarga of Jupiter, if there be 3 benefic dots in the 5th house, or in the Rasi which is 5th from Jupiter, the person concerned should be declared as issueless. But if the said house be occupied or aspected by its lord, the person will beget issue.

**एतैर्बहुप्रकारैस्तु कल्पयेत्कालवित्तमः॥५१॥**

**सर्वलक्षणसंयोगे तदा तस्मिन् समादिशेत्।  
वंशक्षयादियोगा हि वक्ष्यन्तेऽग्रे मयास्फुटम्॥ ५२॥**

**पूर्वोक्तलक्षणेनैव वंशलक्ष्म समादिशेत्।**

* Slokas* 51–52½.—It is by these and other various methods that the astrologer should solve the question. When the Yoga for progeny is clear, children will surely be born to the native. The Yogas for family—extinction will be described separately in a clear manner.

**भृगोरष्टकवर्गं च निक्षिप्याकाशचारिषु॥५३॥**

**त्रिकोणशोधनं कुर्यात्पश्चादेकाधिपत्यजम्।  
येषु भेषु फलानि स्युर्विशेषेण च तेषु च॥५४॥**

**भूमिं कलत्रं वित्तं च कालविन्निर्दिशेन्नृणाम्।  
शुक्रजामित्रतो लब्धिं दाराणां निर्दिशेद् बुधः॥५५॥**

* Slokas* 53–55.—The number of benefic dots derived from the planets should be set up constituting the Ashtakavarga of Venus. The Trikona reduction should be effected, followed by the Ekadhipatya one. Whichever Rasis contain dots, the astrologer should declare lands, wife and wealth in proportion to their number. The number of dots contained in the 7th house reckoned from Venus will reveal the number of wives that one will have.

**दाराधिपांशक्षेत्रं दारजन्मर्क्षमं विदुः।  
तस्योच्चे निजराशौ वा केचिदिच्छन्ति तद्विदः॥५६॥**

**तस्यां शकत्रिकोणे वा भार्याजन्मर्क्षभं वदेत्।  
लग्नेन्द्वोर्भाग्यभं जन्म वदन्ति मुनिसत्तमाः॥५७॥**

**उक्तप्रकारमार्गेण भार्याया जन्मलग्नभम्।  
तयोः समागमर्क्षं च कल्पयेदत्र बुद्धिमान्॥५८॥**

* Slokas* 56-58.—Note where the lord of the Navamsa occupied by the owner of the 7th house is posited. This Rasi will be the Janma Rasi of the wife. Some say that the planet's exaltation or Swakshetra may also denote the same. The wife's Janma Rasi may also be anyone of the
triangular houses with regard to that Navamsa. Some Sages declare that it is the 9th house counted from the Lagna or the Moon. A clever astrologer should guess the most suitable and probable one.

**अनुक्तराशिजन्मर्क्षमस्ति चेन्नास्ति सन्ततिः।  
भाग्यदारेशयुक्तर्क्षफलसङ्ख्याः स्त्रियो विदुः॥ ५९॥**

**क्षेत्रे त्रिगुणना तुल्या नवांशे द्विगुणास्तथा।**

* Slokas* 59, 591/2 — If the Janma Rasi of the wife be some other than that what has been mentioned above, it means there will be no progeny. The ( number of ) benefic dots in the houses occupied by the lords of the 9th and 7th houses represent the number of females one will have. The number will be treble in the case of Rasis and double in that of the Navamsa when these happen to own them.

**मन्दांशे मन्दसंयुक्ते मन्दक्षेत्रगते भृगौ॥ ६०॥**

**नीचांशे पापयुक्ते वा नीचस्त्रीभोगमृच्छति।  
भौमांशकगते शुक्रे भौमक्षेत्रगतेऽथवा॥ ६१॥**

**भौमेन दृष्टे युक्ते वा परस्त्रीभोगमिच्छति।**

* Slokas* 60-61.—When Venus occupies a Navamsa of Saturn, is conjoined with Saturn or occupies a Rasi of Saturn, or is in a depression Navamsa, or is associated with a malefic, the person concerned will have sexual intercourse with a low woman. When Venus occupies a Navamsa or Rasi owned by Mars, or is associated with or aspected by Mars, the person concerned will desire to have sexual intercourse with a woman other than his wife.

**जामित्रे मन्दभौमांश तदीशे मन्दकामगे॥६२॥**

**बेश्या वा जारिणी वाऽपि तस्य भार्या न संशयः।**

* Slokas* 62.62½—When the 7th Bhava is in a Navamsa belonging to Saturn or Mars and the lord of that Bhava occupies the 7th house reckoned from Saturn, the wife of the native will, without doubt, be a courtezan or an adulteress.

**पापारूढांशगे चन्द्रे जामित्रे व्ययभेऽपि वा॥६३॥**

**पापग्रहान्विते शुक्रे स्त्रीहेतोर्भ्रंशमावहेत्।**

* Slokas* 63, 62½—When the Moon occupies the 7th or the 12th house and is in a Navamsa owned by a malefic, and when Venus is associated with a malefic, the person concerned will suffer degradation through a woman (at the bottom).

**शुक्रांशकसमाना स्त्री वर्णरूपगुणान्विता॥६४॥**

**भाग्येशांशपतुल्या वा दारेशस्य गुणान्विता।  
तेषां बलाबलेनैव भार्याया लक्षणं वदेत्॥६५॥**

**एवमादिफलं ज्ञात्वा निर्दिशेत् शुक्रवर्गतः।**

* Slokas* 64-65½.—The woman-partner will have the colour, form and qualities similar to those of the Navamsa occupied by Venus; or of the Navamsa occupied by the lord of the 9th or the 7th Thus, after ascertaining the preponderance of the number of benefic dots in the Ashtakavarga of Venus, one should arrive at the proper conclusion.

**शनैश्चराष्टवर्गं च निक्षिप्याकाशचारिषु॥६६॥**

**लग्नप्रभृतिमन्दान्तं फलान्येकत्र योजयेत्।  
मन्दादिलग्नपर्यन्तं फलान्यन्यत्र योजयेत्॥६७॥**

**फलसङ्ख्यासमानाब्दे व्याधिं दुःखं समादिशेत्।  
तयोर्योगसमानाब्दं मृत्युवर्षं प्रचक्षते॥६८॥**

* Slokas* 66-68.—Prepare the Ashtakavarga of Saturn by finding the benefic dots contributed by the several planets. Add the dots in the houses between the Lagna and Saturn. Add also the dots between Saturn and the Lagna. In the years signified by the two totals, the person concerned will suffer diseases and misery. Add up the two totals. During the year denoted by this sumtotal, the native may suffer death.

**शोध्यसंशोधनं कृत्वा पिण्डं संस्थाप्य रन्ध्रगैः।  
फलैर्हत्वा भजेत्सप्तविंशत्यायुः फलं भवेत्॥६९॥**

**शेषेण मासा दिवसा घटिकाश्च प्रकल्पयेत्।  
दशाछिद्रसमे काले तस्मिन् मृत्युर्न संशयः॥७०॥**

* Slokas* 69-70.—After doing the two reductions enjoined, make up the शोध्यपिण्ड. Multiply this by the dots in the 8th house and divide the
product by 27. The quotient will reveal the Ayus of the native. From the remainder, the months, days, the ghatikas, etc may be computed. If at the time thus revealed, there be also दशाछिद्र, then death will surely hapen.

**मन्दाष्टवर्गे राशौ तु फलहीने क्षयो भवेत्।  
तद्भक्ते भास्करेणेन्दौ तस्मिन् काले मृतिं वदेत्॥७१॥**

* Sloka* 71.—In the Ashtakavarga of Saturn, if there be no benefic dots in any Rasi, it indicates disease or death. When the शोध्यपिण्ड product (*Vide Slokas 69-70*) is divided by 12, and when the Moon transits the sign thus revealed, one may predict death.

**सर्वग्रहान् फलयुतांश्च नियोज्य चक्रे  
मूर्त्या च सर्वमशुभं च शुभं समं च।  
जन्मादितः फलमशेषदशां समीक्ष्य  
यात्राविवाहसमये कथयेद्विधिज्ञः॥७२॥**

* Sloka* 72.—After entering all the planets in their several Ashtakavargas with their respective benefic dots and ascertaining from the Lagna all those houses that are unfavourable, auspicious and medium and their effects in the entire Dasa periods, the astrologer should proceed to fix up the time for travel, marriage etc.

**रव्यादीनां समुदायाष्टवर्गवाक्यानि–बिन्दुसङ्ख्याश्च॥**

**3 3 3 3 2 3 4 5 3 5 7 2**

**रवेः —बालोबलिष्ठो लवणागमो सुरो**

**2 3 5 2 2 5 2 2 2 3 7 1**

**चन्द्रस्य—रागीमुरारी शिखरीन्द्रगाथया।**

**4 5 3 5 2 3 4 4 4 6 7 2**

**कुजस्य—भौमोगणेन्द्रोलघुभावतासुरो**

**3 1 5 2 6 6 1 2 5 5 7 3**

**बुधस्य—गोकर्णरक्तातुपुराणमैथिली॥७३॥**

**2 2 1 2 3 4 2 4 2 4 7 3**

**गुरोः—रुद्रःपरङ्गह्वरभैरवस्थली**

**2 3 3 3 4 4 2 3 4 3 6 3**

**शुक्रस्य—रागीबलीभास्वरगर्भिगाचलाः।**

**3 2 4 4 4 3 3 4 44 6 1**

**शनेः—गिरोविवस्वान्बलवद्विवक्षया**

**5 3 5 5 2 6 1 2 2 6 7 1**

**लग्नस्यः— शूलीममप्रीतिकरोत्रतीर्थङ्कृत्॥७४॥**

मेषादि समष्टयः–सर्वाष्टवर्गविन्दुसमष्टिः—337

| | | | |
|----------|------------|-----------|------------|
| मेषस्य 24 | वृषस्य 22 | मिथुनस्य 29 | कर्कटस्य 26 |
| सिंहस्य 25 | कन्यायाः 34 | तुलायाः 19 | वृश्चिकस्य 26 |
| धनुषः 26 | मकरस्य 36 | कुम्भस्य 54 | मीनस्य 16 |

**सर्वकर्मफलोपेतमष्टवर्गं विदुर्बुधाः।  
अन्यथा तस्य विज्ञानं दुर्ज्ञेयं गुणदोषजम्॥७५॥**

 Sloka75.—All kinds of activities may be ascertained through these figures: else, it is difficult to know their nature, good or bad.

**नगा (30) धिकफला ये स्यू राशयस्ते शुभप्रदाः।  
तत्त्वादि (25) खगुणा (30) न्ताक्षा राशयो मध्यमा मताः॥७६॥**

* Sloka* 76.—Rasis containing 30 or more dots are declared to be productive of good (or auspicious) effects. Those between 25 and 30 are considered as medium.

**अतिक्षीणफला ये स्यू राशयस्तेऽधमाः स्मृताः।  
श्रेष्ठराशिषु सर्वाणि शुभकार्याणि कारयेत्॥७७॥**

* Sloka* 77.—Signs containing very small number of dots are declared as very bad. All auspicious acts should be performed (when the luminaries are) in the good Rasis.

**श्रेष्ठान् राशीन् मुहूर्तेषु योजयेन्मतिमान्नरः।  
यस्य व्ययाधिकं लग्नं भोगवानर्थवान् भवेत्॥७८॥**

**विपरीते तु दारिद्र्यं भविष्यति न संशयः।  
त्रिंशतो मध्यमं पूर्वं परं तस्माच्छुभं भवेत्॥७९॥**

* Slokas* 78-79.—A good astrologer should select only those Rasis which contain good number of benefic dots for celebrating anything auspicious. He, in whose Ashtavarga the benefic dots in the Lagna exceed that of the 12th will enjoy life and be rich. When it is otherwise, poverty will without doubt encircle him. From 25 to 30, it will be middling. After that it is only good that will prevail.

**मूर्त्यादि व्ययपर्यन्तं बोध्यं भावफलं बुधैः।  
अधिके शोभनं विद्याद्धीने दोषं विनिर्दिशेत्॥८०॥**

* Sloka* 80.—The several effects of the Bhavas from the 1st to the 12th should be determined before-hand by the wise man. When benefic dots predominate, the effect of that Rasi will be good. When the number of dots are low, something bad has to be expected.

**षष्ठाष्टमव्ययांस्त्यक्त्वा शेषाण्येवं प्रकल्पयेम्।**

 Omitting the 6th, 8th and 12th houses, the case of the other houses has to be dealt with in the manner stated above,

**मीनादिमिथुनान्तेषु प्रथमं खण्डमिष्यते॥८१॥**

**वृश्चिकादिघटान्तेषु द्वितीयं खण्डमिष्यते।  
कर्कटादितुलान्तेषु तृतीयं खण्डमुच्यते॥८२॥**

**खण्डत्रयं पृथक् स्थाप्यमन्यत् किन्तु निरीक्षयेत्।  
वयोऽनुरूपकर्मादि तेनेवैवं विनिर्दिशेत्॥८३॥**

* Slokas* 81-83.—From the beginning of Meena to the end of Mithuna is called the first Khanda. From the beginning of Vrischika to the end of Kumbha, it is the second Khanda. From the beginning of Karkataka to the end of Tula, it is known as the third Khanda. These three Khandas are to be kept for reference as some functions and acts suitable to the age at the time have to be performed through the guidance of this alone.

**अधिके शोभनं विद्याद्धीने दोषफलं तु वै।  
खण्डत्रयं निरीक्ष्यैव दशानयनमीरयेत्॥८४॥**

**पापग्रहसमारूढं खण्डं क्लेशकरं स्मृतम्।  
सौम्यैः पुष्टफलं ज्ञेयं मिश्रैर्मिश्रफलं स्मृतम्॥८५॥**

**खण्डत्रयफलं ज्ञात्वा दशाफलमुदीरयेत्।**

* Slokas* 84-85½.—In the case of excess of benefic dots, something auspicious should be expected, while when the dots are low in number, matters that are bad will spring up. It is only after noting the three Khanda periods, the Dasa effects should be declared. In the Khanda where malefics prepondrate, the effect will be sorrowful. It will produce good effects when the Khanda consists of 3 or more benefics. In the case of mixed ones, the effect also will be medium.

**लग्नप्रभृति मन्दान्तम् एकीकृत्य फलानि वै॥८६॥**

**सप्तभिर्गुणयेत्तस्मात् सप्तविंशतिभाजितात्।  
तत्फलस्य समानेऽब्दे दुःखं वा रोगमाप्नुयात्॥८७॥**

* Slokas* 86-87.—Total up the benefic dots in the houses beginning with the Lagna and ending with Saturn. Multiply the sum by 7 and divide the product by 27. In the year revealed by this remainder, one meets with sorrow or disease.

**मन्दप्रभृति लग्नान्तमेवमेव प्रकल्पयेत्  
भौमान्तं लग्नतस्तद्वद्भौमाल्लाग्नान्तमेव च॥८८॥**

**क्लेशायासविरोधादील्ँलभते नात्र संशयः।**

* Sloka* 88, 88½.—In the same way, the dots in the (1) houses from Saturn to the end of the Lagna, (2) the dots in the houses beginning from Mars to the Lagna and (3) and those from the Lagna to the end of Mars should be computed. In the years revealed as above, one will meet with sorrow, weariness, enmity and the like undoubtedly.

**ज्ञेया मन्दादिलग्नान्तनवांशकयुतिर्बुधैः॥८९॥**

**तद्योगसदृशे वर्षे चायुधक्लेशमादिशेत्।**

* Sloka* 89, 89½.—Note the Navamsa occupied by Saturn and that of the Lagna. Find the number of Navamsas revealed by this sum. In the year indicated by this figure, one may expect hurt or hit through a missile or weapon.

**राहुभौमादिलग्नान्तमंशयोगसमाब्दके॥९०॥**

**विपदस्त्रक्षतायासदुःखादीनि समादिशेत्।  
शुभग्रहादिलग्नान्तमंशयोगसमाब्दके॥९९॥**

**पुत्रवित्तसुखादीनि लभते नात्र संशयः।**

* Slokas* 90-91½.—The same thing has to be gone through in the case of the Navamsa occupied by (1) Rahu and that of the Lagna and (2) Mars and that of the Lagna. In the years indicated by the respective figures, the person concerned meets with some calamity, hit by a weapon, wound, fatigue, sorrow and the like. In a similar way, during the years indicated by the sum of the Navamsas of benefic planets and the Lagna one will be blessed with issue, wealth, happiness and the like, unfailingly.

**अष्टमाधिपतेरंशसङ्ख्याभिर्गुणयेत्फलम्॥९२॥**

**अष्टमस्थं द्वादशभिर्बिभजेच्छिष्टराशिगे।  
रवौ वा तत्त्रिकोणस्ये मृतिं वा रोगमाप्नुयात्॥९३॥**

**एवमेव विजानीयात् पितृमातृगृहादिषु।**

* Slokas* 92-93½.—The number reckoned from Mesha of the Navamsa occupied by the lord of the 8th house

**एषु स्थानेषु गता दशाधिनाथाद्दशापहर्तारः।  
होरा यदि राहुयुता नो तेषु दशाफलानि सिध्यन्ति॥३॥**

* Sloka* 3.—Planets placed in the several positions aforesaid with respect to the Dasa-lord are the only ones that partake of the entire Dasa period. If Rahu should occupy the Lagna, the Dasa effects will not be felt.

**अन्तर्दशाविभागे रविशशिनोरेव राहुणा सार्धम्।  
यमसदृशफलं वाच्यं नान्येषां केचिदिच्छन्ति॥४॥**

* Sloka* 4.—In the matter of determining the sub-division of an Antardasa, the cases of the Sun and the Moon are peculiar. If one of these be conjoined with Rahu, the sub-period will have to be increased by one half; and their effects will be like those for Saturn and none else. This is the opinion of some.

**इष्टग्रहस्य च दशा नाडी वेदाष्ट (84) सङ्ख्यया गुणयेत्।  
भागांशग्रहतुल्यं तस्मात् संयोज्य तत्रैव॥५॥**

**तत्पिण्डभागहारैर्लब्धं स्वदशाफलस्य तस्यैव।  
पूर्वयुतांशा ग्राह्यास्तस्याश्चान्तर्दशा ग्रहाणां स्युः॥६॥**

**अन्तर्दशा ग्रहाणां पाकक्रमतो दशाफलं योज्यम्।  
क्रूरात् क्रूरं पूर्वं सौम्यात् सौम्यं फलं समत्वेऽपि॥७॥**

* Slokas* 5-7.—Convert the Dasa-period of the planet required into Ghatikas and multiply the same by 84; and add thereto so much portion as is revealed by the degrees travelled. The effects of the Apaharas of the planets will follow in the same order as in the case of the Dasas, and their nature—benefic, malefic, or medium, as the case may be—being more intense than before.

**अर्केन्दुशनिगुरूणां पाकेनान्तर्दशाफलं ब्रूयात्।  
शेषाणां केन्द्राढ्यैर्होराचार्या वदन्त्येवम्॥८॥**

* Sloka* 8.—From the Dasa-periods of the Sun, the Moon, Saturn and Jupiter, one should be able to read their Antardasa effects; in the case of the rest, through thestrongest posited in the Kendras. So, the Astrologers say.

**अथ रविदशान्तर्दशाफलानि॥**

**भानुदशायां चन्द्रः करोति मित्रार्थभोगसम्म्पत्तिम्।  
जलसंश्रयात् प्रमादं पाण्डुग्रहणीयांश्च कष्टदशाम्॥९॥**

* Sloka* 9.—During the Sun's Dasa, when the Moon's Antardasa is in progress, one will get wealth and enjoyments in the company of friends. If the period be bad, a great risk through resorting to water is apprehended, and he may suffer from jaundice, diarrhoea and consumption.

**भानुदशायां भौमः सुवर्णरत्नादिसञ्चयं कुरुते।  
ख्यातिप्रतापयुक्तं पित्तविकाराग्निरोगसन्तप्तम्॥१०॥**

* Sloka* 10.—During the sub-period of Mars in the Sun's Dasa, the person will acquire gold, jewels, etc. He will attain fame and valour. He will suffer from fever, biliousness and the like.

**सौम्यान्तरे च भानोस्त्वग्दोषविकारपीडितो मनुजः।  
ख्यातोऽर्थविहीनः स्यात् सन्नोत्साहः प्रमादबहुलः स्यात्॥११॥**

* Sloka* 11.—In the sub-period of Mercury in the Sun's Dasa. the person will be troubled from skin-disease. He will attain fame, will be full of enthusiasm, but will become moneyless and will suffer a serious mishap.

**जीवान्तरे च भानोर्विद्यावस्त्रान्नसङ्ग्रहणशीलः।  
देवद्विकार्येषु प्रवर्तते ख्यातिमान्नरेन्द्रधनी॥१२॥**

* Sloka* 12.—During the Antardasa of Jupiter in the Sun's Dasa, he will get education, clothing, and he will be busy in collecting articles of food. He will engage himself in helping Brahmins and Gods, attain great fame and riches, and he will become a chief among men.

**शुक्रान्तरे च भानोः प्रवासशीलोऽल्पशुष्कवादरतः।  
कण्ठाक्षिकर्णरोगै रार्तो ज्वरपीडितः स्वतन्त्रश्च॥१३॥**

* Sloka* 13.—In the sub-period of Venus in the Sun's Dasa, one will be away from his place, will engage himself in useless talk, will be troubled by diseases in the neck, eyes and ears; he will suffer from fever; and will be self-willed.

**मन्दापहारकाले भानोनीञ्चारिचोरदुःखार्तः।  
सुहृदप्यमित्रभावं कुरुते क्षीणार्थवृत्तिरुद्योगी॥१४॥**

 Sloka 14.—During the Antardasa of Saturn in the Sun's Dasa, one will be unhappy. He will be troubled by mean persons, enemies, and thieves. Even his friends will begin to hate him. He will spend away all his money and his earnings will become slender.

**अथ चन्द्रदशान्तर्दशाफलानि॥**

**चन्द्रदशायां मानोरन्तरकाले कुदेशकर्मरतः।  
कुस्त्रीजनाभिलाषी क्षीणधनो बन्धुकलहयुतः॥१५॥**

* Sloka* 15.—In the Sun's sub-period of the Moon's Dasa, one will undertake journeys to useless places, and will be intent in doing bad acts. He will seek the company of bad females, will spend away his wealth and will quarrel with his relations.

**इन्दुदशायां भौमान्तरे नरः पुत्रबन्धुरहितः स्यात्।  
रोगी विघातकुशलो मायावी स्थानविच्युतो भवति॥१६॥**

* Sloka* 16.—During the sub-period of Mars in the Moon's Dasa, the native will be bereft of sons and relatives. He will suffer from diseases; his enthusiasm will be dumped; he will be deceitful and will suffer degradation. in his status.

**चन्द्रदशायां सौम्यान्तरकाले गोगजाश्वसम्पन्नः।  
नित्योत्साही गुणवान् गजाश्वभोगी सुतादिलब्धिश्च॥१७॥**

* Sloka* 17.—During Mercury's Antara in the Moon's Dasa, the person will have cows, elephants and horses. He will always evince enthusiasm, and will possess good qualities.

**चन्द्रदशायां गुर्वन्तरकाले धर्मभोगसम्पन्नः।  
विद्याधनैः समेतः प्रसिद्धनामान्वितो विदेशरतः॥१८॥**

* Sloka* 18.—When Jupiter's Antara in the Moon's Dasa progresses, the native will lead a virtuous life and enjoy all comforts. He will acquire learning and wealth, and will get a big title.

**चन्द्रदशायां शुक्रप्रवेशने स्त्रीधनानि सिध्यन्ति।  
जलकृषिपशुमणिपोतप्रयोगतोऽर्थागमः सुखं लभते॥१९॥**

* Sloka* 19.—During the advent of the Antara of Venus, one gets woman, wealth, etc. He will acquire money through water, agriculture, cattle, jewels, and boatrowing and he will be happy.

**नृपचोरमुषितवित्तस्तेजोहीनो विनष्टसुतदारः।  
लभते च महाव्याधिं चन्द्रदशायां प्रवेशने पङ्गोः॥२०॥**

* Sloka* 20.—When Saturn's Antara in the Dasa of the Moon commences, he will get wealth from the sove.

* Sloka 28.*—During the Moon's Antara in Mercury's Dasa, a still-born child will be born. The person will be much dissatisfied. He will associate with bad women and contract disease. He may suffer from leprosy. He will also have to apprehend danger from his Dayadins.

**सौम्यात्कुजापहारे गुह्मरुगार्त्तो न दारपुत्रयुतः।  
ऊर्ध्वाङ्गरोगबहुलो बहुव्ययार्त्तोऽल्पजातिसन्तुष्टः॥२९॥**

* Sloka* 29.—During the Dasa of Mercury and in the Antara of Mars, the native will suffer from trouble in the anus, and will have no wife or son by his side He will be troubled with ऊर्ध्वाङ्गरोग in and heavy expenditure. will get satisfaction from low people.

**जीवापहृतौ सौम्यात् सुतदारसमन्वितां विगतशोकः।  
नृपमन्त्री नेता वा पितृमातृविवर्जितो भवति नूनम्॥३०॥**

* Sloka* 30.—When Jupiter's Antara in Mercury's Dasa is in progress, the person will have no sorrow, but will be happy surrounded by his wife and sons. He will become a minister or a commander under a king; he will be forsaken by both the parents.

**इन्दुसुतस्य दशायां शुक्रविभागे धनान्वितो धीमान्।  
वस्त्रालङ्कारयुतो बुभुक्षितो देवकार्यसन्तुष्टः॥३१॥**

* Sloka* 31.—In the Antara of Venus in Mercury's Dasa, he will possess money; he will be intelligent and will command clothes and jewels. He will suffer from hunger and take delight in doing service to the Gods.

**मन्दापहृतौ सौम्यान्नीचप्रायोऽल्पसन्तुष्टः।  
क्लीबो मृदुस्वभावो वातरुगार्तोऽन्नपाननिरतः स्यात्॥३२॥**

 * Sloka* 32.—During Saturn's Apahara in Mercury's Dasa, he will be almost insignificant. He will be contented with what little he gets. He will be weakminded and kind. He will suffer from wind-disease, but will be intent in eating and drinking.

**अथ गुरुदशान्तर्दशाफलानि॥**

**जीवदशायां भानोरन्तरकाले सुतार्थ भोगयुतः।  
ख्यातो विशिष्टनामा लोकसभापूजितोऽतिमान्यश्च॥३३॥**

 * Sloka* 33.—During the Sun's Apahara in Jupiter's Dasa, the person concerned will be happy in the company of his children and have wealth at his command. He will attain great fame and get a title. He will be highly respected and worshipped by all the people.

**जीवाच्चन्द्रविभागे बहुदारसमन्वितो धनी विद्वान्।  
नृपदयितो विख्यातो नृपार्थलाभान्महोत्साही॥३४॥**

 * Sloka* 34.—In the Moon's Antara of Jupiter's Dasa, the native will possess wealth, be learned and have the company of many wives. He will become the king's favourite and through his favour, attain great fame and be over-enthusiastic.

**जीवात्कुजापहारे मस्तकरोगी गुदाक्षिरोगी वा।  
परगृहवासी विकलो रिक्ततनुर्बाध्यतेऽरिणा नित्यम्॥३५॥**

 *Sloka* 35 - During the Antara of Mars in Jupiter's Dasa, the native will suffer from acute head-ache, trouble in the anus or eye-disease. He will mess in other's houses. He will be dispirited and become useless and bothered always by his enemies.

**जीवाद्बुधापहारे धर्मविरुद्धाश्रितो विदेशरतः।  
मन्दोत्साही चपलो जलप्रमादी विवादी च॥३६॥**

*Sloka* 36.— In Mercury's Antara of Jupiter's Dasa, he will swerve from the path of virtue. His activity will be dull. He will be intent in visiting other places. He will be fickle, of a quarrelling disposition, and have risk in water.

**जीवात्सितान्तराले वात श्लेष्मान्वितोऽग्निदीप्तश्च।  
धर्मक्रियास्वभीष्टो विद्यावस्त्रान्नसङ्ग्रहणशीलः॥३७॥**

 * Sloka* 37.— In the Antara of Venus in Jupiter's Dasa, he will suffer from wind and phlegm. He will also have stomach troubles. He will desire to do virtuous acts. He will engage himself in learning. He will be intent in obtaining clothes and articles of food.

**मन्दापहृतौ जीवात् कृषिपशुवित्तान्वितोऽतिरोगी स्यात्।  
स्त्रीव्यसनकर्शितात्मा प्रेष्यजनैः पीडितो विषाद्यैर्वा॥३८॥**

 * Sloka* 38. — In Saturn's Antara of Jupiter's Dasa, the person will get money through agriculture and cattle. He will suffer much through disease. He will be troubled by women, and will become emaciated and weak. He will have worries through servants, poison and the like.

**अथ शुक्रान्तर्दशाफलानि॥**

**शुक्रात् सूर्यविभागे गुदाक्षिशूलादिपीडितो मनुजः।  
नृपजनितभयाविष्टो बन्धुक्लेशाद्धनक्षयं याति॥३९॥**

 * Sloka* 39.— During the Dasa of Venus in the Sun's sub-period, the person concerned will suffer from trouble in the anus, from sore-eyes, enlargement of spleen and the like. There will also be fear caused through royal displeasure. There will be trouble from his relations and heavy expenditure will be incurred thereby.

**चन्द्रापहृतौ शुक्रात् श्वापदपीडाग्निपित्तरोगयुतः।  
अनिवारितरणवेगो जेता स्त्रीसङ्गमाद्धनप्राप्तिः॥४०॥**
