 * Sloka* 40.— In the Moon's Apahara of Sukra's Dasa, there will be danger from wild beasts, swelling (in the body), and bilious trouble; success (inavertible) impetuosity in a combat and association with another female bring money to the native.

**शुक्रात्कुजापहारे नचिस्त्री भोगवान् विकलदन्तः।  
पैत्तिकरोगोद्रिक्तो मन्दोत्साहः पुमान् भवति॥४१॥**

 *Sloka* 41. — During the Apahara of Mars in the Dasa or Venus, the person will have intercourse with a low woman. He will have decayed teeth, will suffer from a strong bilious disease and his strength will be crippled.

**शुक्रात्सौम्यविभागे दुरन्तकार्यान्वितोऽभिमानी स्यात्।  
पशुफलवृक्षाद्वित्तं लभते दारप्रियोऽतिसन्तुष्टः॥४२॥**

 * Sloka* 42. — When Mercury's Apahara of Sukra's Dasa progresses, he will be engaged in a futile business; he will become proud. He will obtain money through. cattle and fruit-trees. He will be fond of his wife and will be very contented.

**शुक्रदशायां च गुरोरन्तरकाले गतार्थसिद्धिः स्यात्।  
यज्ञक्रियादिनिपुणो सुतदारसमन्वितः सुखी भवति॥४३॥**

 * Sloka* 43.— During the Apahara of Jupiter in the Dasa of Venus, the person gets a suddden gain of money. He will take an active part in the performance of a sacrifice. He will live happily in the midst of his wife and children.

**शुक्रान्मन्दविभागे भूमिस्त्रीसङ्ग्रही विषमशीलः।  
नृपजनितधनप्राप्तिः समानशौर्यान्वितो धनी भवति॥४४॥**

 *Sloka* 44. — In Saturn's Antara of Sukra's Dasa, the person will acquire land and wife. His disposition will not be good He will get money through royal favour. He will be earning wealth befitting his valour.

**अथ शनिदशान्तर्दशाफलानि॥**

**मन्ददशायां भानोर्दशापहारे सुखेतराणि स्युः।  
रिपुभयकलहोद्रिक्तो सुतदारविवर्जितोऽन्यदेशरतः॥४५॥**

 * Sloka* 45.—In the Sun's Apahara of Saturn's Dasa, the person concerned will experience all else except happiness. Danger from enemies, quarrels in abundance, desertion by one's wife and sons, and residence in foreign places—these will be the order of the day.

**मन्ददशायां चन्द्रे प्रविशति मातृक्षयो मनोदुःखम्॥  
भग्नोत्साही चपलो बन्धुक्लेशान्वितो दयाहीनः॥४६॥**

 Sloka 46.—During the Moon's Bhukti of Saturn's Dasa, the person's mother will pass away and thus affliction to the mind will be caused; and his enthusiasm will be retarded; he will become fickle.minded. He will further feel sorrow for the sake of his relations owing to their distress; he will finally become devoid of pity.

**मन्दात्कुजापहारे जायन्ते मृत्युरोगदुःखानि।  
स्थानपशुवित्तनाशः सुतदारविनाशनं वाऽपि॥४७॥**

 Sloka 47.—In the Apahara of Mars in Saturn's Dasa, there will arise miseries through death and disease. Loss of one's position, of cattle and of wealth or even the demise of one's own son or wife will happen.

**मन्दाद्बुधापहारे स्त्रीबालसमन्वितो धनी विद्वान्।  
सत्सेवी नृपदयितो वातश्लेष्मादि पीडितो भवति॥४८॥**

 Sloka 48.—In Mercury's Apahara of Saturn's Dasa, the person concerned will live with his wife and children He will command riches and will acquire learning. He will be doing service to the good people and will be liked by the king. He will be troubled by wind and phlegmatic diseases.

**जीवापहृतौ मन्दात् काव्यकलाज्ञानवान्नरेन्द्रधनी।  
बहुजनपूजितदेहो बहुभोगसमन्वितो महोत्साही॥४९॥**

 Sloka 49.—In Jupiter's Apahara of Saturn's Dasa, the person concerned will study poetry and acquire learning. He will get money from the king. He will be revered by many persons. He will enjoy all comforts, and will be over-enthusiastic.

**मन्दात् सितापहारे पत्नीपुत्रान्वितो धनाध्यक्षः।  
धर्मपरो रिपुहन्ता खाध्यायाध्यापको भवेन्नियतः॥५०॥**

 Sloka 50.—In the Apahara of Venus in Saturn's Dasa, he will live with his wife and children and will have plenty of money at his command. He will be intent in doing virtuous acts. He will overpower his enemies. He will study the Vedas and ultimately become a great preceptor.

**अथ दशान्तर्दशाविशेषफलानि॥**

**अन्तर्दशा यदा द्वित्रिचतुर्णामेकराशिसंस्थानाम्।  
प्रोक्तफलं प्रत्येकं त्यक्त्वा क्लेशांश्च कुर्वन्ति॥५१॥**

 Sloka 51.—When two, three, or four planets combine in a single Rasi, and each of their Antardasa sets in, their respective effects already stated above do not come to pass, but only affliction and unhappiness take their place.

**संयुक्तानां तु दशाक्षेत्रोच्चविवर्जिता सदा दुःखम्।  
जनयेत्प्रतापहीनं धनिन्न प्रेष्यान्वितं सरोगं च॥५२॥**

 Sloka 52.—And if in the above condition the said planets are not also occupying their own or exaltation Rasis, the person concerned will, during their Dasas, be experiencing always only sorrow. Further, he will lose all his original valour and riches, and he will be reduced to abject poverty, and will also be afflicted with diseases.

**सुखदारपुत्रवित्तं जनयुति तस्मात् त्रिकोणसंस्थस्य।  
बन्धुस्थितस्य हि दशामित्रारोग्यं सुखं धनं लभते॥५३॥**

 Sloka 53.—During the Dasa or Antardasa of a planet which is posited in his Moolatrikona Rasi, the person will be blessed with all happiness, wife, issue and wealth. In the case of a planet placed in the 4th house, when his Dasa or Antardasa sets in, the native will get friends, and will command sound health, happiness and wealth.

**जामित्रे स्त्रीद्वेष्यो रन्ध्रस्थे मृत्युरोगो वा।  
प्रकृतिदेशान्तरदशाफलमेवं चिन्तयेद्धि दैवज्ञः॥५४॥**

 Sloka 54.—When the Dasa of a planet occupying the 7th house progresses, the person concerned will hate women. Should the planet be in the 8th house, disease or even death will befall him. The effects of the Dasas and their Antardasas will generally have to be predicted by the astrologer in the manner stated above.

**लग्नाधिपतेस्तुल्यं लग्नदशायां फलं विनिर्देश्यम्।  
यमसदृशफलं वाच्यं दशासु राहोर्दशान्तरे काले॥५५॥**

 Sloka 55.—When the Lagna Dasa is progressing, the effects will be similar to those of its lord In the case of the Dasa and Antardasa of Rahu, the effects will be similar to those of Saturn.

**अर्केन्द्वारशनिभ्यो दशापहारे मृतिं वदेद्राहोः।  
वैषम्यान्मिश्रफलं प्रकृतिदशायां विशेषकरम्॥५६॥**

 Sloka 56.—When Rahu's Dasa or Antardasa is progressing in the Antardasa or Dasa of the Sun, Mars or Saturn, death may happen Owing to the contrary motion (of Rahu), in the otherwise ordinary Dasa, the nature of the Dasa will be specially otherwise.

**दाराधिपतिर्यस्मिन्नंशे पुरुषस्य जन्मकाले स्यात्।  
पाके तु वर्तमाने तस्याधिपतेः कलत्रसंयोगः॥५७॥**

 Sloka 57.—Note the Navamsa occupied by the lord of the 7th house in the person's nativity at birth. In the Dasa of the planet owning that Navamsa will the person get married (or join his wife).

**अष्टमपस्य दशायामधिपेन हृतेऽरिभस्य तस्यैव।  
मरणं हि तत्र काले निर्देश्यं क्रूरयोस्तयोर्नियतम्॥५८॥**

 Sloka 58.—During the Dasa of the lord of the 8th house and in the Apahara of the lord of the 6th, or vice versa death may occur. Whichever of the two is more malefic will surely bring about the event.

**राहुर्यस्मिन्नंशे जनने पुरुषस्य यस्य सभवति।  
तस्य दशायां मरणं शत्रोराह्वारकाले वा॥५९॥**

 Sloka 59.—Note the Navamsa occupied by Rahu at birth; the death of the native may happen during the Dasa of the planet owning that Navamsa and in the Apahara of his enemy.

**लग्नदशायां शत्रोर्लग्नस्य दशाहृतिर्यदा काले।  
निधनमवश्यं तस्मिन् सौम्यग्रहसंयुते न निर्देश्यम्॥६०॥**

 Sloka 60.—During the Lagna Dasa and in the Apahara of the planet inimical to the Lagna, the demise of the native will surely come to pass. But if a benefic planet should occupy the Lagna, this need not be predicted.

**होराजन्माधिपतेः शत्रुर्यो मृत्युसंस्थितो यस्य।  
तस्याष्टवर्गशून्ये दशाविभागे यदा तदा निधनम्॥६१॥**

 Sloka 61.—Find the lords of the Lagna as well as of the sign occupied by the Moon. Find also the planets which are inimical to these two lords. If, in the Ashtakavargas of the aforesaid planets, there be a Rasi devoid of benefic dots, during the Dasa or Apahara of the planet owning that Rasi, death will happen.

**विलग्नाधिपतिर्निचे निधने भार्गवोऽपि वा।  
तद्दाये व्याधिमाप्नोति क्रूरे लग्नं समाश्रिते॥६२॥**

 Sloka 62.—When the lord of the Lagna is in depression, or when Venus is posited in the 8th house, and if a malefic planet occupy the Lagna, the person concerned will meet with his end during the Dasa or Apahara of either the depressed planet referred to Venus.

**षष्ठाष्टमव्ययेशानां स्फुटयोगं गते शनौ।  
मृतिं भ्रातुर्विजानीयात् तत् त्रिकोणमथापि वा॥६३॥**

 Sloka 63.—Add the Sphutas of (1) the lord of the 6th; (2) the lord of the 8th and (3) the lord of the 12th . When Saturn in his transit traverses through the sign revealed by this sum or the sign's Trikona Rasi, the brother of the person concerned will meet with his death.

**लग्नाच्चन्द्रादथवा द्वाविंशदृगाणमाश्रिते जीवे।  
तस्याधिपत्रिकोणं याते वा मृत्युमादिशेत्तस्य॥६४॥**

 Sloka 64—When Jupiter in his transit traverses through the 22nd decanate reckoned from the Lagna or the Moon, or the triangular decanate with respect to the lord of the aforesaid 22nd decanate, the demise of the person concerned may be declared to happen.

**स्फुटेज्यराह्वोः संयोगराशिं यातो यदा गुरुः।  
तदा तु निधनं विद्यात् तत्त्रिकोणमथापि वा॥६५॥**

 Sloka 65.—Add the figures for Jupiter and Rahu. When Jupiter in his transit arrives at the Rasi signified by the sum or at a Rasi Trikona to it. the demise of the person concerned may be predicted.

**निधनेशद्वादशांशत्रिकोणे भास्करे मृतिः।  
निधनेशत्रिकोणे वा सूर्ये व्ययगते तु वा॥६६॥**

 Sloka 66.—Find in what Dwadasamsa Rasi the lord of the 8th house is posited. When the Sun in his transit arrives at a Rasi which is triangular to this, death may happen. The same event may also happen when the Sun traverses through Rasi triangular to the lord of the 8th house or a Rasi that is 12th from the Sun.

**स्फुटार्कस्य कलाः स्थाप्यास्ता राहुकलिकाहताः।  
चक्रलिप्ता (21600) हृतालब्धं योजयेत् स्फुटभास्करे॥६७॥**

**दृश्यते भास्करो यस्मिंस्तस्मिन्मासे मृतं वदेत्।  
तत्त्रिकोणगते वाऽपि चाणक्यवचनं यथा॥६८॥**

 Slokas 67-68.—Convert the Sphuta figures of the Sun into minutes. Multiply the same by the minutes denoting the figures for Rahu. Divide the product by 21600. Add the remainder thus obtained to the figures of the Sun. When the Sun in his transit arrives at the Rasi signified by this sum or a Trikona Rasi to this, death may take place. So has Chanakya stated.

**चन्द्रनिधनेश्वरस्य त्रिकोणमायाति शीतगौ निधनम्।  
योगं विधौ तयोर्वा तस्य नवांशत्रिकोणसंस्थे वा॥६९॥**

 Sloka 69.—Note the Rasi occupied by the lord of the 8th house reckoned from the Moon. When the Moon in her transit arrives at any one of the Rasis triangular to this, death may happen. Or, add the figures for the Moon and the lord of the 8th house. When the Moon in her transit arrives at a Rasi denoted by this sum, death may take place The same event may also happen when the Moon in her transit arrives at a Rasi triangular to the Navamsa Rasi denoted by the sum above referred to.

**जन्मविलग्नोपगताच्चन्द्रोपगतान्नवांशकादथवा।  
षष्ठे वाष्टमराशौ लग्नगते मरणमादेश्यम्॥७०॥**

 Sloka 70—When the Moon in her transit arrives at the following positions, death of the native may happen: (1) Lagna at birth (2) the Moon at birth (3) and (4) their respective Navamsa Rasis, (5) the 6th house from the Lagna and (6) the 8th house from the Lagna.

**जन्मलग्नाष्टमे राशौ जन्मलग्नोदयेऽपि वा।  
लग्ननीचोदये वाऽपि तेषां शून्योदये भृतिः॥७१॥**

 Sloka 71—(1) The 8th Rasi reckoned from the Moon or from the Lagna at birth (2) the Jinma Rasi or the Lagna Rasi at birth (3) the Lagna with a depressed planet at birth—when these Rasis are void of planets, death will happen.

**उत्तमयोगभवा ये तेषामन्तर्दशासु रिष्टफलाः।  
न भवन्ति ग्रहयज्ञैर्दानैर्होमैस्तथा जपैः खेटाः॥७२॥**

इति श्रीवराहमिहिरसुतश्रीपृथुपशोविरचिते होरासारेदशान्तर्दशा  
फलाध्यायोऽष्टादशः

 Sloka 72.—Whichever planets cause great Yogas to the person concerned, they will during their Antardasas cause the native to suffer from diseases. Such planets will not be appeased by Yagnas (sacrifices) and the like. Offering of gifts, worship to the Firegod by Homas or incantations of Japas will not prove efficacious in their cases.

Thus ends the 18th Adhyaya of Horasara entitled  
effects of Planetary Dasas aud Antardasas, a  
work composed by Sri Prithuyasas, the son  
of Sri : Varahamibira.  
**—————**

**एकोनविंशोऽध्यायः**

**अथ चान्द्रयोगाः॥**

**अथ तत्रादौ सुनफानफादुरुधुराधियोगास्तत्फलानि च।**

**चन्द्राद्धनगैः सुनफा व्ययगैरनफा तयोर्दुरुधुरा स्यात्।  
रविरहितैरधियोगः सौम्यैर्जामित्ररन्ध्ररिपुसंस्थैः॥१॥**

 Sloka 1—If the 2nd, the 12th and both the houses from the Moon be occupied by planets other than the Sun, the Yogas are termed **सुनफा** (Sunapha), **अनफा** (Anapha) and **दुरुधुरा** (Durudhura) respectively. When benefics occupy the 6th, the 7th and the 8th house (from the Moon or the Lagna), there results what is called the **अधियोग** (Adhiyoga).

**स्वार्जितधनोपभोक्ता धीमान् नृपसम्मतो नृपो वाऽपि।  
शास्त्रार्थवित्प्रवक्ता धर्मपरः ख्यातिमांश्च सुनफयाम्॥२॥**

 Sloka 2.—The person born in the Sunapha Yoga will possess self-acquired property, will be renowned for his wisdom and will be a king or his equal. He will have studied the Sastras and will be capable of interpreting them cleverly. He will be upright, and of great renown.

**नयविनयज्ञो धृतिमाननेकशास्त्रश्रमो महाविभवः।  
अनफायामुत्पन्नः स्त्रीणां वशगोऽतिमानी स्यात्॥३॥**

 Sloka 3—The person born in the **अनफा** ( Anapha) Yoga will be energetic, will have studied hard the sacred arts and possess great wealth; he will be loved by women and be very proud.

**भोगधनैश्वर्ययुतो वाग्मी रणवल्लभो गणाधिपतिः।  
व्यग्रो नृपतिस्त्यागी पशुमान् जातो दुरुधुरायाम्॥४॥**

 Sloka 4—Taking freely to the joys of life and blessed with abundance of wealth, the person born in the **दुरुधुरा** (Durudhura) Yoga will be eloquent, fond of war and chief of a body of men. He will even be a king. He will have a perplexed mind He will possess cattle and will be liberal.

**अधियोगे भवति नरो मन्त्री पूतनापतिश्च भूपालः।  
धनवान् बहुप्रतापी दीर्घायुर्ज्ञानवान् गतारिगणः॥५॥**

 Sloka 5.—The person born in an **अधियोग** (Adhiyoga) will become a minister or a commander of an army. He will be wealthy, very valorous, and long-lived. He will possess a demoness as his wife. He will have wisdom and will be bereft of enemies.

**सौम्यैरयत्नसिद्धं क्रूरैर्यत्नात्फलं समाप्नोति।  
पापाधियोगजाते विपरीतफलं विनिर्देश्यम्॥६॥**

 Sloka 6.—In the case of an Adhiyoga caused by benefics, the effects of the Yoga will come to pass without any effort at all. If the planets forming the Adhiyoga be malefic, the effects will be felt only after great exertion. When the planets causing the Adhiyoga are untoward, only contrary effects should be expected.

**कष्टं मध्ये श्रेष्ठं भानोः केन्द्रादिसंस्थिते शशिनि।  
चन्द्रे क्षीणे विफलं सुनफादिफलं न सम्यगायाति॥७॥**

 Sloka 7.—According as the Moon occupies a Kendra, a Panapara or an Apoklima house in respect to the Sun, will the resulting Yoga be miserable, medium or best. When the Moon is waning, the effects of Sunapha and other Yogas will not be highly powerful, but will only prove weak and useless.

**अथ केमद्रुमयोगस्तत्फलं च**

**ऐते योगा न स्युः केन्द्रे ग्रहवर्जिते शशाङ्काद्वा।  
केमद्रुमाख्ययोगस्तस्मिन् जातो नृपोऽपि भिक्षाशी॥८॥**

 Sloka 8.—These Yogas will not operate, should the Moon not occupy a Kendra (or when there are no planets in any of the Kendra houses reckoned from the Moon). Then, the Yoga termed Kemadruma sets in, the effects of which will be that even a king born under it becomes a beggar (a seeker of alms).

**अथ वेसिवास्युभयचरीयोगास्तत्फलानि च**

**सूर्याद्व्ययगैर्वासिर्वित्तगतैश्चन्द्रवर्जितैर्वेसिः।  
उभयस्थितैर्ग्रहेन्द्रैरुभयचरी नामको योगः॥९॥**

 Sloka 9.—When (3 or more) planets occupy the 12th house from the Sun, the resulting Yoga is called Vasi. If they occupy the 2nd house from the Sun, it is known as Vesi. In the two Yogas above referred to, the Moon is left out of consideration. If planets are posited on both sides (12th and 2nd) from the Sun, the Yoga is Ubhayachari.

**मन्दगतिर्मृदुवचनो दीनाक्षो बन्धुवत्सलो धृतिमान्।  
आयव्ययतुल्यकरो जातः स्याद्वेसियोगेऽस्मिन्॥१०॥**

* Sloka* 10.—The man born in this Vesiyoga will walk slowly. His speech will be soft; he will have a dejected look. He will be dear to his relations; he will be courageous. In the matter of income and expenditure, he will make both ends meet.

**पापमतिर्विकलाङ्गो निद्रालस्यश्रमान्वितो वासौ।  
पापैरेवं सौम्यैर्बलयुक्तैः सर्वसौख्यसम्पन्नः॥११॥**

* Sloka* 11.—One born in the Vasiyoga will be intent in doing sinful acts. He will be defective of some limb. He will be idle, sleepy and feel wearisome. The above will be the effects when the planets causing the Yoga are malefic; but if such planets be benefic and strong, the native will be endowed with all kinds of happiness.

**मुखरो ज्ञानी बलवान् स्वबन्धुनाथो नरेन्द्रदयितः स्यात्।  
नित्योत्साही वाग्मी धीमान्मनुजः शुभोभयचरीजः॥१२॥**

 *Sloka* 12.—The person born in an Ubhayachari Yoga will be talkative, learned, and strong. He will be a chief among his relations and a favourite of the king. When the planets constituting the Ubhayachari are benefic, the person concerned will be intelligent, ever active and eloquent.

**॥अथ** **सुशुभाशुभकर्तरीयोगास्तत्फलानि च॥**

**लग्नात्** **द्वितीयसंस्थैरर्केन्दुविवर्जितैः सुशुभः।  
अशुभाख्यो व्ययसंस्थैरुभयस्यैः कर्तरी समाख्याता॥१३॥**

 *Sloka 13*.—When (3 or more) planets other than the Sun and the Moon occupy the 2nd house from the Lagna, the Yoga is called **सुशुभ** (Susubha). When such planets occupy the 12th house, the Yoga is termed **अशुभ.** If they should occupy both the the 2nd and 12th, it is termed **कर्तरी**.

**सुशुभे योगे जातो धनवान् वनितादृतो नियमशीलः।  
नित्योद्युक्तश्चपलो भोगी न समञ्जसो धनाध्यक्षः॥१४॥**

 *Sloka* 14.—The person who has had his birth in the Susubha Yoga will be rich and will be closely devoted to a female. He will intently observe religious austerities; he will be ever active, but fickle-minded. He is always bent on sexual enjoyment. He will hold the post of a treasurer in a bank. He will not always be virtuous in his ways.

**अशुभे योगे जातो बलवान् स्वकुलाधिको महोत्साही।  
वक्ता परोपकारी त्यागी जनवल्लभोऽतिविख्यातः॥१५॥**

 *Sloka* 15.—The man born in the **अशुभ** (Asubha) Yoga will possess a strong body. He will be the head of his family and will be very energetic. He will be a good talker, will be very liberal and will help others. He will become very famous and greatly loved by the people.

**अत्युग्रो** **निर्विण्णो पितृमातृद्वेषणो निरुत्साहः।  
कर्तरियोगे पापैः परदेशरतो विषाग्निशस्त्रहतः॥१६॥**

 *Sloka* 16.—Very fierce, overcome with fear and sorrow, hating both the parents and devoid of energy will the peson be, who is born in the **कर्तरी** (Karthari) Yoga caused by malefic plants; he will dwell in foreign places and his end will be through poison, fire or weapons.

**अथ लग्नाधियोगस्तत्फलं च**

**षटसप्ताष्टममस्थैलग्नात् साम्यैरपापदृष्टयुतैः।  
लग्नाधियोग उक्तः पापैः सुखवर्जितभवति॥१७॥**

 *Sloka* 17.—When benefic planets occupy the 6th, the 7th and the 8th houses counted from the Lagna and are also free from the conjunction or aspect of malefics, **लग्नाधियोग**- Lagnadhiyoga results. If malefic planets be in the said houses, the person concerned will have no happiness at all.

**लग्नाधियोगजातो मन्त्री पृतनापतिर्धरस्वामी।  
बहुदारवान्विनीतो दीर्घायुर्धर्मवानशत्रुगणः॥१८॥**

 *Sloka* 18.—The person born in the लग्नाधियोग- Lagnadhiyoga will be a minister, a commander of an army or the chief of his clan. He will have many wives. He will be modest in his behaviour, will be long-lived, will lead a virtuous life and will have no enemies.

**अथ** **पर्वतयोगस्तत्फलं च**

**उदयान्तकर्महिबुके ग्रहयुक्ते रिःफनैधने शुद्धे।  
यः कश्चिन्नमगतो योगोऽयं पर्वतो नाम॥१९॥**

 *Sloka* 19.—When planets occupy the 1st, the 7th, the 10th and the 4th houses, and the 12th and the 8th houses are vacant, and the 9th house is occupied, the resulting Yoga is called पर्वत-Parvata.

**पर्वतयोगे** **जातो भूपालो धर्मवान् विनीतश्च।  
ग्रामपुरनगरकर्ता लोके श्रुतवान् युगान्तकीर्तिश्च॥२०॥**

 *Sloka* 20.—One who takes his birth in the Parvatha Yoga will be a king, virtuously disposed, and gentle in disposition. He will be the originator of a village, town or a corporation. He will be learned and endowed with a fame lasting till the end of the Yuga.

**अथ ध्वजयोगस्तत्फलं च**

**क्रमसंस्थितैर्ग्रहेन्द्रैर्बलवान् कश्चिद्ग्रहोऽन्यराशिगतः।  
ध्वजयोगो विज्ञेयस्तेषामेकोऽपि लग्नस्थः॥२१॥**

 *Sloka* 21.—If, at a birth, the planets in their order occupy the several houses and if any one out of them occupy another's Rasi, the Yoga is called **ध्वज** (Dhwaja ); and one at least of these should be in the Lagna. \[but see मृ.ना. p. 267\]

**प्रख्यातशौर्यकीर्तिर्ज्ञानी धनवान् नरेन्द्रदपितश्च।  
प्रचलितचेष्टाबुद्धिर्ध्वजयोगे जायते मनुजः॥२२॥**

 *Sloka* 22.—The person born in the **ध्वज** (Dhwaja) Yoga will be widely famed for his prowess. He will be rich, learned and a favourite of the king. He will have no fixity of mind.

**अथ कुण्डलयोगस्तत्फलं च॥**

**क्रमसंस्थितैर्ग्रहेन्द्रै रहितावेकान्तरस्थितौ खचरौ।  
अन्तरितौ वा बलिनौ योगोऽयं कुण्डलो नाम॥२३॥**

 *Sloka* 23.—When two strong planets are posited in two houses with one house intervening or two houses intervening, and the rest (of the planets) occupy in their order the other houses, the resulting Yoga is termed **कुण्डल** (Kundala).

**कुण्डलयोगे** **जातः परार्थभाक् क्षिप्रकोपपरितोषः।  
काव्यकलाखतिनिपुणो हीनायुः स्वल्पतनयश्च॥२४॥ **

 *Sloka* 24.—The person born in the Kundala Yoga will share other people's wealth, will be easily irritable and easily satisfied. He will be very clever in poetry and the arts. His life will be short and he will have only limited issue.

**अथ नाभसयोगाः॥**

**अथ तत्रादौ गोलयुगशूलकेदारपाशदामवीणायोगास्तत्फलानि च—**

**एकर्क्षगतैः सर्वैगोंलो द्विगृहाश्रितैर्युगाख्यश्च।  
त्रिगृहाश्रितैश्च शूलश्चतुर्गृहैश्च केदारः॥२५॥**

**पञ्चगृहस्थैः पाशः षट्गृहसंस्थैश्च दामयोगोऽयम्।  
सप्तगृहस्थैः सर्वैर्वीणायोगोऽतिविख्यातः॥२६॥**

 *Slokas* 25-26.—When all the planets occupy a single Rasi, the resulting Yoga is **गोल** (Gola). If they all occupy two Rasis, the Yoga is termed **युग** (Yuga). It is **शूळ** (Sula) when all the planets are distributed among three Rasis. If all of them are distributed among four houses, it is known as **केदार** (Kedara). When all the planets occupy five Rasis, the Yoga **पाश** (Pasa) is formed. If they should be spread over 6 houses, the Yoga will be **दाम** (Dama). When all the 7 planets occupy seven separate houses, the resulting Yoga is **वीणा** (Veena), of wide fame.

**वीणायोगे जातो विद्वान् विविधार्थभोगसम्पन्नः।  
स्वकुलश्रेष्ठो मतिमान् निपुणो नीतिप्रियो महोत्साही॥२७॥**

 *Sloka* 27.—The person born in the **वीणा** Yoga will be highly learned and will be endowed with wealth and all comforts. He will be intelligent and be the head of his clan. He will be very active and impartial.

**गोमान्** **सुखी दयालुः परकार्यरतोऽतिविश्रुतो धीमान्।  
आढ्यो रणप्रतापी जातः स्याद्दामनामके योगे॥२८॥**

 *Sloka* 28.—One born in the **दाम** (Dama) Yoga will possess cows, will be happy and of a generous disposition. He will be busy in helping others in their work. He will be a great scholar. He will possess a great intellect. He will be rich and courageous at battle.

**पाशे बहुव्ययार्त्तो निपुणो जनवल्लभोऽतिमेधावी।  
उत्साही नृपतीष्टो जातो गृहकार्यसंस्थितो भवति॥२९॥**

 *Sloka* 29.—The person born in the **पाश** (Pasa) Yoga will find it difficult to meet his heavy expenditure. He will be clever and greatly loved by the people. He is extremely intelligent and possesses great energy. He is liked by the king. He fully engages himself with the affairs pertaining to his house.

**बन्धूनां हितकारी कृषितो धनवान् स्वधर्मनिरतश्च।  
केदारे सम्भूतो जडस्वभावोऽतिमान्यश्च॥३०॥**

 *Sloka* 30.—The person born in the **केदार** (Kedara) Yoga helps his relations, and enriches himself through cultivating his lands He evinces keenness in attending to his religious duties. He is sluggish, but is very honourable.

**शूले जातो मतिमाननेकवार्तान्वितोऽतिरोगी स्यात्।  
क्रयविक्रयाद्धनी स्याद्द्विस्त्रीजनवल्लभोऽनपत्यः स्यात्॥३१॥**

 *Sloka* 31.—The person born in the **शूळ** (Sula) Yoga is intelligent. He has got many occupations to attend to. He is much troubled by sickness. He earns much money by trading. He has two wives, still, he has no children,

**युगयोगे जातः स्याद्विकलाङ्गो निष्ठुरो विगतलज्जः।  
बहुऋणभागी पुरुषो हीनायुः क्षीणबन्धुश्च॥३२॥**

 *Sloka* 32.—The man born in the **युग** (Yuga). Yoga has a defective limb. He is harsh in speech and is devoid of all shame. He contracts many debts, is short-lived and has almost no relatives.

**गोले** **जातोऽल्पायुर्निःखो विकलेक्षणो निजघ्नश्च।  
बन्धुसुतदारहीनः सदाटनः क्षुद्विवासबहुलश्च॥३३॥**

**कर्मायोदयधर्मादन्यत्र यथोक्तफलमेति।**

 *Slokas* 33,33½.—The person born in the **गोल** (Gola). Yoga will be short-lived. He will have have no wealth of his own. He will have a defective eye-sight, and has no wife, son or relation. He will kill his own child. He will be always on his legs and will be troubled by hunger. He will suffer long banishment.

 In the houses other than the 10th, the 11th, the 1st and the 9th, the respective effects already stated will come to pass.

**॥अथ केन्द्रयोगास्तत्फलानि च॥**

**लग्नकेन्द्रस्थितैः सर्वैर्योगो मङ्गलनामकः॥३४॥**

**मध्यकेन्द्रस्थितैः सर्वैर्मध्ययोग उदाहृतः।  
आपोक्लिमस्थितैः सर्वैः क्लीबयोग उदाहृतः॥३५॥**

**केन्द्रयोगा इमे ख्याता यवनैरप्युदाहृताः।**

 Slokas 34-35½.—When all the planets occupy houses which are Kendra with respect to the Lagna, the Yoga is named **मङ्गल** (Mangala). If they occupy the 10th (Madhya Kendra), the Yoga is termed **मध्य** (Madhya) If all the planets are posited in Apoklima houses (3rd, 6th, 9th and 12th ), the Yoga is called **क्लीब** (Kleeba). All these are called Kendra Yogas and have even been referred to by the Yavanas.

**मङ्गलाख्ये** **नरो जातो नित्यं कल्याणकारकः।  
वाग्मी प्रजावान् धीमांश्च दीर्घमायुश्च विन्दति॥३६॥**

 *Sloka* 36.—The person who has his birth in the **मङ्ङ्गल** (Mangala) Yoga will always be engaged in something auspicious. He will be clever in oratory. He will be blessed with children, will be intelligent and long-lived.

**मध्ये जातः प्रवासी च बन्धुक्लेशभयान्वितः।  
अस्थिरार्थोऽल्पपुत्रश्च दुर्मार्गमृतिमाप्नुयात्॥३७॥**

 *Sloka* 37.–He who is born in the **मध्य** (Madhya) Yoga will always be absent abroad. He will be troubled by fear and distress of his relations. He has no money of his own. His issue will not be many. He will meet with his end through bad ways.

**क्लीबे** **दुःखी प्रवासी च नीचस्त्रीकलहप्रियः।**  
**अल्पायुरल्पबुद्धिश्च प्रायो देशान्तरे मृतः॥३८॥**

 *Sloka* 38.—One who has his birth in the **क्लीब** (Kleeba ) Yoga will not stop in his native place. He will associate with base women, will be fond of quarrels and will be mean-minded. He will be short-lived. His death will occur in a foreign country.

**अथ रज्जुमुसलनलयोगास्तत्फलानि च॥**

**चरराशिस्थितैः सर्वै रज्जुयोग इति स्मृतः।  
मुसलः स्थिरराशिस्थैरुभयस्थैर्नलस्तथा॥३९॥**

 *Sloka* 39.—When all the planets occupy moveable Rasis, the Yoga is called Rajju. **रज्जु**. If they be posited in **(स्थिर)** immoveable signs, it is termed **मुसल** Musala. If they are in dual signs, (**नल** Nala) yoga is formed.

**अल्पश्रमो** **दरिद्रश्च मात्सर्यजनवल्लभः।  
रज्जुयोगे पुमाञ्जातो मध्यमायुश्च जीवति॥४०॥**

 *Sloka* 40.–The man born in the **रज्जु** (Rajju) Yoga will not work hard and will be poor. He will associate with malicious people. He will have medium life.

**मुसले** **सत्वसम्पन्नो दारपुत्रधनैर्युतः।  
सर्वार्थफलभोक्ता च ज्ञानवान् स्वजनप्रियः॥४१॥**

 *Sloka* 41.—The person born in the **मुसळ**- Musala Yoga will be strong and energetic. He will be wealthy and blessed with wife and sons. He will be learned, loved by his relations and he will enjoy life well.

**नलयोगोद्भवो धीमान् विकलाङ्गोऽल्पसन्ततिः।  
पुण्योत्साही धनाढ्यश्च मध्यमायुश्च जीवति॥४२॥**

 *Sloka* 42.—The person born in the **नल** Nala Yoga will be intelligent. He will have defective limb. His issue will be few. He will be virtuous, rich and energetic. His life will be medium.

**अथ** **मालासर्पयोगौ तत्फले च॥**

**सौम्यग्रहैः केन्द्रगतैर्मालायोगः स उच्यते।  
क्रूरैः केन्द्रगतैः सर्वैः सर्पयोग इति स्मृतः॥४३॥**

 *Sloka* 43.– When the benefics occupy Kendra houses, **माला**-Mala Yoga is formed. If all the maletics be posited in the Kendra houses, the Yoga is termed **सर्प**- Sarpa.

**मालायोगे** **समुत्पन्नो ज्ञानवानर्थवान् भवेत्।  
कर्मलग्नयुतैस्तैस्तु कुलनाशो न संशयः॥४४॥**

 *Sloka* 44.—The person born in the **माला**-Mala Yoga will be learned and rich. When these planets restrict themselves to the 10th and the 1st houses, the family will without doubt be destroyed.

**निःखो** **बहुप्रलापी च पितृस्थानविवर्जितः।  
परक्लशैश्च सन्तुष्टो ह्यल्पायुर्भुजगोद्भवः॥४५॥**

 *Sloka* 45.—The man born in the **सर्प** (Sarpa) Yoga will have no wealth, will prattle much and he will be ousted from his place and deserted by his father. He will feel delighted at others' sorrows. He will be short-lived.

**अथ** **षट्पदयोगस्तत्फलं च॥**

**लग्नतष्षट्भवनगैर्ग्रहैष्षट्पद उच्यते।  
तत्रोद्भूतो धनाध्यक्षः सर्वेभ्यः सारसङ्ग्रही॥४६॥**

 *Sloka* 46.—When planets range themselves in the first six houses from the Lagna, the Yoga is known as **षट्पद**-Shatpada One born in this Yoga will be master of much wealth and a hoarder of all essence.

**अथ वराहयोगस्तत्फलं च॥**

**उदयात्मजबन्धुस्थैर्वराहो योग उच्यते।  
क्षेत्रं वित्तं सुखं ज्ञानं लभते नात्र संशयः॥४७॥**

 *Sloka* 47.—If (all) the planets occupy the 1st, 5th and 4th houses, the **वराह**-Varaha Yoga is formed. Persons born in this Yoga will, without doubt, obtain lands, wealth, happiness and learning.

**अथ** **कण्टकयोगस्तत्फलं च॥**

**द्वित्रिबन्धुस्थितैः सर्वैर्ग्रहैः कण्टक उच्यते।  
तत्र जातो धनी विद्वान् मध्यमायुरसन्ततिः॥४८॥**

*Sloka* 48.—If all the planets occupy the 2nd, the 3rd and the 4th houses, the Yoga is called **कण्टक**—Kantaka. Persons born in the Yoga will be rich and learned. They will be middle-aged.

**अथ हलशृङ्गाटकाविहगयोगास्तत्फलानि च**

**लग्नव्ययस्यैर्हलयोगमेतं शृङ्गाटकं लग्नशुभात्मजस्यैः।  
लग्नास्तगैस्तं शकटं ब्रुवन्ति बन्ध्वास्पदस्थैर्विहगाख्ययोगम्॥४९॥**

* Sloka* 49 — If all planets occupy the 1st and 12th houses the **हल**-Hala Yoga is formed. If they occupy the 1st, 9th and 5th houses, the Yoga is **शृङ्गाटक-**Sringataka. When all the planets restrict themselves to the 1st and the 7th houses, the Yoga is **शकट** (Sakata); when they occupy the 4th and 10th houses, the Yoga is Vihaga or Pakshin

In the first line लग्नशुभेतरस्थैः is another reading.

**हलोद्भवः क्रोधपरोऽतिनिःखो हीनाङ्गमायुश्च कृषीवलः स्यात्।  
शृङ्गाटके मारुतकोपदेही महानुभावोऽल्पधनोऽपि जातः॥५०॥**

* Sloka* 50. —The man born in the **हल** (Hala) Yoga will be irascible, very poor, defective of some limb, and not longlived; he will be an agriculturist. One born in the **शृङ्गाटक -**Sringataka Yoga will be windy in temperament, and of an angry temper Though poor, he will be a great personage.

**शकटयोगसशुद्भवमानुषः शकटवत्सततं परिवर्तते।  
तनयदारविनाशनदुःखितो वृजिनवानलसो विकलेक्षणः॥५१॥**

* Sloka* 51. —The man born in the **शकट**-Yoga will always be changing like a wheel. His wife and children will perish before him. He will be wicked, idle and of weak sight.

**विहगोदितमानवः सुखी विविधार्थग्रहणेषु तत्परः।  
अनिवारितविक्रमो गणैः बहुवासः प्रियसंश्रयोऽन्यगः॥ ५२॥**

* Sloka* 52. —The person born in the fan-Vihaga Yoga will lead a happy life and will be intent in collecting various kinds of wealth. His courage and valour in battle are unsurpassed. He will have many resting places and he will have a loving welcome when abroad.

**अथ शङ्खचक्रसमुद्रमहेन्द्र योगास्तत्फलानि च॥**

**धर्मायोदय बन्धुभेषु सहितैः शङ्खः समस्तैर्ग्रह-  
र्लग्नाद्यैर्विषमर्क्षगैश्च सकलेश्चक्रं मुनीन्द्रा जगुः।  
वित्ताद्येषु तथैव षट्सु भवनेषूक्तो ग्रहैर्वारिधिः  
सर्वैर्द्व्यन्तरगैस्तथैव च खगैर्योगः शचीवल्लभः॥५३॥**

* Sloka* 53.—When all the planets occupy the 9th, the 11th, the 1st and the 4th houses, Sankha **(शङ्ख)** Yoga is formed. If all the planets occupy the 6 odd houses, the Yoga produced is Chakra **(चक्र),** so the sages have said. If the 7 planets be ranged in the 6 houses beginning with the 2nd house and separated from one another by an intervening (planetless) house, the resulting Yoga is called **समुद्र** (Samudra). When all the planets similarly occupy houses separated by two intervening houses, the Yoga is termed Indra **(इन्द्र).**

**धीमान् शङ्खसमुद्भवो गुणनिधिर्वीर्यान्वितो ज्ञानवां-  
श्चक्रे सर्वगुणालयो नरपतिः साम्राज्यसिंहासनी।  
जातोऽन्धो जनवल्लमोऽतिकृपणो वित्तेश्वरः सात्मजो  
विख्यातो बहुनामभिर्धनवतां श्रेष्ठो महेन्द्रोद्भवः॥५४॥**

**इति श्रीवराहमिहिरसुतश्रीपृथुयशोविरचिते होरासारे चान्द्रनाभसयोगाध्याय  
एकोनविंशः॥**

* Sloka* 54—The person born in the **शङ्ख **(Sankha) Yoga will be a repository of all good qualities, brave and learned; while the one born in the Chakra (**चक्र**). Yoga will be an altar where all merits congregate. He will be a king occupying a throre of imperial sway. The person born in the **महेन्द्र **(Mahendra) Yoga will be blind from birth, and loved by the people. He will be very miserly, possessing immense riches and blessed with children. He will be very famous, possess many titles of honour, and will be the biggest of the millionaires.

Thus ends the 18th Adhyaya of Horasara, entitled Chandra and  
Nabhasa Yogas, a work composed by Sri Prithuyasas, the  
son of Sri: Varahamihira.  
**————**

**विंशोऽध्यायः**

**अथ राजयोगाः॥**

**वर्गोत्तमगते चन्द्रे लग्ने वा चतुरादिभिः।  
ग्रहैर्निरीक्षिते तस्मिञ्जातो नरपतिर्भवेत्॥१॥**

* Sloka* 1—When the Moon or the Lagna has attained a Vargottama Navamsa and is aspected by four or more planets, the person born will be a king.

**अश्विन्यां लग्नगः शुक्रः सर्वग्रहनिरीक्षितः।  
करोति पृथिवीपालं निर्जितारातिमण्डलम्॥**

* Sloka* 2—When Venus occupies the asterism Aswini in the Lagna and is aspected by all the other planets, the person born will become a king who will conquer the entire hosts of enemies.

**शत्रुनीचग्रहांस्त्यक्त्वा कटुस्वस्थः सभार्गवः।  
लग्नेश्वरो बली यस्य स नरः पृथिवीपतिः॥३॥**

*Sloka* 3.—Note the planets which occupy their inimical or depression houses. If the lord of the Lagna and Venus occupy the 2nd house without being conjoined by any of the planets aforesaid, and at the same time be strong, the person born will rule over the earth.

**नीचांशकान् परित्यज्य त्र्यादिक्षेत्रोच्चसंस्थितः।  
करोति पृथिवीपालं निर्जितारातिमण्डलम्॥४॥**

* Sloka* 4.—When three or more planets occupy their own or exaltation Rasis and do not occupy depression Navamsas, a king will be ushered into the world who will conquer the entire host of enemies.

**नीचांशकान् परित्यज्य ज्यादिक्षेत्रोच्चसस्थितः।  
तेषामेकोऽपि लग्नस्थः करोति पृथिवीपतिम्॥५॥**

* Sloka* 5.— When three or more planets occupy their own or exaltation Rasis and one at least out of them occupy the Lagna, the person born in the Yoga will rule over the earth.

**चन्द्रे भौमे च लग्नस्थे धर्मकर्मगतेऽपि वा।  
गुरौ बलान्विते सूर्ये जातो नरपतिर्भवेत्॥६॥**

* Sloka* 6.—When the Moon and Mars are in the Lagna or occupy the 9th and 10th houses, and if Jupiter and the Sun be endowed with strength, the person born will become a ruler of men.

**दिवौकसां नृपं मन्त्री कुर्यात् पश्यन् बुधं सदा।  
शिरसा शासनं तस्य धारयन्ति नृपालकाः॥७॥**

* Sloka* 7.—When Jupiter casts a full aspect on Mercury, the Yoga will make the person born a king, whose orders will be implicitly obeyed by the other princes.

**अधिमित्रांशगश्चन्द्रो दृष्टो दानवमन्त्रिणा।  
निशायां कुरुते राज्यं नान्यग्रहनिरीक्षितः॥८॥**

*Sloka* 8.—If the Moon at night occupy a Navamsa owned by a very friendly planet and be aspected by only Venus and no other planet, the person born will become a king.

**स्वोच्चाधिमित्रभागस्थो दृष्टो वा देवमन्त्रिणा।  
शशी महीपतिं कुर्याद्दिवसे च न संशयः॥९॥**

 *Sloka* 9.—If, at a birth in day time, the Moon be placed in his own, exaltation Navamsa, or a very-friendly Navamsa, or be aspected by Jupiter, the Yoga will undoubtedly make the person born a king.

**सिंहे सूर्योदये यस्य शुक्रांशकविवर्जिते।  
कन्यागते बुधे जातो नीचोऽपि पृथिवीपतिः॥१०॥**

* Sloka* 10.—If, at Sunrise, sign Simha be rising and the Navamsa at the time be owned by any planet other than Venus, and if Mercury occupy Kanya, the person concerned, though base-born, will rule over the earth.

**मीने मीनांशके लग्ने शुक्रे जातो नृपो भवेत्।  
लग्नात्मजास्पदस्थौ तु कुजमन्दौ यदा तदा॥११॥**

* Sloka* 11. —When the last Navamsa of Meena is rising and Venus occupy it, the person born will become a king. The same will be the case if Mars and Saturn occupy the 5th and 10th houses.

**सम्पूर्णचन्द्रो भाग्यस्थो जातो राजा भविष्यति।  
अधिमित्रगृहे केन्द्रे जन्माधिपतिर्विलग्नपतियुक्तः।  
पश्यति बलपरिपूर्णो लयं स्यात् पुष्कलो योगः॥१२॥**

 *Sloka* 12.—If the Moon be full and occupy the 9th house, the person born will become a king. If the lord of the sign occupied by the Moon be in conjunction with the lord of the Lagna and occupy a Kendra synchronous with a sign owned by a planet very friendly to him, and if the said Moon should also aspect the Lagna, the Yoga formed is called **पुष्कल**- Pushkala.

**पुष्कलयोगे जाता जायन्ते भूमिपालका नियतम्।  
क्षितिपतिवंशे जाता मकुटच्छत्रान्विता भूपाः॥१३॥**

* Sloka*13.—People born in the **पुष्कल**—Pushkala Yoga will surely become rulers of the earth. Those who belong to the royal family will become emperors with crown and umbrella.

**जन्माधिपतिः केन्द्रे बलपरिपूर्णः करोति भूपेशम्।  
मित्रयुतो दृष्टो वा नीचान्वयसम्भवोऽपि राजा स्यात्॥ १४॥**

* Sloka* 14.—1f, at a birth, the planet owning the Rasi occupied by the Moon be posited in a Kendra house and have full strength, the person born will become an emperor. If the planet aforesaid be conjoined with or aspected by a friendly, planet, the person, though baseborn, will become a king.

**लग्नाधिपतिः स्वोच्चे पश्यन् मृगलाञ्छनं नृपं कुरुते।  
बहुगजतुरगबलौघैः क्षपितविपक्षं महाविभवम्॥१५॥**

* Sloka* 15.—If the Lord of the Lagna be in his exaltation and aspect the Moon, the person born in the Yoga will become a king who will have at his command a large number of elephants, horses, army, etc., and who will completely cripple the enemy of his power.

**लग्नं विहाय केन्द्रे सकलकलापूरितो निशानाथः।  
गुरुभृगुजाभ्यां दृष्टः करोति पृथिवीपतिं जातम्॥१६॥**

* Sloka* 16.—If the Moon with her digits full be posited in a Kendra house other than the Lagna and be aspected by Jupiter and Venus, the person born will become the ruler of the earth.

**विदधाति सार्वभौमं लग्नाधिपतिः स्वतुङ्गभे केन्द्रे।  
मुक्त्वारिनीचभागं नान्यग्रहमंयुतो नियतम्॥१७॥**

* Sloka* 17.—When the lord of the Lagna is in his exaltation, unconjoined with any other planet and occupies a Kendra house and is in a Navamsa other than his inimical or depression one, the Yoga will make the native concerned an emperor.

**चापाजसिंहराशिषु लग्नस्थो भूमिजो महीपालम्।  
जनयति च मित्रदृष्टः स्वबाहुबलनिर्जितारिबलपक्षम्॥१८॥**

*Sloka* 18.—If Mars occupy the Lagna identical with any one of the Rasis—Dhanus, Mesha and Simha, and be aspected by a friendly planet, a king will be born who will completely defeat the enemy and cripple his power.

**अश्विन्यनुराधासु स्थितः श्रविष्ठासु पार्थिवं भौमः।  
कुरुते दशमोपगते लग्नस्थे वा रवौ न नीचस्थे॥१९॥**

**\[अश्विन्यां यदि भौमः स्थितः श्रविष्ठानुराधयोर्भूपम्।  
कुरुते दशमोपगतो लग्नस्थो वा रविर्न नीचस्थः॥१९॥\]**

* Sloka* 19.—If Mars occupy Aswini, Anuradha or Dhanishta, identical with the 10th house, or if the Sun occupy the Lagna and be not in his depression sign, the Yoga will make the person born a King.

**जीवनिशाकरसूर्याः पञ्चमदुश्चिक्यधर्मगा वक्रात्।  
यदि भवति तदा राजा कुबेरतुल्यो धनेनासौ॥२०॥**

 *Sloka* 20 —When Jupiter, the Moon and the Sun occupy respectively the 5th, the 3rd and the 9th houses all reckoned from Mars, the person born will become a King possessing wealth like that of Kubera.

**यद्येकोऽप्युच्चगतो मित्रेण निरीक्षितो नृपं जनयेत्।  
मित्रयुतो लग्ने वा धनधान्यसमन्वितो नृपो भवति॥२१॥**

* Sloka* 21.—If one at least of the planets be exalted at a birth, and be aspected by another friendly planet, a King is ushered into the world. The same will be the case if the planet first aforesaid be conjoined with a friendly planet and be posited in the Lagna.

  Cf. जा. पा. VII—56.

**यद्येकोऽयुच्चगतो लग्ने स्वर्क्षे निशाकरो बलवान्।  
भूपतिवंशे जातं राजानं लोकपूजितं जनयेत्॥२२॥**

* Sloka* 22.—If one at least of the planets be exalted and the Moon endowed with strength occupy her own Rasi identical with the Lagna, the person if born in a royal family will become a king and be highly respected by the people.

**उपचयसंस्थैः सौम्यैः क्रूरैर्लग्नाश्रितैः खमध्यं वा।  
जातो भवत्यवश्यं धरणीश्वरवन्दितो नयज्ञश्च॥२३॥**

* Sloka* 23.—When all the benefic planets occupy the Upachaya (3, 6, 10, and 11) houses, and the malefics, the 1st or the 10th house, the person born will without doubt become a king saluted by other chiefs and be skilled in politics.

**लाभे व्यये वा भृगुजे बलान्विते देवेन्द्रतुल्यो नृपतिः प्रजायते।  
मृगोदये भूमिसुते सुनिर्मले शनैश्चरे धर्मगते व्ययस्थिते॥२४॥**

**दिवाकरे सप्तमगे सहेन्दुना चलस्वभावो नृपतिः प्रजायते।**

* Sloka* 24-24—If Venus in strength occupy the 11th or the 12th house, a king equal in prowess to Indra will be born. If sign Makara be rising and Mars occupy it with clear rays, and Saturn be posited in the 9th or the 12th house, a king will be born.

 If the Sun and the Moon occupy the 7th house, the person born will be a king and he will be fickle.minded.

 Cf.आ.पा VII—10, 52.

**आयारिसहजसंस्थैः पापैर्यदि जन्मपश्च शुमदृष्टः।  
भवति तदा धरणीशः समस्तजनवन्दितः साधुः॥२५॥**

* Sloka* 25.—When malefics are placed in the 11th, the 6th and 3rd houses and the lord of the sign occupied by the Moon be aspected by a benefic, the person born will be a king respected by all people and he will be of a righteous disposition.

**ओजस्थिताः सर्व एव ग्रहेन्द्राः शुक्ले चाह्नि त्वोजराशौ विलग्ने।  
जातस्याहुर्भाग्ययोगं च पुंसः स्त्रीणां चाहुस्त्वन्यथा जन्मकालम्॥**

* Sloka* 26.—Should a birth occur in day (as opposed to night), the Ascendant and all the planets being situated in odd signs and the Moon be waxing, the person born is said to have **भाग्य योग** Bhagya Yoga, if he be a male. The same Yoga should be declared in the case of female births, when the birth takes place in the night with all the the planets inclusive of the Ascendant posited in the even signs, and the Moon waxing.

Note: —अन्यथा is purposely not utilised in the case of waxing Moon to mean it as waning Moon, as I believe waxing Moon is an essential condition for **भाग्ययोग** for both the sexes. The distinction is brought about only in the birth being in day or night and planets being in odd or even signs as already explained in the Sloka.

 Cf.फ . दी. VI—14, 15.

**भाग्ये जातः पण्डितो यो नरोऽसौ कल्याणानां कारको भृत्यवांश्च।  
गान्धर्वज्ञो वारणानामधीशो द्रव्याध्यक्षो लग्नगे सौम्यखेटे॥२७॥**

* Sloka* 27.—The person who has his birth in the **भाग्य-** Bhagya Yoga will be well-versed, will take pleasure in doing all auspicious functions and he will possess many elephants and have immense wealth. These effects will fully come to pass when a benefic planet also occupies the Lagna.

**राजयोगेषु ये जाता निहीनास्तेऽपि पार्थिवाः।  
राजवंशोद्भवास्तेषु भवेयुर्भूमिपालकाः॥२८॥**

**इति श्रीवराहमिहिरसुतश्रीपृथुयशोविरचिते होरासारे राजयोगाध्यायो  
विंशः॥ **

* Sloka* 28.—Persons born under Raja Yogas though of low origin will yet become kings, while those born in a royal family under similar Yogas will become emperors and rule over the earth.

Thus ends the 20th Adhyaya entitled "Raja Yogas" in  
the work Horasara composed by Sri : Prithuyasas,  
son of Sri : Varahamihira.  
**—————**

**एकविंशोऽध्यायः**

**अथ ग्रहभावफलानि**

**अथ तत्रादौ रविभावफलानि**

**सूर्योदये न शान्तो नातिसुतो निर्घृणो रणश्लाघी।  
विकलेक्षणोऽल्पभाषी प्रवासशीलो भवेत्सुखी जातः॥१॥**

 *Sloka* 1.—A person born at Sun-rise will not rest quiet. He will not have many issue. He will have no pity ; he will be fond of war; will have a defective eye, sight ; will talk little ; and always be absent from home.

**मेषोदयेऽतिकीर्त्तिर्बलवांस्तिमिरेक्षणो धनी विद्वान्।  
नीचे प्रतापहीनो निःखप्रायोऽतिनचिकरः॥२॥**

* Sloka* 2.—The person born when sign Mesha is rising, will become very famous, energetic, of defective sight, rich, and learned. When the Sun is in his depression, he will be devoid of valour, will for the most part be poor and will be engaged in doing very mean acts.

**सिंहे स्ववंशनाथः कुलीरभे ज्ञानवाननेकमतिः।  
मीने स्त्रीजनसेवी कन्याया दारभाक् कृतघ्नश्च॥३॥**

* Sloka* 3.—When the Sun occupies Simha, the person born will be the head of his family. One born in sign Karkataka will be intelligent and have fixity of mind. When in Meena, he will be serving a woman. When the Sun occupies sign Kanya, the person will be devoted to his wife, and he will be ungrateful.

**धनभे तु वक्त्ररोगी धनवान् नृपचोरतोऽर्थहानिः स्यात्॥  
सहजेऽतिरोषबलवान् निजबन्धुषु सङ्क्षयोऽतिविख्यातः॥४॥**

* Sloka* 4.—If the Sun occupy the 2nd house, the person concerned will suffer from diseases in the face; he will be immensely rich, but will lose his wealth by a royal order or through theft. If the Sun should occupy the 3rd house, the person born will be irascible and he will possess great strength. He will meet with his end in the midst of his relations. He will attain great fame.

**निजधनहीनो हिबुके सन्तापी बुद्धिशौर्यसम्पन्नः।  
त्वरितवचनोऽतिमेधो नातिसुतो नार्थवान् खौ सुतगे॥५॥**

* Sloka* 5.—When the Sun occupies the 4th house, he will be of a provoking temperament. He will be intelligent and brave. He will speak rapidly, have a retentive memory. He will not have many issue, nor much wealth.

**नृपमन्त्री नेता वा बहुश्रुतः ख्यातिमान् रवौ षष्ठे।  
मदने विनोदशीलो दारद्वेषी न शान्तबुद्धिः स्यात्॥६॥**

* Sloka* 6. —He will be a minister to a king or a commander of an army, learned and famous, when the Sun occupies the 6th house. When the Sun is in the 7th house, the person born will be of a playful disposition; he will hate his wife. His mind will be agitated and not calm.

**विकलेक्षणोऽल्पसूनुर्निधने रोगान्वितोऽतिविख्यातः।  
धर्मपरो नमस्थे भानौ सुतदारवान् पितृद्वेषी॥७॥**

* Sloka* 7—When the Sun occupies the 8th house, the person concerned will have a defective sight and be troubled with disease. He will not have many issue. He will be very famous If the Sun be in the 9th house, the person will be intent in doing good deeds; he will be blessed with wife and sons. He will hate his father.

**नृपकर्मरतो दशमे शूरो रणवल्लभोऽतिविख्यातः।  
लाभे प्रभूतधनवान् विधेयभृत्यो नरेन्द्रदयितश्च॥८॥**

* Soka* 8.—When the Sun occupies the 10th house, the person will engage himself in the service of the king. He will be brave and a lover of war. He will be very widely known If the Sun be in the 11th house, it will inake the person very rich. He will have obedient servants; and he will become the king's favourite.

**व्ययभवने धनहीनो हीनाङ्गो दोषवान् विदेशरतः।  
नीचारिमांशकस्थे भानौ भावेषु दोषवृद्धिकरः॥९॥**

 *Sloka 9*.—When the Sun is in the 12th house, the person will have no wealth; he will be defective of some limb. He will have many faults; he will be intent in going to foreign countries. If the Sun should occupy a depression or inimical Navamsa, it will only intensify the faults and shortcomings of the Bhava concerned.

**अथ चन्द्रभावफलानि**

**मेषवृषकर्किलग्ने हिमगौ धनवान् सुखी नृपालसमः।  
वाग्बुद्धिवित्तरहितो लग्नस्थे नोक्तभेषु बलरहिते॥१०॥**

 * Sloka 10*.—If at a birth the Moon occupy the signs Mesha, Vrishabha, or Karkataka identical with the Lagna, the person concerned will be rich, happy and equal to a king. When the Moon occupies any other sign identical with the Lagna, the person will be devoid of speech, intellect and riches and will have no strength too.

**धनगे बहुप्रतापी धनवान् वनितादृतोऽल्पसन्तुष्टः।  
पिशुनो दयाविहीनो मायावी विक्रमाश्रिते शशिनि॥११॥**

 * Sloka 11*.—When the Moon occupies the 2nd house, the person will be very powerful, rich, loved by a damsel and satisfied with small favours. When the Moon s in the 3rd house, the person will be slanderous and wicked; he will be devoid of mercy and deceitful.

**मृष्टान्नग्विनीतः स्त्रीलोलः सौख्यभाक् सुखस्थेन्दौ।  
स्त्रीबुद्धिसत्त्वयुक्तो बहुश्रमोत्पन्नवित्तवान् सुतगे॥१२॥**

 *Sloka 12*.—When the Moon is posited in the 4th house, the person concerned will eat agreeable meals; he will be modest, longing for women and will be happy. He will be blessed with wife, intelligence and strength. He will amass money with great difficulty.

**षष्ठेऽलसो दरिद्रो बहुशत्रुः सोदरादिदमनश्च।  
स्त्रीदयितो नृपनेता प्रदानशीलोऽस्तगे निशानाथे॥१३॥**

 *Sloka 13*.—The man having at his birth the Moon in the 6th house will be lazy, poor and have many enemies; he will be controlling his after—borns. When the Moon at a birth occupies the 7th house, the person concerned will be fond of his wife; he will be a commander in a king's army ; and he will be liberal in his gifts.

**धनवान् निधने भोगी हिमगौ ज्ञानी प्रतापबहुलः स्यात्।  
धर्मप्रियोऽतिभाषी नवमे स्त्रीचञ्चलो धनाध्यक्षः॥१४॥**

  *Sloka 14*.—if at a birth the Moon occupy the 8th house, the person will enjoy life; he will be rich, intelligent and very powerful. He who is born with the Moon in the 9th house will be very garrulous and will long for women ; he will command immense wealth.

**सर्वोपायैर्धनवान् दशमे हिमगौ विदग्धयुवतीशः।  
लाभे धनी सुविद्वान् गोमान् नृपसम्मतो विनीतश्च॥१५॥**

 * Sloka 15*.—The person who has at his birth the Moon in the 10th house will become rich by all possible ways. He will become the husband of a young female who is very shrewd. When the Moon occupies the 11th house, the person will be rich, and very learned. He will possess cows. He will be esteemed by the king and he will be modest in his disposition.

**नयनातुरोऽङ्गहीनो व्ययगे स्त्रीदोषवाननैकमतिः।  
क्षेत्रोञ्चशस्तपक्षे व्ययगे हिमगौ सुखी धनी भवति॥१६॥**

 * Sloka 16*.—A man with feeble eyes and a defective limb will the person be who has at his birth the Moon in the 12th house. He will suffer on account of women. He will have no fixity of mind. In the case of the Moon in the above position and occupying her own or exaltation Rasi, the person will be happy and will become rich.

**अथ कुजभावफलानि॥**

**भौमोदये क्षताङ्गः शूरो बलवान् स्वमानशौर्ययुतः।  
चपलोऽल्पायुः क्रोधी वित्तरुगार्त्तोऽलसो भवेज्जातः॥१७॥**

* Sloka 17.—*If, at a birth, Mars occupy the Lagna, the person concerned will have a wounded limb; he will be brave and strong. He will be rich, respected and powerful. He will be fickle-minded; will be short-lived, irascible, lazy and troubled by a bilious disease

**धनगे बहुव्ययार्त्तो विकृताङ्गो निष्ठुरोक्तिमान् प्रोक्तः।  
भ्रातृद्वेषी सहजे क्लेशात् सम्प्राप्तवित्तवान् सुभगः॥१८॥**

* Sloka 18.*—When Mars occupies the 2nd house, the person will have a very heavy expenditure, have a deformed limb, will speak harshly, will hate his brother, will become rich through earnings by very hard labour, and will be amiable.

**परगृहसंश्रयशीलो रोगी सुखगे धनान्वितो भौमे।  
दुःखात्मको विशीलो मेधावी पञ्चमेऽतितीक्ष्णकरः॥१९॥**

* Sloka 19.—*With a disposition to dwell in other people's houses will the person be at whose birth Mars occupies the 4th house. He will be rich, troubled by disease, always afflicted (grieved), and bad in nature. He will be very intelligent.

**षष्ठेऽल्पबुद्धिरलसो जामित्रे स्त्रीजितो विदेशरतः।  
निधने तु कृच्छ्रजीवी सुतदारविवर्जितो नूनम्॥२०॥**

* Sloka 20*.—Mars in the 6th house makes the man lazy and mean-minded. When he is in the 7th, he will be under his wife's influence and absent in foreign places. When Mars occupies the 8th house, the person will have a miserable existence, being deserted by his wife and children.

**मार्गघ्नो नवमस्थे दशमे जनवल्लभोऽतिमेधावी।  
लाभे धनी गुणाढ्यो व्ययगे पतितोऽङ्गहीनो वा॥२१॥**

* Sloka 21*.—When Mars is in the 9th house, the person will kill men (going) in the road; Mars in the 10th house will make the person concerned very learned and loved by the people. When Mars occupies the 11th house, the person will be of excellent qualities. Lastly, when Mars is in the 12th, the person will be fallen or defective of some limb.

**अथ बुधभावफलानि॥**

**विद्वान् धनी दयावान् बुधलग्ने वित्तगे धनी सुभगः।  
स्व(सु)गुणोपार्जित विभवो दुश्चिक्ये ज्ञानवान् धनी सुखगे॥२२॥**

* Sloka 22.—*When Mercury at birth occupies the Lagna, the person concerned will be very learned, rich and tender-hearted. If Mercury be in the 2nd house, the native will be wealthy and amiable. When Mercury occupies the 3rd house, the person will enrich himself through his own good qualities. If Mercury be posited in the 4th house, he will be rich and learned.

**मेधावी वाङ्मधुरो बुद्धिस्थे सोमजे बुधानुमतः।  
षष्ठे विवादशीलो लोकद्वेषी विदेशवासी च॥२३॥**

* Sloka 23*.—When Mercury occupies the 5th house, the person born will be sweet tongued, intelligent and admired by the learned. When Mercury is in the 6th house, the person concerned will be of a quarrelling disposition. He will hate the people and will be living in foreign countries.

**धर्मज्ञोदारमतिः सप्तमगे लोकविश्रुतः सौम्ये।  
ख्यातो धनाधिनाथो निधने सौम्ये नृपालको धीमान्॥२४॥**

* Sloka 24*.—If Mercury occupy the 7th house, the person born will be familiar with all religious observances; and he will have a liberal mind and be world-famous. When Mercury is in the 8th house, the person concerned will be intelligent, rich and famous ; he may be a king.

**धर्मे प्रतापबहुलो धनधान्यसमन्वितो महोत्साही।  
दशमे वित्ताधीशो दानपरो ज्ञानवान् यशस्वी च॥२५॥**

* Sloka 25*.—When Mercury occupies the 9th house, the person born will be very courageous. He will be blessed with wealth and corn. He will be very persevering. When Mercury is in the 10th house, he will own immense riches, will be liberal in his gifts, very learned and famous.

**लाभे बहुप्रकारैर्धनवान् वनितादृतः सुशीलश्च।  
व्ययगे बुधे नृशंसः कृपाविहीनो व्ययान्वितश्चण्डः॥२६॥**

* Sloka 26*.—When Mercury occupies the 11th house, the person born will become rich by various means, will be revered by women and be of a good disposition. If Mercury occupy the 12th house, the person concerned will be cruel, bereft of mercy and wrathful. He will be spending much.

**अथ गुरुमावफलानि॥**

**जीवोदये चिरायुझीनी सुखवान् न नीचराशिस्थे।  
धनगे धनी सुवक्ता दयापरो देवतार्चनाभिरतः॥२७॥**

* Sloka 27*.—When Jupiter occupies the 1st house, the person born will be long-lived, and happy. The above will not hold good when the Rasi occupied is his depression sign. When Jupiter is in the 2nd house, the person concerned will be a good talker, rich, compassionate and engaged in the worship of the Gods.

**दुःशीलो धनहीनो दुश्चिक्ये भ्रातृबन्धुदोषकरः।  
सुखगे सुखी सुदारो भोक्तासनयानवाहनाध्यक्षः॥२८॥**

* Sloka 28*.—When Jupiter occupies the 3rd house, the person concerned will be of a bad disposition and without wealth. He will do harm to his brothers and relatives. If Jupiter be in the 4th house, the person will be happy with a good wife and enjoying good food, dwelling, vehicles, horses, etc.

**सत्सुतदारः सुभगो मेधावी वाक्पटुश्च बुद्धिस्थे।  
अरिगे शत्रुविहीनो नृपस्य मन्त्री नयान्वितो जीवे॥२९॥**

* Sloka 29*.—When Jupiter is posited in the 5th house at a birth, the person concerned will be blessed with a good son and a good wife. He will be very learned, charming and eloquent. If Jupiter be posited in the 6th house the person born will have no enemies. He will be a minister and will be endowed with prudence.

**शुभदारपुत्रयुक्तो जामित्रे पूर्वतोऽधिको विद्वान्।  
चिरजीवी निधनस्थे भूपालो ज्ञानवान् गतारिगणः॥३०॥**

 *Sloka 30*.—If Jupiter occupy the 7th house, the person born will be blessed with a good wife and sons and he will become more learned than before. When Jupiter is in the 8th house, he will be blessed with long life, be a king and learned and he will have no enemies.

**बहुभाग्ययुतो धीमांस्तेजस्वी धर्मवान् धनी धर्मे।  
विख्यातो दशमस्ये सत्कर्मरतो धनाधिनाथश्च॥३१॥**

* Sloka 31—*When Jupiter occupies the 9th house, the person will be blessed with all kinds of happiness. He will be learned, powerful, virtuous and wealthy; in the 10th house, the person will attain great fame, will be engaged in doing good acts and exceedingly wealthy.

**बहुविधलाभो लाभे कोशाधिपतिः कुलाधिको विद्वान्।  
व्ययगे देवाचार्ये हीनाङ्गो धर्मनृत्यगतवित्तः॥३२॥**

 * Sloka 32*.—When Jupiter occupies the 11th house, the person born will have gains from various sources. He will be master of immense wealth. He will be the chief of his clan and very learned. When Jupiter is in the 12th house, he will have a defective limb. He will spend money in charity and in the art of dancing.

**अथ शुक्रभावफलानि**

**कन्दर्पसमो गुणवान् भृगुलग्ने स्त्रीजितो धनी विद्वान्।  
नयविनयज्ञो धनवान् धनगे सुमुखो दयापरो भवति॥३३॥**

* Sloka 33*.—When Venus occupies the Lagna, the person born will be equal to Cupid (in appearance) and will have very good qualities. He will be influenced by women, will be wealthy and learned. When Venus is in the 2nd house, the person concerned will be prudent, of good breeding, wealthy, with a cheerful face and merciful.

**नीचस्त्रीभोगरतो दुश्चिक्ये वित्तभोगरहितश्च।  
सुखगे सुखी क्षमावान् दयापरो दारपुत्रवान् भृगुजे॥३४॥**

 *Sloka 34*.—The person at whose birth Venus is in the 3rd house will seek the company of a low-born woman. He will have neither wealth, nor enjoyment. When Venus occupies the 4th house, the person born will be happy, of a forgiving disposition, merciful and will be blessed with wife and children.

**नृपमन्त्री नेता वा स्त्रीजनको ज्ञानवान् सिते धीस्थे।  
शत्रुक्षयी च षष्ठे मायावी रोगवान् गतार्थसुतः॥३५॥**

 * Sloka 35*.—When Venus is posited in the 5th house, the person born will be a king's minister or a military commander. He will be the father of daughters. He will be learned. If Venus be in the 6th house, his enemies will dwindle; he will be deceitful and sickly. He will lose his wealth and children.

**स्मरनिपुणो जामित्रे मित्रद्वेषी प्रधानजनबन्धुः।  
निधने स्वभावबहुलो रोगी सुतदारवांश्च सन्तुष्टः॥३६॥**

 * Sloka 36.—*If Venus occupy the 7th house, the person born will be clever in coition. He will hate his own friends. He will be related to prominent men. When Venus occupies the 8th house, the person born will be a man of large heart. He will be sickly and possess wife and children; and he will be contented.

**धीधर्मभोगयुक्तो नवमे सुतदारवान् सिते बलिनि।  
स्त्रीदयितो नृपमन्त्री दशमे शुक्रे जलादिधर्मपरः॥३७॥**

 *Sloka 37*.—When Venus is strong and occupies the 9th house, the person born will be intelligent, righteous in disposition and command all comforts. He will live with his wife and sons. When Venus is in the 10th house, he will be loved by women ; he will be a king's minister, will construct tanks and wells for the use of the public.

**प्राज्ञो धनी दयावाल्ँलाभे शुक्रेऽतिलाभसन्तुष्टः।  
स्त्रीलोलो व्ययसंस्थे धर्मव्यसनी स्वकर्मपरिहीणः॥३८॥**

**क्षेत्रोच्चव्ययभवने धनवान् प्रसिद्धयुवतीशः।**

* Slokas 38-381—*When Venus is posited in the 11th house, the person born will possess great wisdom, will be rich, and merciful, will have great gains and will be contented. When Venus occupies the 12th house, he will be sporting with women, will be virtuous, but When unlucky and deficient in his (religious) duties. Venus is exalted in the 12th house or is in his own house there, the person born will be wealthy, famous and will have a young and famous damsel as his wife.

**अथ शनिभावफलानि॥**

**सौरोदयेऽतिरोगी बाल्ये मलिनोऽटनो नृशंसश्च ॥ ३९ ॥**

**स्त्रीवञ्चनोऽनिलात्मा निःखप्रायोऽङ्गदीनो वा ।  
स्वोच्चे स्वकीयभवने कुलाधिको ज्ञानवान् नरेन्द्रधनी ॥ ४० ॥**

* Slokas 39-40—*If at a birth, Saturn be in the Lagna, the person concerned will during his early age be very sickly and unclean. He will be roaming about and wicked. He will dupe women. He will be of a windy temperament. He will generally be without any money or have a defective limb When Saturn is exalted or posited in his own place, the person born will be a chief of his clan, well-educated, possess wisdom; he will be a king or a rich personage.

**पितृधनहीनो धनगे स्वमानशौर्यान्वितो धनी विद्वान्।  
शूरो दयाविहीनो हास्यरतोऽनादरश्च दुश्चिक्ये॥४१॥**

* Sloka 41*.—When Saturn is in the 2nd house at a birth, the person concerned will have no patrimony and hewill be brave, command self-respect and become rich and learned. When Saturn occupies the 3rd house, he will be brave, without compassion, and he will indulge much in mirth and laughter. He will command no respect.

**बन्धुजनपीडितात्मा बन्धुस्थे नातिपुत्रवान् न सुखी।  
मन्दमतिरल्पपुत्रो नेत्ररुगार्त्तोऽटनः शनौ सुतगे॥४२॥**

* Sloka 42*.—When Saturn is in the 4th house, the person born will be troubled by his near relations. He will not have many issue nor will be happy. If Saturn be in the 5th house, he will be dull-witted, have a few sons, and suffer from eye-complaint. He will be roaming about.

वन्धुसुखनेत्रहीनो नातिसुतो नातिवित्तवान् is another reading.

**षष्ठे सहायशीलो रिपुरोगविवर्जितोऽतिविख्यातः।  
नीचश्चपलो दुःखी जामित्रे सूर्यजे कुदाररतः॥४३॥**

* Sloka 43—*When Saturn occupies the 6th house, the person born has a disposition to help others. He will have no enemies. He will be free from diseases and he will be very widely famed. When Saturn is in the 7th house, the person born will be base, fickle-minded and will be addicted to a bad wife.

**निधने धनवान् रोगी नातिसुतो नेत्रदुर्बलश्चपलः।  
धर्मध्वजोऽतिनिपुणो मेधावी नीतिपुत्रवान् नवमे॥४४॥**

* Sloka 44*.—The man born with Saturn in the 8th house will have money at his command, suffer from sickness, will not have many issue; he will have a weak sight, and be fickle-minded. When Saturn occupies the 9th house, the person born will be a religious hypocrite, very clever, intelligent, decorous and will have children.

**दशमे शनौ सुबुद्धिर्धनवान् स्वकुलाधिकः सुखी भवति।  
प्रभुशीलो विख्यातो लाभे विज्ञानशास्त्रकुशलश्च॥४५॥**

* Sloka 45.—*The person, at whose birth Saturn occupies the 10th house, will behave like a gentleman will be rich, happy and head of the family. He will be widely-known, learned in the arts and sciences and of Dordly virtues, when Saturn is in the 11th house.

**दोषकरो व्ययसंस्थे बहुव्ययार्त्तोसुखी दिनेशसुते।  
क्षेत्राधिपयुतभावे पुष्टफलं पापसौम्ययोस्तुल्यम्॥४६॥**

 * Sloka 46*.—When Saturn is posited in the 12th house, the person born will impute faults to others, will spend much beyond means, and be miserable. When Saturn occupies a house along with its lord, the effect of the Bhava will be full and will be in proportion to the nature—good or bad—of the two planets.

**नीचारिभवनसंस्थो ग्रह उक्तं तत्फलं विनाशयति।  
यत्प्रोक्तं भावफलं लग्नादीनां तथैव चन्द्रर्क्षात्॥४७॥**

 * Sloka 47.—*When a planet occupies his depression or inimical sign, the effect produced from that house will vanish away. Whatever effects have been described above as arising out of the Lagna and other bhavas, the same will also hold good for the respective 12 bhavas when reckoned from the house occupied by the Moon.

**भावफलं च नराणां वक्तव्यं चन्द्रमूर्त्तिफलम्।  
एकैकमेकराशौ भावफलं सम्यगेव वक्तव्यम्॥४८॥**

**द्व्याद्यैरेकर्क्षगतैर्लग्रादिफलं न सम्यगायाति।**

  इति श्रीवराहमिहिरसुतश्रीपृथुयशोविरचिते होरासारे ग्रहभावफलाध्याय एकविंशः॥

 *Sloka 48.—*The effects arising from the bhavas may well be predicted when reckoned from the Chandra Lagna. The Bhavaphala for each and every Rasi so reckoned may be predicted with great accuracy. If two or more planets be posited in a single Rasi, the effects arising from that Bhava counted from the Lagna will be from wide and not be accurate.

Thus ends the 21st Adhyaya entitled "Effects of Planets  
in the several Bhavas" in the work Horasara  
composed by Sri: Prithuyasas, son of  
Sri: Varahamihira.  
**————**

**द्वाविंशोऽध्यायः**  
**अथ कर्माजीवः**

**स्वस्य स्वभावजनितं प्रकारभेदैर्धनं समाप्नोति।  
केषाञ्चिद्दशमस्थैश्चन्द्राद्भानोर्नवशिकादथवा॥१॥**

 *Sloka 1*.—A person gets wealth in various ways suited to his innate nature. According to some, wealth is acquired through planets posited in the 10th house reckoned from the Lagna, from the Moon or the Sun or their Navamsas.

**पितृमातृसहजबान्धवगुरुयोषित्प्रेष्यजातिभिर्वित्तम्।  
लभते दशमर्क्षगतैः सूर्याद्यैस्तद्विकारभेदैर्वा॥२॥**

 * Sloka 2.—*There is acquisition of wealth from the father, mother, brother, a relative, an elder, a wife or an inferior according as the Sun or any other planet taken in order occupies the 10th place from the Lagna, the Sun or the Moon; or from other kinds of relatives.

**ग्रहरहिते दशमगृहे चन्द्राद्भानोस्तथा तयोर्बलिनः।  
तदधीशराशिनाथस्वभावलब्धोपजविनं कुरुते॥३॥**

 * Sloka 3*.—If the 10th house be planetless, then the livelihood will be through that prescribed for the ruler of that house (or of the ruler of the Navamsa occupied by the planet owning the 10th place) reckoned from the Lagna, from the Moon or from the Sun, whichever is stronger or that prescribed for the lord of the Rasi in which the lord of the above 10th house is posited.

**अकांश फलवृक्षैर्भेषज्यैधार्तुविक्रयः शिल्पैः।  
द्यूतानृतशाठ्यकरैर्भूपैर्वा वित्तमाप्नुयात् सततम्॥४॥**

 *Sloka 4*.—If the Sun be the lord of the Navamsa occupied by the lord of the 10th Bhava, the person concerned will earn a living by dealing in fruits, trees, medicine, metals and handicrafts He will obtain money by gambling, by uttering falsehood, by cheating or through kings.

**चन्द्रांशे मणिपतैः कृषिजलवस्त्रदिभिर्धनं लभते।  
गोमहिषशर्कराद्यैः स्त्रीमङ्गान्मन्त्रदेवताद्वाऽपि॥५॥**

 * Sloka 5*.—If the Navamsa under reference be that of the Moon, the person gains a living by dealings in pearls, ships, by agriculture, water, clothes and the like, cows, buffaloes, sugar, or through the medium of women, incantations, or by worshipping deities.

**उपदेशमन्त्रकुशलैः साहसशस्त्राग्निमेषजैर्वाऽपि।  
आपणविक्रयकुशलैर्भौमांशे क्षत्रियादितो धनवान्॥६॥**

 * Sloka 6*.*—*If the Navamsa in question belong to Mars, the person gains a livelihood by teaching, by proficiency in Manthra's, an aggressive bold act, weapon, fire or drug, trading in things in the market, and from Kshatriyas.

**लिपिलेख्यकाव्यगणितैर्द्यूतैर्नृतैः स्तवादिभिर्वित्तम्।  
तदधीशे सौम्यांशे दानाध्ययनादिभिः प्रियालापैः॥७॥**

 *Sloka 7*.—When the Navamsa referred to belongs to Mercury, the person born will earn his livelihood by writing, drawing mathematics poetry, gambling, dancing and panegyrics, by making gifts, studying and pleasant narrations.

**अध्ययनदेवतार्चनमन्त्रजपान्मन्त्रवृत्तिभिर्धनवान्।  
कालज्ञाननिमित्तैर्नृपप्रसादैस्तथा गुरोरंशे॥८॥**

 *Sloka* 8.—When the Navamsa in question belongs to Jupiter, the person born will obtain his livelihood by the chanting of the Vedas, worshipping Gods, chanting Mantras, exposition of the Mantras, by astrology and by royal favour.

**गोमहिषाश्वगजाद्यैस्त्रीसङ्गै**गै**षधैरलङ्कारैः।  
नृत्तादिगीतकुशलैः शुक्रांशे वित्तवान् सुखी भवति॥९॥**

 *Sloka* 9—If Venus be the lord of the Navamsa in question, the person born will be happy and earn his livelihood through cows, buffaloes, horses, elephants, through the association of women, through herbs, by decorations, and dancing.

**सौरांशे फलमूलैः पत्रैर्भारोद्वहैः श्रमैर्धनवान्।  
नीचप्रेष्यजनाद्यैर्धान्यकृधान्यादिविक्रयैर्वाऽपि॥१०॥**

**... ... ... ... ... ... ... ... श्रमवधभारादिनीचकृत्यैश्च।  
तिललवणधान्यशाकैस्तृणकाष्ठजलादिभिर्धनं लभते॥११॥**

 *Slokas* 10-11—If the Navamsa referred to be owned by Saturn, the person born will earn a living through fruits and roots, leaves, by bearing burdens, by doing wearisome work, by trading through low persons, menials, grains and low corn. He will obtain money through base actions and by bearing burdens, by killing, thro sesamum salt, “coriander, vegetables, grass, firewood, water and the like.

**अंशाधिपोऽतिबलवानयत्नतोऽर्थागमं सुखं कुरुते।  
अंशाधिपोऽतिनीचे प्रोक्तफलं स्वल्पमेव विदधाति॥१२॥**

 *Sloka* 12—If the lord of the Navamsa referred to above be very strong, he will earn money without any effort at all and be happy. If the Navamsa–lord be in his extreme depression, the several effects described above will reveal themselves only very little.

**राश्युक्तदिग्विभागे देशं सञ्चिन्तयेत् स दैवज्ञः।  
लग्नाच्च दशमराशेः स्वभावदेशं विनिर्दिशेदथवा॥१३॥**

 *Sloka* 13.—The astrologer should think of a country lying in a direction signified by the particular Rasi; or the nature and country of the native may be predicted through the Rasi that is 10th from the Lagna.

**स्वस्वामिदृष्टयुक्तं स्वदेशफलदायकं मुनय ऊचुः।  
अन्येन सहितदृष्टं परदेशफलप्रदं प्राहुः॥१४॥**

 *Sloka* 14.—Sages have declared that if the said Navamsa be aspected by or conjoined with its lord, the earnings will be in his own native country. If it be conjoined with or aspected by another, the earnings will be in a foreign country.

**तदधीशे चरभांशे प्रवासतोऽर्थागमं सुखं लभते।  
स्थिरभांशके स्वदेशादुभयांशे सर्वतो धनप्राप्तिः॥१५॥**

 *Sloka* 15.—If the lord of the Navamsa referred to above be in a moveable sign or Amsa, the person born will be earning his money easily when he is absent from his native place. If the said lord be in an immoveable sign or Amsa, he will get money in his own place. If he be in a dual Rasi or Amsa, the native will get money everywhere.

**वक्रगते तदधीशे बहुप्रकारैर्धनं समाप्नोति।  
भाग्यानुरूपतोऽर्थान्विनिर्दिशेत् सर्वमेव पूर्वोक्तम्॥१६॥**

 *Sloka* 16—If the said lord be retrograde in motion, the person born will be earning money in various ways. The amount earned will be in proportion to one's luck. All this has already been described.

**चन्द्राद्दशमे सौम्यो बलवानेको न शत्रुयुतदृष्टः।  
जनयेद्युगान्तकीर्तिं स्वान्वययुक्तं च लग्नाद्वा॥१७॥**

 *Sloka* 17.—If only one strong benefic planet which is not conjoined with or aspected by an inimical one occupy the 10th house reckoned from the Moon or the Lagna, the person born will get wide fame lasting for a long time for himself and his family.

Thus ends the 22nd Adhyaya entitled "Profession and Livelihood in the work Horasara, composed by Sri Prithuyasas, the son of Sri: Varahamihira.

**———————**

**त्रयोविंशोऽध्यायः**

**अथ द्व्यादिग्रहयोगास्तत्फलानि च॥**

**द्व्यादिग्रहसंयोगः स्वं स्वं भावं हिनस्ति सर्वेषाम्।  
योगफलं च विदध्यान्मधुघृतयोगो विषं यथा तद्वत्॥१॥**

 *Sloka* 1.—The conjunction of two or more planets does harm to the Bhava occupied. It also produces the effect of the conjunction just as the mixture of honey and ghee (if combined in equal quantitises) turn out as poison.

**तत्र समासाद्वक्ष्ये योगविशेषात् फलं ग्रहाणां च।  
गोचरफलयोगयुतं नृणां सम्यग्विनिर्दिशेत्तज्ज्ञः॥१॥**

 *Sloka* 2.—I shall therefore describe in brief the special effects arising from combinations of planets at birth as well as those formed by planets during their transits as those in the know of the science have to impress well their effects.

**तुर्ये वा निधने वा संयोगे सूर्यसौम्ययोर्लग्नात्।  
जातो नृपतुल्यगुणो धनवानन्यत्र संयुतो गुणवान्॥३॥**

 *Sloka* 3.—If the Sun and Mercury be together in the 4th or the 8th house from the Lagna, the person born will possess all kingly qualities, and will be wealthy. In the other houses, this combination will make the native possessed of good qualities.

**रविशशियोगे भाग्ये धनवान् दशमे युतौ तु विख्यातः।  
पतितोऽन्धो व्यययोगे नान्येषु युतौ तु सम्पत्स्यात्॥४॥**

 *Sloka* 4—When the Sun and the Moon combine in the 9th house, the person born will be wealthy. If the two planets are together in the 10th house, the person will become famous. If they occupy the 12th house, he will become an outcast; he will be blind. In the case of these two planets combining in other houses, the person will not be wealthy.

**लाभारिपुत्रदशमेष्वेकस्मिंश्चन्द्रमन्दयोर्योगे।  
जातो नृपालवंशे नृपतित्वं याति नास्ति सन्देहः॥५॥**

 * Sloka* 5.—When at a birth the Moon and Saturn are posited in a single house, identical with the 11th, the 6th, the 5th or the 10th, the person, if born in a royal family, will surely become a king.

**दशमायोदयरन्ध्रेष्वेकस्मिन् भास्करारयोर्योगे।  
जातो महाकुलीनो बलवानन्येषु संयुतौ निःस्वः॥६॥**

 *Sloka* 6—If the Sun and Mars occupy together any one of the 10th, the 11th, the 1st and the 8th houses, the person must be born in a very high and rich family and possess great strength; if the two planets be together in any one of the other houses, the person born will have no wealth at all.

**गुरुभास्करयोर्लग्ने संयोगे धर्मकर्मलाभे वा।  
आज्ञाबलैः समेतो विख्यातो दुर्गतश्च सञ्जातिः॥७॥**

* Sloka* 7.—If the Sun and Jupiter be together in the Lagna or in any one of the 3 houses, *viz*., the 9th, the 10th and the 11th, the person born will have at his command a powerful army; he will be famous and live in a dwelling well-fortified and difficult to be approached, or is unhappy.

**सूर्यसितयोस्तु योगे दशमे रन्ध्रे च पुत्रभवने वा॥  
नृपसदृशो विख्यातो बलवानन्येषु वित्तसुखहीनः॥८॥**

 *Sloka 8*.—If the Sun and Venus combine in any one of the houses, viz., the 10th, the 8th and the 5th, the person born will be equal to a king, widely famed, and powerful; if they occupy any of the other houses, the native will have neither wealth nor happiness.

**भानुः स्वपुत्रसहितो नवमे धनभेऽपि वा षष्ठे।  
जनयेत् प्रसिद्धकीर्त्तिं सुखिनं शेषेषु वित्तहीनं च॥९॥**

 * Sloka 9.*—When the Sun and Saturn occupy together the 9th, the 2nd or the 6th house, the personi will be very widely-famed and happy; if in any one of the other houses, the native concerned will be devoid of wealth

**रक्तेन्दुयुतौ लग्ने दशमे वा धर्मपुत्रलाभे वा।  
धनवान् भूपतितुल्योऽनुक्तेषु युतौ तु बन्धुसुखहीनः॥१०॥**

 *Sloka* 10.—If the Moon and Mars be together in the Lagna, the 10th, the 9th, the 5th or the 11th, house, the person born will be equal to a king. If they occupy together any one of the other Rasis, the native concerned will be devoid of happiness and he will have no relations.

**काव्यकलासु विदग्धो धनवान् बुधचन्द्रयोः समायोगे।  
सहजव्ययारिनिधनेष्वन्येष्वभयं च निःस्वतां याति॥११॥**

 *Sloka* 11—When the Moon and Mercury combine in any one of the houses, viz., 3rd, 12th, 6th and 8th, the person born will be very clever in poetry and the arts, and he will possess wealth. If they be together in any of the other houses, the person concerned will be free from fear, and will become indigent.

**गुरुचन्द्रयोगजातो धनवान् सुतदारवान् विनीतश्च।  
सर्वत्र फलं प्रोक्तं मुक्त्वा सहजारिमं तयोर्नीचम्॥१२॥**

 *Sloka* 12—When the Moon and Jupiter are together in a single house, the person born will be rich, possess wife and children and will be well-behaved. The same will be the effect in all houses except the 3rd the 6th and the depression house of either of them.

**क्रयविक्रयेषु कुशलो वस्त्राद्युपभोगवान् धनाध्यक्षः।  
शिशिरकरशुक्रयोगे दशभे व्ययभे विदेशतोऽर्थाप्तिः॥१३॥**

 *Slok*a 13.—When the Moon and Venus occupy together the 10th house, the person born will be clever in the selling and buying of things; he will wear good clothes and enjoy life and be very wealthy; and if in the 12th house, he will get wealth from foreign countries.

**आरार्कजयोर्योगे नवमात्मजबन्धुकर्मधनभे वा।  
सुतबन्धुधर्मवित्तैः सम्पन्नोऽन्यत्र दुर्भगो मलिनः॥१४॥**

 *Sloka* 14.—When Mars and Saturn occupy together the 9th, the 5th, the 4th, the 10th or the 2nd house, the person born will be endowed with children, relations, virtue and wealth. When they occupy together houses other than those mentioned above, the person born will be unlucky and dirty.

**शीतांशुमन्दयोगे दुर्बलदेहोऽतिनीचकर्मरतः।  
मातृद्वेषी मूर्खो ह्युपचयभवनेषु सर्वसम्पन्नः॥१५॥**

 *Sloka* 15—When the Moon and Saturn combine in a single house, the person born will have a weak body, will be intent on doing base acts, will hate his mother and will be a fool. If the aforesaid planets occupy any one of the Upachaya houses, the person concerned will be endowed with all comforts.

**कुजबुधयोगे चपलो दुष्टस्त्रीनायकोऽल्पसन्तुष्टः।  
मलिनः परान्नकाङ्क्षी केन्द्रेष्वर्थागमं सुखं लभते॥१६॥**

 *Sloka* 16.—When Mars and Mercury are together in a single house, the person born will be fickle-minded. He will be the husband of a bad woman. He will be easily satisfied, will be unclean, and will be desirous of eating in others houses. If the said combination be in a Kendra the person concerned will earn money and be happy.

**कुजगुरुयोगे बलवान् दीर्घायुः पुत्रवान् विनीतश्च।  
रिपुरन्ध्ररिःफभेषु व्यसनी रोगान्वितोऽल्पवित्तश्च॥१७॥**

 *Sloka* 17.—When Mars and Jupiter combine in one house, the person born will be long-lived, will be endowed with sons, and will be well-behaved. When the said combination happens in the 6th, 8th or 12th house, the person concerned will be addicted to vicious habits, troubled by diseases and will not have much wealth.

**कुजभृगुयोगे चपलः स्त्रीवरागो दुष्टकर्मकरः।  
लग्नसुखास्पदभवने कुलाधिको ग्रामनेता वा॥१८॥**

 * Sloka* 18.—When Mars and Venus are together in a house, the person born will be rash, be influenced by his wife, and will do vicious acts. If the conjunction bein the 1st, 4th or the 10th house, the person concerned will become the chief member of his family or the head of his village.

**कुजमन्दयोस्तु योगे नित्यार्तो वातपित्तरोगाभ्याम्।  
उपचयभवने नैवं नृपतुल्यो लोकसम्मतः ख्यातः॥१९॥**

 *Sloka* 19.—When Mars and Saturn combine in a single house, he will ever be troubled by windy and bilious complaints. If the conjunction referred to above be in an Upachaya house (3, 6, 10, 11) there will be no such bad effect as stated above; the person concerned will be equal to a king, loved by all and famous.

**बुधगुरुयोगे बधिरो विद्वान् नेत्रातुरो नरो भवति।  
व्ययनिधनशत्रुभे स्यात् सुभगो विख्यातधर्मपरः॥२०॥**

 *Sloka* 20.—When Mercury and Jupiter combine in a single house, the person born will be deaf; he will be learned; he will have weak eyes. If the conjunction of the said two planets be in the 12th, the 8th or the 6th house, the person concerned will be amiable; famous, and intent on doing virtuous acts.

**बुधभृगुयोगे विकलो विघातकुशलोऽल्पदारपुत्ररतः।  
भाग्यसुतमूर्तिभे स्याद्विशिष्टनामान्वितो धनाध्यक्षः॥२१॥**

 Sloka 21—When Mercury and Venus are together in a single house, the person born will be dispirited. He will be clever in causing impediments; and he will have a mean wife and few children. If the two planets: be together in the 9th, the 5th, or the 1st, the person will get an important title and command iminense wealth.

**बुधमन्दयोस्तु योगे दशमे लग्नेऽथवा धर्मे।  
धनदारपुत्रमित्रैः समन्वितोन्यत्र कष्टफलम्॥२२॥**

 *Sloka* 22—If Mercury and Saturn combine in the 10th, the 1st or in the 9th house, the person born will possess wealth, wife, sons, and friends. If the said two planets occupy other houses, they will cause untoward effects.

**गुरुभृगुयोगे मतिमानुदयात्मज**वर्ममे**षु वा निधने।  
स्त्रीधनपुत्रसमेतोऽन्यत्र गदैः पीडितोऽतिदुःखार्तः॥२३॥**

 *Sloka* 23—If Jupiter and Venus be together in the 1st, 5th, 9th, or the 8th house the person born will be endowed with wealth, wife and children. If the said two planets occupy any one of the other houses, the person will be troubled by diseases and will be very miserable.

**देवगुरुमन्दयोगेऽनुपचयभवनेषु मानधनहीनः।  
उपचयभवनेषु नरः प्रख्यातो राजपूजितो भवति॥२४॥**

 *Sloka* 24—When Jupiter and Saturn are together in any one of the Anupachaya (1, 2, 4, 5, 7, 8, 9 and 12) houses the person born will be devoid of wealth and he will have no self-respect. If the said two planets combine in any one of the Upachaya houses, the person born will become very famous and honoured by the king.

**शनिसितयोगे लग्ने कोणे केन्द्रेऽथवास्तभं मुक्त्वा।  
स्त्रीवशगो नृपनेता धनवान् शेषेषु सत्वधनहीनः॥ २५॥**

 *Sloka* 25. — When Venus and Saturn combine in the Lagna, a Kona or a Kendra house other than the 7th, the person born will be under the influence of his wife; he will be a Minister or Commander in the king's service and be rich. In the remaining houses, the native concerned will be devoid of wealth and will be weak in health.

**रविचन्द्रभौमयोगः पापिष्ठं स्वल्पजीवितं कुरुते।  
बन्धुसुतदारहीनं विकलाङ्गं लोकनिन्दितं कृपणम्॥२६॥**

 *Sloka* 26.—If the three planets, vis, the Sun, the Moon and Mars be together, the person born will be most sinful and will have a miserable existence. He will have no relatives, no wife and no children. He will have a deficient limb. He will be despised by all and will be a miser.

**रबिकुजबुधयोगोऽयं विरुद्धधर्मान्वितं विदेशरतम्।  
कृपणं दयाविहीनं स्वार्जितधननाशदुःखसन्तप्तम्॥२७॥**
