 *Sloka* 27.—When the Sun, Mars and Mercury combine in one house, he will be opposed to righteous acts; he will be intent in living in foreign places; he will be a miser and have no mercy; the wealth earned by himself will all be destroyed and he will be mentally affected thereby.

**रविबुधगुरुयोगेऽस्मिञ्जातो मतिमान्नरेन्द्रदयितश्च।  
वयसोऽन्ते धनहीनं परान्नपुष्टः परोपतापी च॥२८॥**

 * Sloka* 28.—He who is born when the Sun, Mercury and Jupiter combine in one house, will be intelligent. He will be the favourite of a king. At the last stage of his life, he will be devoid of all money and will be fed at other's cost; he will be causing great pain to others.

**रविगुरुसितसंयोगे दानपरो लोकविश्रुतो नृपतिः।  
स्त्रीद्युतवञ्चितार्थः शत्रुजनैर्बाधितोऽतिदुःखार्तः॥ २९॥**

 *Sloka* 29.—When the Sun, Jupiter and Venus occupy together a single house, the person born will be liberal in his gifts and he will be a renowned king. He will be deprived of his wealth being duped in gambling with women, Tormented by his enemies, he will be very much troubled by misery.

**रविसितशनियोगेऽस्मिंस्त्यक्ताचारोऽतिवञ्चको दुःखी।  
आयविहीनो रोगी च वार्धके किञ्चिदर्थसम्पन्नः॥३०॥**

 *Sloka* 30—If the Sun, Venus and Saturn occupy together a single house, the person born will give up all his religious observances. He will be crafty and miserable. He will have no income and will suffer from sickness. In his old age, he will be able to command some money.

**चन्द्रकुजसौम्ययोगे विख्यातो लोकपूजितो ज्ञानी।  
वाग्मी दयासमेतो वयसो मध्ये दरिद्रश्च॥३१॥**

 *Sloka* 31.—When the Moon, Mars and Mercury combine in a single house, the person born will become famous, loved by all and learned. He will be eloquent, and merciful; he will become poor in his middle life.

**चन्द्रबुधाङ्गिरसानां योगः कथितः प्रशस्तविभवकरः।  
विद्वांसं धनवन्तं प्रतापबहुलं महीपतिं कुरुते॥३२॥**

 *Sloka* 32—The grouping of the Moon, Mercury and Jupiter in one house will make the person born highly exalted. The native concerned will be learned and rich. be learned and rich He will be a very powerful monarch.

**चन्द्रगुरुशुक्रयोगे जातो राजा भवेन्न सन्देहः।  
गजतुरगयानमुख्यैः परिजनकोशादिभिर्युतो भवति॥३३॥**

 * Sloka* 33.—When the Moon, Jupiter and Venus combine in a single house, the person born will, without any doubt become a king, with all the important paraphernalia, viz. elephants, horses, vehicles, followers, treasury and the like.

**चन्द्रसितमन्दयोगे मानी धनवान् दयापरो भोगी।  
नात्युच्छ्रितो न नीचः स्वपुत्रपशुबन्धुपूजितो भवति॥३४॥**

 *Sloka* 34.—When the Moon, Venus and Saturn combine in a single house, the person born will be proud, wealthy and merciful. He will enjoy life. He will not be very high in life, nor low. He will be endowed with sons and cows and will be respected by his relations.

**चन्द्रशनिसूर्ययोगे क्षीणधनो रोगपीडितो दुःखी।  
याञ्चापरोऽङ्गहीनः सेवानृत्योपजीवनं कुरुते॥३५॥**

 *Sloka* 35.—When the Moon, Saturn and the Sun are together in a house, the native will not command much wealth. He will be troubled by disease and will be unhappy. He will resort to begging; he will be defective of some limb. He will earn a living by serving others, by teaching, dancing, etc.

**कुजबुधभृगुयोगोत्थः शिशुभावे रोगपीडितः किञ्चित्।  
सरसकलाविनयज्ञो नरेन्द्रपुत्रोऽतिविश्रुतो लोके॥३६॥**

 *Sloka* 36—When Mars, Mercury and Venus combine in one house, the person born will suffer from troubles in his childhood. He will be skilled in the art of love, will be courteous, will be the son of a king and renowned in the world.

**कुजगुरुकवियोगेऽस्मिन् वाहनपरिवारपूरितः पुरुषः।  
विख्यातो घनपुष्टः पुत्रधरित्र्यन्वितो महाभोगी॥३७॥**

 *Sloka* 37.—When Mars, Jupiter and Venus combine in one house, the person born will be endowed with vehicles and full retinue. He will be widely-famed, immensely rich and will possess sons and lands and will be a voluptuary.

**कुजशुक्रमन्दयोगे मातुरनिष्टो विदेशसञ्चारी।  
परयुवतिरतोऽनार्यो नृपाल कुलतः पराभवं लभते॥३८॥**

 *Sloka* 38—When Mars, Venus and Saturn join together in a house, the person, concerned will be disliked by the mother. He will go to foreign places. He will be addicted to another female; he will behave basely, and will suffer humiliation from the royal family.

**कुजरविजार्कसमाजे पापी परदारवञ्चकोऽल्पायुः।  
निधनं याति विदेशे विषाग्निशस्त्रैर्निपीडितो बन्धैः॥३९॥**

 *Sloka* 39.—If Mars, Saturn and the Sun combine in a single house, the person born will do sinful deeds; he will dupe others wives and will be short lived. He will die in a foreign country through poison, fire, weapon, beating or imprisonment (tied with ropes).

**कुजरविसौम्यसमूहः करोति मनुजं सदाटनाभिरतम्।  
काले काले लभते किञ्चिद्धान्यं स चौदनं यत्नात्॥४०॥**

 *Sloka* 40—When Mars, the Sun and Mercury join together in a house, the person will always be intent on roaming about. He will be getting a small quantity of corn at every time and after great effort have the same cooked.

**बुधगुरुशुक्रा मिलिताः कुर्वन्ति महीपतिं जातम्।  
सुसमृद्धं विनयाढ्य माण्डलिकं कीर्त्तिसम्पन्नम्॥४१॥ **

* Sloka* 41.—When Mercury, Jupiter and Venus combine in a single house, the person born will become a ruler of the earth. He will be endowed with plenty, will be a pink of courtesy, and will become a king with wide fame.

**बुधसितमन्दयुतौ सञ्जातो नरपालको धनाढ्यश्च।  
स्थिरबुद्धिश्चिरजीवी विख्यातो लोकसम्मतो ज्ञानी॥४२॥**

 *Sloka* 42.—When Mercury, Venus and Saturn join together in a single Rasi, the person born, will become a king and he will be very rich, with a steady mind, famous, long-lived, loved by all and very learned.

**बुधशनिदिननाथानां योगे जातोऽतिरक्तपित्तवपुः।  
स्वजनद्वेषी हीनो विदेशवासी सिरालुकृशदेहः॥४३ ॥**

 *Sloka* 43.—If Mercury, Saturn and the Sun be together in a single house, the person born will have a very red body, be bilious, will hate his relations and will be destitute. He will dwell in foreign places. His body will be full of veins and lean.

**बुधरविशुक्रसमाजे भोगधनैश्वर्यसंयुतः पुरुषः।  
मातृपितृबन्धुवर्णैः संयुक्तो मानशौर्यसम्पन्नः॥४४॥**

 *Slok*a 44.—When Mercury, the Sun and Venus combine, the person born will enjoy life being endowed with all objects of life and riches, and live in the company of his parents and other relations. He will shine with honour and bravery.

**बुधरविभौमयोगे जातो वेश्यापतिर्विदेशरतः।  
बन्धुषु वैरं कुरुते निःस्वोऽल्पायुर्विनष्टपशुदारः॥४५॥**

 *Sloka* 45.—When the combination consists of Mercury, the Sun and Mars, the person born will keep a dancing girl as his partner and dwell in foreign places. He will hate his relations, will be without wealth, will be short-lived; and will lose his wife and cattle.

**गुरुशुक्रमन्दयोगे कुलाधिनाथः कुटुम्बसौख्ययुतः।  
मितलाभो मितभोगी विख्यातो लोकसम्मतो जातः॥४६॥**

 *Sloka* 46.—If Jupiter, Venus and Saturn combine in a single house, the person born will become the chief of his race. He will be happy with his wife and children. His gains will be steady and his enjoyment will also be medium. He will attain fame and be loved by the people.

**गुरुभौमसूर्ययोगे वित्ताढ्यो लोकपूजितो विद्वान्।  
रिपुरोगभयत्यक्तः समस्तसौख्यान्वितो जातः॥४७॥**

 *Sloka* 47.—When Jupiter, Mars and the Sun combine, the person born will be very rich, learned and honoured by all. He will have no enemies, and no diseases. He will be free from fear and will be endowed with all kinds of happiness.

**गुरुकुजमन्दा युक्ताः कुर्वन्ति नरं पुराधिपं बलिनम्।  
क्लेशसहिष्णुं धनिनं मात्सरिणं मानशौर्यसम्पन्नम्॥४८॥**

 *Sloka* 48.—If Jupiter, Mars and Saturn combine in a single house, the person born will be the Mayor of a city and endowed with great strength. He will be capable of enduring sorrows, will be rich and will be jealous. He will be honourable and brave.

**गुरुशनिचन्द्रसमाजे स्त्रीलोलः पुत्रसौख्यसम्पन्नः।  
प्रियभाषितजनमित्रं मातापितृदेवगुरुभक्तः॥४९॥**

* Sloka* 49.—If the combination be of Jupiter, Saturn and the Moon, the person born will long for women. He will be endowed with children and happiness. He will befriend people who speak sweetly. He will revere his mother, father, the Gods and elders.

**त्र्यादिग्रहैर्विलग्ने दशमे धर्मेऽथवा युक्तैः।  
बहुकार्यो बहुगुणवान् बहुधिषणः स्याद्धनेशसमभोगः॥५०॥**

 *Sloka* 50—When the Lagna, the 10th or the 9th house is occupied by three or more planets, the person born will be busy with many enterprises. He will be possessed of many good qualities, will be very intelligent, will enjoy like God Kubera.

**चन्द्रगुरुभूमिपुत्रैरेकर्क्षगतैर्ननीचपवनस्थैः।  
षट्सप्ताष्टव्ययभं हित्वा शेषेषु शक्तिवित्तयुक्तः॥५१॥**

 * Sloka*. 51.—If the Moon, Jupiter and Mars combine in any house other than their depression houses, the 6th, the 7th and the 8th houses, the person born a will be possessed of strength and wealth.

**शनिचन्द्रभौमभृगुजैरेकर्क्षैधर्मकर्मलग्ने वा।  
संसारबन्धुरहितो विदेशवासी सुखी भवति॥५२॥**

 *Sloka.* 52.—When Saturn, the Moon, Mars and Venus combine in a single house identical with the 9th, the 10th or the Lagna, the person born will dwell in a foreign place and live happily without the worries of his family and relations.

**एकर्क्षगतैः सोम्यैः शुभातिरिक्तं फलं विनिर्देश्यम्।  
पापसमूहैः कष्टं मिश्रं मिश्रैर्भवेन्नियतम्॥५३॥**

 *Sloka* 53.—When three or more benefics occupy a single house, the good effects produced by the Yoga will be *par excellence*. If the planets forming the Yoga be all malefic, it will be quite the reverse; if it be mixed; the effect also will be mixed

**चतुराद्यैर्विहगेन्द्रैरेकर्क्षगतैस्तु मिश्रफलभोक्ता।  
तेषां दशासु नियतं फलं विपाके शुभाशुनं तुल्यम्॥५४॥**

**इति श्रीवराहमिहिरसुतश्रीपृथुरशोविरचिते होरासारे द्व्यादिग्रहयोगफलाध्यायस्त्रयोविंशः॥**

 * Sloka* 51.—When four or more planets occupy a single house, the person born will enjoy mixed effects; the effects will reveal themselves during their respective Dasa and sub-Dasa periods in proportion to their nature—good and bad.

Thus ends the 23rd Adhyaya entitled "Conjunctions of two or more Planets and their effects" in the work Horasara composed by Sri: Prithuyasas, son of Sri Varahamihira,

**———————**

**चतुर्विंशोऽध्यायः**

**अथ जातकभङ्गास्तत्फलानि च॥**

**अर्केन्दुभूमिपुत्रैः केन्द्रगतैर्भाग्यभे व्यये वाऽपि।  
जलयोग इति ख्यातो नान्यग्रहमिश्रितैस्तु बलहीनैः॥१॥**

 *Sloka* 1—If the Sun, the Moon and Mars, all weak, occupy together Kendra, the 9th or even the 12th house and be not conjoined with any other planets, the famous Jalayoga is formed.

**प्रकृतिजडोऽल्पमनीषो ज्ञानधनैश्वर्यवर्जितश्चफलः।  
स्तब्धः परान्नकाङ्क्षी जलयोगे जायते मनोदुःखी॥२॥**

 * Sloka* 2.—The man born in a जल Yoga will by nature be stupid, insignificant, and devoid of intelligence; he will have no money and be without any wealth whatever. He will be fickle-minded, and stubborn, desiring to take his meals at others' table. He will ever be melancholy.

**भाग्याधिपे व्ययस्ये व्ययेश्वरे वित्तगे बलक्षीणे।  
विक्रमसङ्ख्यैः पापैर्योगः केमद्रुमो ज्ञेयः॥३॥**

 * Sloka* 3—If the lord of the 9th house be in the 12th, the lord of the 12th weak and in the 2nd, and the three malefics occupy the 3rd, the resulting Yoga is known as Kemadruma.

**परदाररतो नित्यं परान्नकाङ्क्षी कुधर्मकर्मरतः।  
बहुऋणभागी पुरुषो जातः केमद्रुमे भवेद्योगे॥४॥**

 *Sloka* 4.—The man born in a Kemadruma Yoga will always go to other people's wives, will desire to eat at others' table, will engage himself in doing vicious acts, and will incur many debts

**सप्ताष्टमगैः पापैर्लग्नेशे नीचगे तदंशे वा।  
गुलिकोदयवेलायां जातः कुलनाशको न सन्देहः॥५॥**

* Sloka* 5.—When malefics occupy the 7th and 8th houses, and the lord of the Lagna is in his depression Rasi or depression Navamsa, and when Mandi is rising in the Lagna, the person born will without doubt be the destroyer of the family (bring the family to extinction) कुलनाशकस्तथाहपायुः is another reading.

**नीचारिभांशकगतैर्ग्रहैः समस्तैः स्वतुङ्गभवने वा।  
शुभकर्मान्यभसंस्थैर्जातो भिक्षाशनो नरो भवति॥६॥**

* Sloka* 16.—When all the planets are in their respective depression or inimical Rasis or depression Navamsas, or occupy their respective exaltation houses, and when these occupied houses do not happen to be the 9th or the 10th, the person born in the Yoga will go a begging for food.

**होरेशे व्ययसंस्थे नभसि क्रूरे सरक्तके चन्द्रे।  
जातोऽभियोग उक्तः परदेशरतो दरिद्रः स्यात्॥७॥**

 * Sloka* 7.—If the lord of the Lagna be in the 12th, a malefic planet occupy the 10th, and the Moon be conjoined with Mars, the person born in this अभियोग will be roaming in foreign places and living as a beggar.

**नवमोदयात्मजस्थौ रविचन्द्रौ भ्रातृकेन्द्रगे जीवे।  
शनिकुजवासरकाले जातः सोन्माद एव स्यात्॥८॥**

* Sloka* 8—When the Sun and the Moon are placed in the 9th, the 1st or the 5th louse, and Jupiter occupies the 3rd or a Kendra house, and when the कालहोरा at the time belongs to Saturn or Mars, the person born under this Yoga will become insane.

 For कालहोरा see notes in page 42 of my edition (1937) of श्री–प.

**बुधचन्द्रौ केन्द्रगतौ नान्यग्रहवीक्षितौ न संयुक्तौ।  
योगोऽयं पैशाचस्तत्रोत्पन्नः ससोन्मादः॥ ९॥**

* Sloka* 9.—If Mercury and the Moon be in a Kendra position and be not aspected by or conjoined with any other planet, the Yoga formed is termed पैशाअ–Paisacha, and the person born therein will be insane.

**भृगुचन्द्रौ केन्द्रगतौ रन्ध्रे वा पञ्चमेऽथवा पापे।  
योगो महागदाख्यस्तत्रोत्पन्नः स सोन्मादः॥१०॥**

 *Sloka* 10.—When Venus and the Moon occupy a Kendra position, and a malefic is posited in the 8th or the 5th house, the Yoga is termed and the person born in that Yoga will suffer from epileptic fits.

**भृगुचन्द्रौ केन्द्रगतौ रन्ध्रे वा पञ्चमेऽथवा पापे।  
योगो महागदाख्यस्तत्रोत्पन्नस्त्वपस्मारी ॥११॥**

* Sloka* 11.—Same as 10.

**सारे शनौ विलग्ने लग्नेशे वित्तरन्ध्रगे चन्द्रे।  
बुधशुक्रौ केन्द्रगतौ श्रेष्ठकुलो नचितां याति ॥१२ ॥**

 * Sloka* 12.—If Mars and Saturn be in the Lagna and the lord of the Lagna and the Moon occupy the 2nd and the 8th, and Mercury and Venus are posited in Kendra houses, the person concerned though born in a high family, will become low in position and habits.

**कुजसौरौ केन्द्रगतौ लग्ने राहुः शुभा व्ययारिस्थाः।  
चण्डालयोग इह चेज्जातो निजवंशकर्मरहितः स्यात्॥१३॥**

* Sloka* 13—If Mars and Saturn be in Kendra houses, Rahu in the Lagna, and the benefics in the 12th and 6th houses, the चण्डाल Yoga is formed. The person The person born in this Yoga will leave off his religious duties pertaining to his caste.

**बुधभृगुचन्द्रा केन्द्रं याता लग्ने च राहुणा सहिते।  
चण्डालयोग उक्तस्तत्रोत्पन्नो हि नीचकर्मा स्यात्॥१४॥**

 *Sloka* 14.—If Mercury, Venus and the Moon Kendra houses, and Rahu occupy the Lagna, the occupy Yoga formed is termed चण्डाल The person born in this will do base acts.

**परिवेषकालजातो लग्नाद्रिपुरन्ध्रगः शनिः सारः।  
लग्नत्रिकोणरहितो सुरपूज्ये जायते त्वपस्मारी॥१५॥**

* Sloka* 15.—One born in परिवेष, when Mars and Saturn occupy the 6th and 8th houses, and when Jupiter does not occupy the Lagna or its triangular signs, will suffer from epileptic fits.

 For परिवेष see जा–पा–II–6 and XIV—13

**सारे शनौ विलग्ने लग्नेशे वित्तरन्ध्रमाग्यस्थे।  
सौम्यैः केन्द्रबहिष्ठैर्जातस्याजीवितं रोगः॥१६॥**

 *Sloka* 16.—If Saturn and Mars occupy the Lagna and the lord of the Lagna be posited in the 2nd 8th or the 9th house, and the benefics, any of the houses other than the Kendras, the person born in the Yoga will be troubled by disease throughout his life.

**शशिशनिशुक्राः केन्द्रे व्ययाष्टगौ भास्करावनीसूनू।  
केमद्रुमोऽपरोऽयं योगेऽस्मिन् जन्मभूमिमात्रपरः॥१७॥**

 *Sloka* 17.—If the Moon, Saturn and Venus be in Kendra houses, and the two planets, *viz*; the Sun and Mars occupy the 12th and the 8th, the Yoga formed is another variety of Kemadruma, and the person born therein will be wholly engaged in his birth place alone.

** षष्ठाष्टमव्ययगताः पापाः कुर्वन्ति जातिविभ्रंशम्।  
कर्मधनस्थैश्च तथा शुभराशौ वर्जिते शुभैर्वाऽपि॥२८॥**

 * Sloka* 18—if malefics be posited in the 6th, the 8th and the 12th houses, they make the native. an outcast. Similarly, if malefics occupy the 10th and the 2nd houses, and benefic houses be devoid of benefics, the same result will follow.

**भाग्याधिपे व्ययस्थे पापयुतौ जन्मलग्नयोर्नाथौ।  
अस्तं यातौ जातः स्वकुलध्वंसी विनष्टसुतदारः॥१९॥**

 *Sloka* 19—If the lord of the 9th house be in the 12th, and the lords of the Lagna and of the Rasi occupied by the Moon be in conjunction with malefics and be eclipsed, the person born will destroy the family and will lose his wife and children.

**अशुभशुभैः केन्द्रस्थैर्होरापतिना निरीक्षितश्चन्द्रः।  
सौरांशगतो वा योगः कुलपांसनो नाम॥२०॥**

 * Sloka* 20.—When benefic as well as malefic planets occupy Kendra houses, and the Moon is aspected by the lord of the Lagna or is posited in a Navamsa of Saturn, the Yoga formed is known as **कुलपांसन** (Kulapamsana), defiling of one's family.

**स्वगृहाच्च्युतो दरिद्रो विदेशवासो विनष्टसुतदारः।  
दोषगणैरभिभूतो योगे कुलपांसने जातः॥२१॥**

 *Sloka* 21.—The man born in a **कुलपांसन**–(Kulapamsana) Yoga will be driven out from his house, will become a beggar, and will dwell in foreign countries. He will lose his wife and children. He will commit many faults and will be humiliated thereby.

**भाग्याधिपेऽर्कयुक्ते स्वसुतस्थाने न चापि शुभदृष्टे।  
पापैः सहजारिस्थैर्जातो नीचप्रवृत्तिजीवी स्यात्॥२२॥**

 *Sloka* 22.—When the lord of the 9th house is conjoined with the Sun in the 2nd or the 5th and is not aspected by any benefic, and malefics occupy the 3rd and the 6th houses, the person born will earn a living by doing base acts.

**मन्दर्क्षे लग्नगते चन्द्रे केन्द्रे शनैश्चरे यस्य।  
व्ययसंस्थे सुरपूज्ये जातो भिक्षाशनोपजीवी स्यात्॥२३॥**

 *Sloka* 23.—When the Moon occupies the Lagna identical with a sign owned by Saturn, Saturn is in a Kendra house and Jupiter is posited in the 12th, the person born in the above Yoga will lead his life through begging and eating at other's houses.

**लग्नाधीशान्मृत्युषष्ठव्ययस्थैः पापैर्जातो जन्मभूमेर्निवृत्तः।  
जन्मेकादशेषाद्वा भाग्यस्थाने वर्जिते स्वाधिपेन॥२४॥**

 * Sloka* 24—If malefics occupy the 6th, 8th and 12th houses reckoned from the lord of the Lagna, the person concerned will have left for good his birth-place. If they occupy the said houses reckoned from the planet owning the Rasi occupied by the Moon, and the 9th house be devoid of its lord, the native concerned will leave the place on account of the sale of his estate or of owiोng to faults committed by him.

**सौम्येड्य(न्दु)शुक्रं रिपुनीचमंस्थैरंशे तथा लग्नगतेऽर्कपुत्रे।  
जातो हि दुःखी कुलदोषभूतः स्त्रीपुत्रहीनो निधनेऽपि कृच्छ्रम्॥२५॥**

 * Sloka* 25.—When Mercury, Jupiter (Moon) and Venus occupy their inimical or depression houses or Amsas and Saturn be in the Lagna, the person born will be miserable owing to faults committed by his family and he will be without wife and children. The same calamity will befall him when the said planets occupy even the 8th house.

**स्वत्रिकोणगृहं केचित्स्वोच्चं यानाः स्वमन्दिरम्।  
अतिनीचो रविश्चैको न तेषां फलसम्भवः॥२६॥**

 * Sloka* 26.—Some may occupy their Moolatrikona houses, some, their exaltation, and some, their Swakshetra places; even then, if the Sun alone should be in his extreme debilitation, the good effects described above for these planets will not come to pass.

**उच्चस्थोऽपि तुलांशे वा स्थितः कमलबोधनः।  
सार्वभौमस्य पुत्रोऽपि नीचत्वमधिगच्छति॥२७॥**

* Sloka* 27.—If the Sun, though exalted, be in the Tula Navamsa, the native concerned, even if he should be the son of the emperor, will degrade himself to a very mean position.

**तुलायां दशमे भागे स्थितः कमलबोधनः।  
सहस्रं राजयोगानां नाशयत्याशु जन्मनि॥२८॥**

* Sloka* 8.—If at a birth, the Sun should occupy the 10th degree of sign Tula, the effects of 1000 Rajayogas will be destroyed very soon.

**सचिवो दानवेड्यस्य नीचांशे समुपस्थितः।  
सम्प्राप्तमतुलं राज्यं क्षिप्रं नाशयते ध्रुवम्॥२९॥**

* Sloka* 29.—When Venus occupies his depression Navamsa (in Kanya Rasi?), the vast kingdom that was built up will, without doubt, be destroyed very soon.

**उल्कापाते व्यतीपाते निर्घाते केतुदर्शने।  
अपि राजकुले जातो भिक्षान्नेनोपजीवति॥३०॥**

* Sloka* 30.—At a time when a meteor is falling, during saaigra, during a portentious thunder, at the sight of a comet, a person even if born in a royal family will be begging for food.

**लग्ने ज्ञद्रेक्काणे शशिना दृष्टे चतुष्टयस्थेन।  
जातो नृपतिकुलेष्वपि शिल्पी स्यान्निश्चितं मुनिभिः॥३१॥**

 *Sloka* 31.—When the decanate of Mercury is rising in the Lagna and is aspected by the Moon posited in a Kendra, the native though born in a royal family will become an artisan; so have sages declared.

**नीचे सौरिनवांशे शुक्रे स्याद्रविशशाङ्कयोर्मदने।  
मन्देनालोकितयोर्मात्रा सार्धं परप्रेष्यः ॥३२॥**

 *Sloka* 32.—If Venus be depressed in the 7th house in a Navamsa of Saturn and be betwixt the Sun and the Moon and also be aspected by Saturn, the person con- cerned will be a servant of another along with his mother,

 See जा. पा. VI- 13.

**सूर्यांशे यदि चन्द्रश्च द्रांशे भास्करः स्थितश्च यदि।**  
**सममेकराशिगतयोर्दुर्बलदेहो भवेत् पुरुषः॥३३॥**

 * Sloka* 33.—If the Moon be in the Sun's Navamsa and the Sun in the Moon's and when they both occupy the same Rasi, the person born will possess a weak body.

**निधनारिधनव्ययगा रविचन्द्रकुजार्कजाः क्रमान्नियतम्।  
नयनविघातं कुर्युर्बलवद्ग्रहदोषसम्भूतम्॥३४॥**

 *Sloka* 34.—If the Sun, the Moon, Mars and Saturn are placed in the 8th, the 6th, the 2nd and in the 12th houses in their order, the m in will lose his eye-sight ht by (due to the excess of) bile phlegm or wind pertaining to the most powerful of the four planets.

 Also compare. बृ.जा. XXIII-10.

**धर्मायसहजसुताः पापाः सौम्यानवेक्षिता बलिनः।  
श्रवणविघातं कुर्युः सप्तमसंस्थाश्च दन्तवैकृतिनम्॥३५॥**

 *Slok*a 35—If the malefic planets occupy the 9th, the 11th, the 3rd and the 5th houses in any order according to cirumstances and be not aspected by benefic planets, they conspire according to their strength to do damage to the organ of hearing of the person born; if they occupy the 7th house and be without benefic aspect, they make the teeth unsightly.

 Compare. बृ.जा. XXIII-11

**उदये दिनकरपुत्रे सप्तमधीधर्मगे कुजे जातः।  
सोन्मादः क्षीणेन्दौ चन्द्रात् सूर्ये व्ययेऽप्येवम्॥ ३६॥**

 *Sloka* 36.—If Saturn be in the Lagna and Mars occupy the 7th, the 5th, or the 9th, the person born will be insane or get epileptic fits. If the Moon be waning and the Sun also occupy the 12th house from the Moon, the effect will be the same.

* ***चन्द्रे** is another reading for **चन्द्रात्**.

 See. बृ.जा. XXIII–13.

**सितचतुरश्रोपगतैः पापैः सौम्यग्रहैरदृष्टयुतैः।  
दहनोद्बन्धविषाद्यैर्जायामरणं विनिर्देश्यम्॥३७॥**

 * Sloka* 37—If in a person's nativity, the 4th and 8th houses reckoned from Venus be both occupied by malefics, the wife will die by a fire-accident, The death will be by hanging by poison, and the like, if Venus be not associated with or aspected by benefics.

**पापद्वयमध्यगते शुक्रे बलवर्जितेऽरिनीचांशे।  
जायामरणं विद्यात् पूर्वोक्तनिमित्तजं च वक्तव्यम्॥३८॥**

 *Sloka* 38.—If Venus be posited betwixt two planets, be without strength and in an inimical or depression Navamsa, the death of the person's wife should be declared to be due to causes already stated above.

 See बृ. जा. XXIII–2.

**उदयास्तमयोर्ग्रहयोः शुक्रे बलवर्जिते च कोणस्थे।  
सार्के च विकलदारो निःस्वप्रायोऽन्यदारनिरतश्च॥३९ ॥**

 * Sloka* 39.—If two planets occupy the 1st and the 7th houses, Venus be weak and occupy a Trikona in conjunction with the Sun, the person born will have a wife defective of a limb; and he will be poor and addicted to another's wife.

**कोणोदयेऽस्तगेऽब्जेऽच्छे वा बन्ध्यापतिर्जातः।  
लग्नव्ययनिधनस्थैः पापैरसुतो भवेत्सुते चन्द्रे॥४०॥**

 *Sloka* 40.—If Saturn be in the Lagna and the Moon or Venus occupy the 7th house, the person born' will have a barren wife. When the three malefics are posited in the 1st, the 12th and the 8th houses and the Moon is in the 5th house, the personcon cerned will be issueless.

**दाराधिपे सुतस्थे दारविनाशो विनष्टतनयो वा।  
लग्नसुतरन्ध्ररिःफेष्वशुभाः कुर्वन्ति वंशविच्छित्तिम्॥४१॥**

 *Sloka* 41.—If the lord of the 7th house occupy the 5th, the person concerned will lose his wife or children. When the malefics are posited in the 1st, 5th, 8th and 12th houses, they make the family of the native extinct.

**बुधभार्गवयोरस्ते सुखगे पापे गुरौ सुखस्थेऽपि।  
वंशच्छेता जातश्चन्द्रानिधनस्थिते पापे॥४२॥**

 *Sloka* 42.—If Mercury and Venus be in the 7th house, a malefic in the 4th, and another malefic occupy the 8th house reckoned from the Moon, the Yoga will make the family extinct even should Jupiter occupy the 4th.

 See जा. पा. VI- 9.

**रन्ध्रेश्वरे सुतस्थे लग्ने पापग्रहे शशी सुखगः।  
सुतभेशे बलहीने जातो वंशक्षयं याति॥४३॥**

 *Sloka* 43.—If the lord of the 8th be in the 5th, a malefic planet in the Lagna, the Moon in the 4th and the lord of the 5th, weak, the person born will bring his family to extinction.

**चन्द्रे वा सूर्ये वा व्ययगे बलवर्जिते स काणः स्यात्।  
द्यूनेऽष्टमगे मानौ पापयुते नेत्रदन्तरोगी स्यात्॥४४॥**

* Sloka* 44.—When the 12th house is occupied by a weak Moon or a weak Sun, the person born will become one-eyed. When the Sun is in the 7th or the Sth along with a malefic, the person concerned will suffer from eye-disease and tooth-trouble.

*Cf*. जा.पा.— 52, 84.

**सुखसुतयुक्तौ पापौ व्ययगे जीवेऽरिनैधने चन्द्रे।  
सौम्ययुतिदृष्टिहीने निःसन्दिग्धं भवत्यन्धः॥४५॥**

 * Sloka* 45.—If the 4th and 5th houses be occupied by malefics, Jupiter be in the 12th, and the Moon be posited in the 6th or the 8th house without being conjoined with or apected by benefics, the person born in the Yoga will without doubt become blind.

**चन्द्रे स्वमध्यसंस्थे द्यूनेऽवनिजेऽर्कसिगे मन्दे।  
जातो भवत्यवश्यं विकलाङ्गो जातिभङ्गो वा॥४६॥**

 *Sloka* 46.—When the Moon is in the zenith, Mars in the 7th, and Saturn in the 2nd house from the Sun, the person born in the Yoga will without doubt have a deficient limb or be expelled from his caste.

**चापमृगमत्स्यभांशे चन्द्रे पापान्विते स कुष्ठी स्यात्।  
अलिकर्क्यजवृषभांशे लग्नं वा पापसंयुते कुष्ठी॥४७ ॥**

 * Sloka* 47.—When the Moon along with a malefic planet is in a Navamsą owned by Dhanus, Makara or Meena, the person born will be leprous. The same will be the case when the Lagna is in a Navamsa owned by Vrischika, Kataka, Mesha, or Vrishabha and is also conjoined with a malefic planet.

**कर्कटवृश्चिकभांशे चन्द्रे पापान्विते स गुह्यगदः।  
क्रोदोदरकर्णगदी चन्द्रे सुखभांशके सपापी स्यात्॥ ४८ ॥**

 *Sloka* 48.—If the Moon occupy the Navamsa be longing to Kataka or Vrischika and be in conjunction with a malefic planet, the person born will suffer from a disease affecting the privities. If the Moon should occupy in the 4th house a Navamsa belonging thereto and be in conjunction with a malefic planet, the person concerned will have disease of the chest, belly or ear.

**राहुग्रस्ते चन्द्रे पापयुते रिःफरन्ध्रनवमे वा।  
सोन्मादः पुरुषः स्यात् कलहप्रायोऽतिरोषी वा॥४९॥**

 *Sloka* 49.—When the Moon in conjunction with a malefic planet and Rahu occupies the 12th, the 8th or the 9th house, the person born will be liable to insanity and will develop a tendency to quarrel or be very irascible.

**जन्मपर्ति विकलाङ्गं पश्यति सौरिश्चतुष्टये प्रबलः।  
यस्य स भाग्यविहीनः प्रव्रज्यां प्राप्नुयात्पुरुषः॥५०॥**

 *Sloka* 50.—If at a birth Saturn, strong in a Kendra, should aspect the lord of the Rasi occupied by the Moon who is weak, the person will be defective of a limb, and be unlucky ; and he will become a religious mendicant.

**आरार्कजीवशनयः सहिता विलग्न-  
केन्द्रत्रिकोणरहिता विबला यदि स्युः।  
जातः कुलात्ययकरो धनपुत्रदारै-  
र्हीनो विदेशनिरतो मुनिरेष उक्तः॥५१॥**

 * Sloka* 51.—If Mars, the Sun, Jupiter and Saturn join together in a Rasi other than the Lagna, a Kendra or a Trikona and be weak in strength, the person born will make the family to become extinct. He will be without wife, children and wealth and be living in a foreign place; and he becomes a recluse.

**गुरुहिमगुरवीणामेक एवोदयस्थो  
गगनतलगतो वा रिःफगश्चाल्पमूर्तिः।  
अविकलबलभाजा सूर्यपुत्रेण दृष्टो  
भवति हि नरनाथो दीक्षितः स्यात्स एव॥५२॥**

 *Sloka* 52.—If only one of the planets, *viz*. Jupiter, the Moon and the Sun, be in the Lagna, or in the 10th thouse and another planet (slightly visible) occupy the 12th shouse and be aspected by an unimpaired strong Saturn, the person born will be a leader of men and he will perform a grand sacrificial ceremony or take the holy order.

**कुमुदगहनबन्धुं सौम्यभागे बलस्थं  
वियति गमनशीलः स्वोच्चमित्रर्क्षसंस्थः।  
यदि दिनकरपुत्रः पश्यति प्राप्तवीर्यो  
जनयति खलु जातं तापसं दुःखभाजम्॥५३॥**

 Sloka 53.—If the Moon, posited in a benefic Navamsa, be strong and be aspected by Saturn who has also attained strength, and who is going to the zenith and is posited in his own exaltation or friendly house, his own exaltation or friend the Yoga formed will make the person born an ascetic who will be unhappy.

**अतिशयबलयुक्तः शीतगुः शुक्लपक्षे  
बलविरहितरक्तप्रेक्षितो लग्ननाथः।  
यदि भवति तपस्वी सन्ततं शोकतप्तो  
धनजनपरिहीणः कृच्छ्रलब्धान्नपानः॥५४॥**

 *Sloka* 54.—If in the bright half of a month the Moon endowed with exceeding strength, and the lord of the Lagna be aspected by weak Mars, the person born in the Yoga will become an ascetic always troubled by sorrow and misery. He will have neither wealth nor people to help him, and an alterna- tive interpretation is that the Moon (posited in Kumbha) may herself be the lord of the Lagna being aspected by Mars occupying his depression Rasi and therefore weak and will obtain his food after a great effort.

**लग्नेश्वरोऽर्कसहितो यदि वीक्षमाण-  
श्चन्द्रं विलग्नभवनं यदि पापदृष्टम्।  
तत्र स्थितो भृगुसुतः सुरपूजितो वा कुर्या-  
न्नितान्तमभिजन्म विनाशयन्तम्॥५५॥**

 * Sloka* 55.—If the lord of the Lagna conjoined with the Sun aspect the Moon and if the rising sign be aspected by a malefic, and if Venus or Jupiter occupy the Lagna, the person born will destroy completely his noble birth.

**नीचारिभांशकगतो भृगुजस्त्रिकोणे  
पापे विलग्नभवने शुभदृष्टिहीने।  
गार्हस्थ्यधर्मरहितो मुनिरस्य चाहु-  
राजीवनं सकललोकमतानुसारि॥५६॥**

 *Sloka* 56.—If Venus occupy his depression or inimical Rasi or Navamsa, a malefic be in a Trikona, and the Lagna be devoid of benefic aspect, the person born will be a recluse and will not follow the duties ordained for a house-holder. He will live throughout without any definite principle of his own.

**इत्यादि योगान् सकलान्निरूप्य बलाबलं चापि शुभाशुभानाम्।  
ज्ञात्वा नराणां प्रकृतिं समक्ष्य समादिशेत्तत्र दशाफलानि॥५७॥**

इति श्रीवराहमिहिरसुतश्रीपृथुयशोविरचिते होरासारे जातकभङ्गाध्यायश्चतुर्विंशः॥

* Sloka* 57.—After examining carefully the various Yogas above described, and the strength or weakness of of the several planets benefic and malefic-and the nature of the several persons concerned, the astrologer should predict the effects of the Dasa-periods required.

Thus ends the 24th Adhyaya entitled the marring of horoscopes, in Horasara, a work composed by Sri: Prithuyasas, son of Sri: Varahamihira.  
**———————**

**पञ्चविंशोऽध्यायः**

**अथ स्त्रीजातकफलानि**

**स्त्रीपुरुषयोः समानं योगादि दशाफलं च पूर्वोक्तम्।  
यद्यदयोग्यं स्त्रीणां तत्तत्सर्वं वदेत्स्वनाथेषु॥१॥**

* Sloka* 1.—The effects derivable from the Yogas and the Dasas described already which are common to both men and women are applicable to both. Those that are found (in female horoscopes) suitable to females should be declared as applicable to them alone; the rest should be ascribed to their husbands.

**वैधव्यं निधनगृहे पतिसौभाग्यं सुखं च जामित्रे।  
सौन्दर्यं तु विलग्ने विचिन्तयेत् पुत्रसम्पदं नवमे॥२॥**

 *Sloka* 2.—The death of the husband is to be deduced through the 8th house (from the Lagna or the Moon whichever is strong). Her happiness and her husband's appearance, etc, are to be declared from the 7th house. Matters relating to her appearance, beauty, etc. should be determined from the Lagna. Children and wealth should be declared through the 7th house.

**एषु स्थानेषु युताः सौम्याः शुभदा बलान्विता ज्ञेयाः।  
क्रूरास्तु नेष्टफलदा भवनेशविवर्जिताः सदा चिन्त्यम्॥३॥**

 *Sloka* 3.—Benefics endowed with strength are known to produce the good effects pertaining to the Bhava they occupy, while malefics, the contrary. In the case of Bhavas which are not occupied by their lords, effects should always be judged in this manner.

**पुरुषर्क्षे पुरुषांशे लग्नेन्द्वोः पापयुक्तयोर्जाता।  
पुरुषाकृतिशीलता भर्त्तुरयोग्याऽसमञ्जसा कन्या॥४॥**

* Sloka* 4.— If the Lagna or the Moon (whichever of them is stronger) be in male signs and male Navamsas, she will be masculine in form and masculine in her bearing; if they be conjoined with (or aspected by) malefic planets, she will be unbecoming and unfit for the husband.

**समराशौ समभागे लग्नेन्द्रः स्त्रीगुणान्विता कन्या।  
सौम्ययुतदृष्टयोर्वा सुभगा साध्वी च विख्याता॥५॥**

 *Sloka* 5.—If both the Ascendant and the Moon are in even signs, the woman born will be truly feminine in character. If in the above benefic planets should also conjoin with or aspect the Lagna and the Moon, she will possess excellent qualities, be of steadfast virtue and famous.

**लग्नेन्द्वोर्यो बलवांस्तस्य त्रिंशांशकैः फलं वाच्यम्।  
त्रिंशांशेशो बलवांस्तत्प्रोक्तफलानि सम्यगायान्ति॥६॥**

 *Sloka* 6.—Of the two signs, *viz*., Lagna Rasi and the Janma Rasi, find which is stronger; it is with reference to the stronger that the Trimsamsa effects should be declared, and they will very well fit in for the particular horoscope, provided the lord of the Trimsamsa is strong.

**भौमर्क्षे भौमांशे कन्या मृतसूतिका गुणैर्हीना।  
मायाविनी बुधांशे मलिनाचाराऽल्पपुत्रा स्यात्॥७॥**

 *Sloka* 7.—When the Lagna or the Moon is in a sign belonging to Mars, the female born in a Trimsamsa of Mars will bring forth a still-born child; and she will If in a Trimsamsa of Mercury, have no good qualitiesnaved; she will have few she will be deceitful, and children.

**पुत्रवती जीवांशे बहुव्ययार्त्ता पतिप्रिया कन्या।  
कन्याजननी कन्या शुक्रांशे जारभोगसन्तुष्टा॥८॥**

 *Sloka* 8.—(When the Lagna or the Moon is in a Rasi owned by Mars), the female born in a Trimsamsa of Jupiter, will have issue, will be troubled by heavy expenditure, and will be loved by the husband. If she be born in a Trimsamsa of Venus, she will be the mother of daughters, and she will be addicted to a paramour.

**मन्दांशे प्रेष्या स्याद्दुःशीला बहुविधा वनिता।  
भानोरप्येवं हि त्रिंशांशफलं समादेश्यम्॥९॥**

 *Sloka* 9.—If she be born in a Trimsamsa of Saturn, the female concerned will be a servant-maid and vicious in her habit in various ways; if the Trimsamsa of birth be the Sun's, the same effect should be declared.

**बुधभवने भौमांशे कन्या जारप्रियाल्पपुत्रा स्यात्।  
सौम्यांशे तु कुलाढ्या पशुधनभोगान्विता च शुक्रांशे॥१०॥**

 *Sloka* 10.—When the Lagna or the Moon is in a sign belonging to Mercury, the female born in a Trimsamsa of Mars will go to a paramour and will have few children ; if in a Trimsamsa of Mercury, she will have a family; if in a Trimsamsa of Venus, she will be blessed with cattle, wealth and other enjoyments.

**साध्वी पतिप्रिया वा जीवांशे क्षेत्रतुङ्गगे जीवे।  
मन्दांशे कविसमा मृतप्रजा वा न भर्तृयुक्ता वा॥१२॥**

 *Sloka* 12.—If the female be born in a Trimsamsa of Jupiter, she will be chaste, if Jupiter be in his exaltation ; if in a Trimsamsa of Saturn, she willbe of the nature of a hermaphrodite; or she will bring forth a still-born child, or she will be separated from her husband.

**जीवर्क्षे भौमांशे कन्या परिचारिणी सुविख्याता।  
जीवांशे तु धनाढ्या सौम्यांशे लोकपूजिता ललना॥१३॥**

**पुत्रवती शुक्रांशे सद्गुणयुक्ता पतिप्रिया साध्वी।  
सौरांशे तु दरिद्रा कन्याजननी स्वतन्त्रनिरता स्यात्॥१४॥**

 *Slokas* 13.14.—If at a birth the Lagna or the Moon be owned by Jupiter, the female born in a Trimsamsa of Mars will be a servant-maid and famous; if in a Trimsamsa of Jupiter, she will command wealth ; if in a Trimsamsa of Mercury she will be respected by all; if in a Trimsamsa of Venus, she will have children, and possess good qualities; she will be loved by the husband and she will be virtuous; if in a Trimsamsa of Saturn, she will be poor, mother of daughters and self-willed.

**सितभवने भौमांशे दुष्टा कलहप्रिया पतिद्वेष्या।  
कुचरित्रा सौम्यांशे काव्यकलागेयवाद्य सन्तुष्टा॥१५॥**

**रूपान्विता गुणाढ्या जीवांशे भर्तृपुत्रसम्पन्ना।  
शुक्रांशे भोगवती विदग्धवनिता जनप्रिया ख्याता॥१६॥**

**मन्दांशे च पुनर्भूर्मृतप्रजा रोगसंयुता नित्यम्।**

 * Slokas* 15-16.—If at a birth the Lagna or the Moon be owned by Venus, the female born in a Trimsamsa of Mars, will be unchaste and quarrelsome and she will be hated by her hushand; she will be ill-behaved. If she be born in a Trimsamsa of Mercury, she will be fond of poetry and all the Arts-vocal and instrumental; if born in a Trimsamsa of Jupiter, she will be endowed with beauty, will be of good qualities, possess a good husband, and children. If she be born in a Trimsamsa of Venus, she will be the favourite of her husband, will be clever and liked by the people and famous; if the Trimsamsa of birth belong to Saturn, she will be remarried, will have her children still-born and will ever suffer from diseases.

**मन्दर्क्षे भौमांशे दासी कुलटा मृतप्रजा कन्या॥१७॥**

**भग्नव्रता च कुलटा मायाविन्यब्जजस्यांशे।  
भर्तुः प्रिया च सुभगा जीवांशे लोकविख्याता॥१८॥**

**शुक्रांशे प्रभुशीला वन्ध्या चारित्रलोपिनी वनिता।  
मन्दर्क्षे मन्दांशे नीचाचाराऽतिदुर्भगा वनिता॥१९ ॥**

 * Slokas* 17.19.—When the Lagna or the Moon belongs to Saturn, the female born in a Trimsamsa of Mars will be a maidservant, will be unchaste, and her children will be still-born. If the Trimsamsa of birth be owned by Mercury, the female will be faithless, unchaste and deceitful. If she be born in a Trimsamsa of Jupiter, she will be liked by her husband, charming will be like and world-famous; if in a Trimsamsa belonging to Venus, she will be of a lordly disposition, will have no children, and she will be of bad conduct; if born in a Trimsamsa of Saturn, she will be vile in disposition and very ugly.

**वाचाटा रविभवने कुजभागे जारिणी विदेशरता।  
पुरुषाकृतिशीलयुता सौम्यांशे कार्यचारिणी कुलटा॥२०॥**

**नृपतिप्रियाऽल्पपुत्रा शुक्रांशे नित्यरोगिणी भवति।  
कुशलाकृतिर्दरिद्रा मन्दांशे राजवल्लभा जैवे॥२१॥**

 *Slokas* 20-21.—If the Lagna at brith or the Moon be the Sun's Rasi, the female born in a Trimsamsa of Mars will be very talkative; she will be an adulteress, will be absent at other places; she will be male-like in form and dispostiion; if she be born in a Trimsamsa of Mercury, she will be attentive to her work, but unchaste. If the Trimsamsa belongs to Venus, she will become the king's favourite, will have few children and will always suffer from diseases; if born in Saturn's Trimsamsa, she will possess a good body, and she will be indigent; and if in Jupiter's Trimsamsa, she will become the king's favourite.

**शशिभवने भौमांशे स्वच्छन्दा कामिनी विनष्टसुता।  
अल्पसुता क्षीणायुर्जीवांशे शिल्पिनी बुधस्यांशे॥२१॥**

**बन्ध्या मृतप्रजा वा शुक्रांशे स्त्री च दुष्टरता।  
मन्दांशे पतिहीना वनिता कृच्छ्रोपजीविनी भवति॥२३॥**

 *Slokas* 22.-23.—When the Lagna at birth or the Rasi occupied by the Moon is Karkataka, the female born, in a Trimsamsa of Mars will be self-willed, lustful and will lose children; if in a Trimsamsa of Jupiter, she will have few children and will be short-lived; if in Mercury's Trimsamsa, she will be skilled in the arts. If the Trim. samsa of birth belong to Venus, she will be barren or will lose children and she will love wicked persons. If the Trimsamsa of birth be owned by Saturn, she will lose her husband and will earn her living with great difficulty.

**त्रिंशांशकफलमेवं वक्तव्यं देवविद्वद्भिः।  
स्फुटचन्द्रतरणियोगात् त्रिंशाञ्चफलं विनिर्दिशेत्तस्याः॥२४॥**

**लग्नेन्द्वोर्योगवशात् त्रिंशांशफलं विनिर्दिशेदथवा।**

 * Sloka* 24-24½—Thus should the effects of the several Trimsamsas be predicted by the astrologers; or, the effects due to the particular Trimsamsa indicated by the sum-total of the figures for (1) the Sun and the Moon or (2) the Lagna and the Moon should be examined and declared.

**शून्येऽस्ते दुर्बले यस्याः पापग्रहनिरीक्षिते॥२५॥**

**सौम्यग्रहदशा हीने भर्ता कापुरुषो भवेत्।**

 *Sloka* 25-25½—When the 7th house is vacant and without strength, and is aspected by a malefic planet and is devoid of benefic aspect, the female born will have a contemptible wretch for her husband.

**बुधमन्दयुतेऽस्ते च पतिः क्लीबसमो भवेत्॥२६॥**

**बन्ध्या वा दुर्भगावाऽपि सा च नित्यं प्रवासिनी।  
सप्तमे चरराशौ च तदीशे चरमांशके॥२७॥**

**भर्ता प्रवासशीलः स्यात् स्थिरभे स्वगृहे वसेत्।**

 *Slokas* 26-27½—If Mercury conjoined with Saturn be in the 7th house, the husband of the female born will be impotent. She will be barren or loathed by the husband, and she will always be away from home. When a moveable sign represents the 7th Bhava and its lord is also posited in a moveable Rasi or Navamsa, the husband will always be away from home. an immoveable one, he will stick to his house.

**अस्तभेऽर्केऽरिभिर्दृष्टे भर्त्रोत्सुष्टा भवेत्स्वयम्॥२८॥**

**सप्तमस्थे कुजे तद्वद्बाल्ये सा विधवा भवेत्।  
मन्दे सप्तमराशिस्थे तथा शत्रुनिरीक्षिते॥२९॥**

**कन्या वा विधवा भूत्वा जारानपि च गच्छति।**

 *Slokas* 28-29½—If the Sun occupying the 7th Bhava be aspected by inimcal planets, the woman herself will be cast away by her husband; if Mars occupy a similar position, she will become a widow at an early age. If Saturn in the 7th Bhava be aspected by an inimical planet, she will remain unmarried or become a widow and she will be addicted to other men.

**द्यूने शुभाशुभैर्युक्ते पुनर्भूर्वा भविष्यति॥३०॥**

**अस्तगावारमन्दौ चेत् पापर्क्षे विधवा भवेत्।**

* Sloka* 30-30½—If the 7th house be occupied by planets both benefic and malefic-the female concerned will remarry. If Mars and Saturn occupy the 7th house and if that house be a malefic one, the woman concerned will become a widow.

**बहुभर्त्री भवेत्कन्या सार्के राहौ तु सप्तमे॥३१॥**

**बलहीनेऽस्तगे पापे सौम्यग्रहनिरीक्षिते।  
भर्त्रा विसृज्यते नारी नीचारिस्थे च वैरिणी॥३२॥**

* Slokas* 31-32.—If the Sun along with Rahu be in the 7th house, the female concerned will have many husbands. If a weak malefic occupy the 7th house and has no benefic aspect, the woman concerned will be cast away by her husband; and if the said malefic be in 2 depressed or an inimical house, she will be at variance with her husband.

**अन्योन्यांशे सितारौ चेञ्जारासक्ता भवेद्वधूः।  
तथैव सप्तमे चन्द्रे सा पत्या दुश्चरेत्सह॥३३॥**

 * Sloka* 33.—If Venus and Mars mutually occupy each the other's Navamsa, the female born will be addicted to a paramour. If in the above case the Moon should also be posited in the 7th Bhava, she will misbehave in this fashion along with her husband.

**मन्दारर्क्षे विलग्नस्थौ शशिशुक्रौ यदा तदा।  
वन्ध्या भवति सा नारी पञ्चमे पापसंयुते॥३४॥**

* Sloka* 34.—If the Moon and Venus occupy Rasis owned by Saturn and Mars identical with the Lagna, and the 5th house be conjoined with a malefic planet, the female concerned will become barren.

**अस्तराश्यंशगे भौमे सूर्यजेऽस्तांशगेऽपि वा।  
सौरेण भूर्भुवा दृष्टे व्याधियोनिश्च दुर्भगा॥३५॥**

* Sloka* 35.—(1) Mars in the 7th Rasi or Navamsa and aspected by Saturn, or (2) Saturn in the 7th Rasi or Navamsa and aspected by Venus will make the female born to have a diseased womb and a repulsive appearance.

**अस्तर्क्षे शुभदृष्टे च शुभस्यांशे शुभक्षिते।  
चारुश्रोणी प्रिया भर्तृवल्लभा च भवेद् ध्रुवम्॥३६॥**

* Sloka* 36.—If the 7th Rasi be a benefic one and be aspected by a benefic planet and if the setting Navamsa be owned by a benefic and aspected by a benefic, the female concerned will have beautiful hips and surely be- come lovely and her husband's favourite.

**अस्तेऽर्के स्वांशके चर्क्षे भर्ता रतिपरो मृदुः।  
चन्द्रेऽस्ते स्वांशके चर्क्षे मृदुः परवशः पतिः॥३७॥**

**भौमेऽस्ते स्वांशके क्षेत्रे स्त्रीलोलो निर्धनः पतिः।  
सौम्येऽस्ते स्वांशके क्षेत्रे भर्ता विद्वान् सुखी भवेत्॥३८॥**

**जीवेऽस्ते स्वांशके क्षेत्रे गुणवान् निर्जितेन्द्रियः।  
शुक्रेऽस्ते स्वांशके क्षेत्रे कान्तः सौभाग्यवान् सुखी॥३९॥**

**मन्देऽस्ते स्वांशके क्षेत्रे वृद्धो मूर्खो भवेत् पतिः।  
एवं सप्तमराशिस्थैर्ग्रहः स्त्रीणां फलं वदेत्॥४०॥**

 *Slokas* 37-40.—When the Sun occupies his own Rasi and Navamsa in in the 7th house, the female born will have a husband gentle and ever bent upon sensual pleasure. When the Moon occupies such a position, the husband will be of a gentle disposition and henpecked. When Mars is in the same position, the husband will be running after women and will be penniless. If Mercury be in such a position, the husband will be learned and happy; if the planet be Jupiter, the female concerned will get a spouse who will have good qualities and have all his senses under control; if it be Venus, the husband will be handsome and voluptuous; lastly, if it be Saturn, he will be an old dolt. Thus should the effects of planets occupy- ing the 7th Bhava in the horoscopes of females. be declared.

**अस्तराशिफलं प्रोक्तं लग्नराशेः फलं तथा।  
फलं भवति दम्पत्योर्बहुयोगफलं वदेत्॥४१॥**

 *Sloka* 41—The effects declared above as arising from the 7th house as also those due to the Lagna Bhava constitute the elaborate combined effects of the couple; e elaborat effects of the and such other effects following from various other planetary positions should be declared for the couple.

**सौम्यक्षेत्रोदये चन्द्रे शुक्रेण सहिते वधूः।  
सुखान्विता पतिद्वेष्या नित्यमस्थिरचारिणी॥४२॥**

 *Sloka* 42—If the Lagna be owned by Mercury and the Moon be cojoined with Venus, the female concerned will live in ease and comfort, will be hated by her husband, will be fickleminded and always roaming about.

 Another interpretation **:** When the Moon occupying the Lagna owned by Mercury, is associated with Venus, etc.

**चन्द्रज्ञौ यदि लग्नस्थौ कुलाढ्या ब्रह्मवादिनी।  
शुक्रज्ञौ यदि लग्नस्थौ सौभाग्यस्था कुलाढ्यका॥४३॥**

**चान्द्रिचन्द्रसिता लग्ने बहुसौख्यधनैर्युता।  
जीवे लग्नेऽतिसम्पन्ना पुत्रवित्तसुखप्रदा॥४४॥**

* Slokas* 43-44.—If the Moon and Mercury occupy the Lagna, the female concerned will have a large family; she will become a philosopher expounding the scriptures. If Venus and Mercury be in the Lagna, she will be blessed with beauty, happiness and become the chief member of the family. If the Moon, Mercury and Venus be in the Lagna, the female concerned will be endowed with wealth and all kinds of comfort. When Jupiter is in the Lagna, she will be exceedingly prosperous and be blessed with children, wealth and happiness.

**क्षेत्रोज्ञ संस्थिता लग्ने ह्यशुभास्ते शुभप्रदाः।**

* Sloka* 44^(_(1/2)).—If planets in their own or exaltation house occupy the Lagna, they will, even if they be malefic, prove auspicious.

**क्ररेऽष्टमे विधवता पापदृष्टे विशेषतः।  
निधनेशांशकपतेर्दशायां निश्चयं वदेत्॥४५॥ **

* Sloka* 45.—When the 8th Bhava is occupied by a malefic planet, the woman concerned becomes a widow, and the widowhood will be a certainty when the Bhava in question is also aspected by a malefic, and it will occur invariably during the Dasa of the ruler of the Navamsa occupied by the lord of the 8th house.

**सौम्येऽष्टमस्थे कन्याया भर्त्तुः पूर्वं मृतिर्भवेत्।  
पापसौम्ययुते तस्मिन् समकाले तयोर्मृतिः॥४६॥**

**बलाबलं तयोर्ज्ञेयं पुरुषेण विजानता।**

* Slokas* 46-46½_(^(.))—If a benefic planet be in the 8th house, the demise of the female concerned will occur prior to that of her husband. If the 8th house be occupied by planets—both benefic and malefic—their exit from the world will be simultaneous. The astrologer should declare this after ascertaining the strength or otherwise of the planets concerned.

**भाग्यस्थाने स्थिते सौम्ये सपापेऽस्तेऽष्टमेऽपि वा॥४७॥**

**भर्तृपुत्रसुखैः सार्धं दीर्घकालं च जीवति।**

* Sloka* 47-47½.—If a benefic planet occupy the 9th house and a malefic one be posited in the 7th or the 8th house, the female concerned will lead a life of happiness for a long period in the company of her husband endowed with children and wealth, load

**धनुःकर्कि षे लग्ने भर्तृपुत्रादि दुःखदा॥४८॥**

* Sloka* 48.—When the Lagna happens to be Dhanus, Karkataka or Meena, she will cause misery to her husband, children and others.

**सिंहालिवृषकन्यासु चन्द्रे तिष्ठति पञ्चमे।  
अल्पापत्यां विजानीयात्पुरुषेषु तथा वदेत्॥४९॥**

* Sloka* 49.—When Simha, Vrischika, Vrishabha or Kanya happens to be the 5th house and the Moon occupies the same, the female concerned will have few children. The same remark will hold good in the case of men.

**लग्नास्ताष्टमभाग्यस्थैः पापैर्दुःख फलान्विता।  
सौम्यग्रहैरसम्मिश्रैः सर्वथा क्लेशमाप्नुयात्॥५०॥**

 * Sloka* 50.—If malefic planets occupy the Lagna, the 7th, the 8th and the 9th houses, the female concerned will experience unhappiness and misery. If the said houses are not intermixed with benefic planets, she will undoubtedly be miserable.

**क्रूरग्रहे हैः) सुखगते (तैः) बहुप्रसवमादिशेत्।  
कन्याप्रदानकालेषु प्रोक्तमार्गविचिन्तयेत्॥५१॥**

इति श्रीवराहमिहिरसुतश्रीपृथुयशोविरचिते होरासारे  
स्त्रीजातकाध्यायः पञ्चविंशः॥

 *Sloka* 51.—If a malefic planet occupy the 4th house in a female’s nativity, her progeny will be many. The astrologer should adopt the method above cited at the time when a girl is married.

Thus ends the 25th Adhyaya entitled “Horoscopes of  
Women” in Horasara, a work composed by Sri: Prithuyasay  
son of Sri **:** Varahamihira.

**\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_**

**षड्विंशोऽध्यायः**

अथ नैर्याणिकलक्षणानि॥

**प्रजातानी च जन्तूनां मरणं येन केनचित्।  
तन्निमित्तपरिज्ञानं वक्ष्ये निर्याणलक्षणम्॥१॥**

* Sloka*1.—In the case of all creatures born in this, world, Death will happen through some reason or other In order to find out the time when it will come off, I shall describe the several causes by which the same happens.

**शिखिजलशस्त्रनिपातैर्ज्वरामयक्षुत्कृतैरिनाद्यैः स्यात्।  
विश्वनखैर्पतिहेतुः पश्वेशाभ्वस्वके चरावैश्च ॥२॥**

* Sloka* 2.—If the 8th house be occupied by several planets, death will happen through the following causes: when the occupying planet is the Sun, death will be due to fire; if the Moon, it will be by water; if Mars, by a weapon; if Mercury, by a fall; if Jupiter, by fever; if Venus, by indigestion; and if Saturn, by hunger. And according as the 8th house is a moveable, fixed or a mutable sign, death will be in a foreign place, in one’s own house, or on the road.

**बहुलग्रहसंयुक्ते निधने बहुदोषसंश्रयान्निधनम्।  
शशिलग्नयोर्विशेषाद्बलिनो रन्ध्रस्थितैर्ग्रहश्चिन्त्यम्॥३॥**

* Sloka* 3.—When there are many planets posited in the 8th house, death will be due to diseases of various kinds pertaining to these planets. The reckoning of the 8th house should be specially with reference to the Moon or the Lagna whichever is stronger.

**लग्नादष्टमराशेः स्वभावदोषोद्भवां मृतिं विद्यात्।  
निधनेशस्य नवांशस्थितराशिनिमित्तदोषजनितां वा॥४॥**

* Sloka* 4.—One’s death should be expected to happen through diseases caused by the humour belonging to the 8th house or to the Navamsa Rasi occupied by the lord of the 8th house.

**मेषांशे मेषे वा ज्वरविषजठराग्निपित्तसम्भूताम्।  
येन ग्रहेण युक्ते दृष्टे वा तत्समानदोषेण॥५॥**

* Sloka* 5.—If such a Rasi or Navamsa belong to Mesha, death will be due to fever, poison, disorder in the stomach and biliousness. If it be conjoined or aspected by a planet, death will be caused by a disorder peculiar to that planet.

**वृषभे वृषभांशे वा त्रिदोषसाङ्कर्यशस्त्रदाहाद्यैः।  
ग्रहरहिते प्रोक्तफलं ग्रहयुक्ते तत्समानदोषेण॥६॥**

 *Sloka* 6.—If the Rasi or Navamsa belong to Vrishabha, and be unoccupied, death will happen through vitiation of the three humours of the body, by weapon, or fire ; if occupied by a planet, it will be caused by a morbid affection peculiar to that planet.

**मिथुने मिथुनांशे वा कासश्वासोष्णरोगशूलाद्यैः।  
चन्द्रगृहे चन्द्रांशे वातोन्मादातिरेचनाद्वापि॥७॥**

* Sloka* 7.—If the Rasi or Navamsa belong to Mithuna, it will be due to cough, asthma, excessive heat, colic and the like. If Karkataka be the Rasi or Navamsa, death will happen through rheumatism, insanity or diarrhoea.

**स्फोटकविषशस्त्राद्यैर्ज्वरेण सिंहस्थिते तदशे वा।  
जठराग्निगुह्यकलहप्रपातनाद्यैश्च कन्यायाम्॥८॥**

 *Sloka* 8.—If the Rasi or Navamsa be Simha, death will be due to a boil, poison, weapon and the like, or fever. If it be Kanya, death will be caused by the disorder of the stomach, or privities, quarrel, a fall a from a precipice and the like.

**तौलिनि तदंशके वा स्वबुद्धिदोषेण हन्यते पुरुषः।  
ज्वरसन्निपातदोषैर्मरणं ब्रूयाद्दशाफलोक्तैर्वा॥९॥**

* Sloka* 9.—If the Rasi or Navamsa belong to Tula, the person meets with death through some fault of his own, a dangerous fever, or some cause pertaining to the Dasa at the time.

**वृश्चिकमवनतदंशे पाण्डुग्रहिणीप्लिहादिदोषवश्चात्।  
वृक्षजलशस्त्रकाष्ठैश्चापांशे पापसंयुते मृत्युः॥१०॥**

* Sloka* 10.—If the Navamsa or Rasi be Vrischika, the cause of death will be jaundice, enlargement of the spleen aud the like. When it is the Dhanur Rasi or Navamsa and a malefic be posited therein, death will be due to a tree, water, weapon or wood.

**मकरे मकरांशे वा शूलात्कृषिबुद्धिसम्भ्रमान्मृत्युः।  
पापयुते व्याघ्राद्यैः कासज्वर यक्ष्म कृत्रिमैर्मरणम्॥११॥ **

 *Sloka* 11.—If the Rasi or Navamsa be owned by the sign Makara, death will be caused by impalement, ploughing, or derangement of the mind. If the Rasi or Navamsa be also conjoined with a malefic, death may be caused by being mauled by tigers, by cough, fever, consumption or through an unnatural cause.

**कुम्भे कुम्भांशे वा पापयुते व्याघ्रशस्त्रभुजगाद्यैः।  
कासज्वरयक्ष्मकृतैर्मरणं ब्रूयात्समुद्दिष्टम्॥१२॥**

 *Sloka* 12.—When the Rasi or Navamsa is conjoined with a malefic, death will be caused by tigers, weapons, serpents and the like, through cough, fever, pulmonary diseases, etc.

**मीने मीनांशे वा सर्पेण वधोऽध्ववातयन्त्रैर्वा।  
नौभेदाञ्जलमध्ये जलधरशब्देन पीडितो म्रियते॥१३॥**

* Sloka* 13.—If the Rasi or Navamsa belong to Meena, death will be through serpent-bites, while on a journey, through a storm or machine, dashing of a steamer (on a rock), or through thunder.

**अतिसारज्वरदाहोदरामयैर्विषहतान्नविच्छेदैः।  
देहौचित्यजरोगैः सामान्यं मृत्युमादिशेन्नृृणाम्॥१४॥**

 *Sloka*14.—In the case of human beings, death should be declared as due to dysentery, fever, burning, disease of the belly, poison, beatings, discontinuance of food, and diseases inborn with the body generally.

अथ नैर्याणिकयोगाः॥

**पूर्वोक्तमृत्युभागे शशिनि विलग्ने व्ययेऽथवा निधने।  
जलयन्त्रकारणैर्वा निधनं नृृणां समुद्दिष्टम्॥१५॥**

 * Sloka* 15.—When the Moon happens to be in the fatal degree mentioned before of the Lagna, the 12th or the 8th house, death should be expected in the case of human beings as arising through water, machinery, etc.

**अर्केन्दू लग्नगतौ द्विदेहभवनेषु पापयुतदृष्टौ।  
कुरुतः प्राणविनाशं जलमध्ये निश्चितं ब्रूयात्॥१६॥**

* Sloka* 16—When the two luminaries (the Sun and the Moon) occupy the Lagna identical with a dual sign and aspected by or conjoined with a malefic planet, they bring about the death of the person concerned in the midst of water invariably.

**हिबुकास्तदशमसंस्थैः सौरेन्दुधरासुतैः क्रमान्नियतम्।  
वृक्षाग्रे कूपे वा मरणं नृृणां विनिर्देश्यम्॥१७॥ **

* Sloka* 17.—If Saturn, the Moon and Mars respectively occupy the 4th, the 7th and the 10th houses in a nativity, death will be by a fall from the top of a tree or in a well.

**भौमार्कजभवनेन्दो पापद्वयमध्यगे न सौम्ययुते।  
कन्यायां वा हिमगौ रज्वाऽशनिपातशस्त्रदोषैर्वा॥१८॥**

* Sloka* 18.—When the Moon is in a house owned by Mars or Saturn and is hemmed in betwixt two malefics and is not conjoined with a benefic, for when the Moon occupies sign Kanya, the death of the person concerned will be by a rope, a fall of thunderbolt or a hit from a weapon.

**सुखदशमसथैः पापैः सौम्यैर्निधनोदयस्थितैस्तस्य।  
शूलप्रोतान्मरणं हृच्छूलाद्वा न सन्देहः॥१९॥**

* Sloka* 19.—If malefics occupy the 4th and 10th houses, and benefics be posited in the 8th and the 1st houses, the death of the person concerned will happen through impalement or by an acute pain in the chest.

**सौरे हिमगौ व्ययगे रिपुरन्ध्रगतेऽथवा सुखे वाऽपि।  
निधनं वारिनिधौ स्यान्निधने पापद्वयान्तःस्थे॥२०॥**

* Sloka* 20.—If Saturn and the Moon occupy the 12th, the 6th, the 8th or the 4th house, the demise of the person may happen in the sea. The same will be the case if the lord of the 8th house (or the 8th house itself) be betwixt two malefics.

**चन्द्रात् त्रिकोण संस्थैः पापैर्लग्नात् त्रिकोणसंस्थैर्वा।  
उद्बन्धनाच्च निधनं निधनेशे भोगिसंयुक्ते॥२१॥**

* Sloka* 21.— When malefics occupy triangular houses with respect to the Moon or the Ascendant, death will be caused by hanging. The same will be the case when the lord of the 8th house is conjoined with Rahu.

**राहुयुतेऽर्के लग्ने चन्द्रे रिपुसंस्थितेऽथवा निधने।  
व्ययसंस्थितैश्च पापैर्विषेण शस्त्रेण वा मृत्युः॥२२॥**

* Sloka* 22.—When the Sun is conjoined with Rahu in the Lagna and the Moon is posited in the 6th or the 8th house and the malefic planets occupy the 12th house, death will be caused by poison or through a weapon.

**चतुरश्रव्ययसंस्थे राहौ निधनेश्वरेण सन्दृष्टे।  
पापयुते दृष्टेः वा निधने विषशस्त्रवह्निदोषेण॥२३॥**

* Sloka* 23.—When Rahu is posited in the 4th, the 8th or the 12th house and is aspected by the lord of the 8th house, or if the 8th house be conjoined with or aspected by a malefic, death will be due to poison, weapon or fire.

**राहुध्वजान्वितेऽर्के जामित्रे रन्ध्रसंस्थिते शुक्रे।  
पापग्रहे तनुगते ह्युद्बन्धेनोपहन्यते पुरुषः॥२४॥**

 * Sloka* 24.—When the Sun combined with Rahu or Ketu is in the 7th house, Venus is posited in the 8th and a malefic occupies the Lagna, the person concerned meets with his death through hanging.

**पापद्वयमध्यगते होरेशे केन्द्रसंस्थिते तस्य।  
यः कश्चिन्निधनगतो निधनं स्यादात्मकोपदोषेण॥२५॥ **

* Sloka* 25.—If the lord of the Lagna be hemmed in betwixt two malefics and occupy a Kendra house, and any other planet be posited in the 8th house therefrom, the person concerned will meet with his death through his own anger (or by the vitiation of the humour relating to that planet.

**अर्कोदयेऽर्कपुत्रे सुतगे कुजेऽपि धनभाग्ये।  
वृक्षाशनिकुड्याद्यैर्योगे जातस्य निर्दिशेन्मृत्युम्॥२६॥**

* Sloka* 26.—When the Sun is in the rising sign, Saturn is in the 5th house, and Mars occupies the 2nd or the 9th house, the person concerned meets with his end by a fall from a tree, thunderbolt, or a wall (or by being beaten with a club).

**क्षीणेन्दौ निधनस्थे सुखगे सूर्ये शनौ च जामित्रे।  
भौमे कुटुम्बसंस्थे योगे जातस्य काष्ठपातेन॥२७॥**

* Slokas* 27.—The waning Moon in the 8th house, the Sun in the 4th, Saturn in the 7th and Mars in the 2nd bring about the death of the person through the fall of a wood.

 **जातस्य निर्दिशेन्मृत्युम्** is another reading for **काष्ठपातेन** in the last quarter.

**क्षीणेन्दौ दशमगते नवमे सारे शनौ विलग्नस्थे।  
दिननाथे सुतसंस्थे जातस्याग्नौ निबन्धने निधनम्॥२८॥**

* Sloka* 28.—When the waning Moon occupies the 10th house, Mars is in the 9th, Saturn is in the Lagna and the Sun is in the 5th, the person concerned will meet with his end by being bound and thrown into the fire.

**तुलायां रुधिरे जातः कुजर्क्षे भास्करे स्थिते।  
चन्द्रे मन्दारभं याते विण्मध्ये मरणं व्रजेत्॥२९॥**

* Sloka* 29. —Mars being in Tula, the Sun in a Rasi owned by Mars, and the Moon in a Rasi belonging to Saturn or Mars, the death of the person concerned will be in the midst of filth and feces.

**भौमे सुखेऽस्तगेऽर्के मन्दे दशमेऽष्टमे ग्रहः कश्चित्।  
भूपालकोपजनितं निधनं ब्रूयात् स्वशस्त्रदोषाद्वा॥३०॥**

* Sloka* 30.—When Mars occupies the 4th, the Sun is in the 7th, Saturn is in the 10th, and some other planet is in the 8th house, the death of the native will be through the anger of the sovereign or by his own weapon.

**यस्य सौरे धने सौख्ये शीतांशुश्च खमध्यगः।  
भौमेऽस्तराशिसंस्थे च कृमिदोषेर्मृतिर्भवेत्॥३१॥**

* Sloka* 31.—When Saturn is in the 2nd or the 4th, the Moon in the 10th and Mars in the 7th (is in the 6th or 12th), the person concerned will die of worms.

 **भौमेक्षतान्त्यसंस्थे** is another reading in the 3rd quarter.

**हिबुके दशमे पापैः क्षीणेन्दौ रन्ध्ररिःफषष्ठे वा।  
यात्राकाले मरणं प्रपातनादशनिदोषाद्वा॥३२॥ **

* Sloka* 32.—If malefics occupy the 4th and 10th houses, and the waning Moon be in the 6th, the 8th or the 12th house, the person concerned meets with his end while travelling or by the fall of thunderbolt.

**अर्ककुजौ व्ययसंस्थौ शशिराहू सप्तमे गुरौ केन्द्रे।  
जातस्य मृतिः काले प्रवासभूमौ सुरालयोद्याने॥३३॥**

* Sloka* 33.—If the Sun and Mars occupy the 12th house, the Moon and Rahu be in the 7th and Jupiter be in a Kendra, the person born will die in a foreign place, in a temple, or in a garden.

**रन्ध्रेशे मृतिभवने जलसंस्थे शत्रुरिःफभवने वा।  
व्यालमृगोरगहेतुर्मृत्युः कूपे गृहेऽथवा भवति॥३४॥**

 Slokas 34.—If the lord of the 8th house occupy the 8th, 4th, 6th or 12th house, death will be due to wild animals, serpents, falling into a well or in his house through ordinary causes.

**शिखिसहितेऽष्टमराशौ निधनेशे केन्द्रगे व्यये पापे।  
लग्नेशे क्षीणबले निधनं दुर्भार्गदोषजनितं स्यात्॥३५॥ **

* Sloka* 35.—If Ketu be in the 8th house, the lord of the 8th be in a Kendra, a malefic occupy the 12th house, and the lord of the Lagna be not strong, death will be due to one's own bad way of livings.

**विषघटिकायां जातो निधने क्रुरे विषाग्निशस्त्रैर्वा।  
निधनेशे विषभागे क्रूरयुते तन्निमित्तदोषेण॥३६॥**

* Sloka* 36.—If a person has his birth at a **विषघटीकाल** (see **ज. पा.** V-112, p. 124), and the 8th house be occupied by a malefic planet, the person concerned will die through poison, fire or a weapon. If the lord of the 8th house be in a **विषभाग** (फ. दी p. 132), and also be conjoined with a malefic, death will be due to that cause.

For **मृत्युभाग**, see **ज. पा**. II-57. p. 36.

**भौमार्कजौ यदि परस्परमंशयातौ  
क्षेत्रेऽथवा निधनभागयुते च केन्द्रे।  
तस्यावसानसमये क्षितिपालकोपा-  
च्छूलादिकायुधकृतं निधनं समेति॥३७॥**

* Sloka* 37.—If, at a person’s birth, Mars and Saturn occupy Navamsas or Rasis owned by each other and are in Kendra positions, as well as in fateful degrees, the person will at his end incur the displeasure of the sovereign and suffer death by being impaled at the stake or by some other instrument of execution.

**लग्ने शशी दिनकरे विबलेऽष्टमस्थे  
लग्नव्यये सुरगुरौ सुखगे च पापे।  
जातस्य हस्तनयनच्युतिदोषमृत्युः  
शस्त्रेण वा निशि निषादकृतेन वा स्यात्॥३८॥**

* Slokas* 38.—With the Moon in the Lagna, the Sun weak in strength in the 8th house, Jupiter in the 12th and a malefic posited in the 4th, the person born will meet with his death by being deprived of his hands and eyes or through weapons or by a base-minded outcast at night.

**निधने कुजे बुधे वा लग्नेशे सौम्यमे तदंशे वा।  
दंशकसरीसृपाद्यैर्मरणं नृृणां समादिशेत्प्राज्ञः॥३९॥**

* Sloka* 39.—When Mars or Mercury occupy the 8th house, and the lord of the Lagna is posited in a benefic house or Amsa, the person concerned will, it is declared, meet with his end through flies, venomous reptiles and the like.

**यदि बहुलग्रहयुक्ते हिबुके लग्नेश्वरेऽष्टमेशयुते।  
बहुजनमरणावसरे निधनं जातस्य निश्चितं ब्रूयात्॥४०॥**

* Sloka* 40.—If the 4th house be occupied by many planets, and the lord of the Lagna be conjoined with the lord of the 8th, the death of the person concerned will happen at a time when many others also have their exit from the world, and this will be a certainty.

**लग्नसुतरन्ध्रभानां पतियोगे यत्र कुत्र राशौ वा।  
सार्धं सुतेन मरणं तथैव दारेशसंयुते दारैः॥४१॥**

 *Sloka* 41.—When the lords of the Lagna, the 5th and the 8th houses are conjoined in any Rasi, the native will die along with his son. Similarly if the lords of the Lagna, the 7th and the 8th houses are combined in any Rasi, he will die along with his wife.

**प्रकृते दशावसाने सामान्येनैव निर्दिशेन्मरणम्।  
दारुणदशान्तराले निधनारिष्टेन निर्दिशेन्मरणम्॥४२॥ **

* Sloka* 42.—Generally, when a Dasa that is running is coming to a close, death may happen in the ordinary way. During the interval of a Dasa which is severe and cruel, one will die through the malefic planetary conditions pertaining to the 8th house.

**निधनेश्वरांशराशेः समानभूमौ मृतिं विजानीयात्।  
स्थलजलराश्यंशवशाद्देशेऽन्तं कल्पयेत् स्वदिग्भागे॥४३॥**

* Sloka* 43—The place of one’s death and surroundings will be indicated by the Rasi or Navamsa occupied by the lord of the 8th house. The place whether land or water, and the direction will be indicated by the nature of the Rasi or Amsa.

**निशिबलिराशौ लग्ने मरणं रात्रौ दिवाबले दिवसे।  
ग्रहरहिते प्रोक्तफल ग्रहयुक्ते तत्फलं समादेश्यम्॥४४॥**

* Sloka* 44.—When the Lagna at birth is a night-sign (declared strong at night), the death of the person concerned will happen at night. If the sign in question be a day-sign, it will be at day-time. When there is no planet in the Lagna, the effect declared as due to the Rasi will alone come to pass; else, i, e., when the Lagna is occupied by a planet, the effect due to that planet should also be taken into consideration.

**अनुदितनवांश कालप्रतिमो मोहः शुभग्रहे लग्ने।  
क्षेत्रोच्चांशकयुक्ते निधनेशे पापसंयुते त्रिगुणः॥४५॥**

* Sloka* 45.—The unconscious state at the time of death lasts for such time as is measured by the interval taken for the rising period of the portion of the Lagna below the horizon provided the Lagna is occupied by a benefic. If the lord of the 8th house be in his exaltation Rasi or Navamsa and be conjoined with a malefic, then the period is trebled.

**लग्नेशे जलमांशे जलराशौ चन्द्रशुक्र सन्दृष्टे।  
व्ययनिधनो पापयुतौ जलमध्ये तद्बधः समादेश्यः॥४६॥**

* Sloka* 46.—If the lord of the Lagna be in a watery sign or Navamsa, and the 4th house be aspected by the Moon and Venus, and the 8th and the 12th houses be occupied by malefics, the person concerned will meet with his end in the middle of water.

**लग्नेशे निधनांशे मूढे वा शत्रुगेहगे वाऽपि।  
बन्धुजनरहितदेशे मरणं स्यात् प्रकृतिसम्भवे काले॥४७॥**

* Sloka* 47.—When the lord of the Lagna, is (1) in a Navamsa owned by the 8th Rasi counted from the Lagna, (2) is eclipsed or (3) is posited in his inimical house, death will happen in a spot devoid of relatives or other people and at the time expected in the natural course of things.

**होरेश्वरांशनाथो लग्ने लग्नेश्वरेण युतदृष्टः।  
जन्मेश्वरांशनाथादेवं देशान्तरे मृतिर्भवति॥४८॥**

* Sloka* 48.—When the lord of the Navamsa occupied by the lord of the Lagna or the house of the Moon is posited in the Lagna or the Janma Rasi as the case may be, and is aspected by or conjoined with the lord of the Lagna, death may happen. Death will take place in a foreign place when the planet owning the Navamsa occu- pied by the Moon conjoins with or is aspected by the lord of the Lagna.

**जीवक्षेत्रोदये वर्गे सुरलोकं गमिष्यति।  
चन्द्रशुक्रोदये क्षेत्रे पितृलोके महीयते॥४९॥**

**सूर्य भौमोदयक्षेत्रे मर्त्यलोकमवाप्नुयात्।  
केतूदये मृतो मर्त्यो रौरवादिषु तिष्ठति॥५०॥**

**बुधोदये तथा क्षेत्रे तिर्यग्जातिषु संविशेत्।  
मन्दराहूदये क्षेत्रे भूतपित्रादिषूद्भवः॥५१॥**

* Slokas* 49-51.—When the Lagna or its Amsa belongs to Jupiter, the departed person goes to heaven. If the Lagna or its Amsa belong to Venus or the Moon, the native goes to the world of the Manes. If the Lagna or its Amsa be owned by the Sun or Mars, the native goes to the world of Mortals. If Ketu occupy or own the Lagna Rasi or its Amsa, the departed will be in Hell. If the Lagna or its Amsa belong to Mercury, he will become an animal of the brutal kind. If the Lagna or its Amsa belong to Saturn or Rahu, the native will be reborn in the world of Devils or Manes

**ग्रहदृष्टियोगहीने राशौ राशेः फलं समादेश्यम्।  
ग्रहयुक्तदृष्टराशौ ग्रहभावफलं विनिर्देश्यम्॥५२॥**

* Sloka* 52.—When the Lagna Rasi or Amsa is not conjoined with or aspected by any planet, the effect for the Rasi or Amsa will alone apply. If the Rasi or Amsa in question be occupied or aspected by any planet, the effects may be declared as derived from the said planet or the Bhava owned by it.

**भवनान्ते गुरौ लग्ने जन्तोर्मोक्षो भविष्यति।  
गुरुक्षेत्रोदये सूर्ये भवनान्ते तथैव च॥५३॥**

* Sloka* 53.—If Jupiter be in the Lagna synchronous with the end of a Rasi, the creature concerned will attain final emancipation. If Jupiter own the Lagna Rasi and the Sun be there synchronous with the last portion of a sign, the effect will be the same as stated above.

 **गुरुक्षेत्रोदये **may also be interpreted as “when Jupiter is posited in the beginning of the Lagna”

**जन्मादिमृत्युपर्यन्तं नराणां च शुभाशुभम्।  
होराशास्त्रेषु यत्प्रोक्तं तत्सर्वमिह कीर्त्तितम्॥५४॥**

इति श्री वराहमिहिरसुतश्रीपृथुयशोविरचिते होरासारे नैर्याणिकाध्यायः  
षड्विंशः

* Sloka* 54.—Whatever effects have been declared—both auspicious and inauspicious–for the human beings from birth to death in ancient astrological works, all these have been stated here as above.

Thus ends the 26th Adhyaya entitled Nairyanika–Exit from  
the world–in Horasara, a work composed by Sri Prithuyasas,  
son of Sri **:** Varahamihira.

**\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_**

**सप्तविंशोऽध्यायः**

अथ नष्टजातकविधिः॥

**जन्मायनर्तुमासाद्यमर्धमासो दिनं तथा।  
नवांशद्वादशांशौ च जन्मर्क्षं राशिरेव च॥१॥ **

**यस्य न ज्ञायते पुंसः सर्वमेतद्धि पृच्छकः।  
स्वच्छेऽम्बरे तु समये दैवज्ञं पूजयेत्तदा॥२॥**

**सुवर्णफलपुष्पादीन् दत्वा तं हितमादरात्।  
चिन्तयेत् स्वानि कार्याणि पृच्छेत् सर्वं यथा तथा॥३॥**

 *Slokas* 1-3.—In the case of a person whose year, Ayana, Ritu, month, etc. fortnight, day, the Navamsa, Dwadasamsa, Lagna, Nakshatra, and the Rasi occupied by the Moon at the time of birth are not known, all these may be ascertained by the querist from the astrologer. At a time when the sky is clear and cloudless, the querist should approach the astrologer with kind enquiries, worship him by offering Dakshina, fruits, flowers, etc. and then consult him about his own business.

**आरूढोदयलग्नादीन कृतिं पृच्छकस्य च।  
लक्षणानि निमित्तानि सर्वमालोक्य दैववित्॥४॥**

**वर्षायनर्तुमासर्क्षराशीस्तैः परिकल्पयेत्।  
बहुप्रकारैः सञ्चिन्त्य सर्वं प्रष्टुर्वदेद्बुधः॥५॥ **

* Slokas* 4-5.—The astrologer should, after an inspection of the querist, his form and his surroundings, find out the **आरूढ** (Arudha) Lagna and also the Lagna rising and the indications at the time, and from all these, deduce the year, Ayana, Ritu, month, Nakshatra and the Rasi of birth of the querist, and fix them up after trying various methods and then reveal them to the querist.

**तात्कालिकांशसंयुक्ते जीवे जातो न संशयः।  
तत् त्रिकोणगते वाऽपि ह्युदयारूढयोर्बलात्॥६॥ **

* Sloka* 6.—The Navamsa Rasi occupied by Jupiter or its triangular Rasi will invariably be the Janma Rasi of the querist. As for the Lagna, find the stronger of the two, *viz.* the Arudha and the Lagna at the time.

**कर्तुर्वयोनुमानेन तेषामेवं प्रकल्पयेत्।  
प्रश्नकाले विलग्नस्य पूर्वार्द्धेऽप्युत्तरायणम्॥७॥ **

**परार्द्धे दक्षिणं ब्रूयाज्जन्म सम्पृच्छते बुधः।**

* Slokas *7, 7½.—The things mentioned in the previous sloka should be determined as explained below by an inference of the querist’s age**:** if the Lagna at the time of query belongs to the first half of a Rasi, the birth must have happened in the Uttarayana; if the second half, in the Dakshinayana. Thus should the astrologer declare to the person making the query.

**ऋतुर्वाच्यो दृगाणेशो लग्नसंस्थोऽथवा ग्रहः॥८॥**

**शनिशुक्रकुजा ईशा ऋतूनामुत्तरायणे।**

**दक्षिणे शशिविज्जीवा नाथाः प्रोक्ताः क्रमाद्बुधैः॥९॥**

* Slokas* 8-9.—And the Ritu of birth should be guessed through the planet occupying or owning the Lagna decanate. In the Uttarayana, the lords of the three Ritus are Saturn, Venus and Mars, while in the Dakshinayana, the corresponding lords are the Moon, Mercury and Jupiter.

**अर्कोदये तु होरायां द्रेक्काणे भास्करस्य वा।  
ग्रीष्मे जातं विजानीयान्नान्यग्रहदृशा युते॥१०॥**

 *Slokas* 10.—If the Lagna, Hora or Drekkana rising at the time of query belong to the Sun, and be not (conjoined with or) aspected by any other planet, it should be understood that the querist should have been born in the Greeshma Ritu.

**अयनस्य तु वैलोम्ये परिवर्तः परस्परम्।  
शशिज्ञगुरुभिः सार्द्धं सितलोहितसूर्यजाः॥११॥**

 *Sloka* 11.—When the Ritu does not fit in with the Ayana, it has to be exchanged thus **:** the Moon, Mercury and Jupiter should be substituted for Venus, Mars and Saturn respectively.

**द्रेक्काणार्द्धे भवेत्पूर्वे मासः पूर्वोऽपरे परः।  
पूर्वोत्तरमुखो भूत्वा दक्षिणाङ्गं यदि स्पृशेत्॥१२॥**

**उत्तरायणमासे तु जन्तुर्जातो न संशयः।  
विपरीतं तदा स्पृष्ट्वा दक्षिणायनमाश्रितः॥१३॥**

**पुष्प संस्पर्शनादेवमृतुर्वाच्यो न संशयः।  
अधः कायं स्पृशेत्पूर्व ऊर्ध्वाङ्गस्पर्शने परः॥१४॥**

**पुनः स्पर्शे पुनर्मासो वक्तव्यो दैववित्तमैः।  
तयोर्निरूपणादैक्यं यत्तथ्यं तन्न संशयः॥१५॥**

* Sloka* 12-15.—If the Lagna rising at the time be in the first half of a decanate, the month of birth will be the first of the two months constituting the Ritu; if it be the second, it will be the second of the two months. Facing the North-East, if you touch a limb in the right side, the birth must have been in a month of the Uttarayana. If you touch any in the other side, the birth was in a month of the Dakshinayana. The Ritu may also be guessed correctly by touching a flower.

 If the querist should touch first a lower limb of the body, the birth was in the Purva Ayana; if an upper limb, the birth was in the Dakshinayana. By a similar touch again, the month of birth may be guessed by the astrologer. When the two inferences coincide, the correctness of the inference is assured.

**यदि वृश्चिककुम्भौ च कन्यामीनतुलाधराः।  
रात्रौ सिंहश्च विज्ञेयो जन्तुर्जातो न संशयः॥**

 *Sloka* 16.—If Vrischika, Kumbha, Kanya, Meena, Tula or Simha be the Lagna, the birth should undoubtedly have been in the night.

**वृषभे कर्किभे चैव मिथुने मृगधन्विनोः।  
दिवा विनिर्दिशेज्जातमर्कहोरोदयेऽपि च॥१७॥ **

 *Sloka*17.—When one of the signs Vrishabha, Karkataka, Mithuna, Makara and Dhanus is rising or if the rising Hora belong to the Sun, the birth should have happened in day-time.

**मीनोदये नवांशे वा सन्ध्याकाले विनिर्दिशेत्।  
अथवा दिनसन्धौ वा मध्याह्ने वार्द्धरात्रिके॥१८॥**

 *Sloka*18.—When Meena Rasi or Meena Navamsa is rising, the birth should have been at a Sandhya-Sunset or Sunrise, or, during juncture in the day, midday or midnight.

**यावन्तोऽभ्युदिता भागा राशौ प्रश्नविधौ ततः।  
तावत्यो घटिका वाच्या दिवा रात्रौ च जन्मनि॥१९॥**

* Sloka* 19.—The degrees that have risen in the Lagna or the Moon at query indicate the Ghatikas after Sunrise or Sunset at birth,

**ऊर्ध्वकाये चरं विद्यान्मध्यमे स्थिरराशिकम्।  
अधमे तूभयो ज्ञेय एवं देहविभागतः॥२०॥**

* Sloka* 20.—The upper portion of the body represents a moveable Rasi, while the middle portion, an immoves able one. The lower portion denotes a mutable Rasi.

**शीर्षादि संस्पृशेत्प्रष्टा प्रश्ने तद्राशिमादिशेत्।  
भक्ष्याहृताकाररुतैश्चिन्तयेत्तद्विशेषकम्॥२१॥**

* Sloka* 21.—If at query the querist should touch the head or any limb of his body, the birth should be declared to have happened when that Rasi indicated by the limb was rising. The details of it may also be determined by the articles of food if any that may be brought, any forms that may appear on the scene or any cry that may be heard at the time.

**ग्रहेष्वधिकविर्यो यः स यत्रास्ते गृहे ततः।  
प्रश्नलग्नं भवेद्यावात्तावल्लग्नमितीरयेत्॥२२॥**

* Sloka* 22.— Find the strongest of the planets at the time of query and also note the Rasi occupied by the same, and how far the Lagna at query is removed from that Rasi. The Lagna at birth will be so far removed from that Rasi,

**आरूढराशिं जन्मर्क्षं तत्त्रिकोणमथापि वा।  
ग्रहयोगेक्षणे वाऽपि तत्क्षेत्रं जन्ममं विदुः॥२३॥**

 *Sloka* 23.— Or, the Rasi at birth will be the same as the **आरूढराशि** or its triangular Rasi. Or, it will be the Rasi which is conjoined with or aspected by the relative planets.

**आरूढोदयपर्यन्तं यावन्तो राशयस्तदा।  
तावन्त्यश्व्यादि भानि स्युर्जन्मर्क्षं पृच्छकस्य तु॥२४॥**

 *Sloka* 24.—Find the number of Rasis between the Arudha and the rising signs; and count so many asterisms reckoning from Aswini. This will be the Janma Nakshatra of the querist.

**आरूढराशेरुदयो द्विगुण्यो नक्षत्रसङ्ख्यासहितो विभक्तः।  
सुरैश्च शिष्टा तुरगादिवारा जन्मर्क्षमस्मादथवा त्रिकोणः॥२५॥**

 *Slokas* 25.— Note the distance between the **आरूढलग्न** and the **उरुदयोलग्न **and multiply the same by 2. Add to this the number of the asterism at the time and divide this sum by 27. The Janma Nakshatra will be so many stars after Aswini when reckoned by this remainder or its triangular one.

**द्विगुणास्त्रिगुणाः कार्या मात्राः प्रष्टुर्मुखोद्गतास्तास्तु।  
विभजेत्सुरैश्च शिष्टं नक्षत्रं चाश्विनीपूर्वम्॥२६॥**

* Sloka* 26.—Note the words emanating from the lips of the querist and find the number of Matras in the same. Take twice and thrice this number and add up. Divide the sum by 27. The remainder represents the number of the Janma Nakshatra of the querist when reckoned from Aswini.

**नववसुविश्वेन्द्रभवा नवरससप्तेन्द्रियाणि दिग्वसवः।  
मनवश्चोक्ता भानां मेषादीनां क्रमेण किरणाः स्युः॥२७॥**

* Sloka* 27.—The Kiranas or Rays for the 12 Rasis from Mesha onwards are 9, 8, 14, 8, 11, 9, 6, 7, 5, 10, 8, and 14 respectively.

 Here **विश्व** and **इन्द्र** are tentatively taken to represent 14 and 8 respectively, since the universe consists of 14 worlds and Indra means 8 **लोकपालाः**

**विंशत्यष्टादशरविमनुभूपालः स्मृतिर्दिशः सूर्यात्।  
किरणानां सङ्ख्याः स्युः पूर्वोक्तास्ते मयात्र निर्दिष्टाः॥२८॥**

* Sloka* 28.—The Kiranas or rays of the several planets from the Sun onwards are represented by the numbers : 20, 18, 12, 14, 8, 18, and 10. This is as stated by ancient authors, and I have only repeated them here.

**आरूढोदयसङ्ख्या ग्रहोक्तकिरणैश्च वर्धयेद्विधिना।  
मण्डलहृताविशिष्टं मेषाश्विन्यादि निर्दिशेत्प्रष्टुः॥२९॥**

* Sloka* 29.—The numbers denoting the **आरूढ **and the rising signs, should be multiplied by the Kiranas of the composed Rasis according to the Rules and the products divided respectively by 12 and 27. The respective remainders will reveal the Rasi and Nakshatra of the querist.

**ग्रहहीने प्राग्राशौ सङ्ख्यामानेन वर्धयेदथवा।  
नक्षत्रराशिमण्डलशोध्याच्छेषं नरस्य जन्मर्क्षम्॥३०॥**

* Sloka* 30.—Or, when the Rasi aforesaid has no planet in it, it should be multiplied by the appropriate rays of the Rasi of the planet posited and the product divided by 27 and 13. The remainder will reveal the Nakshatra and the Rasi required.

**आरूढभसङ्ख्यायां ग्रहोक्तसङ्ख्यां च योजयेदथवा।  
मण्डलहृतावशिष्टं जन्मर्क्षं निर्दिशेत्तस्य॥३१॥**

इति श्रीवराहमिहिरसुतश्रीपृथुयशोविरचिते होरासारे नष्टजातकाध्याया  
सप्तविंशः

* Sloka* 31.—Or the Nakshatra may be determined in the following manner**:** Add to the figures of the **आरूढलग्न** the figures denoting the planet. Divide the sum by 27. The remainder counted from Aswini will reveal the number of the asterism at birth.

Thus ends the 27th Adhyaya entitled **नष्टजातक** “Lost Horoscope”  
in Horasara, a work composed by Sri Prithuyasas,  
son of Sri Varahamihira.

**\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_**

**अष्ठाविंशोऽध्यायः**

॥अथाश्विन्यादि नक्षत्रशीलानि॥

**प्रज्ञो धृतिमान् दक्षः स्वधर्मनिरतः कुलाधिको मानी।  
लघुभोजनोऽतिमान्यो मध्यः स्यादश्विनीमनुजः॥१॥**

* Sloka *1.—The person born under the star Aswini will be learned, resolute, skilful, intent on his duties, an important member of his family and possessed of self- respect. He will eat sparingly, will be highly respected and of moderate means.

**शान्तात्मा चलचित्तः स्रीलोलो भ्रातृवल्लभो मानी।  
धीरो मित्रसहायश्चिरजीवी नातिपुत्रवान्याम्ये॥२॥**

* Sloka* 2.—If, at a person’s birth, the Moon be in the star **भरणी** (Bharani), he will be fickle-minded, clever in coition, loved by his brothers, proud, energetic, disposed to be of help to his friends, and long-lived. He will not have many children.

**भ्रान्तिविहीन बलवांश्चपलोऽनैकाशनोऽतितेजस्वी।  
सत्यपरो बहुनिलयो बहुप्रलापी च जायतेऽनलभे॥३॥**

* Sloka 3.—*The person born under the star Krittika will have a correct notion of things, will be strong in body, fickle-minded, will eat all kinds of food, and will be very brilliant in appearance. He will be truthful, own many houses and will be prattling much.

**ऊर्ध्वाङ्गरोमबहुलो गणेश्वरो वक्त्रपार्श्वपृष्टाङ्कः।  
कुहको मातुरनिष्टो रोहिण्यां जायते धनी विद्वान्॥४॥**

* Sloka 4.*—The man born in Rohini (रोहिणी) will have much hair in the upper part of his body; he will have many attendants; will have marks or moles on the face, back and sides. He will cheat others, will hate his mother, will be rich and learned.

**चपलो विशालदेहो रोगी बाल्ये प्रमादबहुलः स्यात्।  
उत्साही चलचित्तो बहुशत्रुः क्लेशवांश्चान्द्रे॥५॥**
