* Sloka 5.*—He who is born in **मृगशीर्ष** (Mrigasirsha) will be of a wavering disposition; will possess a broad body; will be sickly, and suffer calamities in his early years. He will be persevering, unsteady in mind, will have many enemies and suffer miseries.

**चलचित्तः शठवाक्यः परस्वहारी विकत्थनो मानी।  
अल्पसुतश्चिरजीवी राजद्रव्यान्वितश्च रौद्रर्क्ष॥६॥**

 * Sloka 6.*—The person who is born in the star **आर्द्रा** (Ardra) will be fickle-minded, crafty in his speech, will rob others’ wealth, will be bagging much and haughty. He will not have children, will be long-lived and will be enriched by the Govt.

**दाता सुखी सुशीलो दुर्मेधा रोगभाक् पिपासुश्च।  
अल्पेन च सन्तुष्टः पुनर्वसौ जायतेऽल्पबुद्धिश्च॥७॥**

* Sloka* 7.—He who has his birth in the star **पुनर्वसु** (Punarvasu) will be literal in gifts, happy, of a gentle disposition, dull-header, sickly and thirsty. He will be satisfied with small earnings. He will be weak-minded.

**तीव्रः क्रोधी मतिमान् धृष्टो वाग्मी ह्यनेकशास्त्रज्ञः।  
बन्धूनां हितकारी चोरो धनवान् स्वतन्त्रकः पुष्ये॥८॥**

* Sloka* 8.—The person who is born in the star **पुष्य** (Pushya) will be extremely irascible, intelligent, courageous, talkative; he will be proficient in many sciences; will help his relations, will rob others, will be wealthy and uncontrolled,

**क्रूरश्चपलो वाग्मी गणेश्वरो ज्ञानवाननेकधनः।  
बह्वायाससमेतो नातिसुतो वञ्चकश्च भौजङ्गे॥९॥**

* Sloka* 9.—The person born in the star Aslesha (**आश्लेषा**) will be eloquent, a leader among men, intelligent, and will earn money through various ways. He will exert himself in many undertakings to earn money, His issue will not be many and he will be deceitful.

**ज्ञानी विनीतिशीलः स्थिरवैरी सञ्जनैः स्तुतः क्रूरः।  
बहुभृत्यधनो भोगी सुरपितृभक्तो महोद्यमः पित्र्ये॥१०॥**

* Sloka* 10.—The person whose birth is in the star **माघा** (Magha) will be learned, well-behaved, and of lasting enmity ; he will be praised by the good; he will be cruelly disposed. He will have many servants and command riches; he will indulge in sensual pleasures. He will revere Gods and Manes and will be very industrious.

**प्रियवाग्दाता नीचो बहुव्ययार्तो विधेयभृत्यश्च।  
विख्यातो नृपतीष्टो रणभीरुर्जायते च फल्गुन्याम्॥११॥**

* Sloka* 11.—The man born in Purvaphalguni—**पूर्व फल्गुनी** will speak sweetly, will be mean-minded, and troubled by heavy expenditure. He will have obedient servants. He will be famous, and liked by the sovereign, but will be timid in battle.

**स्त्रीणामिष्टः सुभगो गणेश्वरो ज्ञानवान् नृपात्तधनः।  
बहुदारोदारमतिर्भोगी मुखरो द्वितीयफल्गुन्याम्॥१२॥**

* Sloka* 12.—The person born under the star **उत्तरफल्गुनी**—Uttara-phalguni–will be liked by women, will be amiable, a leader of men and learned. He will earn money through a king. He will have many wives and will be noble-minded. He will indulge in sexual pleasures, and he will be very talkative.

**कामी कुशलो वाग्मी चौर्यमतिर्वित्तवान् विदेशरतः।  
युद्धोत्सुकोऽतिनिपुणो रिपुहन्ता जायते च हस्तर्क्षे॥१३॥**

* Sloka* 13.—One who has had his birth in the star **हस्ता**—Hasta—will be lustful, clever, oratorical, of a thievish disposition, rich and intent on going to foreign places. He will be eager to fight in battle, will be very clever and a killer of enemies.

**दुष्टस्त्रीष्टः पापो विविधोत्साही विवादशीलः स्यात्।  
चित्राम्बरमाल्यधरो विदेशवासी सुखी च चित्रायाम्॥१४॥**

* Sloka* 14.—One whose birth was in the star **चित्रा**—Chittra–will associate with a wicked woman, will be sinful, will persevere in various pursuits, and will be of a quarrelling nature. He will wear beautiful garments, will reside in foreign places and be happy.

**दान्तः सुखी कृपालुः प्रियवाग्धर्माश्रितो भवेत् स्वातौ।  
ऋणवान् विदेशवासी बन्धुद्विट् स्वल्पवेषतनयश्च॥१५॥**

* Sloka* 15.—The person born in the star **स्वाति**—Swati— will be mild in disposition, happy, compassionate, sweet in speech, and virtuous. He will incur debts, will dwell in foreign places, and will hate his relations. His dress will be simple, and he will have few children.

**द्वेष्यो बहुप्रलापी सुतदारसमन्वितो धनी प्राज्ञः।  
विबुधगुरुद्विजभक्तो न दातृशीलोऽक्षिरुग्विशाखासु॥१६॥**

* Sloka* 16.—One whose birth is in the star **विशाखा**—Visakha—will be odious; He will be prating much. He will be living with his wife and children, and will command wealth. He will be learned, will revere Gods, elders and Brahmins. He will not be of a generous disposition, and he will suffer from eye-disease.

**क्षत्तृष्णार्त्तः शोकी दयापरो धर्मसंश्रितः सुभगः।  
अटनो विदेशवासी मैत्रर्क्षे जायते मनुजः॥१७॥**

* Sloka* 17.—The person born under the star **अनूराधा** Anuradha— will suffer from hunger and thirst, will be dejected, full of compassion, of a virtuous disposition and beautiful. He will be wandering from place to place and living in foreign places.

**सन्तुष्टो धर्मपरो बहुसुतमित्रान्वितोऽतिरोषी स्यात्।  
बन्धुजनपीडितात्मा कुलाग्रणीर्देवराजनक्षत्रे॥१८॥**

* Sloka* 18.—The person born in the star **ज्येष्ठा** (Jyeshta) will be contented; intent on doing virtuous, actions. He will have many issues and friends and he will be of a very angry temperament. He will be worried through his relations. He will become the chief of his family.

**ज्ञानी सुखी धनाढ्यो व्याधिप्रायोऽतितस्करः सुभगः।  
नैकमतिः सहजाग्र्यो मूले जातो नृपो भवति॥१९॥**

* Sloka* 19.—He who is born in the star **मूला** Moola will be learned, happy and wealthy. He will be mostly suffering from diseases and will be a great thief. He will have a charming person. He will not have a resolute mind. He will be the eldest of the family and may become a king.

**दृढसौहृदो विनीतो बहुप्रजावान् गणेश्वरो धीमान्।  
मृष्टान्नभुक्कलत्रजभोगी नृपसम्मतश्च जलदैवे॥२०॥**

* Sloka* 20.—If a person has his birth in **पूर्वाषाढा**, he will be firm in his friendship, of gentle manners, possess many issue, be the leader of a clan and highly intelligent. He will eat savoury food, and enjoy with his wife all sensual pleasures. He will will be liked by the king.

**हास्यप्रियो विनीतो बहुशत्रुः क्लेशवान् विशिष्टमतिः।  
अटनो ह्यनेकभार्यो दयापरो वैश्वदेवनक्षत्रे॥२१॥**

* Sloka* 21.—The person born in the star **उसराषाढा**-Uttarashadha-will be fond of mirth; he will be well-behaved and will have many enemies, will suffer distress, possess superior intellect and will be rambling about. He will have many wives and will be very merciful.

**श्रुतवान् विदेशवासी प्रकृष्टदारो धनान्वितः ख्यातः।  
अल्पसुतो बहुशत्रुर्बहुव्ययार्तो विभुः सुखी श्रवणे॥२२॥**

* Sloka* 22.—He who has his birth in the star **श्रवणा**-Sravana will have proficieney in sacred knowledge, will dwell in foreign places, will possess an excellent wife, and will be wealthy and famous. He will have few children, possess many enemies and his expenditure will be very heavy ; he will be a lord and happy.

**धनवान् दाता शूरो नष्टकलत्रो विदेशसन्तुष्टः।  
आनृतिको वाचाटः प्रनृत्तगीतप्रियो धनिष्ठासु॥२३॥**

* Sloka* 23.—The person who is born in the star **धनिष्टा**- Dhanishta-will be liberal in gifts, courageous and likes to go to foreign places. He will lose his wife. He will utter lies, and will be talkative. He is fond of dancing and singing.

**मुखरो धूर्तो वश्यो मृतसुतसहजो धनाधिकश्चपलः।  
कृपणो मायातिरतो रिपुहन्ता जायते च शततारे॥२४॥**

* Sloka* 24.—The person who has his birth in the star **शतभिषक्** Satabhishak-will be garrulous, will be a cheat and a servant. He will lose his children and brothers; he will be rich but fickle-minded. He will be a miser, intent on playing trickery; and he will kill his enemies.

**स्त्रीलोलश्चलवासो दुर्ग्राह्यो भोगवान् नृपात्तधनः।  
क्षुद्रः स्वकर्मनिरतश्चिरजीवी पूर्वभाद्रजातः स्यात्॥२५॥**

* Sloka* 25.—The person born in the star पूर्वाभाद्रा- Purvabhadra-will be longing for women, moving from place to place, difficult to be won over, enjoy all sensual pleasures, get wealth through the king, miserly, intent on his duties, and long-lived.

**वक्ता सुखी प्रजावान् स्थिरशत्रुर्धार्मिको बिभीतश्च।  
लुब्धो बलार्थनिरतो द्वितीयभाद्रासु जायते मनुजः॥२६॥**

* Sloka* 26.—He who is born under the star **उत्तराभाद्रा**—Uttarabhadra—will be clever in speaking, happy, possess children, will always have enemies, be virtuous and exceedingly timid. He will be greedy and specially interested in hoarding wealth.

**सम्पूर्णायुः सुभगो वशगः स्त्रीणां स्वमानदर्पयुतः।  
मनसि प्रतापबहुलो मात्सर्ययुतो भवेत् पौष्णे॥२७॥ **

* Sloka* 27.—The man born in the star-**रेवती** will live his full age, will be liked by all, will be hen-pecked, possessed of self-respect and pride. He will be spirited energetic, and spiteful.

**पक्षद्वये चाल्पफलानि दद्युस्ताराबलर्क्षेषु शुभप्रदाः स्युः।  
शुभग्रहालोकितसंयुतास्ताः समस्तवीर्याः सकला भवन्ति॥२८॥**

* Sloka* 28.—The effects of birth in either of the Pakshas are negligible, while those derivable from the asterisms will bring in luck if they are auspicious to the native. If the stars aforesaid be conjoined with or aspected by benefic planets, they become fully beneficial.

**अर्द्राश्लेषावारुणातिष्यमूलाश्चित्राज्येष्ठकृत्तिका वर्जनीयाः।  
स्त्रीणां सूतौ भ्रातृपुत्रादिशोकं मृत्युं शोषं विग्रहं चापि विद्यात्॥ **

* Sloka* 29.—If girls are born under the stars **आर्द्रा** Ardra, Aslesha—**आश्लेषा**, Satabhishak—**शतभिषक्**, Pushya—**पुष्य**, Moola—**मूला**, Chittra—**चित्रा**, Jyeshta—**ज्येष्ठा**, and Krittika—**कृतिका**, they are to be avoided as they will engender sorrow through brothers, sons, etc., or death, consumption or strife.

**पितृजन्मर्क्षे पुत्रा जाताश्चेन्मातुरन्तका ज्ञेयाः।  
तद्वत्पितुरन्तकरा मातुर्जनिभे न तु स्त्रीणाम्॥३०॥**

इति श्रीवराहमिहिरसुतश्रीपृथुयशोविरचिते होरासारे  
नक्षत्रशीलाध्यायोऽष्टाविंशः॥

* Sloka* 30.—Sons born in their father’s Nakshatras at birth cause the death of their mother; similarly, if they be born in their mothers’ Nakshatras, they bring about the death of their fathers. This does not apply to births of girls in similar circumstances.

Thus ends the 28th Adhyaya entitled **नक्षत्रशील**—the properties  
of the several asterisms—in Horasara, a work composed by  
Sri Prithuyasas, son of Sri **:** Varahamihira.

**\_\_\_\_\_\_\_**

**एकोनत्रिंशोऽध्यायः**

**अथ मेषादिराशिफलानि॥**

**वृत्ताक्षो जनवल्लभोऽतिचपलो गोमान् व्ययार्तोटनो  
वाचालो लघुभोजनः कुटिलगो ज्ञानी सभापूजितः।**

**पित्तात्मा वनितादृतोऽल्पतनयः क्रोधी स्वशौर्यान्वितो  
मेषोत्यः सहजाग्रजोऽतिकृपणः क्लेशान्वितो बन्धुभिः॥१॥**

* Sloka* 1.—The person born, with the Moon in Mesha, will have round eyes, will be favourite of the people, very fickle minded, will rear cows and buffaloes will be troubled by heavy expenditure and wandering, will be clever in speaking, will eat sparingly, will walk crookedly, will be learned, will be honoured by an assembly, will be of bilious temperament, will be liked by women, will have meagre issues, will be of iry temperment, and will be endowed with his own valour and strength. He will be the important person of his family, will be very miserly, and will be troubled by misery through his relatives.

**उद्वृत्तो बलवान् पृथूरुवदनो भोगी सुखी ज्ञानवान्  
आसीनो गिरिकन्दरेषु निपुणो नानार्थवागीश्वरः।**

**पूर्वोत्थैः सुतबन्धुभिर्विरहितः कन्याप्रजावान् क्षमी।  
मध्यान्त्ये सुखवान् वृषोत्थमनुजो दारप्रियो दीप्तिमान्॥२॥**

* Sloka* 2.—The person at whose birth the Moon is in Vrishabha will be tail in stature, strong in body, with broad thighs and a big face, will indulge in sensual pleasures, will be happy and learned. He will be be seated in mountains and caves. He will be clever and an orator. He will be deserted by his elders, and children. He will be the father of daughters. He will be of a forgiving disposition. He will be happy in the middle and concluding portions of his life. He will be fond of his wife. He will be brilliant in appearance.

**कन्दर्पप्रतिमो विशालवदनो विस्पष्टवागस्थिरो  
क्लीबो वा मदनातुरोऽल्पतनयः सद्यूतगानप्रियः।**  
**बन्धुद्विटे कफमारुतात्महृदयो दारप्रियो दानवान्  
हास्यज्ञो मिथुनेऽन्नपाननिरतो जातः प्रतापी पटुः॥३॥**

 * Sloka* 3.—When the Moon occupies Mithuna, the person born will be like Cupid, with a broad face, clear voice, and a fickle mind. He will be either impotent, or will be tormented by the God of Love. He will have few children. He will be fond of gambling and music. He will hate his relations. He will have much wind and phlegm in his composition. He will be fond of his wife, will be liberal in gifts, fond of mirth, fond of eating and drinking and clever and valiant.

**मेधावी गुणवान् स्वबन्धुविजयी वाताग्निमानार्दितो  
वाचालो दृढविग्रहोऽतिबलवानल्पात्मजो नैकगः।**  
**दैवज्ञस्त्वरितः सुखी क्षयधनो गूढात्मजो ज्ञानवा  
नैकाकी बहुवाक् कुलीरभवने जातोऽर्थवान् भूपतेः॥४॥**

 *Sloka* 4.—The person at whose birth the Moon occupies Cancer will be intelligent and endowed with good qualities; he will overpower his relations, will be troubled by wind, fire and pride ; he will be garrulous, firm in quarrel and strong in body, will have few issue, will have association with many female friends, will be an astrologer, be prompt and speedy, happy, spending much, father of sons born. secretly of another woman and intelligent. He will always be in company and never alone; he will know many languages; and he will be rich through the help of the king. ⋅

**गाम्भीर्योन्नतिमान् विशालवदनो धीधर्मभोगान्वितो  
मायावी सुमुखी कृपालुरभयोऽकार्ये चिरं कुप्यति।**  
**क्षुत्क्षामः स्वबलान्वितोऽतिविभवो मातृप्रियो नैष्ठिको  
विक्रान्तो विजनोऽस्थिरोऽल्पतनयः सिंहे प्रसूतो नरः॥५॥**

 * Sloka* 5.—If a person be born when the Moon is in Simha, he will be profound (in knowledge), exalted, with a broad face, endowed with intellect, virtuous, will indulge in sensual pleasures, be skilled in magic, lovely in appearance, compassionate, free from fear, will be angry at trifles for a long time, will be lean, emaciated, strong, very rich, powerful, liked by his mother and abstinent. He will overpower his enemies, will live alone, and will not be steady. His issue will be limited.

**कन्यायां मलिनोऽल्पसौख्यविभवो जातः सुधी धार्मिको  
बन्धुद्विट् सुखवान् कफानिलयुतः कन्याप्रजोऽल्पात्मजः।**  
**मुग्धास्यो युवतिप्रियोऽतिचपलो बन्धुप्रियो ज्ञानवान्  
दीर्घायुः प्रियभाषणोऽर्थनिरतः स्वन्तोऽन्य माध्ये रतः॥६॥**

* Sloka* 6.—If a person be born when the Moon is in Virgo, he will be unclean, will have।ittle happiness, will not have much wealth, possess good intellect and be virtuous He will hate his relations, and will।ive happily; He he will be of phlegmatic and windy temperament. He will be the father of daughters and have few sons. He will possess a।ovely face, will be fond of young females, will be exceedingly fickle, and be ।iked by his relatives. He will be ।earned,।ong-lived, sweet-tongued, be intent on hoarding money and his end will be peaceful. He takes delight in the prosperity of others.

**धर्मात्मा गुणवान् विशालहृदयो मन्दस्मितो दारवान्।  
क्लेशात्मा क्रयविक्रयेषु कुशलो हास्यप्रियो ज्ञानवान्।**  
**बन्धूनां हितकृत्सुतैर्विरहितः स्थूलेतरो वा धनी  
देवाख्यो द्रवभोजनोऽन्त्यतनयो जातस्तुलायां भवेत्॥७॥**

* Sloka* 7.—The person at whose birth the Moon is in ।ibra will be virtuously-disposed, of very good qualities, broad-minded, with a smiling face, will।ive with his wife, suffer distress, will be clever in trading, will be a।over of mirth, will be।earned, help his relations, will have no sons, will have a।ean and a frail body, will be wealthy, will have a God’s name as his second name ; he will be fond of।iquid diet, and will be the।ast child of his parents.

**मध्वाक्षो विगुरुर्विवादकुशलो दीर्घाननो दारुणो  
नखन्तो मनुजेश्वरस्य दयितो रोगी च बाल्ये सदा।**  
**क्षीणायुः परबन्धुमान् कवनधीर्धर्मध्वजो वीर्यवा-  
नालस्य श्रमपीडितोऽलिभवने जातोऽल्पजातिप्रियः॥८॥**

* Sloka* 8.—The man born when the Moon is in Vrischika will have eyes resembling honey, will separate from his parents and preceptors, will be clever in his arguments, and will have a long face. He will do cruel acts, and his later life will not be good. He will be the favourite of a king and will suffer from diseases during his childhood. He will hate his relations, will be a poet, a religious hypocrite and powerful. He will suffer from sloth and weariness, and will be popular with men of low caste.

**दीर्घास्यः सुमुखी विपक्षबहुलः श्यामेक्षणः शास्त्रविद्  
दान्तः क्षीणधनो व्ययव्यतिकरः पौत्रीसुतद्वेषणः।**  
**विद्वद्भिः प्रतिपूजितः स्ववशगो मानी गुणी वर्यिवा-  
नत्यायुः कृपणो नदारतनयः स्याद्धन्विजातो नरः॥९॥**

 *Sloka* 9.—The person at whose birth the Moon occupies sign Dhanus will have a long and expanded lovely face; he will have many enemies; his eyes will be of a dark and blue colour; he will have read all the scriptures, will be self-controlled, with all his money spent away, coupled with losses, he will have grand-sons but hate his own sons. He will command the respect of the learned and will be independent, honourable, possessed of merits and will be endowed with great strength. He will be long-lived, be a miser and without wife and childrens.

**ह्रस्वाङ्गो निपुणः प्रतापबहुलो मध्येऽर्थहीनोऽटो  
दीर्घाध्वा चपलो दुराशयगतिः क्लेशैश्च सम्पीडितः।**  
**सत्वाढ्यो, जनवल्लभो विचलितज्ञानेन्द्रियः स्त्रीमतिः  
पुत्रार्तोऽनिलवांश्च वृद्धवनिताप्रेमान्वितो नक्रजः॥१०॥**

 * Sloka* 10.—The following will be the characteristics of a person who is born when Makara is the Janma Rasi **:** He will be dwarfish in stature; he will be shrewd vigorous, will suffer for want of money in the middle portion of his life, and will be rambling from place to place, He will cover long distances, will be wicked in disposition, and fickle, and he will be troubled by calamities. His vitality will be strong; he will be liked by the people. His knowledge and energy will be diffused, will be intent on women. will be troubled by his sons, suffer from rheumatism. He will be attached to old women.

**दीर्घाङ्गो घटजो घटाकृतितनुः प्रच्छन्नपापे रतो  
वाचालो बहुपुत्रवानिह सुखी पूर्वार्थहीनोऽटनः।**  
**सद्द्वेष्यो बधिरो रुगार्तहृदयः सेर्ष्योऽलसात्मा शठः  
कामी व्यग्रमतिः स्वकर्मवचनैः क्लेशी परार्थान्वितः॥१॥**

* Sloka* 11.—The person at whose birth the Moon occupies sign Aquarius will be long-limbed, will have a body similar to a water-pot, will secretly commit sinful deeds. He will be talkative, will have many sons and be happy. He will lose his ancestral property and will be roaming about. He will be hated by the good, will be deaf, and will be troubled by heart-diseases. He will be envious, indolent and perfidious and lustfully-inclined. He will be distracted in mind. He will suffer from his own actions and words and will be utilising other’s wealth.

**चार्वङ्गो बलवानदीनवचनो रोगी प्रवासी सदा  
स्त्रीजेता बहुदारकोऽति चपलो ज्ञानी सभापूजितः।**  
**विख्यातो बहुदारवान्नृपधनी मीनोत्थितः स्यान्नरो  
हीनाङ्गो रिपुनिर्जितोऽतिनिपुणो दारप्रियो भोगवान्॥१२॥**

 *Sloka* 12.—If at a birth the Moon be in Meena, the person concerned will be beautiful in appearance, possess a strong body, high-spirited in his speech, suffer- ing from disease, living always in foreign places, will control women, will have many children, will be very fickle, learned and respected in an assembly. He will be famous, possess many wives, will become rich through the king. He will be deficient in a limb, will be over-powered by his enemies, very clever, and liked by his wives. He will enjoy all sensual pleasures.

 In the 2nd line **सतां पूजितः** is another reading.

**ग्रहयुतिदृष्टिविहीनो राशिस्तत्प्रोक्तलक्षणं कुरुते।  
ग्रहयोगेक्षणयुक्ते ग्रहस्वभावः फलं च वक्तव्यम्॥१३॥**

इति श्रीवराहमिहिरसुत श्रीपृथुयशोविरचिते होरासारे  
राशिशीलाध्याय एकोनत्रिंशः

 *Sloka* 13.—When the Moon is in a Rasi and is not occupied or aspected by any other planet, the effect aforesaid as due to the Rasi alone will apply. But should any planet occupy or aspect the same, its effect also should be predicted.

Thus ends the 29th Adhyaya entitled **राशिशीलाध्याय**  
“Effects of Birth in Mesha and other signs” in Horasara,  
a work composed by Sri**:** Prithuyasas, son of Sri**:** Varahamihira.

**\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_**

**त्रिंशोऽध्यायः**

**अथ मेषाद्यंशशीलानि॥**

**हिंस्रोऽल्पमतिः कुष्ठी चोरो विकलेक्षणो नशान्तमतिः  
पित्तप्रकृतिः कामी मेषांशे जायते मनुजः॥१॥**

 * Sloka* 1.—The person born in the Mesha Navamsa will be mischievous, base-minded, suffering from leprosy, thievish, weak-eyed, of a restless mind, and of a bilious temperament. He will be lustfully inclined.

**द्वादशे पञ्चविंशेऽव्दे पञ्चाशे पञ्चषष्टिके।  
अंशारिष्टं विजानीयाद्रोगमेवात्र निर्दिशेत्॥२॥**

* Sloka* 2.—The 12th, 25th, 50th and the 65th year, of life should be understood as untoward owing to the malefic influences of the Amsa and disease alone should then be expected.

**वृषभांशके तु जातो मतिमान् भोक्ता पृथूदरो बलवान्।  
दीर्घास्यो विकृतगतिश्चपलेक्षणो दारिकाबहुत्वयुतः॥३॥**

* Sloka* 3.—One who has his birth in the Vrishabha Navamsa, will possess good intellect, enjoy life and will have a broad belly. He will be strong, have a long face, walk crookedly, and his eyes will be rolling. He will be the father of many daughters.

 In the last **पाद**, **दारबहुलश्च** is another reading.

**द्वाविंशे दशमे वर्षे द्वात्रिंशे वा द्विसप्ततौ।  
अरिष्टस्थानमेतेषु निर्दिशेद्रोगमेव वा॥४॥**

* Sloka* 4.—The 10th, 22nd, 32nd, or the 72nd year will be a period of evil. During these years, there will be trouble or disease to the native concerned.

**कान्तश्चपलो वाग्मी शास्त्रज्ञो भोगवान् विनीतश्च।  
स्त्रीचञ्चलोऽतिमेधो मिथुनांशे जायते नरोऽदारः॥५॥ **

* Sloka* 5.—The person born in the Mithuna Navamsa will have a beautiful appearance, will be fickle, eloquent, versed in the several sciences, happy, and well-behaved. He will be inconstant with regard to women. He wil have to very good intellect and will be a wife-less.

**षोडशे च चतुर्विंशे चतुर्स्त्रिंशे त्रिषष्टिके।  
मृत्युस्थानं विनिर्दिष्टं चत्वारिंशे तथापि वा॥६॥**

* Sloka* 6.—The 16th, 24th, 34th, 40th. or 63rd year of life will prove troublesome, to the life of the person concerned

**क्रोधी विषमितगात्रो धनवान् कुटिलेक्षणो विदेशरतः।  
बन्धूनां हितकारी स्वजनोद्रिक्तः कुलीरभांशे तु॥७॥**

* Sloka* 7.—One who has his birth in the Karkataka Navamsa will be easily irritable, will have a crooked body, a malevolent look, will be rich and intent to go to foreign places, will help his relations and be greatly influenced by his people.

**अष्टादशेऽष्टमे वर्षे द्वाविंशे चैकविंशके।  
द्विसप्ततावशीतौ च मृत्युस्थानमुशन्ति हि॥८॥**

* Sloka* 8.—The 8th, 18th, 21st, 22nd. 72nd and 80th year of life will prove dangerous to the life of the native.

**विजनस्थितोऽतिमानी कृशोदरो लोकसर्वज्ञः।  
दुर्बलदन्तो बलवान् सिंहांशे जायते मनोदुःखी॥९॥**

* Sloka* 9—He who is born in the Simha Navamsa, will live in a solitary place, will be very proud, thin-waisted and knowing the world; his teeth will be weak and he will be distressed in mind.

 In the first line, for **लोकसर्वज्ञः** some books read **लोकसम्मतोनृपतिः**

**विंशेऽब्दे दशमेवाऽश्च त्रिंशे वर्षेऽश्च षष्टिके।  
द्व्यशीतावंशकारिष्टं विशेषेण विनिर्दिशेत्॥१०॥**

* Sloka* 10.—The years 20th, 10th. 30th, 60th, or 82nd should be specially marked as dangerous to one’s life.

**बाल्ये सुखी कलाज्ञः क्लीबो जारोऽल्पपुत्रवान् सुभगः।  
परकार्यरतो दाता कन्यांशे जायते विदेशरतः॥११॥ **

* Sloka* 11.—The person born in **कन्यानवांश** will be happy in his early years, will know all the arts, will be impotent, will be a gallant, will have few sons, and will be amiable; he will be intent in doing other people’s work; he will be liberal in gifts, and will spend his time in foreign places.

**षष्ट्यां विंशे वर्षे पञ्चाशे वाऽत्र संशयो भवति।  
जीवति साष्टशताब्दं विवर्धमानो धनैरेषः॥१२॥**

* Sloka* 12.—Doubts will arise about the person’s existence in the 20th, or the 60th year of his life. With his wealth on the increase, the person concerned will live for 108 years.

**प्रचलितनिवास बुद्धिः कृशगात्रो नातिपुत्रवान् कृपणः।  
बन्धुद्विट्कफरोगी निःस्वप्रायस्तुलांशके जातः॥१३॥**

* Sloka* 13.—With a mind to be always moving about from place to place, with a lean body, with few sons, and miserly, the person born in Tula Navamsa will hate his relations. He will suffer from consumption; He will be almost indigent.

**तृतीयेऽब्दे त्रयोविंशे द्विगुणे सप्तविंशके।  
अष्टत्रिंशे च षट्सप्तत्यब्देऽरिष्टं विनिर्दिशेत्॥१४॥**

* Sloka* 14.—The 3rd, 23rd, 38th, 54th or the 76th year of one’s life will be unfavourable, as during these years, the person concerned will suffer from diseases.

**गुरुजनरहितो हिंस्रो मेधावी नेत्रदुर्बलः क्रूरः।  
प्रच्छन्नपापशीलो दीर्घो लम्बोदरश्च कौर्प्यशे॥१५॥**

* Sloka.* 15.—The person at whose birth the Vrischika Navamsa was rising will have no father or elderly people; he will be mischievous but intelligent. He will have weak sight, will be cruel, will secretly do sinful acts. He will be pot-bellied.

**अष्टादशे त्रयोविंशेऽष्यष्टाविंशे त्रयोदशे।  
सप्ततौ पञ्चपञ्चाशे प्रोक्तस्थानेषु संशयः॥१६॥**

* Sloka* 16.—Doubts will arise with regard to the person’s life during his 18th, 23rd, 28th, 13th, 70th or the 55th year.

 In the 2nd quarter, some books read as **चैकविंशे द्विसङ्गुणो**

**स्वार्जितधनी गुणाढ्यो दीर्घग्रीवोऽलसोऽल्पसन्तुष्टः।  
पृथुनासिकोऽतिभाषी धन्व्यंशे जायते धनाधिपतिः॥१७॥**

 *Sloka* 17.—The person who is born in the Dhanur Navamsa will be moneyed, of good qualities, possess a long neck, will be lazy and will be easily satisfied with a little. He will have a broad nose, will talk much and will hoard wealth.

**वसुद्वये वा नवमे चतुर्थे रवित्रये तद्विद्विगुणेऽथवाब्दे।  
प्राणात्ययं रोगमुशन्ति तेषु द्वाविंशयुग्मे परिवत्सरे वा॥१८॥**

 * Sloka *18.—During the 4th, 9th, 16th, 36th, 44th or the 72nd year of his life, the person will suffer from risk and disease.

**ह्रस्वाङ्गश्चलचित्तो हिंस्रो लघुविक्रमो महाभोगी।  
स्त्रीदुर्भगोऽनिलात्मा मकरांशे शत्रुसञ्ज्ञितो भवति॥१९॥**

 *Sloka* 19.—The person who has his birth in the **मकर** Navamsa will be short-limbed, fickle-minded, cruel, quick-footed, will indulge in sensual pleasures. He will have an ill-tempered woman as his wife.

**एकोनविंशे खलु सप्तविंशे चाब्दे चतुर्स्त्रिंशकसप्तवर्गे।  
वर्षे समाने द्विगुणेऽष्टषष्ट्यामरिष्टमाहु नयो मुनांशे॥२०॥**

* Sloka* 20.—Sages have declared in the case of people born in Makara Navamsa, that they will suffer from diseases in their 19th, 27th, 34th, 49th, 34th, 68th year of life.

**पिशुनो दयाविहीनो मायावी दुर्बलश्चलो दीर्घः।  
अटनो व्ययार्थनिरतो जातः कुमांशके मनोदुःखी॥२१॥**

 * Sloka* 21.—The man who has his birth in Kumbha Navamsa will be slanderous, without mercy, deceitful, weak confused and long limbed. He will be wandering, intent in spending money and will be mentally miserable.

**चतुर्दशे च विंशेऽष्टाविंशे द्वात्रिंशके क्रमात्।  
एकषष्टिमिते चाब्दे संशयः सप्तवार्धिषु॥२२॥**

 *Sloka* 22.—The dangerous and doubtful period of his will be in the middle of his 7th, 14th, 20th, 28th, 2nd, or 61st year.

**स्त्रीलोलः कृशगात्रो जलोपजीवी झषोदरो विद्वान्।  
परगृहवासी वसुमाननेकभार्यान्वितश्च मीनांशे॥२३॥**

 * Sloka* 23.—The person born in Meena Navamsa will long for women (not his own), will be slender-bodied and his livelihood will be through watery products; he will be fish-bellied and learned; he will live in other people’s houses; he will possess wealth and will have many wives.

**दशमे द्वादशे चैकविंशे षड्विंशके क्रमात्।  
द्विपञ्चाशे चकषष्ट्यां मृत्युस्थानमुदीरितम्॥२४॥**

 * Sloka* 24.—The dangerous periods in his life, will be the 10th, 12th, 21st, 26th, 52nd and the 61st years.

**एकोनषष्टिद्वात्रिंशदष्टमाब्देषु सूरयः।  
सामान्यमेषु सर्वानां क्लेशस्थान शन्ति हि॥२५॥**

 * Sloka* 25.—Sages declare that the following are generally the periods of sorrow and anxiety in a man’s life**:** 59th, 32nd and 8th, years.

**दारुणान्तर्दशाकाले राशिरिष्टसमन्विते।  
मरणं तस्य जानीयादन्यथा रोगमाप्नुयात्॥२६॥**

 *Sloka* 26.—When the Antardasa of an untoward planet is ruling, and the Rasi owned or occupied by the planet is also a harmful one, the death of the person concerned may be expected to happen, or he will be troubled by some serious disease.

**राशिवद्द्वादशांशेषु फलं ब्रूयाद्विचक्षणः।  
वर्गोत्तमांशस्थेषु तत्तद्द्विगुणमादिशेत्॥२७॥**

इति श्रीवराहमिहिर सुतश्री पृथुयशोविरचिते होरासारे  
अंशशीलाध्यायस्त्रिंशः॥

 *Sloka* 27.—A clever astrologer should foretell similar effects for the several Dwadasamsas as for the Rasis. When the planets concerned occupy Vargottama Amsas, the effects will be happy and two-fold.

Thus ends the 30th Adhyaya entitled ‘Effects of Birth  
in the several Amsas’ in the work Horasara  
composeed by Prithuyasas, son of  
Sri Varahamihira.

**\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_**

**एकत्रिंशोऽध्यायः**

**ADHYAYA-XXXI**

अथ नक्षत्रजातकम्॥

**भानोस्तंशशिनो नटःसनिधरापुत्रस्य राहोर्दया  
तापोदेवगुरोर्धयाननशनेः सायं विदो वत्सराः। **

**केतोः सानिभृगोर्नखाश्च कथितास्त्वाग्नेयनक्षत्रका  
द्भानामर्यमदैवताश्च खचरा विश्वर्क्षतः स्वामिनः॥१॥**

* Sloka* 1.—The Dasa-period reckoned in years of the Sun, the Moon, Mars, Rahu, Jupiter, Saturn, Mercury, Ketu and Venus are in their order 6, 10, 7, 18, 16, 19, 17, 7 and 20, and these planets preside over the nine triads of stars, counted from Krittika, thus:

| | | | |
|:---------------:|:----------------:|:------------:|:--------:|
| Krittika, | Uttara Phalguni, | Uttarashadha | Sun |
| Rohini, | Hasta, | Sravana | Moon |
| Mrigasiras, | Chitra | Dhanishta | Mars |
| Ardra | Swati | Satabhishak | Rahu. |
| Punarvasu | Visakha | Purvabhadra | Jupiter. |
| Pushya | Anuradha | Uttarabhadra | Saturn. |
| Aslesha | Jyeshta | Revati | Mercury. |
| Magha | Moola | Aswini | Ketu. |
| Purva- Phalguni | purvashadha | Bharani | Venus. |

**स्वजन्मनक्षत्रविलग्नतो वा ब्रूयात्क्रमेणैव दशाफलानि।  
दशावसानेष्वशुभं च सर्वे कुर्वन्ति सामान्यमिदं नराणाम्॥२॥**

* Sloka* 2.—The effects of the several Dasas should be predicted to happen in regular order reckoned from one’s natal star or from the Ascendant. All planets prove malefic at the concluding periods of their Dasas; this is generally the case for all persons.

**आदित्यभौमशनिराहुदशावसाने  
रोगार्थनाशकलहास्त्वशुभानि सन्ति।**  
**पापग्रहेण सहितस्य दशावसाने  
मृत्युं वदेन्निधनसंस्थितखेचरस्य॥३॥**

* Sloka* 3.— At the close of the Dasa-periods of the Sun, Mars, Saturn and Rahu, diseases will crop up, wealth will be destroyed, quarrels and such untoward events will generally happen. In the case of a planet conjoined with a malefic or situated in the 8th house, the death of the person concerned may be expected.

**पापग्रहान्वितर्क्षस्य दशायां क्लेशमाप्नुयात्।  
यावद्गते दशेशर्क्षे तत्फलं तत्र निर्दिशेत्॥४॥**

 *Sloka* 4.—When a malefic planet is in an asterism whose Dasa is ruling at the time, the person concerned will be afflicted with sorrow and the same will occur at the time signified by the distance travelled in the Rasi occupied by the aforesaid malefic.

**त्रिमण्डलेष्वथैकस्मिन् पापस्तिष्ठति दुर्बलः।  
सौम्यग्रहयुतो न स्याद्दशान्ते मृत्युमाप्नुयात्॥५॥**

* Sloka* 5.—When in one of the three cyclic divisions (into which the 12 houses may be arranged under certain conditions for **आयुर्दाय**—Ayurdaya purposes), there is a malefic planet devoid of strength and unassociated with a benefic planet, the person affected by this Yoga will meet with his demise at the conclusion of the Dasa of the weak malefic planet in question.

**राशिसन्धौ स्थिते काले व्याधिं तत्र विनिर्दिशेत्।  
त्रिंशद्भागमनुक्रान्ते दशान्ते मृत्युमाप्नुयात्॥६॥**

* Sloka* 6—The Dasa period of a planet occupying the end of a sign brings on desease; death may happen in the Dasa to the planet in question when the planet has progressed no further than the 30th degree of the **राशि**— Rasi,

**जन्मतश्चोर्ध्वनाडीभिर्वर्धयेत्तन्महादशाम्।  
षष्ट्याहृतं फलं वर्षं शेषं मासादिकल्पयेत्॥७॥**

* Sloka* 7.— Find the portion still to elapse of the asterism of birth and multiply the same by the Dasa years allotted for it. Divide the product by 60. The quotient will reveal the Dasa years. Out of the remainder, the months, days, etc. may be similarly calculated.

**तस्मात्क्रमेण संयोज्य दशाप्रोक्तफलं वदेत्।  
वर्तमानदशास्थाप्या चेष्टग्रहदशाहता॥८॥**

**प्रमाणभक्ता यल्लब्धं दशास्वन्तर्दशा भवेत्।  
अन्तर्दशाफलं प्रोक्तं पूर्वमेवात्र निर्दिशेत्॥९॥**

* Slokas *8-9.—It is only after a careful scrutiny in this way that one should predict the effects described above. To calculate the Antara period of a particular planet in any Dasa, the following is the procedure: Multiply the years of the Maha Dasa by the years of the planet whose Antar Dasa is required. Divide the product by 120. The quotient will represent the years of the Antardasa. Whatever has been stated before as the effects of the Antardasa should be tacked on here.

**अङ्गारकफलं केतो राहोरप्यर्कजस्य वै।  
शेषं समानमित्युक्तं शुभाशुभफलं वदेत्॥१०॥**

* Sloka* 10.—The effects derivable from Ketu will be like those from Mars; those from Rahu will be similar to Saturn’s. In the case of the rest, the good and evil effects will be equal.

**नक्षत्रजातकं प्रोक्तं सर्वेषां सम्मतं नृणाम्।  
अतिसूक्ष्मतरं ज्ञात्वा दशाफलमुदीरयेत्॥११॥**

 *Sloka* 11.—Whatever has been declared as derivable from the several asteresisms is invariably acceptable to all. After a close scrutiny of the several details, the effects of the Dasas should be predicted.

**अन्तर्दशाधिपक्षेत्रे वर्तते भास्करो यदा।  
तस्स्मन् काले दशाप्रोक्तफलं भवति निश्चितम्॥१२॥**

 *Sloka* 12.—If during the Antardasa of any planet the Sun transits the sign owned by that planet, the effects of the Antardasa will, without doubt, be fully felt by the person concerned.

**लग्नेन्द्वोर्बलवान्यो वा तस्मात्प्रभृति चिन्तयेत्।  
प्रोक्तं क्रमेण संयोज्य फलं ब्रूयाद्विचक्षणः॥१३॥**

इति श्रीवराहमिहिर सुत श्रीपृथुयशोविरचिते होरासारे  
नक्षत्र जातकफलाध्याय एकत्रिंशः॥

 *Sloka* 13.—Of the Lagna and the Moon, find which is stronger**:** the effects of the several Bhavas described above should be predicted by a clever astrologer reckoning from the significator which possesses greater strength.

Thus ends the 31st Adhyaya entitled “Effects arising from the  
Nakshatra Jataka” in Horasara, a work composed by Prithuyasas,  
the son of Varahamihira.

**द्वात्रिंशोऽध्यायः**

**ADHYAYA—XXXII**

अध जातकलक्षणम्॥

**एकान्ते जनरहिते शुद्धे देशे सुखासने भूत्वा।  
प्रणिपत्य स्वाचार्यं विघ्नेशं च ग्रहान् सर्वान्॥१॥**

**मौनी मान्यमतिः सन् सूर्याभिमुखोऽभिविश्य दैवज्ञः।  
अथ शकुनादीन् सम्यक्परीक्ष्य यत्नाच्च सिद्धसेनोक्तान्॥२॥**

**शस्त्राभिघातकलहप्रपातदुःखानि दुर्निमित्ताद्याः।  
जायन्ते गणितादौ मरणवियोगार्थनाशसूचनदाः॥३॥**

**कृकलासोरगगोधाकपालनग्नादिदर्शनं नेष्टम्।  
तेषां कथाप्रलापैरनर्थमायान्तमीरयेन्न्नम्॥४॥**

* Sloka* 1-4.—On a clean spot in a lonely place, the astrologer should seat himself comfortably facing the Sun; and after saluting his preceptor, God Ganapati and all the planets and observing silence and having a lofly ideal closely watch all the omens as directed by sage Siddhasena. Any hit by a weapon, quarrel, fall from a precipice, crying etc., are declared as bad omens at the commencement of prediction (by the astrologer) and they indicate death, separation or destruction of property. Should a snake, or a camelion, an alligator, a leper, (a skull ?) or a naked mendicant etc., appear on the scene, it is untoward**:** even a reference or a talk about them is indicative of evil and certainly forebodes danger or disaster.

**वामे रुतं तु गौल्याः क्षुतं च वामेतरस्थले न शुभे।  
जम्बुकमहिषपशूनां स्वरश्च तद्वत् समीपतो मृत्युः॥५॥**

* Sloka* 5.—A cry of the lizard in the left, and a sneezing on the right side are inauspicious. So also are the sounds (howling) of a jackal, buffalo or a cow very near as they portend death.

**वाक्प्रश्नपरिज्ञानं शुभाशुभं तत्र चिन्तयेन्मतिमान्।  
वर्षद्वयादधस्तात् पूर्वोक्तफलं समादिशेत्तज्ज्ञः॥६॥**

* Sloka* 6.—The person will be able to correctly answer enquiries into one’s future, and intelligently predict good or evil by observing good or evil omens occurring at the time, within a limit of two years.

**कर्तुर्वयःप्रमाणं मासं नक्षत्रलग्न होराद्यम्।  
गतकलिदिवसान् ज्ञात्वा ग्रहचारं प्रारभेत पुण्यतिथौ॥७॥**

* Sloka* 7.—After knowing the probable age, month, the asterism, Lagna, Hora, etc., and the number of days that have elapsed in the Kaliyuga, the astrologer should begin on an auspicious Tithi the calculation of the position of the several planets at the time.

**मृदुशीघ्रवक्रकाले मूढोदययुद्धकालभेदेषु।  
पैतामहवरगणिताद्भूयो भूयोऽवधानतो गणयेत्॥८॥**

* Sloka* 8.—When the planet’s motion is slow, swift, retrograde, when he is eclipsed, is rising, when he is at war, etc., the astrologer should carefully calculate the planetary positions verifying them at every step with Brahmagupta’s treatise of calculations.

**अतिसूक्ष्मतरं ज्ञात्वा गतिं ग्रहणामनेन चारज्ञः।  
द्रेक्काणनवमभागद्वादशखगुणांशकादींश्च॥९॥**

* Sloka* 9.—After ascertaining the minute details of the movements of the planets as stated above, the astrologer should draw the charts of the Drekkana (Decanate), Navamsa, Dwadasamsa and Trimsamsa, etc.

**प्राक्फलदावर्ककुजौ बुधगुरुमन्दास्तु पृष्ठफलदाः स्युः।  
उदयफलं शीतांशोः शुक्रस्य फलं गतिसमानम्॥१०॥**

* Sloka* 10.—The Sun and Mars bestow their effects at the commencement; Mercury, Jupiter and Saturn, at. the end; the Moon, at the time of her rising. The ripening of Sukra’s effects will depend on the nature of his motion.

**वक्रानुवक्रकाले भृगुचारो ज्ञातुमेव न च शक्यः।  
तस्माद्बहुप्रकारैर्गणितविशेषैश्च चिन्तयेत्तज्ज्ञः॥११॥**

 *Sloka* 11.—It is not possible to correctly ascertain the exact position of Venus when he changes his movements from Retrograde to Direct motion. Therefore a clever astrologer should calculate and verify through different methods the correct location of that planet.

**इष्टं स्फुटं दिविचरं नवभिर्गुणयेद्विशेषयेत क्रमशः।  
मण्डलहृतावशिष्टं तस्यैवांशस्फुटं समानं तत्॥१२॥**

 * Sloka* 12.—In the case of any planet, find the exact position in signs, degrees, etc. Multiply the same by 9 and divide the product by 12. The remainder will represent the correct **स्फुट** of the planet’s Amsa.

**इष्टः स्फुटश्च खचरो द्वादशगुणितः स्फुटेन संयुक्तः।  
मण्डल हृतावशिष्टो ज्ञेयो राश्यंशकस्फुटः सुधिया॥१३॥**

 *Sloka* 13.—Take the case of any planet; multiply the figures denoting his position by 12 and add to the product the planet’s own figures. Divide the sum by 30. The remainder will represent the **स्फुट**
of the Amsa.

**एकादशांशभानुस्फुटयोगफलं निशाकरे योज्यम्।  
चतुरंशं शेषाण्णामेवं कुर्याद्धनक्षयं तुल्यम्॥१४॥**

 *Sloka* 14.—Add 1/11 th of the figures denoting the Sun’s position to the figures for the Moon. Take a fourth of the figures for the remaining planets; this should be added to or subtracted as the case may be from the figures of the planets.

**शुक्रज्ञयोर्द्विगुणितं भानुस्फुटवद्धनक्षयं कुर्यात्।  
मूढोदयवक्रेषु च कुर्यादेवं तयोस्तु नान्यत्र॥१५॥**

* Sloka* 15.—In the case of Venus and Mercury, the figures have to be doubled; addition or subtraction should be resorted to as in the case of the figures for the Sun; when the two planets are eclipsed or reappearing (after eclipse) or are retrograde in their motion, then alone, this has to be done and nowhere else.

**रक्तसुमाक्षतगन्धैः सम्पूज्य दिवाकरं नमस्कृत्य।  
प्रष्टा स्वशक्तिविभवैर्दैवज्ञं पूजयेद्ग्रहान् ध्यात्वा॥१६॥**

* Sloka* 16.—After performing Puja (worship) to the Sun-God with red flowers, camphor, rice and sandal and saluting him and worshipping the planets, the querist may honour the astrologer according to his means.

**आयुःप्रमाणमस्मिन् गतागतं वर्तमानमशुभशुभम्।  
एतत्सर्वं श्रोतुं भवत्प्रसादात् प्रयोगमिच्छामि॥१७॥**

* Sloka* 17.—“I wish to know the probable length of life, the good and bad in the past, present and the future ; all these results, I want to hear through your favour”.

**प्रारभ्य सन्मुहूर्ते सुचन्द्रताराबलान्विते प्रष्टुः।  
जातमखिलं च विलिखेन्नान्यमनाः स्वायुरादिकं प्रष्टुः॥१८॥**

* Sloka* 18.—Commencing at an auspicious Muhurta, when the Moon is benefic and endowed with the strength of the Nakshatra occupied by her, the astrologer should give an account in writing of all that has happened, that is now happening, and is going to happen, as regards the querist, and his longevity, etc., with the equanimity of mind.

**फलदं ज्योतिश्चक्रं ग्रहर्क्षचारस्तथैव गुणकारः।  
दैवज्ञः कालनरश्चैवं सम्भावयेन्नर श्रेष्ठः॥१९॥**

* Sloka* 19.—The Zodiac is fully effective; the planets and their transit through the several signs of the Zodiac is similarly productive of (good) effects. The astrologer and the Kala purusha—all these, the person concerned should duly honour with suitable presents.

**पृथुविरचितमन्यैः शास्त्रमेतत्समस्तं  
तदनुलघुमयेदं तत्प्रदिष्टार्थमेव।**

**कृतमिह हि समर्थ धीविषाणामलत्वे  
मम यदि न सदुक्तं सज्जनैः क्षम्यतां तत्॥२०॥**

* Sloka* 20.—The whole of this has been composed by me, in a succinct manner after a perusal of the meaning of the exhaustive works by others on the subject. I have only abridged them for sharpening the intellect of my readers. If anything has been done or described incorrectly through my ignorance, I crave the indulgence of the benevolent public to excuse the same.

**होराशास्त्रसमुद्रं प्रमथ्य धीमन्दराद्रिणा सम्यक्।  
लोकस्यालोककरः शास्त्रशशाङ्कः समुत्क्षिप्तः॥२१॥**

इति श्रीवराहमिहिरसुत श्रीपृथुयशोविरचिते होरासारे  
जातकलक्षणाध्यायोऽद्वात्रिंशः॥

* Sloka* 21.—Having churned well the ocean of Astrology with the intellect as the Churning Stick (Mandara inountain), the Moon in the form of this scientific treatise has been well taken out for lighting (enlightening) the entire world.

Thus ends the 32nd Adhyaya entitled “Jataka Lakshana”  
in Horasara, a work composed by Sri Prithuyasas,  
son of Sri Varahamihira.

**\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_ **

**श्लोकानुक्रमणिका**  
**————**

**आ (95)**
